# Obi-Wan Kenobi

[View source](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi?action=edit) 

* [History](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi?action=history)

:   "*You can kill me, but you will never destroy me. It takes strength to resist the dark side. Only the weak embrace it.*"  
    "*It is more powerful than you know.*"  
    "*And those who oppose it are more powerful than you'll ever be.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Maul — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ab/ObiWan-Maul-DarkSide.flac/revision/latest?cb=20251220051958)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:ObiWan-Maul-DarkSide.flac "File:ObiWan-Maul-DarkSide.flac"))[[16]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-16)

**Obi-Wan Kenobi** was a legendary [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") [human](/wiki/Human "Human") [male](/wiki/Gender "Gender") [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") who served on the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council") during the final [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") of the [Republic Era](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era"). As a [High Jedi General](/wiki/High_Jedi_General "High Jedi General"), Kenobi served in the [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic") that fought against the [Separatist Droid Army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army") during the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"), and was nicknamed "**the Negotiator**." Kenobi, however, was forced into [exile](/wiki/Exile_(punishment) "Exile (punishment)") as a result of the [Great Jedi Purge](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") initiated by the Republic's own [clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper") when Republic [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor"), secretly [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"), implemented [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66"). As a mentor, Kenobi was responsible for [training](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training") two members of the [Skywalker family](/wiki/Skywalker_family "Skywalker family"), [Anakin](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") and [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker"), both of whom served in turn as his [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") in the ways of [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force").

Kenobi was [born](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") on the [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Stewjon](/wiki/Stewjon "Stewjon") in [57 BBY](/wiki/57_BBY "57 BBY"). He was Force-sensitive, and therefore taken from [his family](/wiki/Kenobi_family "Kenobi family") and [inducted](/wiki/Jedi_Initiate "Jedi Initiate") into the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") as a [child](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling"). Raised in the [Jedi Grand Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace") on the planet [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant"), Kenobi was assigned to [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Qui-Gon Jinn](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn "Qui-Gon Jinn"). In [32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY "32 BBY"), Kenobi attained the rank of [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") by [defeating](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo") the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") [Darth Maul](/wiki/Maul "Maul") during the [Invasion of Naboo](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo"). He also chose to train Anakin Skywalker—the prophesied [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One") who was destined to destroy the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") and restore balance to the Force—having promised Jinn who [died](/wiki/Death "Death") in the [lightsaber duel](/wiki/Lightsaber_duel "Lightsaber duel") against Maul.

With the [advent](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis") of the [Clone](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") Wars in [22 BBY](/wiki/22_BBY "22 BBY"), Kenobi adopted the [military rank](/wiki/Military_rank "Military rank") of High Jedi General in the Grand [Army](/wiki/Army "Army") of the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic"), and was given command of the [Open Circle Fleet](/wiki/Open_Circle_Fleet "Open Circle Fleet"), the [Third Systems Army](/wiki/Third_Systems_Army "Third Systems Army"), and the [7th Sky Corps](/wiki/7th_Sky_Corps "7th Sky Corps"). [Clone Marshal Commander](/wiki/Clone_Marshal_Commander "Clone Marshal Commander") [Cody](/wiki/Cody "Cody") served as his second-in-command throughout [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy")-wide conflict, with their forces achieving multiple victories over the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems"). In the midst of the war, his old enemy Maul re-emerged into [galactic](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") affairs, bent on revenge against Kenobi for his debilitating defeat [decades](/wiki/Standard_decade "Standard decade") prior. Though they clashed in heated duels on multiple occasions, Maul failed to end Kenobi's life or cripple his spirit, despite murdering his former love, [Satine Kryze](/wiki/Satine_Kryze "Satine Kryze"), [Duchess](/wiki/Duchess "Duchess") of [Mandalore](/wiki/Mandalore "Mandalore").

In [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"), Kenobi killed the Separatist [Supreme Martial Commander](/wiki/Supreme_Martial_Commander_of_the_Separatist_Droid_Armies "Supreme Martial Commander of the Separatist Droid Armies"), [General](/wiki/General "General") [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous"), during the [Battle of Utapau](/wiki/Battle_of_Utapau "Battle of Utapau"), effectively ending the Clone Wars. He later survived the initial onslaught of the Great Jedi Purge against the Jedi Order, which resulted from the [machinations](/wiki/Grand_Plan "Grand Plan") of the Sith [Lord](/wiki/Lord "Lord") Darth Sidious. After discovering that Skywalker had turned to the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force"), becoming Sidious' [Sith apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice") under the name of [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Vader, Kenobi [defeated](/wiki/Duel_on_Mustafar "Duel on Mustafar") his former Padawan on [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar") and exiled himself to the [Outer Rim](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories") planet [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine") as the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") [rose to power](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era"). Adopting a [hermit](/wiki/Hermit "Hermit") lifestyle as "**Ben Kenobi**," he watched over Vader's and [Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala")'s son, Luke.

[Ten years later](/wiki/9_BBY "9 BBY"), Kenobi left exile to [rescue](/wiki/Search_for_Princess_Leia "Search for Princess Leia") [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo"), Luke's [twin](/wiki/Twin "Twin") sister, and was pursued by the Empire's [Inquisitorius](/wiki/Inquisitorius "Inquisitorius") and Vader himself. Later, Kenobi was hunted down once again by Maul, whom he finally slew to protect the young Luke. Kenobi began the boy's Jedi training in [1 BBY](/wiki/1_BBY "1 BBY"), and soon after [encountered](/wiki/Rescue_of_Princess_Leia "Rescue of Princess Leia") Vader aboard the [first](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station") [Death Star](/wiki/Death_Star "Death Star"), where he sacrificed himself to ensure that Luke and his allies escaped from the Sith Lord. In death, Kenobi became [one with the Force](/wiki/Immortality "Immortality") which allowed him to continue guiding Luke throughout the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War"). In [4 ABY](/wiki/4_ABY "4 ABY"), Kenobi reunited with his former student, Anakin Skywalker, who died [destroying](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor") his [Sith Master](/wiki/Sith_Master "Sith Master") in order to save his son. Kenobi was remembered as a legendary Jedi Master during the [rise](/wiki/New_Republic_Era "New Republic Era") of the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic"); [Ben Solo](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo"), the son of Luke's twin sister, Princess Leia Organa, was named after Kenobi. Solo's [turn to the dark side](/wiki/Destruction_of_the_Jedi_Temple "Destruction of the Jedi Temple") left Luke disillusioned with the Jedi Order's legacy, and he held Kenobi responsible for Anakin's transformation into Vader. However, Luke's faith would eventually be restored with the aid of Darth Sidious's granddaughter [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker"), to whom Kenobi would lend his voice and strength in a [final battle and victory](/wiki/Battle_of_Exegol "Battle of Exegol") against her resurrected ancestor on [Exegol](/wiki/Exegol "Exegol") in [35 ABY](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY").

## Biography

### Early life

:   "*As Jedi, we're taken from our families when we're very young. I still have glimpses, flashes really, my mother's shawl, my father's hands. I remember a baby. [...] I think I had a brother. Really don't remember him. I wished I did.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi[[10]](#cite_note-Kenobi_3-10)

Obi-Wan Kenobi was [born](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") on the [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Stewjon](/wiki/Stewjon "Stewjon") in [57 BBY](/wiki/57_BBY "57 BBY").[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) Despite being very [young](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling") when he left his [family](/wiki/Kenobi_family "Kenobi family"), he still had glimpses of [his father's](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi%27s_father "Obi-Wan Kenobi's father") [hands](/wiki/Hand "Hand"), his [mother's](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi%27s_mother "Obi-Wan Kenobi's mother") shawl and he remembered a [baby](/wiki/Unidentified_Kenobi_baby "Unidentified Kenobi baby") he believed to be his brother although he barely remembered him.[[10]](#cite_note-Kenobi_3-10)

### Joining the Jedi Order

:   "*…I never had problems with that as a youngling. Being independent, I mean. I broke rules right and left. They even called me rebellious. Probably the Masters were surprised anyone was willing to take me on as an apprentice.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi to Qui-Gon Jinn, about his early life — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/ObiWanKenobi-MA2.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250303212611)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:ObiWanKenobi-MA2.flac "File:ObiWanKenobi-MA2.flac"))[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18)

 [![Obi-Wan Kenobi as a Jedi youngling](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/57/YoungKenobi-AORObiWan1.png/revision/latest?cb=20220406012620) [![Obi-Wan Kenobi as a Jedi youngling](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/57/YoungKenobi-AORObiWan1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20220406012620)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/57/YoungKenobi-AORObiWan1.png/revision/latest?cb=20220406012620) 

Obi-Wan Kenobi as a Jedi youngling

 

When Kenobi was discovered to be [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive"), he was taken from his [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld") to the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace") on the [Core Worlds](/wiki/Core_Worlds "Core Worlds") planet [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant") to be [trained](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training") as a [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi")[[4]](#cite_note-USW_NE-4) within the first six [months](/wiki/Standard_month "Standard month") of his life.[[1]](#cite_note-Geektionary-1)[[4]](#cite_note-USW_NE-4) In the [Jedi crèche](/wiki/Jedi_cr%C3%A8che "Jedi crèche") he was placed with other [Jedi younglings](/wiki/Jedi_Initiate "Jedi Initiate")[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18) in the [Kybuck Clan](/wiki/Kybuck_Clan "Kybuck Clan") during his early [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year"), including his friends [Gehren](/wiki/Gehren_Rand "Gehren Rand")[[12]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_1-12) and [Prie](/wiki/Prie "Prie").[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18) Kenobi received basic Initiate training alongside his peers in the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order")'s Temple[[11]](#cite_note-Age_Kenobi-11) and began training in several simple [Force techniques](/wiki/Force_power "Force power") by the age of three[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18) in [54 BBY](/wiki/54_BBY "54 BBY").[[19]](#cite_note-SWCT-19)

Kenobi studied in the ways of [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force")[[1]](#cite_note-Geektionary-1) and Jedi traditions[[20]](#cite_note-There_is_Always_Another-20) under [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master") [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda"),[[1]](#cite_note-Geektionary-1) eventually coming to respect him and the [Jedi Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council") greatly.[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18) He also received instruction in the art of [lightsaber combat](/wiki/Lightsaber_combat "Lightsaber combat") from [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Cin Drallig](/wiki/Cin_Drallig "Cin Drallig")[[21]](#cite_note-Complete_Visual_New-21) in the basic [lightsaber](/wiki/Lightsaber "Lightsaber") forms and techniques.[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18) At some point before he was selected as a [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan"), Kenobi attended a class centered around [meditation](/wiki/Meditation "Meditation").[[11]](#cite_note-Age_Kenobi-11) Unlike how he acted as he got older,[[22]](#cite_note-Master_and_Apprentice-22) Kenobi, during his days as a youngling, gained a reputation for breaking rules and having a rebellious nature,[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18) resulting in very few Masters who were willing to train the boy as their Padawan.[[22]](#cite_note-Master_and_Apprentice-22) To curb Kenobi's behavior, Yoda searched for a teacher for Kenobi that had unorthodox methods, which would mold the student into rebelling by being dutiful.[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18)

### Qui-Gon Jinn's Padawan

#### Initial endeavors

:   "*It worries me, this misunderstanding between you and your Padawan. This isn't the first time you've reported such difficulties.*"  
    "*It worries me as well. Obi-Wan is strong in the Force, and eager to do his duty. The failure must be mine. Fundamentally, I fear we are a mismatch.*"
:   ―Depa Billaba and Qui-Gon Jinn, about Obi-Wan Kenobi's training — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/ObiWanKenobi-MA1.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250303212609)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:ObiWanKenobi-MA1.flac "File:ObiWanKenobi-MA1.flac"))[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18)

 [![Kenobi was chosen by Qui-Gon Jinn to be his Padawan.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/87/ObiWanKenobiPadawan-TLC.png/revision/latest?cb=20230613020519) [![Kenobi was chosen by Qui-Gon Jinn to be his Padawan.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/87/ObiWanKenobiPadawan-TLC.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230613020519)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/87/ObiWanKenobiPadawan-TLC.png/revision/latest?cb=20230613020519) 

Kenobi was chosen by Qui-Gon Jinn to be his Padawan.

 

Around [44 BBY](/wiki/44_BBY "44 BBY"),[[23]](#cite_note-Apprenticedate-23) Jedi Master [Qui-Gon Jinn](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn "Qui-Gon Jinn") chose Kenobi as his Padawan learner when he was thirteen years old. During his apprenticeship he became friends with [Jape](/wiki/Jape "Jape"), a fellow Padawan who he kept correspondence with, and also maintained contact with crèche-mate Prie[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18) and the [Mon Calamari](/wiki/Mon_Calamari "Mon Calamari") [Bant Eerin](/wiki/Bant_Eerin "Bant Eerin").[[24]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_&_Anakin_Adventure-24) In their first months together, Jinn attempted to adapt his teaching methods to suit Kenobi's strengths, but felt he failed to do so adequately.[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18) At some point during his training, Kenobi constructed his [first lightsaber](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi%27s_first_lightsaber "Obi-Wan Kenobi's first lightsaber"), modeled after Jinn's [lightsaber](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn%27s_lightsaber "Qui-Gon Jinn's lightsaber") hilt style and his own personality.[[25]](#cite_note-LightsabersEncyclopedia-25) As the pair struggled to establish a workable affinity, the Master continued to train his Padawan in the basic [cadences](/wiki/Cadence "Cadence") of lightsaber combat, preventing him from picking a specialty.[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18) Jinn was proud of his apprentice's skills, and sparred with him in training sessions[[11]](#cite_note-Age_Kenobi-11) while at the Temple between missions. Kenobi, in turn, spent a significant amount of [time](/wiki/Time "Time") in the training dojos to hone the techniques taught to him.[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18)

In their lessons, Jinn taught Kenobi that there was a strength and nobility in restraint.[[26]](#cite_note-SW7-26) As time passed, Kenobi's demeanor shifted to become more serious and respectful of the Council, in contrast to[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18) the maverick[[27]](#cite_note-SW_Book-27) Jinn's usual way of approaching situations based on his instincts in the present,[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18) even if that meant going against the Council's wishes.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_I-14) Both carried differing philosophies on focusing on the future versus the present, and interpreted the Force in varying ways. Despite their differences, Kenobi strived to be a good student, and supported his Master's hobbies regarding ancient Jedi prophecy research. To Kenobi's chagrin, the majority of his free time in the Temple was consumed by gathering information from the [Jedi Archives](/wiki/Jedi_Archives "Jedi Archives") and the [holocron of prophecy](/wiki/Holocron_of_prophecy "Holocron of prophecy") under the watchful [eye](/wiki/Eye "Eye") of the Jedi Master librarian [Jocasta Nu](/wiki/Jocasta_Nu "Jocasta Nu"). Over time, he learned the [language](/wiki/Language "Language") [Old Alderaanian](/wiki/Old_Alderaanian "Old Alderaanian"), which many of the [holocron](/wiki/Holocron "Holocron")'s prophecies were written in. As an escape from the workload, Kenobi played rounds of[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18) the game[[4]](#cite_note-USW_NE-4) [dejarik](/wiki/Dejarik "Dejarik") in the lower levels of Coruscant in the evenings after finishing his Master's research requests.[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18)

#### Early travels and visit to Kashyyyk

:   "*The Trandoshans—they capture and hunt for sport. And they knew today was Life Day. And they knew the Wookiees would be vulnerable. Come Obi-Wan…we have to stop them!*"
:   ―Qui-Gon Jinn to Obi-Wan Kenobi[[28]](#cite_note-Life_Day_Part_1-28)

 [![Obi-Wan Kenobi and Brennonn planning a rescue](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/BrennonnKenobi.png/revision/latest?cb=20220330233541) [![Obi-Wan Kenobi and Brennonn planning a rescue](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/BrennonnKenobi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220330233541)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/BrennonnKenobi.png/revision/latest?cb=20220330233541) 

Obi-Wan Kenobi and Brennonn planning a rescue

 

The pair's continuing training issues were discussed with Jedi Councilors [Depa Billaba](/wiki/Depa_Billaba "Depa Billaba") and [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu") in an attempt to find a remedy, without success. At some point during his time as a Padawan, Kenobi and Jinn visited a [fortress](/wiki/Chief%27s_fortress "Chief's fortress") on[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18) the planet[[4]](#cite_note-USW_NE-4) [Lah'mu](/wiki/Lah%27mu "Lah'mu"), the world [Alderaan](/wiki/Alderaan "Alderaan")'s [royal palace](/wiki/Royal_Palace_of_Alderaan "Royal Palace of Alderaan"), and[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18) the planets[[4]](#cite_note-USW_NE-4) [Ryloth](/wiki/Ryloth "Ryloth") and [Gatalenta](/wiki/Gatalenta "Gatalenta").[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18) While training, he became acquainted with the Jedi trainee [Siri Tachi](/wiki/Siri_Tachi "Siri Tachi") and developed some feelings for her, but refrained from acting on them.[[20]](#cite_note-There_is_Always_Another-20) Not long after Kenobi became Jinn's Padawan, he was eager to prove himself on a mission, but when he and Jinn were set to leave on one, his Master was nowhere to be found. Feeling angry by his master's abandonment, Kenobi decided to set off on the [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Lenahra "Mission to Lenahra") to the planet [Lenahra](/wiki/Lenahra "Lenahra") alone. While he was there, he encountered a group of teenagers and [datachips](/wiki/Datachip "Datachip") hidden on the world by the Jedi [Orla Jareni](/wiki/Orla_Jareni "Orla Jareni") long before his visit.[[29]](#cite_note-Padawan-29) He met a [Besalisk](/wiki/Besalisk "Besalisk") named [Dexter Jettster](/wiki/Dexter_Jettster "Dexter Jettster"), who became a close friend.[[30]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-30)

During his training, Kenobi traveled to[[28]](#cite_note-Life_Day_Part_1-28) the planet[[4]](#cite_note-USW_NE-4) [Kashyyyk](/wiki/Kashyyyk "Kashyyyk") with his Master during the [Life Day](/wiki/Life_Day "Life Day") holiday. Jinn used the trip to teach his student about the Wookiee's way of life and harmony, and how it related to their own connection to the Force. The festivities slightly overwhelmed Kenobi, though he took the lessons to heart, and met one of Jinn's acquaintances, the Wookiee [Brennonn](/wiki/Brennonn "Brennonn"). However, their gathering was interrupted by [Trandoshans](/wiki/Trandoshan "Trandoshan") who captured several Wookiees, intending to use them in a [hunt](/wiki/Hunting "Hunting") for sport. Despite Kenobi's best efforts, Jinn was snared in a net as well and taken away.[[28]](#cite_note-Life_Day_Part_1-28)

Though held captive, Jinn believed that his Padawan would rescue him from the Trandoshan hunters. Kenobi, though reluctant to put any more Wookiees in danger, formulated a plan with Brennonn to break the imprisoned individuals free. He proceeded to surrender himself to the Trandoshans, claiming that as a simple student, he stood no chance against them. While conversing with the hunters' leader, Kenobi subtly used the Force to open the cage holding Jinn. Once both Jedi brandished their lightsabers, several other Wookiees rushed to the scene and assisted in setting their friends free. After the situation was settled, the Wookiees opted to leave the group in peace, citing Life Day as reason to pursue a resolution without violence. When back at the festivities area, Kenobi remained confused as to why Jinn did not break himself free. However, the Master informed him that it was intended as a learning experience, and to gain insight from Wookiee perspectives on life.[[31]](#cite_note-Life_Day_Part_2-31)

#### Protecting Satine Kryze

:   "*You and Satine have a history.*"  
    "*An extended mission when I was younger. Master Qui-Gon and I spent a year on Mandalore protecting the duchess from insurgents who had threatened her world. They sent Bounty hunters after us. We were always on the run, living hand-to-mouth, never sure what the next day would bring.*"
:   ―Anakin Skywalker and Obi-Wan Kenobi[[32]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot-32)

Sometime between the years [41 BBY](/wiki/41_BBY "41 BBY") and [39 BBY](/wiki/39_BBY "39 BBY"),[[33]](#cite_note-Mandalore_date-33) Kenobi and Jinn spent a year on the planet [Mandalore](/wiki/Mandalore "Mandalore") protecting [Duchess](/wiki/Duchess "Duchess") [Satine Kryze](/wiki/Satine_Kryze "Satine Kryze") from insurgents who were [threatening](/wiki/Great_Clan_Wars "Great Clan Wars") her world. [Bounty hunters](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") were sent after them, forcing them to live as fugitives, never knowing what the next day would bring them.[[34]](#cite_note-Voyage_of_Temptation-34) The mission forced them to work and fight together as a team, resulting in them forging a close bond.[[35]](#cite_note-KenobiShadow-35)

Kryze called Kenobi by the nickname "Ben."[[30]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-30) During that time, they had an incident with a swarm of [venom-mites](/wiki/Venom-mite "Venom-mite") on the terrestrial object [Draboon](/wiki/Draboon "Draboon"), where Kenobi carried Kryze to safety. However, he fell and dropped the Duchess, who then acquired a scar as a result. Kenobi fell in love with Satine during his stay on Mandalore, but despite his feelings toward her, he continued with his training and was reassigned to another mission after his objectives were complete. Kenobi regretted leaving her, but ultimately followed the [Jedi Code](/wiki/Jedi_Code "Jedi Code") he had sworn to live by. Meanwhile, Satine chose to stay and lead her people, having not asked Kenobi to stay, knowing it would have been a difficult choice.[[34]](#cite_note-Voyage_of_Temptation-34)

#### Incident on Teth

:   "*Master? Are you all right?*"  
    "*Just get us a ship if you can!*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Qui-Gon Jinn on Teth — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/ObiWanKenobi-MA3.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250303212612)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:ObiWanKenobi-MA3.flac "File:ObiWanKenobi-MA3.flac"))[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18)

 [![Kenobi and his Master were sent to Teth on a mission.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/72/Teth-TVE.png/revision/latest?cb=20190423045047) [![Kenobi and his Master were sent to Teth on a mission.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/72/Teth-TVE.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/170?cb=20190423045047)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/72/Teth-TVE.png/revision/latest?cb=20190423045047) 

Kenobi and his Master were sent to Teth on a mission.

 

In [40 BBY](/wiki/40_BBY "40 BBY"),[[23]](#cite_note-Apprenticedate-23) Kenobi and Jinn were [sent](/wiki/Mission_to_Teth "Mission to Teth") to the planet [Teth](/wiki/Teth "Teth") to investigate the disappearance of agricultural shipments through the [Triellus trade route](/wiki/Triellus_Trade_Route "Triellus Trade Route"). The pair ran into difficulties finding information, and their investigations quickly aroused the suspicions of the guilty parties. As their situation rapidly turned violent, Kenobi and Jinn stormed a building, using their lightsaber skills to force their way through the compound. In the chaos, Jinn felt that Kenobi was not responding to instructions well, and chose to make an escape.[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18)

Jinn instructed Kenobi to find a [ship](/wiki/Starship "Starship"), though the Padawan failed to do so upon being stopped in a hangar. Kenobi was briefly held hostage by [Wanbo](/wiki/Wanbo "Wanbo") the Hutt's [majordomo](/wiki/Majordomo "Majordomo"), [Thurible](/wiki/Thurible "Thurible"), but was soon released in exchange for Wanbo, who had been captured by Jinn. Eventually, the Jedi managed to depart the planet after making tenuous peace with Wanbo. Though both Jedi attempted to remain lighthearted about the outcome of the mission, Kenobi felt that he had failed his Master.[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18)

Once on Coruscant, Jinn recounted the communication issues that had plagued him and Kenobi during the Teth mission to the Jedi Council. While citing their continued inability to form a strong bond, he surmised that they may not have been meant to be a pair. Jinn received an invitation to join the Council after the mission, which displeased Kenobi when he found out shortly after during a meeting with [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") [Kirames Kaj](/wiki/Kirames_Kaj "Kirames Kaj"). Jinn resolved to make a decision regarding the invitation after meditation, knowing accepting the invite would result in Kenobi's reassignment to another Master.[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18)

#### Mission to Pijal

:   "*The Jedi Council—the Council has named me the rightful representative of the Republic, for the purposes of the ceremony.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, on Pijal — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b0/ObiWanKenobi-MA4.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250303212614)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:ObiWanKenobi-MA4.flac "File:ObiWanKenobi-MA4.flac"))[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18)

 [![Obi-Wan, during the mission to Pijal](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/PijalCover.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210404112612) [![Obi-Wan, during the mission to Pijal](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/PijalCover.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/197?cb=20210404112612)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/PijalCover.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210404112612) 

Obi-Wan, during the mission to Pijal

 

[Days](/wiki/Standard_day "Standard day") after his mission to Teth, a [political](/wiki/Politics "Politics") dispute erupted on the [Inner Rim](/wiki/Inner_Rim_Territories "Inner Rim Territories") planet [Pijal](/wiki/Pijal "Pijal"), which caught the attention of Kaj. Initial reports suggested a performance troupe called the [Opposition](/wiki/Opposition "Opposition") was engaging in increasingly violent initiatives protesting the signing of the [Governance Treaty](/wiki/Governance_Treaty "Governance Treaty")— a move would end the absolutist [monarchy](/wiki/Pijali_monarchy "Pijali monarchy"). Jinn and Kenobi were informed that [Lord](/wiki/Lord "Lord") [Regent](/wiki/Regent "Regent") [Rael Averross](/wiki/Rael_Averross "Rael Averross") had requested their aid on the planet and its [moon](/wiki/Pijal%27s_moon "Pijal's moon") to curb the attacks, discover more about their origins, and ensure the opening of the [Pijal Hyperspace Corridor](/wiki/Pijal_Hyperspace_Corridor "Pijal Hyperspace Corridor") [hyperspace route](/wiki/Hyperspace_route "Hyperspace route"). Both Jedi were additionally instructed to to protect the [Pijali](/wiki/Pijali "Pijali") [Crown](/wiki/Crown "Crown") [Princess](/wiki/Princess "Princess") [Fanry](/wiki/Fanry "Fanry") until she could sign the treaty at her [coronation](/wiki/Coronation_of_Queen_Fanry "Coronation of Queen Fanry"), and ratify the initiative on behalf of the Republic.[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18)

Kenobi and Jinn were dispatched to the planet, and the Master took the opportunity to inform his Padawan about Averross's training under Dooku. Upon their arrival to the [Pijal system](/wiki/Pijal_system "Pijal system"), they spotted several [soulcraft](/wiki/Soulcraft "Soulcraft") vessels suffering from [plasma](/wiki/Plasma "Plasma") attacks, and moved to save the ships. Helped by an antiplasma charge, Kenobi and Jinn rescued several soulcraft and the slaves inside. Jinn and Kenobi were regally greeted by Fanry upon their arrival to the [Pijali palace](/wiki/Pijali_palace "Pijali palace"). Upon being briefed on the situation, the pair used a small [shuttle](/wiki/Shuttle "Shuttle") to meet with the [gemstone](/wiki/Gemstone "Gemstone") thieves [Rahara Wick](/wiki/Rahara_Wick "Rahara Wick") and [Pax Maripher](/wiki/Pax_Maripher "Pax Maripher") on the world's [moon](/wiki/Moon "Moon"). After some negotiation, the thieves agreed to assist the Jedi in their search for the Opposition and its leader, [Halin Azucca](/wiki/Halin_Azucca "Halin Azucca").[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18)

Kenobi and Jinn made several trips to the moon, and their scans for the Opposition came up unsuccessful. While on the palace grounds, Kenobi participated in the ritual [Grand Hunt](/wiki/Grand_Hunt "Grand Hunt") while riding a [Pijal varactyl](/wiki/Pijal_varactyl "Pijal varactyl"). During the ceremonial hunt, the [crab droid](/wiki/LM-432_crab_droid "LM-432 crab droid") prey of the event attacked Fanry, prompting Kenobi to destroy the threat. Upon investigation, he and his Master concluded that the sabotage must have been conducted by someone within the palace, and not the Opposition.[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18)

Eventually, Kenobi and Jinn met with Azucca on Pijal's moon, and she claimed that her group of performance artists had been framed for the attacks blamed on them. With this knowledge, Jinn refused to ratify the Governance Treaty at Fanry's upcoming coronation after receiving a violent [Force vision](/wiki/Force_vision "Force vision") about the events. Azucca later provided information to the Jedi proving that the attacks on Czerka facilities were found to have originated from [blackguards](/wiki/Blackguard "Blackguard"), a division of the Pijali [royal guards](/wiki/Royal_guard_(Pijal) "Royal guard (Pijal)") secretly under the orders of Captain [Deren](/wiki/Deren "Deren") and Fanry.[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18)

Kenobi, knowing that Jinn would refuse to sign the treaty, was appointed to ratify the initiative on the Republic's behalf in his place by the Jedi Council. However, at Fanry's coronation, the princess violently seized power as an absolute monarch to prevent the signing of the treaty, decrying democracy. Kenobi attempted to protect the [Skykeeper](/wiki/Unidentified_Skykeeper "Unidentified Skykeeper") leader from her when Fanry ordered the [death](/wiki/Death "Death") of those she percieved had betrayed her. Kenobi listened to Fanry's speech about the greed of her elders, and used his [kohlen crystal](/wiki/Kohlen_crystal "Kohlen crystal") sabotaged lightsaber to attack Deren. Following the injury of her captain, the newly crowned queen escaped the [Celestial Chalice](/wiki/Celestial_Chalice "Celestial Chalice") where the event had been held with her confidante [Cady](/wiki/Cady "Cady"), leaving the Skykeeper, the [jeweler](/wiki/Unidentified_court_jeweler "Unidentified court jeweler"), and Kenobi behind.[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18)

While Jinn tried to negotiate with Fanry over [hologram](/wiki/Hologram "Hologram"), Kenobi helped the slaves aboard the Czerka cruiser, *[Leverage](/wiki/Leverage "Leverage"),* with Maripher's help. Eventually, Cady ended her rule by holding her at [blaster](/wiki/Blaster "Blaster")-point until she surrendered. However, because Fanry had threatened to harm Kenobi while he was acting as a Republic representative, the crowning was deemed illegitimate. Kenobi and Jinn helped the planet establish a democratic [Assembly](/wiki/Assembly_(Pijal) "Assembly (Pijal)") after Fanry's abdication, and reported back to Coruscant afterwards. Kenobi felt that the mission had been one of the first that he and his Master were able to work well together.[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18) However, he also realized that his pairing with Jinn had strengthened his resolve to be a "Perfect Jedi" and follow the Jedi Code in all aspects, if only to be rebellious towards an unorthodox teacher.[[20]](#cite_note-There_is_Always_Another-20)

#### Saving Th'er

:   "*Where are we heading, Master?*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi to Qui-Gon Jinn when escaping from the Metal Clan[[36]](#cite_note-Age_Jinn-36)

 [![Obi-Wan during the rescue of priestess Th'er](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4f/ObiWanPiloting-AORQuiGonJinn1.png/revision/latest?cb=20181215070531) [![Obi-Wan during the rescue of priestess Th'er](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4f/ObiWanPiloting-AORQuiGonJinn1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/190?cb=20181215070531)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4f/ObiWanPiloting-AORQuiGonJinn1.png/revision/latest?cb=20181215070531) 

Obi-Wan during the rescue of priestess Th'er

 

The Jedi Order later sent Kenobi and Jinn to the planet [Bri'n](/wiki/Bri%27n "Bri'n") to resolve a [conflict](/wiki/Conflict_on_Bri%27n "Conflict on Bri'n") on the world. On Bri'n, the [leader](/wiki/Metal_Clan_leader "Metal Clan leader") of the [Metal Clan](/wiki/Metal_Clan "Metal Clan") attempted to capture [priestess](/wiki/Priestess "Priestess") [Th'er](/wiki/Th%27er "Th'er") so that either her word or her [blood](/wiki/Blood "Blood") could be used to destroy her [trees](/wiki/Tree "Tree"). Surrounded by forces of the Metal Clan, Jinn chose to escape with Th'er in an [*Eta*-class shuttle](/wiki/Eta-class_shuttle "Eta-class shuttle") and return to Coruscant. Once on planet, Kenobi watched, without interjection, as Th'er attempted to convince Qui-Gon to intervene in her conflict. However, she eventually chose to seek allies on Coruscant instead.[[36]](#cite_note-Age_Jinn-36)

#### Operating near Botor

:   "*Holy…blaster bolts. How did [Yoda] take out a whole room full of pirates?*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi[[37]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_26-37)

 [![Obi-Wan and Qui-Gon landed on Botor, to discover Yoda rescued a young Force-sensitive child from a pirate gang who attempted to sell him.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3c/ObiWanAndQuiGon-2015StarWars26.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220328071739) [![Obi-Wan and Qui-Gon landed on Botor, to discover Yoda rescued a young Force-sensitive child from a pirate gang who attempted to sell him.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3c/ObiWanAndQuiGon-2015StarWars26.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/233?cb=20220328071739)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3c/ObiWanAndQuiGon-2015StarWars26.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220328071739) 

Obi-Wan and Qui-Gon landed on Botor, to discover Yoda rescued a young Force-sensitive child from a pirate gang who attempted to sell him.

 

At some point around [40 BBY](/wiki/40_BBY "40 BBY"),[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) Jinn and Kenobi were operating in the vicinity of a [planet](/wiki/Botor "Botor") that served as a base of the [Flesh Mongers](/wiki/Flesh_Mongers "Flesh Mongers") [pirate](/wiki/Pirate "Pirate") group, flying a pair of [Delta-7 *Aethersprite*-class light interceptors](/wiki/Delta-7_Aethersprite-class_light_interceptor "Delta-7 Aethersprite-class light interceptor"). The two received a message from the surface of the planet from Jedi Master Yoda, who was asking for assistance. Landing on the planet, Jinn and Kenobi discovered that Yoda had taken out the entire pirate gang in order to rescue a young Force-sensitive child, known as [Lo](/wiki/Lo "Lo"), as the pirate had planned to sell him due to his abilities in the Force. After leaving the child in Kenobi and Jinn's care, Yoda departed for his next objective.[[37]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_26-37)

### Invasion of Naboo

#### Ambassadors to the Supreme Chancellor

:   "*I have a bad feeling about this.*"  
    "*I don't sense anything.*"  
    "*It's not about the mission, Master. It's something elsewhere… elusive.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Qui-Gon Jinn — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/39/BadFeelingAboutThis-TPM.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250407192615)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:BadFeelingAboutThis-TPM.flac "File:BadFeelingAboutThis-TPM.flac"))[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_I-14)

 [![Kenobi during the invasion of Naboo](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/PadawanKenobi-TPM.png/revision/latest?cb=20240526152512) [![Kenobi during the invasion of Naboo](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/PadawanKenobi-TPM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/215?cb=20240526152512)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/PadawanKenobi-TPM.png/revision/latest?cb=20240526152512) 

Kenobi during the invasion of Naboo

 

In 32 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system"),[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) by the time Jinn considered Kenobi to be ready for his [trials](/wiki/Jedi_Trials "Jedi Trials"), they were sent by Galactic Republic Supreme Chancellor [Finis Valorum](/wiki/Finis_Valorum "Finis Valorum") to negotiate with the [Trade Federation](/wiki/Trade_Federation "Trade Federation"), who had set up a [blockade](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo") around the planet of [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo").[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_I-14) Both Jedi extensively studied political documents and trade relations between the parties prior to the endeavor, sensing its necessity.[[38]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-38) The two Jedi were tasked with negotiating a settlement with Trade Federation representatives.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_I-14)

The pair traveled to the system on the [*Consular*-class space cruiser](/wiki/Consular-class_light_cruiser "Consular-class light cruiser") *[Radiant VII](/wiki/Radiant_VII "Radiant VII")* and landed on the modified [*Lucrehulk*-class LH-3210 cargo freighter](/wiki/Lucrehulk-class_LH-3210_cargo_freighter "Lucrehulk-class LH-3210 cargo freighter") *[Saak'ak](/wiki/Saak%27ak "Saak'ak")*, the [flagship](/wiki/Flagship "Flagship") of the [blockade](/wiki/Blockade "Blockade"). There, Kenobi and Jinn were brought to a conference room, where [protocol droid](/wiki/Protocol_droid "Protocol droid") [TC-14](/wiki/TC-14 "TC-14") informed them that a Trade Federation representative would be with them shortly, and invited the pair to make themselves comfortable. However, upon learning that the pair were Jedi from TC-14, [Viceroy](/wiki/Viceroy "Viceroy") [Nute Gunray](/wiki/Nute_Gunray "Nute Gunray") of the Trade Federation instead sent the protocol droid back into the room to distract them, with the droid offering Kenobi and Jinn drinks. Gunray then ordered his security to get rid of the Jedi and their assets, with an overhead [turret](/wiki/Turret "Turret") destroying the *Radiant VII* and its crew.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_I-14)

The two Jedi sensed the loss of their vessel and rose from their seats, drawing their lightsabers before noticing [poisonous](/wiki/Poison "Poison") [dioxis](/wiki/Dioxis "Dioxis") [gas](/wiki/Gas "Gas") being pumped into the room around them and holding their breaths. [OOM-series security droids](/wiki/OOM-series_security_droid "OOM-series security droid") were then sent to confirm that the Jedi were dead, however Kenobi and Jinn escaped into the hallway and destroyed the [battle droids](/wiki/Battle_droid "Battle droid") before making their way to the *Saak'ak*'s bridge. Kenobi held off the battle droids while Jinn attempted to cut through the doors to the bridge. However, [droidekas](/wiki/Droideka "Droideka") summoned by Gunray arrived, and the two Jedi were forced to flee into a nearby ventilation shaft, using [Force speed](/wiki/Force_Dash "Force Dash") to escape. The two [escaped](/wiki/Escape_from_the_Saak%27ak "Escape from the Saak'ak") to Naboo's surface by stowing away on separate [C-9979 landing crafts](/wiki/C-9979_landing_craft "C-9979 landing craft") in the Saak'ak's [hangar](/wiki/Hangar "Hangar") bay, discovering a droid [army](/wiki/Army "Army") preparing to invade Naboo in the process.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_I-14)

#### Rescuing Queen Amidala

After arriving on Naboo, Kenobi was attacked by two Federation [Single Trooper Aerial Platforms](/wiki/Single_Trooper_Aerial_Platform "Single Trooper Aerial Platform") while en route to Jinn's location. He was rescued by his Master, who was accompanied by [Jar Jar Binks](/wiki/Jar_Jar_Binks "Jar Jar Binks"), a member of Naboo's native [Gungan](/wiki/Gungan "Gungan") [species](/wiki/Species "Species"). After some debate, Binks agreed to lead the two Jedi to [Otoh Gunga](/wiki/Otoh_Gunga "Otoh Gunga"), a hidden [underwater](/wiki/Water "Water") Gungan [city](/wiki/City "City") where the group was brought before the Gungan leader [Boss](/wiki/Boss "Boss") [Nass](/wiki/Rugor_Nass "Rugor Nass"). Though unable to convince the Gungans to help the humans of Naboo, Jinn [influenced](/wiki/Mind_trick "Mind trick") Nass to obtain [transport](/wiki/Tribubble_bongo "Tribubble bongo"), to allow them to reach Naboo's [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") [Theed](/wiki/Theed "Theed"). [Piloting](/wiki/Pilot "Pilot") the transport through the planet's [core](/wiki/Naboo_Abyss "Naboo Abyss"), the trio was attacked by an [Opee sea killer](/wiki/Opee_sea_killer "Opee sea killer") at one point, which led to the ship being damaged and electronic systems shutting down. Kenobi quickly fixed the issue with some rewiring, and after a brief encounter with a [Sando aqua monster](/wiki/Sando_aqua_monster "Sando aqua monster"), Kenobi, Jinn, and Binks reached Theed.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_I-14)

Upon their arrival, the group discovered that the Trade Federation had already taken control of Theed, finding empty streets. The two Jedi came across a group of battle droids taking [Queen](/wiki/Monarch_of_Naboo "Monarch of Naboo") [Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala") and several others to an internment camp, and quickly engaged the droids, freeing the queen and her companions. Following this, the Jedi moved to a nearby hangar, intending to use a Naboo starship to take the queen to Coruscant. Kenobi moved to liberate several pilots who were held [prisoner](/wiki/Prisoner "Prisoner") by battle droids, while his master took the rest of their group to a ship. After a brief skirmish, the group fled Naboo in the queen's [starship](/wiki/Naboo_Royal_Starship "Naboo Royal Starship") in an attempt to reach Coruscant with news of the Trade Federation invasion. During the escape, the ship's [hyperdrive](/wiki/Hyperdrive "Hyperdrive") was damaged by droid [starfighters](/wiki/Starfighter "Starfighter"), preventing them from jumping straight to Coruscant and forcing them to instead land on [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine") for repairs.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_I-14)

#### Return of the Sith

 [![Kenobi meets Anakin Skywalker.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6a/NiceToMeetYouFutureMassMurderer-TPM.png/revision/latest?cb=20200915083929) [![Kenobi meets Anakin Skywalker.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6a/NiceToMeetYouFutureMassMurderer-TPM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200915083929)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6a/NiceToMeetYouFutureMassMurderer-TPM.png/revision/latest?cb=20200915083929) 

Kenobi meets Anakin Skywalker.

 

After landing on the [desert](/wiki/Desert "Desert") world, Kenobi remained on the ship, while Jinn, Binks, the droid [R2-D2](/wiki/R2-D2 "R2-D2"), and Amidala, who was disguised as a [handmaiden](/wiki/Naboo_Royal_Handmaidens "Naboo Royal Handmaidens"), went to search for a new hyperdrive unit. While searching, Jinn discovered [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"), a young enslaved human from whom he retrieved a blood sample for analysis, believing the child to be strong in the Force. Jinn sent the data to Kenobi on the ship, with instructions for Kenobi to analyze it. Kenobi's analysis revealed that the boy's [midi-chlorian](/wiki/Midi-chlorian "Midi-chlorian") count was higher than that of any Jedi. When Jinn arrived, accompanied by Skywalker, [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") [Maul](/wiki/Maul "Maul"), a Sith apprentice, attacked Jinn prompting Kenobi to order the ship to take off, with Jinn leaping into the ship as it ascended. The group then proceeded to Coruscant.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_I-14)

Upon their arrival on the planet, Jinn and Kenobi went directly to the Jedi Council to report on the mysterious attacker, whom Jinn believed to be a [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord"). After being briefed on what to do about their mysterious attacker, Jinn discussed about Skywalker with the Council, believing him to be the [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One"). Nevertheless, the Council was determined that the boy not be trained. However, Jinn persevered, telling them that he would take the boy as his Padawan, despite the Jedi Code's restrictions, but Kenobi insisted he was ready to take the trials, and his master agreed. Instead of discussing the matter further, Mace Windu sent the pair back to Naboo to protect the Queen and also as an attempt to lure out the mysterious assailant.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_I-14)

 [![Obi-Wan Kenobi fighting Darth Maul after his Master was impaled.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/Kenobi_Maul_clash.png/revision/latest?cb=20200915084106) [![Obi-Wan Kenobi fighting Darth Maul after his Master was impaled.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/Kenobi_Maul_clash.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/262?cb=20200915084106)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/Kenobi_Maul_clash.png/revision/latest?cb=20200915084106) 

Obi-Wan Kenobi fighting Darth Maul after his Master was impaled.

 

After returning to Naboo, Binks located the Gungans and Amidala, revealing herself to be the true Queen, [begged](/wiki/Boss_Meetup "Boss Meetup") Boss Nass to provide assistance in fighting the droid armies of the Trade Federation. Boss Nass agreed to [fight](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo") the droids as a diversion, while the Queen's forces slipped into Theed and captured Gunray. However, they soon encountered Maul once again and engaged in a duel with him, biding time for Amidala and her forces to reach the throne room. During the duel with Maul, Kenobi was separated from his master and forced to watch as Maul impaled Jinn with [his](/wiki/Darth_Maul%27s_double-bladed_lightsaber "Darth Maul's double-bladed lightsaber") [double-bladed lightsaber](/wiki/Double-bladed_lightsaber "Double-bladed lightsaber") so, when the opportunity arose, Kenobi, filled with rage, retaliated against the Sith. However, the [Dathomirian](/wiki/Dathomirian "Dathomirian") [Zabrak](/wiki/Zabrak "Zabrak") gained the upper hand and knocked Kenobi into a nearby shaft, where he was barely able to grab onto a knob jutting out from the side before falling to his death. Maul used this opportunity to kick his lightsaber into the shaft. Despite his predicament, Kenobi was able to use his Jinn's lightsaber to [cut](/wiki/Dismemberment "Dismemberment") the Sith in half, whose body fell down the shaft, presumably dead. Kenobi then ran to his master's side and promised a dying Jinn that he would train Skywalker.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_I-14)

### Master of the Chosen One

#### The first years

:   "*Confer on you the level of Jedi Knight, the Council does. But agree with your taking this boy as your Padawan learner, I do not.*"  
    "*Qui-Gon believed in him.*"  
    "*The Chosen One, the boy may be. Nevertheless, grave danger, I fear, in his training.*"
:   ―Yoda and Obi-Wan Kenobi — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/53/ObiWanKnighted-TPM.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250407192800)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:ObiWanKnighted-TPM.flac "File:ObiWanKnighted-TPM.flac"))[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_I-14)

 [![Kenobi and Skywalker at Jinn's funeral.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/You_will_be_a_Jedi.png/revision/latest?cb=20240220053910) [![Kenobi and Skywalker at Jinn's funeral.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/You_will_be_a_Jedi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20240220053910)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/You_will_be_a_Jedi.png/revision/latest?cb=20240220053910) 

Kenobi and Skywalker at Jinn's funeral.

 

Following the end of the Battle of Naboo, Kenobi was promoted to the rank of [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") by the Council, with Yoda reluctantly accepting his decision to train Skywalker. Kenobi was later present during Jinn's [funeral](/wiki/Jedi_funeral "Jedi funeral"), where he informed the boy that he would become a Jedi.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_I-14) Along with Amidala and her court, Kenobi and Skywalker remained at the funeral long after the Jedi Council had left, waiting until every last ember had gone out.[[38]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-38) Though he deeply grieved the loss of his teacher, Kenobi also felt that Jinn had abruptly cast him aside in favor of prophecies and unbending belief in Skywalker as the Chosen One. Nonetheless, as he watched his mentor's body in its final moments, he promised that he would chose to believe the prophecies.[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18) Later on, Kenobi, alongside his new Padawan and several members of the Jedi Council, took part in a victory celebration in Theed.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_I-14)

During his first year as Skywalker's Master, he sometimes woke up at night to see his Padawan was sleeping on the floor next to his bed; he realized Skywalker, having lost both his mother and Jinn, was clinging onto him, desperate to ensure his new master did not vanish one night.[[20]](#cite_note-There_is_Always_Another-20) During one of their many adventures, Kenobi fell into a nest of [gundarks](/wiki/Gundark "Gundark"), prompting Skywalker to rescue him.[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39) At the Jedi Temple, Kenobi trained Skywalker in meditation and levitating rocks. Though Skywalker wished to know more about his mentor's early life, he did not remember much of it by that point.[[11]](#cite_note-Age_Kenobi-11) Kenobi had several misgivings toward taking on Skywalker as his Padawan, but stuck to his firm commitment of honoring his late master's dying wish. But Kenobi was still mourning Jinn, and he began to have the perspective that Skywalker got a very raw deal being forced to be with a master who was hardly fit to be a teacher and had just barely got beyond the Jedi trials himself.[[40]](#cite_note-Family_at_War-40)

#### Mission to Dallenor

:   "*Thank you for coming master Jedi. My name is Clatriffe. I'm in charge of the Dallenor excavation.*"
:   ―Clatriffe[[11]](#cite_note-Age_Kenobi-11)

Kenobi was given a [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Dallenor "Mission to Dallenor") to go to the planet [Dallenor](/wiki/Dallenor "Dallenor"), where an archaeology team had discovered a [Jedi holocron](/wiki/Jedi_holocron "Jedi holocron"). Kenobi decided to take Skywalker with him as part of his training. Kenobi went to the Temple Archives to find information on Dallenor and about any Jedi that went there, to no avail. He told Master Yoda that he would bring his apprentice with him, to which Yoda surprisingly agreed. Kenobi and Skywalker took a [T-6 shuttle](/wiki/T-6_shuttle "T-6 shuttle") to Dallenor.[[11]](#cite_note-Age_Kenobi-11)

 [![Kenobi prepares to defend against the Krypder Riders.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/MissionToDallenor-AORObiWan1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190105195733) [![Kenobi prepares to defend against the Krypder Riders.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/MissionToDallenor-AORObiWan1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190105195733)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/MissionToDallenor-AORObiWan1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190105195733) 

Kenobi prepares to defend against the Krypder Riders.

 

Upon their arrival, Kenobi met mistress [Clatriffe](/wiki/Clatriffe "Clatriffe"), who told of her troubles with the local pirates. Kenobi was told of Clatriffe's discovery of centuries-old droids and how she had to hire several of the locals for protection. Kenobi examined the Holocron, but did not open it due to the arrival of the [Krypder Riders](/wiki/Krypder_Riders "Krypder Riders") and their leader, [Hudso Shaku](/wiki/Hudso_Shaku "Hudso Shaku"). Kenobi attempted to convince them to leave, but Shaku and the riders demanded the artifacts and [Kenobi's lightsaber](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi%27s_second_lightsaber "Obi-Wan Kenobi's second lightsaber"). Kenobi fought the riders and subdued them. Kenobi then saw that Shaku had taken Skywalker hostage and demanded his lightsaber. Before Obi-Wan could give a reply, Anakin was able to knock Shaku out with rocks.[[11]](#cite_note-Age_Kenobi-11)

#### Other adventures with Skywalker and a crisis of faith

:   "*To leave the Order, does Anakin wish?*"  
    "*Possibly, Master Yoda. He believes that his path lies elsewhere. He wishes to leave his training behind, at least for now. He says he will return, but… I don't know where I* failed*. I have done my best to* teach *him. He* belongs *here. He's not* ready*. He's too* young*.*"  
    "*As are you, Obi-Wan. As are you. Your fault it is not. A child Anakin remains. His path before coming to us…difficult. His questions…natural.*"
:   ―Yoda and Jedi Knight Obi-Wan Kenobi debate about the future of Anakin Skywalker[[41]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_&_Anakin_1-41)

 [![Jedi Knight Obi-Wan Kenobi](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/ObiWan_hood.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070930051008) [![Jedi Knight Obi-Wan Kenobi](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/ObiWan_hood.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/170?cb=20070930051008)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/ObiWan_hood.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070930051008) 

Jedi Knight Obi-Wan Kenobi

 

A couple of years later, Obi-Wan and Anakin traveled to the planet [Ilum](/wiki/Ilum "Ilum") so that Skywalker could build [his first lightsaber](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker%27s_first_lightsaber "Anakin Skywalker's first lightsaber");[[42]](#cite_note-SW:AEYNTK-42) after its construction, Kenobi said to him, "Anakin, this weapon is your life."[[43]](#cite_note-Hostage_Crisis-43)[[44]](#cite_note-The_Big_Bang-44) When Skywalker was twelve years old, Kenobi was assigned a mission to study a [star system](/wiki/Unidentified_dead_star_system "Unidentified dead star system") that revolved, seemingly impossibly, around a [dead dwarf star](/wiki/Black_dwarf "Black dwarf"). Upon realizing Skywalker had secretly snuck aboard his starship, Kenobi elected to turn the mission into a teaching experience, telling Skywalker of the dead [star](/wiki/Star "Star") as a metaphor for how Jedi needed to learn to let go of their attachments.[[30]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-30) Despite his initial misgivings about Skywalker, having once believed him to be dangerous and would do more harm than good, Kenobi soon grew to view the boy as a his equal, finding a partner in their missions, and came to see him as his brother.[[40]](#cite_note-Family_at_War-40)

At some point, Kenobi and Skywalker, during a mission in which they were they were joined by Jedi Master [Shaak Ti](/wiki/Shaak_Ti "Shaak Ti"), were involved in complicated business on the terrestrial astronomical object of [Naran-Shiv](/wiki/Naran-Shiv "Naran-Shiv").[[30]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-30) In [29 BBY](/wiki/29_BBY "29 BBY"),[[45]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_and_Anakin_date-45) Skywalker sought to impress his peers at the Jedi Temple. During a training session, he defeated a [training droid](/wiki/Jedi_training_droid "Jedi training droid"), which he had programmed to mimic the appearance of the Sith of Naboo. All the while, Mace Windu, Kenobi and Supreme Chancellor [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") watched—the latter of whom was impressed.[[41]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_&_Anakin_1-41)

Sometime later, Skywalker struggled to learn the [skill of taming creatures](/wiki/Taming_beasts "Taming beasts") when Kenobi told him that the Chancellor wanted to see him. The two arrived at [his office](/wiki/Emperor%27s_office "Emperor's office"), where Palpatine requested that Skywalker accompany him on an errand, declining Kenobi's company.[[46]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_&_Anakin_2-46) Upon Skywalker's return to the Jedi Temple, he confided in Kenobi that he wished to leave the Order, feeling uncomfortable at the prospect of his entire life being decided when he was only nine years old, and surrendered his lightsaber to his master. Though Kenobi took the weapon, he pleaded Skywalker to reconsider.[[47]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_&_Anakin_4-47)

Kenobi later confided to Yoda about Skywalker's thoughts about leaving the Jedi Order and that he himself thought he had failed Skywalker despite doing the best he could to teach him, that Skywalker belonged with the Jedi Order and that he was too young not ready to be out on his own. Yoda confirmed that Kenobi himself was still young as well and that Skywalker was still a child and that it was natural for him to have questions. Yoda then asked if Kenobi would be breaking his vow to Qui-Gon Jinn by allowing Skywalker to leave, but Kenobi asserted that he would still train Skywalker in the Force in case the dark side found him. Yoda reminded Kenobi that Jedi training was exclusive to the Jedi Order, to which Kenobi responded that if Skywalker left, so would he.[[48]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_&_Anakin_5-48)

#### Mission to Carnelion IV

:   "*The road lies before you, Anakin Skywalker. Will you walk it alone?*"  
    "*No, Master. As a Jedi. If you'll show me the way.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker[[48]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_&_Anakin_5-48)

 [![Obi-Wan traveled to Carnelion IV with his padawan Anakin Skywalker.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fe/CarnelionIV-ObiWanAnakin1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160112013113) [![Obi-Wan traveled to Carnelion IV with his padawan Anakin Skywalker.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fe/CarnelionIV-ObiWanAnakin1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/199?cb=20160112013113)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fe/CarnelionIV-ObiWanAnakin1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160112013113) 

Obi-Wan traveled to Carnelion IV with his padawan Anakin Skywalker.

 

Before Skywalker could give his definite answer, at Yoda's behest, both student and master [responded](/wiki/Mission_to_Carnelion_IV "Mission to Carnelion IV") to a mysterious distress signal from the supposedly-dead world of [Carnelion IV](/wiki/Carnelion_IV "Carnelion IV") that specifically called for Jedi intercession. They began their journey to the coordinates, but their shuttle was damaged due to the planet's [atmospheric](/wiki/Atmosphere "Atmosphere") debris field and the two had to eject from the doomed vessel, landing below the [Celadon Sea](/wiki/Celadon_Sea "Celadon Sea"). Not too long afterwards, they came to be aware of there being life on the planet as a sky battle raged over them, and Kenobi returned his lightsaber to him so that he could defend himself. As one of the combatant airships began to fall, Skywalker and Kenobi saved its two-person crew by delaying the crash.[[41]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_&_Anakin_1-41)

The survivors, [Kolara](/wiki/Kolara "Kolara") and Mother [Pran](/wiki/Pran "Pran"), were unaware of the distress signal and who the Jedi were.[[41]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_&_Anakin_1-41) Kenobi was then able to use a mind trick on Pran to lower her weapons. However, they came under attack by the other airship. Kenobi then used his lightsaber to destroy the airship. Kenobi then stopped the pilot, [Grecker](/wiki/Grecker "Grecker") from shooting at Skywalker, Pran, and Kolara. After Skywalker destroyed their blasters, Kenobi then pulled their knives away. Kenobi reasoned with Grecker, Kolara, and Pran that they needed to get to safety. As they made their way, they came across [Corpse-leeches](/wiki/Corpse-leech "Corpse-leech"). Kenobi and Skywalker then drew their lightsabers and tried to use the force to connect with them to no avail. Kenobi and the others then boarded an airship.[[46]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_&_Anakin_2-46)

 [![War on the planet Carnelion IV.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/CorpseLeeches-ObiWanAnakin2.png/revision/latest?cb=20190219031035) [![War on the planet Carnelion IV.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/CorpseLeeches-ObiWanAnakin2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/227?cb=20190219031035)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/CorpseLeeches-ObiWanAnakin2.png/revision/latest?cb=20190219031035) 

War on the planet Carnelion IV.

 

Kenobi then refused to give them the location of the distress signal. He also told Grecker that Skywalker was not his son, but his Padawan at the dying request of his master. Kenobi and Grecker then defended the airship against the corpse-leeches. However, Pran and Kolara took Skywalker with them and abandoned the airship. Kenobi was then left behind on the airship as Pran destroyed it.[[49]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_&_Anakin_3-49)

Kenobi and Grecker were then able to jump off the airship before it crashed. Kenobi was then able to use the force to make the creatures understand him. Kenobi then asked Grecker to tell him where Skywalker was taken to. Grecker told him that he did not know where the open was. Kenobi then decided to go after him with Grecker after getting air masks on. Kenobi and Grecker then found the location of the distress signal. They then came under attack by a creature. Grecker then fired a flare. Kenobi and Grecker then fought until a masked man came out and let them in. Kenobi was able to get inside before Grecker closed the door. The man, [Sera](/wiki/Sera "Sera"), then showed Kenobi his collection of his world's remnants. Kenobi was then told that Sera was the one who sent the distress signal. He then told Kenobi about his collection of relics and how both the open and closed wanted him dead.[[47]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_&_Anakin_4-47)

Kenobi then learned about how Sera sent the signal and learned about both the Jedi and Sith. Kenobi and Sera then went to the roof to watch as Grecker's forces attacked his fortress. Despite Sera's pleas for Kenobi to kill them, Kenobi told her that the Jedi spare everyone. Kenobi then spoke with Grecker and convinced him to stop their attack. However, Mother Pran attacked with her machines. Kenobi was then saved by Skywalker. Kenobi then took Skywalker to the Sera's communication unit. There, Skywalker was able to send out a signal off-planet. Republic and Jedi forces arrived where they ended the conflict.[[48]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_&_Anakin_5-48)

#### Mission to Glee Anselm

:   "*Master Yoda has been kidnapped from the Jedi Temple!*"
:   ―Anakin Skywalker[[24]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_&_Anakin_Adventure-24)

Grand Master Yoda was [captured](/wiki/Rescue_of_Yoda "Rescue of Yoda") by battle droids and taken to the planet [Glee Anselm](/wiki/Glee_Anselm "Glee Anselm"). Kenobi and Skywalker were sent to rescue him. Whilst on Glee Anselm, they located Yoda in an underwater base, where they learned that the Grand Master had never really been captured. In reality, the operation was a test for Kenobi and Skywalker, which they passed. The adventure marked the start of Kenobi and Skywalker coming to view each other as brothers.[[24]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_&_Anakin_Adventure-24) Kenobi and his Padawan were also dispatched on a [mission to Taris](/wiki/Mission_to_Taris "Mission to Taris") at one point.[[30]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-30)

#### Capturing a thief

:   "*Not at all, Dex. What are friends for?*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi to Dexter Jettster[[50]](#cite_note-Stop,_Thief-50)

 [![Obi-Wan tricks Tri Tellon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b2/Obi-Wan_tricks_Tri_Tellon.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181209024223) [![Obi-Wan tricks Tri Tellon](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b2/Obi-Wan_tricks_Tri_Tellon.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/213?cb=20181209024223)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b2/Obi-Wan_tricks_Tri_Tellon.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181209024223) 

Obi-Wan tricks Tri Tellon

 

While visiting Dex's Diner, the [Pa'lowick](/wiki/Pa%27lowick "Pa'lowick") thief [Tri Tellon](/wiki/Tri_Tellon "Tri Tellon") stole an object from Kenobi. She escaped through the world's lower levels, through [CoCo Town](/wiki/CoCo_Town "CoCo Town") and to her den, which she shared with the old rogue [Magreda](/wiki/Magreda "Magreda"). Expecting to find Magreda, she instead found Kenobi who explained that the object she had stolen was just a tracking device wrapped in some paper. In came Dexter, who had asked Kenobi to trick Tellon as she had stolen a lot of goods from his customers. Dexter thanked him and told Kenobi he owed him one, which the Jedi accepted.[[50]](#cite_note-Stop,_Thief-50)

#### Humbling the Chosen One

:   "*A Jedi's goal is to defend life, not take it.*"  
    "*Mercy doesn't defeat an enemy, Master. Which is why you're going to lose.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker[[51]](#cite_note-Kenobi_5-51)

 [![Kenobi conducts a sparring session with Skywalker.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/19/Ani_Obi_Temple_Fight.png/revision/latest?cb=20220725161454) [![Kenobi conducts a sparring session with Skywalker.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/19/Ani_Obi_Temple_Fight.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20220725161454)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/19/Ani_Obi_Temple_Fight.png/revision/latest?cb=20220725161454) 

Kenobi conducts a sparring session with Skywalker.

 

Sometime after Skywalker reached adulthood, Kenobi and Skywalker would engage in a lightsaber sparing session in the Jedi Temple. After Skywalker thought he was victorious, Kenobi told him that despite his victory, his need to win blinded him, and Kenobi was able to overpower Skywalker and take Skywalker's lightsaber away from him.[[51]](#cite_note-Kenobi_5-51)

### Separatist Crisis

#### Protecting Senator Amidala

:   "*You know I don't like it when you do that!*"  
    "*Sorry, Master, I forgot you don't like flying.*"  
    "*I don't mind flying, but what you're doing is suicide!*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39)

 [![Kenobi and his Padawan are reunited with Padme Amidala.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/19/Anakin_Padme_Reunite.png/revision/latest?cb=20140716004451) [![Kenobi and his Padawan are reunited with Padme Amidala.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/19/Anakin_Padme_Reunite.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140716004451)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/19/Anakin_Padme_Reunite.png/revision/latest?cb=20140716004451) 

Kenobi and his Padawan are reunited with Padme Amidala.

 

In [22 BBY](/wiki/22_BBY "22 BBY"),[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) Kenobi and Skywalker were involved in a [border dispute on Ansion](/wiki/Border_dispute_on_Ansion "Border dispute on Ansion")[[52]](#cite_note-Anakin_Encyclopedia-52) that involved [Presidente](/wiki/Presidente "Presidente") [Shu Mai](/wiki/Shu_Mai "Shu Mai") of the [Commerce Guild](/wiki/Commerce_Guild "Commerce Guild"). Following their success on [Ansion](/wiki/Ansion "Ansion"),[[53]](#cite_note-Prelude_to_the_Clone_Wars-53) the two Jedi were sent by the Jedi Council—at the behest of Supreme Chancellor Palpatine—to protect the now [Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") Amidala from future attacks following an [assassination](/wiki/Assassin "Assassin") [attempt](/wiki/Plot_to_assassinate_Senator_Amidala "Plot to assassinate Senator Amidala") on her life. Kenobi and Skywalker made their way to [Padmé's Apartment](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9%27s_Apartment "Padmé's Apartment") and whilst they traveling up a turbolift, Kenobi sensed Skywalker's anxiety and warned him of over-stepping their duties, only to be told later of Amidala's plan to use herself as bait.[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39)

That night, [Zam Wesell](/wiki/Zam_Wesell "Zam Wesell") attempted to kill the Senator with venomous [kouhun](/wiki/Kouhun "Kouhun") deployed from a [probe droid](/wiki/Probe_droid "Probe droid"), but her plot was foiled when Kenobi and Skywalker sensed a disturbance in the Senator's room. While Skywalker eliminated the creatures, Kenobi leaped out of the window and held onto the droid as it attempted to flee into the skylanes of Coruscant. The probe droid moved rapidly between the express ways in an attempt to dislodge the Jedi, unsuccessfully. As the droid moved closer to Wesell's position, the assassin shot the droid with her rifle, destroying it and causing Kenobi to fall rapidly towards the surface of the planet. Skywalker was quickly approaching Kenobi's position in a speeder, and moved beneath him in order to catch him. The pair then proceeded to pursue the bounty hunter through the skyways of Coruscant through traffic lanes and industrial areas, until Skywalker leaped to her speeder and disabled it, causing it to crash outside the [Outlander Club](/wiki/Outlander_Club "Outlander Club").[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39)

The pair followed her in, realizing she was a [changeling](/wiki/Clawdite "Clawdite"), able to mask her appearance. Kenobi made his way to the bar where he was offered [death sticks](/wiki/Death_stick "Death stick") by [Elan Sel'Sabagno](/wiki/Elan_Sel%27Sabagno "Elan Sel'Sabagno"), an offer he declined. Kenobi encouraged Sel'sabagno to return home and rethink his life, using the force for persuasion. He sensed Wesell's presence and cut her arm off with his lightsaber before she could shoot him. Before she could tell the Jedi who she was working for, Wesell was shot and killed by a toxic dart fired by [Jango Fett](/wiki/Jango_Fett "Jango Fett").[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39)

 [![Kenobi investigating the Kamino saberdart at Dex's Diner](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/Investigate_SWDL.png/revision/latest?cb=20180321060115) [![Kenobi investigating the Kamino saberdart at Dex's Diner](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/Investigate_SWDL.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20180321060115)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/Investigate_SWDL.png/revision/latest?cb=20180321060115) 

Kenobi investigating the Kamino saberdart at Dex's Diner

 

Subsequently, Kenobi and Skywalker were sent on separate missions by the Council—while Kenobi continued an investigation on Amidala's aggressors, Skywalker would protect her on Naboo. Despite thinking his Padawan was not prepared for his first solo mission, he abided by Council's request. Kenobi, then, took the toxic dart to his friend [Dexter Jettster](/wiki/Dexter_Jettster "Dexter Jettster"), who told him that it was a [Kamino saberdart](/wiki/Kamino_saberdart "Kamino saberdart"). Using Dex's information about [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino"), Kenobi visited the Archives, but he was unable to locate the system. When he asked Jocasta Nu about it, she surmised that the system must not exist since it was not in the archives. Unconvinced, Kenobi visited Master Yoda, who was teaching the [Bear Clan](/wiki/Bear_Clan "Bear Clan"), and the two agreed that someone had erased the files on Kamino from the Archives, and that Kenobi needed to visit the location of the lost planet.[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39)

#### Discovery of the Clone Army

:   "*I have successfully made contact with the Prime Minister of Kamino. They are using a bounty hunter named Jango Fett to create a clone army.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to Mace Windu and Yoda[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39)

Upon arriving on Kamino, Kenobi was greeted by the [Kaminoan](/wiki/Kaminoan "Kaminoan") [Taun We](/wiki/Taun_We "Taun We") who told the Jedi that they had been expecting him. She took Obi-Wan to Prime Minister [Lama Su](/wiki/Lama_Su "Lama Su"), who said [Sifo-Dyas](/wiki/Sifo-Dyas "Sifo-Dyas") would have been proud of the army they had created in accordance with his request—to create a [clone army](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic") for the Republic. Kenobi was then shown the [clones'](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper") prowess and growth, and was told that the original template was Jango Fett. After asking to meet Fett, Taun We took Kenobi to Fett's quarters, where the Jedi Knight asked the bounty hunter questions concerning any recent visits to Coruscant.[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39)

 [![Kenobi engaging Jango Fett on Kamino.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/Fight_on_Kamino.png/revision/latest?cb=20150325141544) [![Kenobi engaging Jango Fett on Kamino.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/Fight_on_Kamino.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/238?cb=20150325141544)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/Fight_on_Kamino.png/revision/latest?cb=20150325141544) 

Kenobi engaging Jango Fett on Kamino.

 

After their meeting, Jango and his clone son, [Boba Fett](/wiki/Boba_Fett "Boba Fett"), attempted to flee Kamino in the bounty hunter's ship, *[Slave I](/wiki/Slave_I "Slave I")*. Obi-Wan confronted Jango, and the two fought on the landing platform. At the end of the battle, Obi-Wan fell off the platform, and Jango believed he had fallen into the sea. However, Obi-Wan managed to catch hold of a bridge, and he returned to the platform to see *Slave I* taking off with just enough time for Obi-Wan to attach a homing beacon to Jango's hull.[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39)

#### Capture on Geonosis

:   "*You must join me, Obi-Wan… and together, we will destroy the Sith!*"  
    "*I will never join you, Dooku.*"  
    "*It may be difficult to secure your release.*"
:   ―Count Dooku and Obi-Wan Kenobi[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39)
