 [![Kenobi evades fire from Fett's Slave I in the asteroid belt around Geonosis](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/Obi-Wan_Kenobi_Delta-7_Aethersprite_XW2.png/revision/latest?cb=20190205041954) [![Kenobi evades fire from Fett's Slave I in the asteroid belt around Geonosis](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/Obi-Wan_Kenobi_Delta-7_Aethersprite_XW2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190205041954)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/Obi-Wan_Kenobi_Delta-7_Aethersprite_XW2.png/revision/latest?cb=20190205041954) 

Kenobi evades fire from Fett's *Slave I* in the asteroid belt around Geonosis

 

Kenobi pursued the *Slave I* in his starfighter all the way to [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis") and managed to survive Fett's attacks with [seismic charges](/wiki/Seismic_charge "Seismic charge"). Tricking him into believing he had died, Kenobi managed to land on the planet, where he discovered a multitude of Trade Federation ships. Furthermore, he infiltrated and overheard [Count Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku") addressing the [Separatist](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems") [Council](/wiki/Executive_Separatist_Council "Executive Separatist Council") and mentioning the attempts on Senator Amidala's life were at the request of Nute Gunray. Realizing the importance of his discoveries, Kenobi sent a message to Skywalker in Tatooine as his signal could not reach Coruscant on its own. Before he could end his message, however,[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39) Kenobi was attacked by a droideka and knocked unconscious,[[54]](#cite_note-Epic_Adventures:_Attack_of_the_Clones-54) captured by the Separatists and imprisoned.[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39)

Inside the [prison tower](/wiki/Dooku%27s_tower "Dooku's tower"), Dooku visited him; he revealed that the Republic was under the influence of a Sith Lord named Darth Sidious, and tried to convince Kenobi to join him and destroy the Sith together, but Kenobi refused.[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39) Kenobi did not believe what Dooku said about the Republic being controlled by the Sith, just as Dooku had hoped.[[21]](#cite_note-Complete_Visual_New-21)

### The Clone Wars

:   "*You fought in the Clone Wars?*"  
    "*Yes. I was once a Jedi knight, the same as your father.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker and Obi-Wan Kenobi[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

#### First Battle of Geonosis

:   "*No, sir, I wasn't involved in the first assault on Geonosis.*"  
    "*You didn't miss much. Last time, I was chained to a pole and attacked by several humongous monsters.*"  
    "*That sounds entertaining.*"  
    "*It was, for the Geonosians.*"
:   ―Commander Cody and Obi-Wan Kenobi[[55]](#cite_note-Landing_at_Point_Rain-55)

 [![Kenobi fought in the Petranaki Arena alongside other Jedi on Geonosis.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/66/PetranakiArenaBattle-CGSWG.png/revision/latest?cb=20250127032041) [![Kenobi fought in the Petranaki Arena alongside other Jedi on Geonosis.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/66/PetranakiArenaBattle-CGSWG.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20250127032041)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/66/PetranakiArenaBattle-CGSWG.png/revision/latest?cb=20250127032041) 

Kenobi fought in the Petranaki Arena alongside other Jedi on Geonosis.

 

Sentenced to execution in Geonosis' [Petranaki Arena](/wiki/Petranaki_Arena "Petranaki Arena"), Kenobi was joined in the arena by Skywalker and Amidala who were also captured in their attempt to rescue him. Though reassured that his message had been re-transmitted, he expressed disappointment that Skywalker had come and failed to free them from the situation. The trio worked to control the three creatures deployed to kill them—a [reek](/wiki/Reek "Reek"), an [acklay](/wiki/Acklay "Acklay"), and a [nexu](/wiki/Nexu "Nexu"). After they had freed themselves from their restraints, Kenobi fought the[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39) most formidable[[56]](#cite_note-HJJEncylopedia-56) of the three creatures—the acklay. Kenobi, Amidala, and Skywalker were saved by the arrival of a [Jedi task force](/wiki/Jedi_assault_team "Jedi assault team") led by Mace Windu who refused to surrender to Dooku, intending to complete their rescue. The Jedi fought back against the overwhelming droid armies, but soon only a few survivors were left in the center of the arena surrounded by battle droids. When Windu declined Dooku's offer to let the Jedi surrender,[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39) Kenobi stood in solidarity with the decision, intending to go down fighting.[[56]](#cite_note-HJJEncylopedia-56)

Moments prior to their execution, clone army forces arrived in transports led by Master Yoda. The clones fought back against the droids and rescued the Jedi and Amidala, forming a perimeter around the survivors. Kenobi then boarded the same Republic [LAAT/i transport](/wiki/Low_Altitude_Assault_Transport/infantry "Low Altitude Assault Transport/infantry") with Skywalker and Amidala while the rest of the Jedi task force also escaped. As they flew, Skywalker instructed their [clone](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") pilots on how best to shoot down enemy forces, which Kenobi complimented. Soon, both caught sight of Dooku fleeing on his speeder with a droid escort. Kenobi felt that there was not enough time to pursue reinforcements, assuring Amidala that he and his Padawan could handle the situation alone. When Dooku's escort rattled their LAAT/i, the Senator fell out of their vehicle, causing Skywalker to panic.[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39)

 [![Kenobi fought Dooku on Geonosis.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/Sai.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120615105442) [![Kenobi fought Dooku on Geonosis.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/Sai.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120615105442)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/Sai.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120615105442) 

Kenobi fought Dooku on Geonosis.

 

Skywalker pleaded to rescue her, though Kenobi insisted that catching up to Dooku was the highest priority and that if the Padawan stayed behind he would be removed from the Jedi Order. Once they landed, Kenobi and Skywalker pursued Dooku as he prepared to flee the planet. After confronting him about the Jedi he had killed earlier that day, the pair engaged in a lightsaber duel with Dooku. The former Jedi's use of [Force lightning](/wiki/Force_lightning "Force lightning") revealed his fall to the dark side, prompting Kenobi to be wary when his apprentice was downed by it.[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39) Now knowing that he had underestimated Dooku's skills,[[56]](#cite_note-HJJEncylopedia-56) dueled Dooku, but was eventually disarmed by the former Jedi during the duel and injured on the shoulder and thigh. Kenobi tossed his lightsaber to Skywalker so that he could continue the fight.[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39)

However, after the Padawan's arm was cut off by Dooku's lightsaber, he too was tossed to the floor beside his Master. Dooku moved toward them both, but Yoda arrived shortly after to fight his former apprentice in a lightsaber duel. However, he was forced to focus on saving Skywalker and Kenobi from being crushed to their deaths by falling debris moved loose by Dooku. As a result, the Separatist leader escaped in his ship, leaving the three Jedi behind. Amidala arrived with a group of clone [troopers](/wiki/Trooper "Trooper") shortly afterward, embracing Skywalker as Kenobi stood nearby.[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39)

#### Promotion to Jedi General

:   "*I must admit without the clones, it would not have been a victory.*"  
    "*Victory? Victory, you say? Master Obi-Wan, not victory. The shroud of the dark side has fallen. Begun, the Clone War has.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Yoda about the Geonosis battle[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39)

 [![Obi-Wan Kenobi constructed his third lightsaber after Geonosis.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b2/ObiWanKenobisLightsaber-GalacticFiles2018Weapons.png/revision/latest?cb=20251108051555) [![Obi-Wan Kenobi constructed his third lightsaber after Geonosis.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b2/ObiWanKenobisLightsaber-GalacticFiles2018Weapons.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20251108051555)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b2/ObiWanKenobisLightsaber-GalacticFiles2018Weapons.png/revision/latest?cb=20251108051555) 

Obi-Wan Kenobi constructed his third lightsaber after Geonosis.

 

Following the [Geonosis battle](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis"), Kenobi traveled back to Coruscant while his Padawan escorted Amidala to Naboo.[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39) Skywalker's absence was noticed by[[57]](#cite_note-QueensHope-57) [Vice Chancellor](/wiki/Vice_Chair "Vice Chair")[[4]](#cite_note-USW_NE-4) [Mas Amedda](/wiki/Mas_Amedda "Mas Amedda"), who informed Chancellor Palpatine of his whereabouts after seeing he did not return with Kenobi.[[57]](#cite_note-QueensHope-57) In the Temple on Coruscant, Kenobi met with Mace Windu and Yoda in the Jedi Council room to discuss the confrontation that had just taken place. He told the Councillors that his apprentice was escorting Amidala back to Naboo before returning to the Temple, which they accepted. Although Kenobi noted that the Geonosis battle would not have been a victory without the clones, Yoda did not think of it as victory, as it marked the beginning of the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"). Though Kenobi passed on Dooku's warning about a Sith controlling the Senate to his peers—both mostly dismissed it due to the former Jedi's actions and fall to the dark side. However, the trio resolved to continue monitoring the Senate instead.[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39)

While Skywalker was on Naboo to escort Amidala home,[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39) he wondered how his Master was doing in the aftermath of the battle. Additionally, the Padawan reflected on what their responsibilities in the upcoming war would be like while having to collaborate with clone troopers in battle. However, he firmly chose to keep knowledge of his relationship with the Senator secret from Kenobi despite the strain of the deception. Skywalker [married](/wiki/Wedding_of_Anakin_Skywalker_and_Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Wedding of Anakin Skywalker and Padmé Amidala") Amidala, despite knowing his Master would disapprove. As days passed, Skywalker eventually chose to return to Coruscant, citing that he had not informed his Master of a reason to remain on Naboo. After meeting with their superiors, both Kenobi and Skywalker were sent on their first deployment.[[57]](#cite_note-QueensHope-57)

 [![Clone Commander Cody (Cody's helmet pictured) was Kenobi's second-in-command.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/CodyHelmet-TheVisualEncyclopedia.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170604214431) [![Clone Commander Cody (Cody's helmet pictured) was Kenobi's second-in-command.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/CodyHelmet-TheVisualEncyclopedia.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20170604214431)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/CodyHelmet-TheVisualEncyclopedia.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170604214431) 

Clone Commander Cody (Cody's helmet pictured) was Kenobi's second-in-command.

 

Now greatly respected both in and outside of the Jedi Order, Kenobi was promoted to [Jedi General](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") like many of his colleagues and was later bestowed the rank of [High Jedi General](/wiki/High_Jedi_General "High Jedi General") while he led the [Third Systems Army](/wiki/Third_Systems_Army "Third Systems Army") and commanded the [Open Circle Fleet](/wiki/Open_Circle_Fleet "Open Circle Fleet") in the Grand Army of the Republic during the Clone Wars. While deployed, he held [command](/wiki/Commanding_officer "Commanding officer") of the [7th Sky Corps](/wiki/7th_Sky_Corps "7th Sky Corps") and often led its [212th Attack Battalion](/wiki/212th_Attack_Battalion "212th Attack Battalion") into combat personally until the war's end. The [Clone Marshal Commander](/wiki/Clone_Marshal_Commander "Clone Marshal Commander") [Cody](/wiki/Cody "Cody") served as his second-in-command, accompanying him on many missions against the [Separatist Droid Army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army") and other Separatist targets. Kenobi's military engagements, often alongside Skywalker, led to many famed victories that he was praised for by the Republic.[[56]](#cite_note-HJJEncylopedia-56)

For his diplomatic skills, he came to be known as "the Negotiator"—[[4]](#cite_note-USW_NE-4) a title mirrored by the name of his flagship, the [*Venator*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Venator-class_Star_Destroyer "Venator-class Star Destroyer") *[Negotiator](/wiki/Negotiator "Negotiator")*.[[58]](#cite_note-Cat_and_Mouse-58) Early in the Clone Wars, Kenobi met the [Supreme Martial Commander of the Separatist Droid Armies](/wiki/Supreme_Martial_Commander_of_the_Separatist_Droid_Armies "Supreme Martial Commander of the Separatist Droid Armies"), [General](/wiki/General "General") [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous"). The two developed a rivalry and fought each other numerous times during the war,[[56]](#cite_note-HJJEncylopedia-56) with Grievous considering Kenobi to be a Jedi he needed to kill "face to face."[[59]](#cite_note-Grievous_Intrigue-59) Their skills were equal, and they quickly became mortal enemies.[[60]](#cite_note-Jedi_Vs._Sith_-_Sith_Fugitives-60) Grievous harbored a deep animosity for Kenobi.[[61]](#cite_note-Chrome_Star_Wars_Legacy-61) At some point during his travels, Kenobi visited the planet [Gazian](/wiki/Gazian "Gazian"), which was strong in the Force. The planet, which had a Force [vergence](/wiki/Vergence "Vergence"), captured an imprint of those who traveled there, including Kenobi.[[62]](#cite_note-StarWars20-62) As his last lightsaber was destroyed,[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39) Kenobi built a [new lightsaber](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi%27s_third_lightsaber "Obi-Wan Kenobi's third lightsaber"), which he would break in through his service in the conflict[[63]](#cite_note-The_Lightsaber_Collection-63) and use throughout the remainder of his life.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

#### Initial engagements

##### Rocky planet deployment

Shortly after the battle on Geonosis, Kenobi was [sent](/wiki/Battles_on_a_rocky_planet "Battles on a rocky planet") to a [rocky planet](/wiki/Unidentified_rocky_planet "Unidentified rocky planet") alongside his Padawan, Commander Cody, and several troopers, including a clone soldier named [Sister](/wiki/Sister "Sister"), to destroy Separatist forces. Kenobi was dismayed by how much Skywalker seemed to enjoy combat, and asked how his apprentice found enjoyment in their combat. After receiving a reply, Kenobi worked with his student to complete their objectives and resolved to find better cover for their future engagements. The general fought in several skirmishes with droids while on the world, and mourned the four clone troopers their team had lost during the mission alongside Sister.[[57]](#cite_note-QueensHope-57)

Feeling that the Jedi needed more generals, he resolved to suggest to the Jedi Council that Skywalker take the Jedi trials after watching him in combat. He mused that it was a move that would allow them to work together, but also afford the younger man the freedoms of a higher rank along with his own command. Not long after on Coruscant, the handmaiden Sabé initially worried that Kenobi would notice her posing in Amidala's place while at a meeting in the Jedi Temple. When Skywalker left the gathering, Sabé noticed Kenobi attempt to convince his former apprentice to talk to the [Alderaanian](/wiki/Alderaanian "Alderaanian") Senator [Bail Organa](/wiki/Bail_Prestor_Organa "Bail Prestor Organa"). Skywalker's time as a Padawan ended, as he was risen to the rank of Jedi Knight[[57]](#cite_note-QueensHope-57) for the war not long after.[[30]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-30) As a result, Kenobi was promoted to Jedi Master after his apprentice's knighting.[[4]](#cite_note-USW_NE-4)

##### Rising through the ranks

After Skywalker had already been promoted, Kenobi attended his former apprentice's [official Knighting Ceremony](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker%27s_Knighting_Ceremony "Anakin Skywalker's Knighting Ceremony"), which was being officiated by Master Windu. Kenobi had just recently become the next of many Jedi to rotate into the council seat of the late Coleman Trebor, and it was unknown if this arrangement would be permanent. Kenobi treated the tasks presented to him in this role with a certain amount of seriousness, and even treated the ceremony as if it was a war decision. As Windu gave his speech, Kenobi stared at Skywalker, who could feel the weight of the stare. When Windu brought up the possibility of the recently-knighted Jedi receiving Padawans of their own, Kenobi caught Skywalker's eye, smirking as the thought of an apprentice irked Skywalker.[[30]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-30)

Following the conclusion of Windu's speech, Kenobi, confused, glanced around the other Jedi Masters present. Despite his usual skill with improvisation and negotiations, Kenobi found himself flustered by scheduling problems. Skywalker was amused by Kenobi's confusion, as his former master ran his fingers through his now-longer hair. Upon noting that the Chancellor, various senators, and multiple clone commanders were still not present, Kenobi commented that their guests were late, albeit certain that they would arrive shortly. However, the Chancellor's attendance was not in person, but instead via a holo-transmission. Addressing Yoda and Windu, Palpatine announced that the [Purse World](/wiki/Purse_world "Purse world") [Cato Neimoidia](/wiki/Cato_Neimoidia "Cato Neimoidia") had been [bombed](/wiki/Cadesura_disaster "Cadesura disaster"). As Yoda instructed the Padawans and younglings to leave, Kenobi grabbed Skywalker's shoulder, ensuring him that they were equals, and he was welcome to stay. Skywalker then asked if he still had to call Kenobi "Master," and Kenobi jokingly replied that it would only be the case if he knew his place.[[30]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-30)

As the group was informed that the [Cadesura district](/wiki/Cadesura_district "Cadesura district") of Cato Neimoidia's [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") [city](/wiki/City "City"), [Zarra](/wiki/Zarra "Zarra"), had collapsed, Kenobi stood side by side with Skywalker. His thoughts lingered on his former apprentice for several [seconds](/wiki/Second "Second"), pondering how his emotional transition into a Jedi Knight had been rougher than expected. He believed that, while Skywalker had made progress in coming to decisions confidently, he often reverted into deference, unsure of what his place was. It reminded Kenobi of his own ascension to the rank of Jedi Knight, thinking about how long it had taken for him to feel as though he had earned his title, in contrast to his peers who had taken their promotions in stride. Remembering Jinn's advice to not linger on his anxieties, Kenobi exhaled, focusing his mind on the moment.[[30]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-30)

##### The Cato Neimoidia affair

:   "*…you owe me one, and not for saving your skin for the 10th time.*"  
    "*Ninth time. That business on Neimoidia doesn't—doesn't count.*"
:   ―Anakin Skywalker and Obi-Wan Kenobi[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

 [![Kenobi and Skywalker were sent to Cato Neimoidia to investigate an explosion following Skywalker's promotion to Jedi Knight.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/Mission-to-Cato-Neimoidia-final.png/revision/latest?cb=20220421234615) [![Kenobi and Skywalker were sent to Cato Neimoidia to investigate an explosion following Skywalker's promotion to Jedi Knight.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/Mission-to-Cato-Neimoidia-final.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220421234615)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/Mission-to-Cato-Neimoidia-final.png/revision/latest?cb=20220421234615) 

Kenobi and Skywalker were sent to Cato Neimoidia to investigate an explosion following Skywalker's promotion to Jedi Knight.

 

Kenobi was then [sent to look into the explosion](/wiki/Mission_to_Cato_Neimoidia_(Kenobi_and_Skywalker) "Mission to Cato Neimoidia (Kenobi and Skywalker)"), which was being blamed on the Republic[[30]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-30) by the Purse World Cato Neimoidia, the headquarters of the Trade Federation.[[64]](#cite_note-Battles_that_Changed_the_Galaxy-64) As Kenobi investigated with the help of a [Neimoidian guard](/wiki/Neimoidian_Royal_Guard "Neimoidian Royal Guard") named [Ruug Quarnom](/wiki/Ruug_Quarnom "Ruug Quarnom"), the newly-knighted Skywalker disobeyed orders and joined him.[[30]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-30) During their mission, events transpired that led to a situation where the two Jedi were in peril. Skywalker believed that he had saved his former mentor from the danger, while Kenobi believed the action did not count towards the ever-growing total of times his former apprentice had saved his life.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

For his actions on Cato Neimoidia, it was decided Kenobi's council seat would be permanent. Skywalker and Kenobi also [returned to Cato Neimoidia](/wiki/Rescue_of_Ruug_Quarnom "Rescue of Ruug Quarnom") shortly thereafter to rescue Quarnom. With the passage of the [Jedi Military Integration Act](/wiki/Jedi_Military_Integration_Act "Jedi Military Integration Act"), Kenobi was provided with body armor to wear over his robes,[[30]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-30) but he did not immediately adopt that gear, much like Skywalker.[[65]](#cite_note-HS_5-65) Accepting they were no longer master and apprentice, the two left the Cato Neimoidia mission as brothers-in-arms.[[30]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-30)

##### Krystar rescue

:   "*You clones will **never** be fodder, not on my watch. The Jedi, clones, senators, our allies—all of us. We're in this **together**. And I will fight for each and every one of us in equal measure, now and until the very last day of this was.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi to his troopers[[66]](#cite_note-BT3-66)

 [![Obi-Wan Kenobi and Padmé Amidala heading to Krystar](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/df/KenobiAmidalaKrystar-TCWBattleTales3.png/revision/latest?cb=20220419230807) [![Obi-Wan Kenobi and Padmé Amidala heading to Krystar](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/df/KenobiAmidalaKrystar-TCWBattleTales3.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20220419230807)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/df/KenobiAmidalaKrystar-TCWBattleTales3.png/revision/latest?cb=20220419230807) 

Obi-Wan Kenobi and Padmé Amidala heading to Krystar

 

At some point that year,[[67]](#cite_note-BT3Date-67) Kenobi and his [battalion](/wiki/Battalion "Battalion") were [sent](/wiki/Mission_on_Krystar "Mission on Krystar") to the planet [Krystar](/wiki/Krystar "Krystar") to rescue several clones being held captive. Though hesitant to pursue an assault on the planet, which was aligned with the Republic, he agreed with Cody that saving the hostages was important. After meeting with Amidala, he was made aware of intelligence gathered from Senator [Vishar Koss](/wiki/Vishar_Koss "Vishar Koss") of Krystar. Using this, Kenobi helped form a plan for the operation to infiltrate a [compound](/wiki/Unidentified_compound "Unidentified compound") rumored to be built near the [Krystar palace](/wiki/Krystar_palace "Krystar palace") with Amidala's assistance. Escorted to the planet's surface by Amidala under the guise of an aid mission, Kenobi and his troopers investigated the claims of the captured clones.[[66]](#cite_note-BT3-66)

Though his soldiers wished to take action immediately to free their brothers, the Jedi insisted on having adequate proof before responding accordingly due to the planet's Republic affiliation. Kenobi's men proved able to confirm the claims made by Koss when they found trapped troopers in the compound and contacted their commanding [officer](/wiki/Officer "Officer") about it. Kenobi then received a transmission from Amidala, who informed him that Krystar's Regent [Queb](/wiki/Queb "Queb") was selling the captured clones to Trandoshans. Kenobi instructed his men to free their brothers, which they did successfully before returning to their ship. Though a [Trandoshan hunter](/wiki/Unidentified_Trandoshan_hunter_(Krystar) "Unidentified Trandoshan hunter (Krystar)") was upset at the recapture of the clones, Kenobi faced his fury by throwing him out of range with the Force. The general then allowed Koss and Amidala to travel off the planet with them, with the former seeking protection until Queb was taken care of. After the event, Kenobi vowed to protect his allies until the end of the war as much as possible—despite the political challenges—and promised that Queb would be arrested.[[66]](#cite_note-BT3-66)

##### Caliban bridge building

:   "*As clearly stated in the Galactic Accords regarding prisoners of war, no prisoner shall be forced into manual labor or—*"  
    "*Jedi scum! You belong to me, Kenobi, and you will do as I say…or you will die.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Grievous on Caliban[[68]](#cite_note-BT5-68)

 [![Obi-Wan Kenobi and Grievous on Caliban](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/GrievousAndKenobiInTheSnow-TCWBattleTales5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220420060536) [![Obi-Wan Kenobi and Grievous on Caliban](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/GrievousAndKenobiInTheSnow-TCWBattleTales5.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20220420060536)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/GrievousAndKenobiInTheSnow-TCWBattleTales5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220420060536) 

Obi-Wan Kenobi and Grievous on Caliban

 

Kenobi and his troopers were present on the Outer Rim moon [Caliban](/wiki/Caliban "Caliban") and were captured by General Grievous. Though the Jedi attempted to argue that prisoners of war cannot be forced into labor due to a provision in the [Galactic Accords](/wiki/Galactic_Accord_of_Systems "Galactic Accord of Systems") war statutes, Grievous insisted that they build a lunar ice bridge for him. Grievous claimed he would kill them if they did not complete the task, and that they would be lucky to leave alive. Despite the frigid temperatures, Kenobi made a plan to construct a sabotaged project to replace the bridge the Separatist leader had originally destroyed and instructed the clone troopers with him to assist.[[68]](#cite_note-BT5-68)

Near the build site, the Jedi and his men climbed a rise and met a [qubey](/wiki/Qubey "Qubey") native of the world trapped on one side of a ravine, attempting to reach its [parent](/wiki/Parent "Parent") on the opposite end. After Kenobi saw this, he decided to rebuild the bridge out of compassion and relayed this order to his troopers. Further observation of the creatures showed indication of their displeasure with the Separatist presence on their world, leading to Kenobi counting them as allies. As the structure was being made, the qubey distracted Grievous enough for Kenobi to retrieve his lightsaber when the enemy leader came to inspect it's construction in a surprise ambush. After the bridge's completion, Kenobi implored the general to let his men leave the planet. When Grievous declined, the qubey [attacked](/wiki/Battle_on_Caliban "Battle on Caliban") him and his droids while the Jedi also engaged the Separatist in lightsaber combat. Kenobi goaded the general into stepping onto the sabotaged new bridge, then used the Force to start an avalanche. Grievous fell into the ravine after being swept away, allowing Kenobi to escape the planet with his men in a ship and destroy the bridge after takeoff.[[68]](#cite_note-BT5-68)

##### Hisseen siege

:   "*Sorry we were late, Cody. We were still in pursuit of Ventress and Dooku when we received Rex's distress call.*"  
    "*Not to worry, General. Everything went as* easily *as always.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Cody[[68]](#cite_note-BT5-68)

 [![Obi-Wan and Cody during the Hisseen siege](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/ObiWanHisseen-TCWBattleTales1.png/revision/latest?cb=20220401050406) [![Obi-Wan and Cody during the Hisseen siege](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/ObiWanHisseen-TCWBattleTales1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20220401050406)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/ObiWanHisseen-TCWBattleTales1.png/revision/latest?cb=20220401050406) 

Obi-Wan and Cody during the Hisseen siege

 

Kenobi traveled to the planet [Hisseen](/wiki/Hisseen "Hisseen") and participated in a [siege](/wiki/Siege_of_Hisseen "Siege of Hisseen") of the planet alongside Skywalker, Jedi Master [Plo Koon](/wiki/Plo_Koon "Plo Koon"), and their battalions. After working swiftly to destroy an encampment of battle droids, Koon instructed the trio that their objective was to prevent the [Hisseenian premier](/wiki/Unidentified_Hisseenian_premier "Unidentified Hisseenian premier") from revealing the location of his fellow [parliament](/wiki/Hisseen%27s_parliament "Hisseen's parliament") members to Dooku and[[69]](#cite_note-BT1-69) his apprentice,[[4]](#cite_note-USW_NE-4) [Asajj Ventress](/wiki/Asajj_Ventress "Asajj Ventress")—who would kill or threaten them. The Jedi leave and headed into mountainous terrain while leaving their troopers to handle the Separatist ground assault.[[69]](#cite_note-BT1-69) The Jedi searched to discover the location of the parliament, initially coming up with nothing. However, they soon met Dooku and Ventress, engaging in a lightsaber fight with the pair that prevented them from seeking out the parliament. Koon attempted to contact their clone commanders of the deteriorating situation while Kenobi and Skywalker fought the Separatist darksiders,[[70]](#cite_note-BT2-70) though the message broke up[[69]](#cite_note-BT1-69) due to the mountainous terrain surrounding them.[[70]](#cite_note-BT2-70)

Koon relayed the coordinates of the Hisseenian government members to Wolffe, trusting him and the other commanders to rescue them while he helped Skywalker and Kenobi. As Dooku continued keeping the trio occupied,[[70]](#cite_note-BT2-70) their soldiers freed the parliament members by destroying the droids guarding them, reminded of the situational similarity of the Krystar mission that Kenobi had embarked on.[[66]](#cite_note-BT3-66) The siege on Hisseen continued with more waves of droids attacking, reminding Cody of the mission to Caliban. As the clone troopers prepare to fight, Kenobi, Skywalker, and Koon return, slicing the Separatist reinforcements into pieces. Though Ventress and Dooku escaped, Kenobi congratulated the soldiers on their success rescuing the parliament. He then relayed that Yoda had called them back to Coruscant for their next deployment.[[68]](#cite_note-BT5-68)

##### Deployment to Kudo III

:   "*…you're not wrong. The people in the foundry **aren't** soldiers. But if he's right about the risk to our clone soldiers…*"  
    "*There has to be a better way to approach this. Isn't that thr whole reason the Jedi are a part of this war? To help **save** lives?*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker[[71]](#cite_note-AoR_Anakin-71)

 [![Kenobi and Skywalker went on a mission to Kudo III.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/22/KenobiKudoIII-AORAnakin1.png/revision/latest?cb=20220418052012) [![Kenobi and Skywalker went on a mission to Kudo III.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/22/KenobiKudoIII-AORAnakin1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20220418052012)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/22/KenobiKudoIII-AORAnakin1.png/revision/latest?cb=20220418052012) 

Kenobi and Skywalker went on a mission to Kudo III.

 

Kenobi traveled to the [Corvair sector](/wiki/Corvair_sector "Corvair sector") with Skywalker during the [Battle of Corvair](/wiki/Battle_of_Corvair "Battle of Corvair"), watching the skirmish take place from a *Venator*-class Star Destroyer. Following the battle, the pair received instructions to investigate rumors of a droid foundry being established on a moon in the sector, [Kudo III](/wiki/Kudo_III "Kudo III"). Kenobi encouraged his former Padawan to trust in the Force in the investigation, and while acknowledging the skepticism of Yularen, supported Skywalker's intuition on the matter.[[71]](#cite_note-AoR_Anakin-71)

As they shared a meal together, Kenobi shared Skywalker's concerns about civilians being involved in the Kudo III developments. He encouraged him to protect any innocents, while still dealing with discovered Separatist threats. Ultimately, Skywalker found that the Separatists had been attempting to goad the Republic into attacking the facility with falsely fed information to kill the innocent slaves inside, then using the assault as negative war propaganda against the Jedi. Kenobi praised Skywalker for his approach of the situation and discovery of the plot. Afterward, Kenobi and Yularen discussed the implications of attacking a neutral party, and whether the planet [Kudo](/wiki/Kudo "Kudo") would consider joining as a result of the discovery on their moon.[[71]](#cite_note-AoR_Anakin-71)

##### Arrival on Christophsis

:   "*Well, here I am. Tell me about this new weapon.*"  
    "*You're looking at it.*"  
    "'I'm looking at what?*"  
    "'Two steps forward, and you'd actually be kissing it.*"
:   ―Anakin Skywalker and Obi-Wan Kenobi, about the stealth ship[[58]](#cite_note-Cat_and_Mouse-58)

 [![Kenobi revealing the stealth ship to Skywalker](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/Stealth_Ship_Decloaks.png/revision/latest?cb=20220420061145) [![Kenobi revealing the stealth ship to Skywalker](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/Stealth_Ship_Decloaks.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20220420061145)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/Stealth_Ship_Decloaks.png/revision/latest?cb=20220420061145) 

Kenobi revealing the stealth ship to Skywalker

 

Kenobi and Skywalker were sent on a [mission](/wiki/Battle_of_Christophsis "Battle of Christophsis") to bring relief supplies to Senator Organa and the Republic forces that were trapped on the planet [Christophsis](/wiki/Christophsis "Christophsis") because of[[58]](#cite_note-Cat_and_Mouse-58) a thirty-ship strong[[64]](#cite_note-Battles_that_Changed_the_Galaxy-64) [Separatist blockade](/wiki/Christophsis_blockade "Christophsis blockade") led by [Admiral](/wiki/Admiral "Admiral") [Trench](/wiki/Trench "Trench"). Kenobi, who arrived later than his former apprentice, brought with him a [stealth ship](/wiki/IPV-2C_Stealth_Corvette "IPV-2C Stealth Corvette") prototype provided by the Republic. He ordered Skywalker to retreat from his current position and meet him aboard his cruiser, where he presented the stealth ship and its capabilities to his companion. Kenobi then gave orders to Skywalker to sneak past the blockade and deliver the supplies to Organa's encampment in secret, which his former apprentice felt was similar to an errand. Though Skywalker wished for more of the prototypes, Kenobi informed him that only one was available—which was not to be used to attack Trench's ship alone.[[58]](#cite_note-Cat_and_Mouse-58)

Emboldened by his own skills, Skywalker tested the capabilities of the ship further and found that Trench's initial [missiles](/wiki/Missile "Missile") were unable to detect it. Kenobi attempted to order his former apprentice to cease and head to Christophsis' surface with increasing urgency after making contact with Organa's bombarded command center and hearing the senator's pleas, but was ignored. Closing communications with his former Master, Skywalker proceeded to attack the flagship of the Separatist Admiral Trench with his stealth ship and broke the blockade with the attack. Afterward, Kenobi issued Skywalker his congratulations after the supplies were safely delivered to Organa on the world's surface.[[58]](#cite_note-Cat_and_Mouse-58) Following the skirmish in space, the two Jedi Generals and their clone troopers were sent to the planet's surface to fight off the droid army taking control of the world.[[72]](#cite_note-The_Hidden_Enemy-72)

##### Traitorous clone

:   "*…I believe the number of eyes watching us has been steadily growing.*"  
    "*Great. Perhaps this means our adversary has learned about our mission. Of course, nobody's tried to stop us yet.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker[[72]](#cite_note-The_Hidden_Enemy-72)

 [![Kenobi and Skywalker were ambushed by droids.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/05/Ambush_on_Christophsis.png/revision/latest?cb=20120929023056) [![Kenobi and Skywalker were ambushed by droids.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/05/Ambush_on_Christophsis.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120929023056)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/05/Ambush_on_Christophsis.png/revision/latest?cb=20120929023056) 

Kenobi and Skywalker were ambushed by droids.

 

After flying to Christophsis' surface on gunships, he and the troopers with him established a [base of operations](/wiki/Christophsis_Republic_base "Christophsis Republic base") on the planet.[[64]](#cite_note-Battles_that_Changed_the_Galaxy-64) Kenobi and Skywalker then planned and prepared to lead a surprise assault on Separatist forces in the world's crystalline capital city [Chaleydonia](/wiki/Chaleydonia "Chaleydonia") with their men. However, they were forced to abort their mission due to a large droid ambush. Skywalker led his troopers to Kenobi's trapped position and both escaped with their soldiers into a ship from the roof of a [double-towered building](/wiki/Christophsis_double-towered_building "Christophsis double-towered building"). One of the troopers with them took the severed head of a [T-series tactical droid](/wiki/T-series_military_strategic_analysis_and_tactics_droid "T-series military strategic analysis and tactics droid").[[72]](#cite_note-The_Hidden_Enemy-72)

After analysis, Cody and Skywalker's clone officer, [Clone Captain](/wiki/Clone_Captain "Clone Captain") [Rex](/wiki/Rex "Rex"), reported to the Jedi that the enemy had known exactly where their ambush was going to be. Kenobi ordered both to root out the spy within the Republic's forces, insisting on the secrecy of the operations at hand while he left base with Skywalker to further investigate. When the Jedi took [BARC speeders](/wiki/BARC_speeder "BARC speeder") behind enemy lines, Separatist forces jammed their transmissions, which left Rex and Cody unable to contact them. Acting under their generals' orders, both clone officers discovered that the clone trooper [Slick](/wiki/Slick "Slick") was the traitor and arrested him, but not before the traitor destroyed the majority of the Republic base's weapons depot. As Kenobi and Skywalker continued heading towards the [Separatist headquarters](/wiki/Christophsis_Separatist_headquarters "Christophsis Separatist headquarters"), both surmised whatever was waiting for them there was a trap due to the number of droids observing them from a distance.[[72]](#cite_note-The_Hidden_Enemy-72)

 [![Kenobi and Skywalker confronting Slick](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/92/SlickApprehended.png/revision/latest?cb=20120929022842) [![Kenobi and Skywalker confronting Slick](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/92/SlickApprehended.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120929022842)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/92/SlickApprehended.png/revision/latest?cb=20120929022842) 

Kenobi and Skywalker confronting Slick

 

Upon entering the headquarters, both Jedi met minimal resistance on the lower level. After meeting Ventress in the building, however, Kenobi and Skywalker engaged in a lightsaber duel with her. Kenobi exchanged banter with Ventress as they engaged, but eventually was forced to escape with his colleague on stolen droid STAPs after an ambush. When the two Jedi returned to the command center, Rex and Cody presented an apprehended Slick. Kenobi and Skywalker expressed disappointment in Slick and the destruction of the weapons depot.[[72]](#cite_note-The_Hidden_Enemy-72) Fearing more troopers would decide to defect, they decided to keep the knowledge of Slick's incident secret.[[64]](#cite_note-Battles_that_Changed_the_Galaxy-64) The Jedi Master informed Rex and Cody that they should prepare for a large number of incoming battle droids, with minimal [heavy cannons](/wiki/AV-7_Anti-vehicle_Artillery_Cannon "AV-7 Anti-vehicle Artillery Cannon") to defend their position with.[[72]](#cite_note-The_Hidden_Enemy-72) As Republic forces prepared to engage the droids, the blockade above Christophsis began reforming.[[64]](#cite_note-Battles_that_Changed_the_Galaxy-64)

##### Chaleydonia defense

:   "*That shield is certainly putting a crimp in my day.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi during the Battle of Christophsis — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/CrimpInMyDay-TCWf.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250404190201)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:CrimpInMyDay-TCWf.flac "File:CrimpInMyDay-TCWf.flac"))[[73]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-73)

 [![Kenobi fighting droids on Christophsis](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/95/ObiWanBattleofChristophsis-TCWf.png/revision/latest?cb=20121011231921) [![Kenobi fighting droids on Christophsis](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/95/ObiWanBattleofChristophsis-TCWf.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20121011231921)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/95/ObiWanBattleofChristophsis-TCWf.png/revision/latest?cb=20121011231921) 

Kenobi fighting droids on Christophsis

 

Kenobi and Skywalker maintained control over the planet for a short period of time, reporting its capture to the Jedi Council. The Jedi Master then sent a ship back to the Republic [fleet](/wiki/Fleet "Fleet") above Christophsis for a supplies restock, regretting the decision shortly after. Not long after, Palpatine requested that Jedi be sent to return [Rotta](/wiki/Rotta "Rotta")—the son of the [Hutt](/wiki/Hutt "Hutt") [crime lord](/wiki/Crime_lord "Crime lord") [Jabba](/wiki/Jabba_Desilijic_Tiure "Jabba Desilijic Tiure")—to his father in exchange for the usage of Outer Rim trade routes. As a result, Windu and Yoda sent orders through Admiral [Wullf Yularen](/wiki/Wullf_Yularen "Wullf Yularen") to ensure that the new Padawan [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano") landed on Christophsis to inform Kenobi and Skywalker of their next rescue mission assignment—assuming that the Jedi pair was done with their current engagement. However, on Christophsis, the Jedi pair continued to fight against more waves of enemy Separatist droids. While deflecting blast fire alongside Cody, Kenobi surmised that reinforcements would be needed soon.[[73]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-73)

 [![Kenobi and Skywalker waiting to greet a supply ship](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/07/City_Plaza.png/revision/latest?cb=20121008214003) [![Kenobi and Skywalker waiting to greet a supply ship](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/07/City_Plaza.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20121008214003)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/07/City_Plaza.png/revision/latest?cb=20121008214003) 

Kenobi and Skywalker waiting to greet a supply ship

 

Kenobi defended the Republic's defensive positions alongside his men, helping Skywalker with a plan to wipe out droids in a large avenue while heavy [cannons](/wiki/Cannon "Cannon") gave them cover fire. The Separatist General [Whorm Loathsom](/wiki/Whorm_Loathsom "Whorm Loathsom") decided to order his forces into a tactical retreat, surprising the Jedi. Seeing a Republic ship fly overhead, both assumed reinforcements or assistance had arrived. However, Kenobi and Skywalker then met Tano, who had arrived in the ship alone. Kenobi and his former apprentice used the ship to contact Yoda, who told them to return to Coruscant for a new [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Jabba%27s_Palace_(Clone_Wars) "Mission to Jabba's Palace (Clone Wars)"). When Yoda learned of the impending Separatist threat preventing their departure from Christophsis he promised to send reinforcements, but cut off mid-transmission. Though the Kenobi assumed Tano would be his new apprentice, she corrected him, relaying that Skywalker was to be her teacher.[[73]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-73)

 [![Kenobi captured Loathsom after his shield was destroyed](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/57/Loathsom_surrender.png/revision/latest?cb=20121010042632) [![Kenobi captured Loathsom after his shield was destroyed](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/57/Loathsom_surrender.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20121010042632)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/57/Loathsom_surrender.png/revision/latest?cb=20121010042632) 

Kenobi captured Loathsom after his shield was destroyed

 

While they awaited assistance, Loathsom used a deflector shield to protect his droids from attack while steadily advancing on the Republic's heavy cannons. Kenobi used a holographic display to brief others about the location of the shield generator, after which Skywalker and Tano brainstormed a plan to take it out while the Jedi Master and Rex stayed behind as a diversion. As the shield boundary increased, Kenobi ordered his men to fall back to a position further into the city. Meanwhile, he went under the shield with some of his troopers and began attacking enemy forces. Seeing that their efforts were in vain, Kenobi instructed Rex to have his men guard the heavy cannons while he delayed the droids. The Jedi Master proceeded to offer himself up in defeat to Loathsom, claiming that there were terms of surrender to discuss.[[73]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-73)

After Kenobi spent an extended period of time stalling by delaying to set terms of surrender or offer a flag of truce during which he was held at blasterpoint, Skywalker and Tano destroyed the shield using explosive charges. His refusal to stand down his forces angered and distracted Loathsom who had Kenobi seized and threatened to destroy him. On the destruction of the shield, Kenobi freed himself and was able to quickly restrain the Separatist general as Republic reinforcements arrived on the planet. Upon landing in a gunship before Kenobi, Yoda greeted the Jedi Master to begin telling him of Rotta's capture.[[73]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-73) While he managed to give Tano and Skywalker enough time to win the day for the Republic, his capture and subsequent stalling was a boon to Separatist propaganda for they were able to paint Kenobi's ruse as a false surrender and proof of Republic treachery. Ultimately, it ensured very few peace talks were held over the course of the war,[[74]](#cite_note-On_the_Front_Lines-74) with Kenobi indeed coming to show regret for the conflict's ongoing bloodshed.[[8]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-8)

##### Teth and Tatooine

:   "*We know of Dooku's plot to turn the Hutts against us. It will not succeed.*"  
    "*It will when the truth dies with you.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Asajj Ventress[[73]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-73)

 [![Kenobi negotiating with Jabba the Hutt.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/61/Obi-Wan_Jabba_negotiations.png/revision/latest?cb=20121013061829) [![Kenobi negotiating with Jabba the Hutt.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/61/Obi-Wan_Jabba_negotiations.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20121013061829)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/61/Obi-Wan_Jabba_negotiations.png/revision/latest?cb=20121013061829) 

Kenobi negotiating with Jabba the Hutt.

 

After greeting Yoda on Christophsis, Kenobi gave parting advice to Skywalker about training Tano before heading to Tatooine to negotiate with Jabba. The Jedi Master promised that Republic forces would successfully rescue his son, and listened to the Hutt's additional terms about capturing the kidnapper of his son, dead or alive. Kenobi then informed Skywalker that he had one planetary rotation to return Rotta[[73]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-73)—and also privately reflected that his meeting with Jabba had made him believe the Hutt had never [bathed](/wiki/Bath "Bath") in his life due to the smell.[[26]](#cite_note-SW7-26) The Jedi Master ordered his troops to depart for Teth next in an effort to [reinforce](/wiki/Battle_of_Teth "Battle of Teth") his former Padawan's forces. After Skywalker and Tano rescued Rotta from Teth's [B'omarr Order Monastery](/wiki/B%27omarr_Order_Monastery "B'omarr Order Monastery"), Kenobi arrived and fought with a fleet of fighters in Teth's atmosphere, but was unable to contact the other Jedi due to jammed transmissions.

 [![Kenobi dueling Ventress](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0c/KenobiVsVentress1.png/revision/latest?cb=20121013061544) [![Kenobi dueling Ventress](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0c/KenobiVsVentress1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20121013061544)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0c/KenobiVsVentress1.png/revision/latest?cb=20121013061544) 

Kenobi dueling Ventress

 

From the skies, he noticed a battle occurring on the rooftop of a building and followed his men down to the surface to find Skywalker. Kenobi found Ventress inside the monastery and fought in a brief lightsaber duel with her while exchanging banter. Skywalker and Tano escaped the planet with Rotta during their fight, and he eventually forced Ventress to flee after disabling one side of her [lightsabers](/wiki/Asajj_Ventress%27s_lightsabers "Asajj Ventress's lightsabers"). Once the fight concluded, Kenobi contacted his former apprentice and informed him that he would come to Tatooine to help as soon as Teth's situation settled. After Skywalker and Tano successfully returned Rotta to Jabba and cleared their name from the framing schemes of the Hutt [Ziro](/wiki/Ziro_Desilijic_Tiure "Ziro Desilijic Tiure") and Dooku, Kenobi and Yoda met the Jedi pair on Tatooine to negotiate a treaty with the crime lord.[[73]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-73)

##### A suspected defection

:   "*Our spies have spotted Separatist agents at the port where the* Halcyon *arrives tomorrow... That's where he'll try to make a rendezvous. And Obi-Wan already has it staked out with a unit of clone troopers, so—*"
:   ―Anakin regarding Obi-Wan's role in the Jedi Council's plan to catch the defected senator Zast Tri'vak[[75]](#cite_note-Halcyon3-75)

At some point following the negotiation of the Hutt Clan and Republic's treaty, the Jedi Council caught wind of [Lannik](/wiki/Lannik "Lannik") Senator [Zast Tri'vak](/wiki/Zast_Tri%27vak "Zast Tri'vak")'s plans to defect to the Confederacy of Independent Systems. Due to the risk Tri'vak's defection would present to important Republic supply routes, the Council took action. Skywalker and Senator Amidala were [sent](/wiki/Skirmish_on_the_Halcyon "Skirmish on the Halcyon") on board the Hutt-owned [MPO-1400 Purgill-class star cruiser](/wiki/MPO-1400_Purgill-class_star_cruiser "MPO-1400 Purgill-class star cruiser") known as the *[Halcyon](/wiki/Halcyon "Halcyon")* to catch the rogue senator, while Kenobi staked out the planned arrival port of the *Halcyon* with a unit of clone troopers. As things went awry on board the star cruiser when Asajj Ventress arrived to extract Tri'vak, the [Dark Acolyte](/wiki/Dark_Acolyte "Dark Acolyte") taunted Skywalker, claiming he was not much of a challenge without Kenobi by his side. Ultimately, the risk of Tri'vak's defection was negated with his death, as Ventress killed him to prevent him from spilling Separatist secrets to the Hutt Clan.[[75]](#cite_note-Halcyon3-75)

##### Ryloth's blockade

:   "*Senator, the fleet protecting Ryloth has been destroyed, and the supply lines have been cut. The troops are out of fuel, food, ammunition. And the civilian population is starving.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to Senator Bail Organa[[76]](#cite_note-Supply_Lines-76)

 [![Obi-Wan Kenobi in a Jedi Council meeting with Senator Bail Organa](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/Jedi_council_supply_lines.png/revision/latest?cb=20220330000658) [![Obi-Wan Kenobi in a Jedi Council meeting with Senator Bail Organa](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/Jedi_council_supply_lines.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20220330000658)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/Jedi_council_supply_lines.png/revision/latest?cb=20220330000658) 

Obi-Wan Kenobi in a Jedi Council meeting with Senator Bail Organa

 

At some point, Kenobi met with members of the Jedi Council in a hologram call to meet with Admiral [Dao](/wiki/Dao "Dao") from his post in the [orbit](/wiki/Orbit "Orbit") of the planet Ryloth, who was calling for aid at Jedi General [Ima-Gun Di](/wiki/Ima-Gun_Di "Ima-Gun Di")'s request. Dao informed the Councillors that his fleet was unable to continue aiding Republic forces on the world's surface due to the Separatist blockade around the planet, and his plea for help cut off mid-sentence when [his flagship](/wiki/Dao%27s_flagship "Dao's flagship") was destroyed. Following this, the Kenobi and his colleagues sent a [CR90 corvette](/wiki/CR90_corvette "CR90 corvette") blockade runner loaded with relief supplies to planet [Toydaria](/wiki/Toydaria "Toydaria") accompanied by [Representative](/wiki/Junior_Representative "Junior Representative") Jar Jar Binks of Naboo.[[76]](#cite_note-Supply_Lines-76)

Kenobi and his colleagues then proceeded to contact Senator Bail Organa and request his assistance in [negotiating](/wiki/The_Matter_of_Using_Toydarian_Territory_to_Aid_the_Shipment_of_Relief_Supplies_to_the_Citizens_of_Ryloth "The Matter of Using Toydarian Territory to Aid the Shipment of Relief Supplies to the Citizens of Ryloth") with [King](/wiki/King "King") [Katuunko](/wiki/Katuunko "Katuunko") of the planet Toydaria. Doing this, Kenobi explained, would allow Republic relief supplies to flow through the world as a [staging ground](/wiki/Staging_area "Staging area"). Moved by Kenobi's words, Organa agreed to travel to the negotiations to help the starving citizens of Ryloth. Eventually, the Senator was successful in delivering some of the supplies and gaining the favor of the Toydarian king.[[76]](#cite_note-Supply_Lines-76)

#### Missions across the galaxy

##### A secret superweapon

:   "*Tell me, has there been any word from Master Plo Koon or his fleet?*"  
    "*…actually, I just received word that Anakin has found the remains of Master Plo's fleet and is searching the debris for survivors.*"
:   ―Chancellor Palpatine and Obi-Wan Kenobi[[77]](#cite_note-Rising_Malevolence-77)

 [![Obi-Wan Kenobi in a conference about Plo Koon's fleet destruction.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6a/AbregadohologramKenobi.png/revision/latest?cb=20220419222017) [![Obi-Wan Kenobi in a conference about Plo Koon's fleet destruction.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6a/AbregadohologramKenobi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20220419222017)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6a/AbregadohologramKenobi.png/revision/latest?cb=20220419222017) 

Obi-Wan Kenobi in a conference about Plo Koon's fleet destruction.

 

When Master Plo Koon's fleet was destroyed in the [campaign](/wiki/Malevolence_Campaign "Malevolence Campaign") of the *Malevolence*—a secret Separatist superweapon—during the [Battle of Abregado](/wiki/Battle_of_Abregado "Battle of Abregado"), and Skywalker reported the [Kel Dor](/wiki/Kel_Dor "Kel Dor")'s interrupted message and loss of contact from the [Abregado system](/wiki/Abregado_system "Abregado system"). Kenobi watched his report alongside with Chancellor Palpatine, Windu, and Yoda, remarking that the Separatist operations were unusually tidy to maintain the secrecy of their weapon. In the meeting, Skywalker was ordered to reinforce Kenobi's fleet to protect supply convoys and not send a rescue for the attack's possible survivors from the Abregado system. Though Tano disagreed, she was overruled, with Kenobi fondly remarking that her outspoken behavior was likely learned from her Master.[[77]](#cite_note-Rising_Malevolence-77)

Kenobi's forces were joined by Admiral Yularen, who was commanding Skywalker's fleet. Upon questioning where his former apprentice was, Yularen explained the other general's self-redeployment to search for survivors in the Abregado system against orders. Kenobi then confronted Skywalker about his deviation from orders in a holographic call, prompting the wayward Jedi to meet with the Republic fleet as soon as possible. Though Tano claimed that the idea was hers, the Jedi Master doubted her claim, ordering them back to defensive escort duty upon learning no survivors had been found. In a meeting with Palpatine, Windu, and Yoda, Kenobi relayed Skywalker's detour and his hope to find Koon and his troopers still alive. Though the decision was deemed reckless by Yoda, Kenobi assured the group that his former apprentice's fleet was where it needed to be in defensive formation, as he had gone with only a small ship and his Padawan. Shortly after, Skywalker and Tano managed to rescue Koon and some of his men from the debris of their destroyed ships, escaping Separatist pursuit. As the first survivors of the superweapon, they were able to report to the Jedi Council what the *Malevolence*'s capabilities were, including its [ion cannons](/wiki/Ion_cannon "Ion cannon").[[77]](#cite_note-Rising_Malevolence-77)

 [![Kenobi and Yularen reporting to Nala Se](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/95/Obi-Wan_reports_to_Nala_Se.png/revision/latest?cb=20120918003237) [![Kenobi and Yularen reporting to Nala Se](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/95/Obi-Wan_reports_to_Nala_Se.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120918003237)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/95/Obi-Wan_reports_to_Nala_Se.png/revision/latest?cb=20120918003237) 

Kenobi and Yularen reporting to Nala Se

 

Upon learning of the *Malevolence*'s next target—the [Kaliida Shoals Medical Center](/wiki/Kaliida_Shoals_Medical_Center "Kaliida Shoals Medical Center") in the Outer Rim—Kenobi and Skywalker formulated a daring plan to engage and destroy the *Malevolence*'s ion cannons with his [Shadow Squadron](/wiki/Shadow_Squadron "Shadow Squadron") clone pilots. While Skywalker traveled through the nearby [Kaliida Nebula](/wiki/Kaliida_Nebula "Kaliida Nebula") with his squadron, Kenobi led the Republic fleet of ships through [hyperspace](/wiki/Hyperspace "Hyperspace") to the medical station. As his former apprentice [engaged](/wiki/Battle_of_the_Kaliida_Nebula "Battle of the Kaliida Nebula") the enemy vessel, Kenobi entered the system and began destroying the massive warship using the combined firepower of his fleet as the enemy vessel fled. Along with Wullf Yularen, Kenobi helped organize the evacuation of the medical center with Yularen, dispatching medical frigates. While Skywalker's task force proved successful in destroying its cannons,[[78]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_Malevolence-78) the *Malevolence*'s defenses withstood the fire of Kenobi's fleet for some time.[[79]](#cite_note-Destroy_Malevolence-79) After thanking Skywalker for his assistance, Kenobi ordered the ships under his command to continue pursuit of the *Malevolence* as it fled to Separatist space[[78]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_Malevolence-78) with a damaged hyperdrive.[[79]](#cite_note-Destroy_Malevolence-79)

##### *Malevolence* encounter

:   "*That's your plan— Just fly there, land, hope they don't spot us, and walk in the door?*"  
    "*Basically.*"  
    "*Oh, brilliant. Let's get going.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f3/AnakinMalevolencePlan.flac/revision/latest?cb=20251109031215)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:AnakinMalevolencePlan.flac "File:AnakinMalevolencePlan.flac"))[[79]](#cite_note-Destroy_Malevolence-79)

 [![Kenobi during the Malevolence pursuit](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c8/MalevolencePursuit.png/revision/latest?cb=20220420055328) [![Kenobi during the Malevolence pursuit](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c8/MalevolencePursuit.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20220420055328)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c8/MalevolencePursuit.png/revision/latest?cb=20220420055328) 

Kenobi during the *Malevolence* pursuit

 

During the pursuit, Kenobi discussed contacting additional reinforcements with Koon, but resolved to continue with the ships he had due to a lack of available forces in the area. The Master concluded that this could be the Republic's opportunity to destroy Grievous by firing on the enemy ship's bridge, having surmised that the *Malevolence*'s hyperdrive was damaged due to the vessel not fleeing. Shortly after, in a trap arranged by Dooku and executed by Palpatine, Amidala arrived at the battle's scene having been fed false information regarding a diplomatic mission in the system. Using her as a hostage, Grievous forced the Republic's fleet to stall their attack, further encouraged by Skywalker's insistence on mounting a rescue.[[79]](#cite_note-Destroy_Malevolence-79)

Kenobi joined Skywalker in a small ship, intending to sneak on the Separatist warship by slipping past the ship's damaged sensors and docking at an emergency airlock. Though the older Jedi was skeptical of the plan and his former apprentice's flying tricks, Skywalker claimed that the enemy forces were focused on handling repairs rather than watching for intruders. After successfully landing on the *Malevolence*, the pair quickly destroyed the battle droids greeting them. Kenobi and Skywalker were patched through to direct communication with Amidala, who informed them of her location and also berated them for coming to rescue her rather than continue with destroying the warship. Tano informed the trio that the best place to meet would be a large, open area in the center of the ship, which the Jedi and Senator began heading to.[[79]](#cite_note-Destroy_Malevolence-79)

 [![Kenobi clashing with Grievous onboard the Malevolence.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/Kenobi_vs_Grievous_Malevolence.png/revision/latest?cb=20120918231002) [![Kenobi clashing with Grievous onboard the Malevolence.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/Kenobi_vs_Grievous_Malevolence.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120918231002)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/Kenobi_vs_Grievous_Malevolence.png/revision/latest?cb=20120918231002) 

Kenobi clashing with Grievous onboard the *Malevolence*.

 

After the Jedi rescued Amidala from droids at their rendezvous, Kenobi used the Force to levitate C-3P0 toward him, though the droid got carried away by a [rail jet](/wiki/Rail_jet "Rail jet") [hovertrain](/wiki/Hovertrain "Hovertrain"). He informed Skywalker of this, and left his former apprentice to reacquire the droid while he would sabotage the hyperdrive. Kenobi's transmission was intercepted by Grievous, who challenged the Jedi's skills in front of the droids on his bridge. The Jedi Master then made his way to the ship's hyperdrive, but was met with an ambush consisting of many battle droids and Grievous himself. After escaping the situation by destroying the majority of the droids, Kenobi fled to the rail jets on the *Malevolence* while followed by Grievous. He and the cyborg engaged in a brief lightsaber duel that ended when the Jedi landed on a lower platform and made his way to Skywalker's escape ship.[[79]](#cite_note-Destroy_Malevolence-79)

Amidala, Skywalker, Kenobi, and their droids fled the *Malevolence* and contacted the Republic fleet as Grievous pursued in a personal starship. As they fled towards safety, the droids aboard the enemy warship completed repairs of its hyperdrive. Grievous gave the order for the *Malevolence* to flee, which resulted in the warship crashing into the nearby [Dead Moon of Antar](/wiki/Dead_Moon_of_Antar "Dead Moon of Antar") due to the coordinates in its [navi-computer](/wiki/Navigation_computer "Navigation computer") being sabotaged. Kenobi was surprised by the move, and was informed by Skywalker that it was always part of their plan. After the destruction of his warship, Grievous fled in his ship while the Jedi and their fleet celebrated.[[79]](#cite_note-Destroy_Malevolence-79)

##### Attack of Rishi Station

:   "*General Kenobi, General Skywalker.*"  
    "*Cody. How goes the inspections?*"  
    "*The tracking station in Pastil is fully operational. Captain Rex and I are proceeding to the outpost in the Rishi system.*"  
    "*Good. Report back once you've arrived.*"
:   ―Cody and Obi-Wan Kenobi[[80]](#cite_note-Rookies-80)

 [![Kenobi honored troopers that defended Rishi Station.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/62/EchoFivesHonored-Rookies.png/revision/latest?cb=20200515142201) [![Kenobi honored troopers that defended Rishi Station.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/62/EchoFivesHonored-Rookies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20200515142201)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/62/EchoFivesHonored-Rookies.png/revision/latest?cb=20200515142201) 

Kenobi honored troopers that defended Rishi Station.

 

As weeks passed, Kenobi and Skywalker continued their search for Grievous and his fleet and sent Cody and Rex on an inspection run of their quadrant of space. The pair briefly discussed the intelligence they had regarding the matter, with Kenobi noting that they would find the enemy general eventually. He and his former apprentice were present for Cody's report on his inspections to a [Pastil](/wiki/Pastil "Pastil") tracking station, and the commander further said that his next inspection would be at a [listening post](/wiki/Listening_post "Listening post") [station](/wiki/Rishi_Station "Rishi Station") in the [Rishi system](/wiki/Rishi_system "Rishi system")—an outpost crucial to warning Kamino of potential Separatist attacks. After thanking Cody for his work, Kenobi praised the clone to Yularen and Skywalker, then suggested that his former Padawan get some rest.[[80]](#cite_note-Rookies-80)

While on the [Rishi Moon](/wiki/Rishi_Moon "Rishi Moon") outpost, which had been taken over by droid forces, Cody and Rex's ship was [destroyed](/wiki/Defense_of_Rishi_Station "Defense of Rishi Station") and they lost contact with Kenobi's fleet. [Hours](/wiki/Standard_hour "Standard hour") after their scheduled check in, Yularen attempted to contact them to no avail. Though Kenobi felt that perhaps Rex was the cause of the delay, Skywalker retorted that the opposite could be true of Cody. Both resolved to devise a more efficient strategy to find Grievous, leaving Yularen in charge of contacting the clone officers. Not long after, Yularen was notified that the all-clear-signal on Rishi had been deactivated, prompting Kenobi to sound an invasion alarm and order his fleet to the Rishi system. The Jedi's fleet arrived just in time to force Grievous' ships out of the system, foiling the cyborg's plot to launch a surprise attack on Kamino. After the incident, Kenobi thanked the surviving clones that had defended the station—[Echo](/wiki/Echo "Echo") and [Fives](/wiki/Fives "Fives")—in a [medal](/wiki/Unidentified_medal_(Defense_of_Rishi_Station) "Unidentified medal (Defense of Rishi Station)") ceremony.[[80]](#cite_note-Rookies-80)

At some point, Kenobi and Skywalker crashed their [Y-wing](/wiki/BTL_Y-wing_starfighter "BTL Y-wing starfighter") into a shield protecting a city near the [Senatorial Palace](/wiki/Senatorial_Palace "Senatorial Palace") as they [investigated](/wiki/Investigation_on_Rodia "Investigation on Rodia") the activities of some rogue Nightsisters on [Rodia](/wiki/Rodia "Rodia"). When the shield was abruptly activated, the starfighter was entirely destroyed, while the dome remained unaffected.[[81]](#cite_note-Mustafar_and_Other-81)

##### Skytop Station campaign

:   **Ahsoka Tano**: "*Suicide is not the Jedi way, Master.*"
:   **Obi-Wan Kenobi**: "*You should listen to your Padawan.*"
:   **Anakin Skywalker**: "*As you listened to yours, my old master? No, we're going to stay and fight.*"
:   ―Ahsoka Tano, Obi-Wan Kenobi, and Anakin Skywalker [Listen](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e2/StayAndFight-DoaD.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250329120406 "StayAndFight-DoaD.flac") ([help](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Media_help "wikipedia:Wikipedia:Media help")·[info](/wiki/File:StayAndFight-DoaD.flac "File:StayAndFight-DoaD.flac"))[[82]](#cite_note-Downfall_of_a_Droid-82)

 [![Kenobi ordered Skywalker to retreat from his post at Bothawui.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/ReportFromFalleen-DOAD.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120612164141) [![Kenobi ordered Skywalker to retreat from his post at Bothawui.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/ReportFromFalleen-DOAD.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120612164141)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/ReportFromFalleen-DOAD.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120612164141) 

Kenobi ordered Skywalker to retreat from his post at Bothawui.

 

Following his escape, Grievous began ambushing Republic fleets in the [Skytop Station campaign](/wiki/Skytop_Station_campaign "Skytop Station campaign") and [defeated](/wiki/Battle_of_Falleen "Battle of Falleen") forces on[[82]](#cite_note-Downfall_of_a_Droid-82) the planet[[83]](#cite_note-TarkinNovel-83) [Falleen](/wiki/Falleen_(planet) "Falleen (planet)").[[82]](#cite_note-Downfall_of_a_Droid-82) Both the Jedi and the Republic has struggles against Grievous, who achieved many victories for the Separatists, proving to be a nearly indestructible opponent for them, leaving a trail of conquest and destruction across the galaxy.[[84]](#cite_note-The_Separatists-84) Kenobi advised Skywalker to retreat from his post at[[82]](#cite_note-Downfall_of_a_Droid-82) the [gas giant](/wiki/Gas_giant "Gas giant")[[85]](#cite_note-Galactic_Atlas-85) [Bothawui](/wiki/Bothawui "Bothawui"), citing that Grievous' fleet outnumbered his. Tano agreed with the Master, though Skywalker insisted on staying to protect the [sector](/wiki/Bothan_Space "Bothan Space"). Skywalker managed to [destroy](/wiki/Battle_of_Bothawui "Battle of Bothawui") the cyborg's flotilla at the cost of losing his droid, R2-D2.[[82]](#cite_note-Downfall_of_a_Droid-82)

A captured R2-D2 managed to send the coordinates of [Skytop Station](/wiki/Skytop_Station "Skytop Station")—a secret Separatist listening post—to Skywalker and Tano. After reporting the information to Kenobi using [scramble code 1477](/wiki/Scramble_code_1477 "Scramble code 1477"), he instructed them to wait for reinforcements. Though Skywalker wanted to rescue his droid, Kenobi ordered him to destroy the station instead. After the [mission](/wiki/Raid_on_Skytop_Station "Raid on Skytop Station") and unsanctioned rescue, an exasperated Kenobi grudgingly accepted Skywalker's retrieval to the [droid](/wiki/Astromech_droid "Astromech droid") with only a brief rebuke for the reckless behavior. While Tano agreed that the Kenobi's reasoning, Skywalker explained that he knew she could complete the mission on her own so he could rescue R2-D2.[[86]](#cite_note-Duel_of_Droids-86)

##### Dooku on Vanqor

:   "*Anakin when I tell you to run, run.*"  
    "*Master! You're alive.*"  
    "*And where's your lightsaber?*"  
    "*It got knocked out of my hand.*"  
    "*By a rock?*"  
    "*Yeah, by a rock.*"
:   ―Anakin Skywalker and Obi-Wan Kenobi, in Vanqor's caves[[87]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured-87)

 [![Obi-Wan Kenobi using an enviro-suit](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/Kenobi_space_walk.png/revision/latest?cb=20120924045022) [![Obi-Wan Kenobi using an enviro-suit](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/Kenobi_space_walk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20120924045022)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/Kenobi_space_walk.png/revision/latest?cb=20120924045022) 

Obi-Wan Kenobi using an enviro-suit

 

In their efforts to track the location of Dooku, Kenobi helped devise a plan to trick the Sith into revealing his location. As part of this [plot](/wiki/Skirmish_at_Vanqor "Skirmish at Vanqor"), Skywalker allowed himself to be captured[[87]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured-87) by pretending his [Delta-7B *Aethersprite*-class light interceptor](/wiki/Delta-7B_Aethersprite-class_light_interceptor "Delta-7B Aethersprite-class light interceptor") was dead in space, which prompted the Count to tow it aboard a Separatist [*Munificent*-class](/wiki/Munificent-class_star_frigate "Munificent-class star frigate") [star frigate](/wiki/Count_Dooku%27s_frigate "Count Dooku's frigate") to discover where it was stationed. Kenobi then traveled to his friend's last known location—an ice field near the Outer Rim planet [Vanqor](/wiki/Vanqor "Vanqor")—using an [enviro-suit](/wiki/Environment_suit "Environment suit")[[88]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured_ShortStory-88) and [jetpack](/wiki/Jetpack "Jetpack") to travel through space. After sneaking aboard the frigate, Kenobi successfully freed Skywalker from his detention cell and returned his [lightsaber](/wiki/Skywalker_lightsaber "Skywalker lightsaber") to him. The younger Jedi felt annoyed that he had been the one to be captured, which led Kenobi to tease that when he became a Jedi Master, he could make the plans.[[87]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured-87)

 [![Kenobi in a cave on Vanqor](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/37/ObiWanKenobi-ArdentAvenger-SWDConv.png/revision/latest?cb=20190416025038) [![Kenobi in a cave on Vanqor](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/37/ObiWanKenobi-ArdentAvenger-SWDConv.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20190416025038)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/37/ObiWanKenobi-ArdentAvenger-SWDConv.png/revision/latest?cb=20190416025038) 

Kenobi in a cave on Vanqor

 

Kenobi and Skywalker confronted Dooku in his meditation chamber, acting in a proud way that disgusted the older man. The Sith quickly used an escape chute to head towards the vessel's hangar to head to his [*Punworcca 116*-class](/wiki/Punworcca_116-class_interstellar_sloop "Punworcca 116-class interstellar sloop") [interstellar sloop](/wiki/Count_Dooku%27s_solar_sailer "Count Dooku's solar sailer"), followed by Skywalker. After Dooku successfully took off in his escape vessel,[[88]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured_ShortStory-88) Kenobi and Skywalker pursued him in a stolen [*Sheathipede*-class transport shuttle](/wiki/Sheathipede-class_transport_shuttle "Sheathipede-class transport shuttle") and called on Tano to rally Republic reinforcements.[[87]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured-87) The Jedi scored a direct hit on Dooku's sloop that knocked out his engines, forcing him to make a crash landing on Vanqor.[[88]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured_ShortStory-88) However, the damage done to Kenobi and Skywalker's stolen shuttle by the Sith's escort also necessitated their own emergency landing on the same world. As their ship touched ground, both Jedi exchanged playful banter about piloting and destroyed the [homing beacon](/wiki/Homing_beacon "Homing beacon") on Dooku's crashed ship.[[87]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured-87)

The Jedi pair surveyed the area, deciding to start their search for the Sith in Vanqor's caves.[[87]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured-87) Dooku manipulated the Force to flare the barest hint of his Force presence within the caves, which the Jedi picked up as he had planned.[[88]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured_ShortStory-88) When Kenobi and Skywalker entered the caves, Dooku crashed down the loosened rock above the entrance using [telekinesis](/wiki/Telekinesis "Telekinesis"), trapping them inside. Though both survived, Skywalker had lost his lightsaber, which Kenobi chided him for while cleaning his own weapon. The Jedi Master watched in amusement as a large gundark went after his former apprentice, but eventually helped him throw rocks at the creature to cease its attacks. When the caves started to fill with poison gas, Tano rescued the pair—though both indignantly claimed that they had not needed help and were productively tracking Dooku. After escaping, Kenobi and Skywalker contacted the Jedi Council.[[87]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured-87)

##### Ohnaka's pirates
