:   "*They are devious and deceitful and, most importantly, stupid.*"  
    "*It's a wonder you don't get along with them, Dooku. You have so much in common.*"
:   ―Dooku and Obi-Wan Kenobi, about Ohnaka's pirates[[87]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured-87)

 [![Kenobi and Skywalker with a captured Dooku](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/47/Epguide11.png/revision/latest?cb=20120924044609) [![Kenobi and Skywalker with a captured Dooku](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/47/Epguide11.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20120924044609)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/47/Epguide11.png/revision/latest?cb=20120924044609) 

Kenobi and Skywalker with a captured Dooku

 

After learning that Dooku was captured by [Captain](/wiki/Captain "Captain") [Hondo Ohnaka](/wiki/Hondo_Ohnaka "Hondo Ohnaka")'s [pirates](/wiki/Ohnaka_Gang "Ohnaka Gang") on Vanqor and brought to the planet [Florrum](/wiki/Florrum "Florrum"), who hoped to trade him for a hefty ransom from the Republic, the Jedi Council agreed to send Kenobi and Skywalker to verify his capture following the suggestion of Amidala. Windu informed the Jedi of their next assignment, and the stipulation that they arrive unarmed. Though both Kenobi and Skywalker were uneasy with what could become a hostile situation, Windu insisted on the importance of the mission. After landing in a small ship, both were led to the pirates' [stronghold](/wiki/Hondo%27s_complex "Hondo's complex") cells and saw Dooku hanging from restraints. Though the Sith attempted to warn the pair that the pirates would turn traitor on them, both refused spent time sneering and scoffing at him. When the two Jedi reported in after speaking to Ohnaka, Palpatine had Binks and Senator [Kharrus](/wiki/Kharrus "Kharrus") lead a diplomatic [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Florrum "Mission to Florrum") to trade a ransom for the Count.[[87]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured-87)

 [![Kenobi and Skywalker with Ohnaka](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/Skywalker_Ohnaka_Kenobi.png/revision/latest?cb=20120924051504) [![Kenobi and Skywalker with Ohnaka](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/Skywalker_Ohnaka_Kenobi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120924051504)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/Skywalker_Ohnaka_Kenobi.png/revision/latest?cb=20120924051504) 

Kenobi and Skywalker with Ohnaka

 

Kenobi and Skywalker attended a feast after their business concluded, and accepted offered refreshments. However, before a [toast](/wiki/Toast_(ritual) "Toast (ritual)") both swapped their cups with their pirate neighbors and discovered shortly after that Ohnaka had attempted to poison them when both collapsed.[[87]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured-87) After taking a sip of their drinks, both woke up in restraints connected to the Dooku's bindings. After briefly arguing with the Sith, Kenobi and Skywalker agreed that they would form a plan to escape their situation. When Dooku opened their cell using a Force-levitated knife, Kenobi grudgingly told his former apprentice to let the Separatist focus. Though the trio escaped from the room they were in, they were recaptured by Ohnaka's pirates shortly after.[[89]](#cite_note-The_Gungan_General-89)

Ohnaka confronted Kenobi, Skywalker, and Dooku, warning them not to escape again to ruin his chance at a profit. When the captain left Kenobi mind tricked a guard into opening their cell. The trio crept through the pirate compound, exchanging tense banter. Eventually, Dooku broke them through a wall and they raced to the edge of the compound. However, Ohnaka caught up to them and put them back in a cell, eventually having them separated from Dooku and hung by restraints in front of a group of pirates. The captain informed them that their Republic had not arrived with Dooku's ransom and proceeded to electrocute the pair. When Dooku escaped the compound and knocked out the area's electrical supply, Kenobi and Skywalker were freed, holding Ohnaka as a hostage using their lightsabers. Binks and his clone escort arrived, providing the Jedi with transport off Florrum. Though it surprised Ohnaka, Kenobi ordered Skywalker to let him go free, as Jedi do not take revenge—though warned that Dooku did not share their same mindset.[[89]](#cite_note-The_Gungan_General-89)

##### Orto Plutonia

:   "*Now that you have created peace between your people and the Talz, remember one crucial thing…*"  
    "*Yes, Master Kenobi?*"  
    "*Make it last, senator. Make it last.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Riyo Chuchi[[90]](#cite_note-Trespass-90)

 [![Kenobi and Skywalker met with the Talk people.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Chieftains_hut.png/revision/latest?cb=20120928034307) [![Kenobi and Skywalker met with the Talk people.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Chieftains_hut.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120928034307)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Chieftains_hut.png/revision/latest?cb=20120928034307) 

Kenobi and Skywalker met with the Talk people.

 

Called to the cold planet [Orto Plutonia](/wiki/Orto_Plutonia "Orto Plutonia") to ascertain why the Republic had lost contact with a clone [outpost](/wiki/Glid_Station "Glid Station"), Kenobi and Skywalker, along with [Pantoran](/wiki/Pantoran "Pantoran") [Chairman](/wiki/Chairman "Chairman") [Chi Cho](/wiki/Chi_Cho "Chi Cho") and Senator [Riyo Chuchi](/wiki/Riyo_Chuchi "Riyo Chuchi") from the nearby moon [Pantora](/wiki/Pantora "Pantora"), traveled to the Republic base. They found it to be to be devoid of life, as all clones [stationed](/wiki/Orto_Plutonia_clone_security_force "Orto Plutonia clone security force") there having been killed—with a monument of their [helmets](/wiki/Helmet "Helmet") erected inside. After visiting a nearby [Separatist base](/wiki/Separatist_outpost_(Orto_Plutonia) "Separatist outpost (Orto Plutonia)"), similar destruction was found, leading Kenobi to believe that the murders at the Republic's base were done by a third unknown party. Logs showed mysterious warriors had taken out the Separatist droids when investigating the world's southern canyon, which Kenobi decided would be a good starting point for their investigation.[[90]](#cite_note-Trespass-90)

 [![Kenobi surprised by a hug given by Thi-Sen in lieu of a handshake.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d9/ObiWanHugged-Trespass.png/revision/latest?cb=20120928033012) [![Kenobi surprised by a hug given by Thi-Sen in lieu of a handshake.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d9/ObiWanHugged-Trespass.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120928033012)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d9/ObiWanHugged-Trespass.png/revision/latest?cb=20120928033012) 

Kenobi surprised by a hug given by Thi-Sen in lieu of a handshake.

 

When Skywalker and Kenobi headed to the location they met the leader of the [Talz](/wiki/Talz "Talz") people [Thi-Sen](/wiki/Thi-Sen "Thi-Sen") and their associates, communicating with the natives using rudimentary hand signals and drawings. The Jedi learned that battle droids had attacked the Talz and the clones were accidentally caught in the middle of the conflict. The pair returned to the Republic base, and knowing that the Talz only wanted peace, arranged a diplomatic meeting between the Pantorans and Talz. However, Chi Cho angrily refused to accept any peaceful outcome and provoked a war between him and Thi-Sen's people as he refused to accept peace despite the protests of Chuchi and the Jedi. He declared it an internal affair of Pantora to remove the Jedi from the equation, ordering them to submit to him because they were under the Senate's jurisdiction.[[90]](#cite_note-Trespass-90)

When Skywalker and Kenobi appealed to Chuchi to find a way to resolve the political matter diplomatically, she contacted the Speaker of the [Pantoran Assembly](/wiki/Pantoran_Assembly "Pantoran Assembly") who granted her the authority to negotiate peace and declared the Chairman out of order. Though Chuchi wanted the Jedi to negotiate on Pantora's behalf, they refused, as it was her people who the Talz were warring with. However, the solution came too late as Chi Cho was [attacked](/wiki/One-Day_War "One-Day War") before Kenobi, Skywalker, and Chuchi landed and halted the Talz's attack. To settle the conflict between the Pantorans and the Talz, Chuchi met with Thi-Sen, establishing an agreement that allowed the Talz to live in peace on the planet. As the Senator and the Jedi boarded a gunship off-world, Kenobi congratulated the Senator in establishing peace and urged her to make it last and act as an example to others.[[90]](#cite_note-Trespass-90) The Jedi Master felt that the peace achieved through the balancing of both sides had been a unique challenge.[[56]](#cite_note-HJJEncylopedia-56)

##### Blue Shadow Virus

:   "*A great leap forward often requires taking two steps back.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi[[91]](#cite_note-Mystery_of_a_Thousand_Moons-91)

 [![Kenobi in the virabl bomb room of Nuvo Vindi's bio-lab](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/Obi-Wan_virus_bombs.png/revision/latest?cb=20121002025500) [![Kenobi in the virabl bomb room of Nuvo Vindi's bio-lab](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/Obi-Wan_virus_bombs.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20121002025500)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/Obi-Wan_virus_bombs.png/revision/latest?cb=20121002025500) 

Kenobi in the virabl bomb room of Nuvo Vindi's bio-lab

 

The Jedi Council later agreed to send Kenobi, Skywalker, and Tano, to Naboo in response to intelligence that suggested that a Separatist bio-lab had been set up on the planet at Amidala's suggestion. When Amidala and Binks lost contact while searching for the lab, Skywalker sent Tano along with the Gungan native [Peppi Bow](/wiki/Peppi_Bow "Peppi Bow") to locate them. Meanwhile, Kenobi and Skywalker arrived on Naboo learned from new information discovered by Captain [Gregar Typho](/wiki/Gregar_Typho "Gregar Typho") that Separatist scientist [Nuvo Vindi](/wiki/Nuvo_Vindi "Nuvo Vindi") was using the lab to perfect the deadly [Blue Shadow Virus](/wiki/Blue_Shadow_Virus "Blue Shadow Virus") so as to release it into key Republic star systems. Kenobi and Skywalker proceeded to plan an [infiltration](/wiki/Raid_on_Nuvo_Vindi%27s_laboratory "Raid on Nuvo Vindi's laboratory") of the facility to prevent the virus from being spread across [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy").[[92]](#cite_note-Blue_Shadow_Virus-92)

While they waited in the hangar bay, Kenobi took note of Skywalker's increased levels of agitation during the mission. After being contacted by Tano, Kenobi and Skywalker left instructions for her to cause a diversion. On the other side of the lab, the pair entered and met with her before beginning a search for Vindi's [viral bombs](/wiki/Viral_bomb "Viral bomb"). Kenobi located the room where the bombs were held with his clone troopers, instructing his men to deactivate them all. Though Vindi attempted to release the virus, the Jedi were able to apprehend him and rescue Amidala and Binks.[[92]](#cite_note-Blue_Shadow_Virus-92)

 [![Kenobi talking to an Angel on Iego](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/de/Angel2.png/revision/latest?cb=20121002230157) [![Kenobi talking to an Angel on Iego](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/de/Angel2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20121002230157)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/de/Angel2.png/revision/latest?cb=20121002230157) 

Kenobi talking to an Angel on Iego

 

As Kenobi and Skywalker prepared to transfer Vindi to Coruscant for trial, Tano, Amidala, and several clones discovered that a vial of the virus was missing. Though the alarm was sounded prior to the vial's detonation, the virus was released throughout the lab. Tano, Amidala, and the clones with them were compromised and infected by the virus. As they worked to ensure droids would not escape the facility, Skywalker and Kenobi implored the Naboo as to what the cure for the virus was. Upon learning it, the Jedi then flew to planet [Iego](/wiki/Iego "Iego") to [search](/wiki/Mission_to_Iego "Mission to Iego") for the [reeksa](/wiki/Reeksa "Reeksa") root antidote to the virus found there.[[91]](#cite_note-Mystery_of_a_Thousand_Moons-91)

While on Iego, Skywalker destroyed a number of reprogrammed battle droids owned by the local native [Jaybo Hood](/wiki/Jaybo_Hood "Jaybo Hood"), which Kenobi chided him for. Hood then told the pair where to find the antidote they were looking for, though warned it was dangerous. The young man also informed the Jedi that the phantom leader of Iego, [Drol](/wiki/Drol "Drol"), would not allow any individual to leave the planet. Kenobi and Skywalker rode a [xandu](/wiki/Xandu "Xandu") to the bottom of a ravine and quickly gathered some reeksa root before escaping from the carnivorous plant. Upon trying to leave Iego, the two Jedi discovered that "Drol" was actually a Separatist [laser security system](/wiki/LaserWeb_Defense_Station "LaserWeb Defense Station") surrounding the planet and enlisted Hood's help in destroying it despite the skepticism of the other natives. When successful, Kenobi and Skywalker traveled back to Naboo and delivered the antidote that saved Tano, Amidala, and the clone troopers. Kenobi also offered Binks blaster training to hone his skills, which the Gungan enthusiastically accepted.[[91]](#cite_note-Mystery_of_a_Thousand_Moons-91) After the event, the Jedi Master became more keenly aware of Skywalker's emotional instability when around Amidala and resolved to watch the pair more closely as the war continued.[[56]](#cite_note-HJJEncylopedia-56)

##### Invasion of Ryloth

:   "*We need to remember why we're here. We came to aid the Twi'leks, not destroy their home.*"
:   ―Kenobi to Ghost Company aboard the *Crumb Bomber* — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6c/AidTheTwileks-InnocentsOfRyloth.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250329114349)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:AidTheTwileks-InnocentsOfRyloth.flac "File:AidTheTwileks-InnocentsOfRyloth.flac"))[[93]](#cite_note-Innocents_of_Ryloth-93)

 [![Obi-Wan Kenobi and Mace Windu preparing to invade Ryloth](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/70/Obi-Wan_and_Mace_Storm_Over_Ryloth.png/revision/latest?cb=20121003232220) [![Obi-Wan Kenobi and Mace Windu preparing to invade Ryloth](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/70/Obi-Wan_and_Mace_Storm_Over_Ryloth.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20121003232220)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/70/Obi-Wan_and_Mace_Storm_Over_Ryloth.png/revision/latest?cb=20121003232220) 

Obi-Wan Kenobi and Mace Windu preparing to invade Ryloth

 

After the [Techno Union](/wiki/Techno_Union "Techno Union") leader [Wat Tambor](/wiki/Wat_Tambor "Wat Tambor") seized control of the planet Ryloth and its [inhabitants](/wiki/Twi%27lek "Twi'lek"), he implemented a blockade around the world with his [*Lucrehulk*-class Battleship](/wiki/Lucrehulk-class_battleship "Lucrehulk-class battleship") and two  *Munificent*-class frigates. The Jedi Council devised a plan for Kenobi and Windu to lead a ground assault to [invade and liberate](/wiki/Battle_of_Ryloth "Battle of Ryloth") the planet after the Senate requested them to intervene. Skywalker and Tano were dispatched to destroy the [Separatist blockade](/wiki/Ryloth_blockade "Ryloth blockade") surrounding the planet to support their effort.[[94]](#cite_note-Storm_Over_Ryloth-94)

The initial attempt to break the blockade was unsuccessful, which Skywalker reported to Kenobi and Windu as a heavy loss through hologram, considering the deceased clone pilots and sacrifice of the *Venator*-class Star Destroyer *[Redeemer](/wiki/Redeemer "Redeemer")*. Kenobi advised him to give Tano time to grieve the loss of [her squadron](/wiki/Blue_Squadron_(Galactic_Republic) "Blue Squadron (Galactic Republic)"), but added that he would need her assistance to complete their objectives. Windu informed Skywalker that he needed to break the blockade within the next planetary rotation for the invasion to continue. When Skywalker and Tano's second attempt is successful, Kenobi arrived with the rest of the [invasion forces](/wiki/Ryloth_invasion_fleet "Ryloth invasion fleet") in the planet's vicinity. Kenobi contacted Tano and she cleared them to begin their ground assault.[[94]](#cite_note-Storm_Over_Ryloth-94)

 [![Kenobi landed on Ryloth with Ghost Company troopers.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/85/Ghost_Company3.png/revision/latest?cb=20121004230204) [![Kenobi landed on Ryloth with Ghost Company troopers.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/85/Ghost_Company3.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20121004230204)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/85/Ghost_Company3.png/revision/latest?cb=20121004230204) 

Kenobi landed on Ryloth with Ghost Company troopers.

 

In preparing their assault, Windu asked Kenobi to consider capturing the city [Nabat](/wiki/Nabat "Nabat") first to secure a landing zone, which he agreed to. Kenobi then boarded a small transport with some of his men from [Ghost Company](/wiki/Ghost_Company "Ghost Company") and instructed them to do minimal damage to the local habitat and not harm natives. In space, the rest of Windu's fleet came under attack by Separatist forces. Windu contacted Kenobi and informed him that the Republic would be unable to use [*Acclamator*-class transgalactic military assault ships](/wiki/Acclamator-class_transgalactic_military_assault_ship "Acclamator-class transgalactic military assault ship") and other gunships from *[Crumb Bomber](/wiki/Crumb_Bomber "Crumb Bomber")* until the Separatist surface [proton cannons](/wiki/J-1_proton_cannon "J-1 proton cannon") were wiped out.[[93]](#cite_note-Innocents_of_Ryloth-93)

Kenobi and his men landed and steadily made their way to the outskirts of the city, taking out droids as they went. Using telekinesis, the Jedi helped levitate the [droid poppers](/wiki/Electromagnetic_pulse_grenade "Electromagnetic pulse grenade") thrown by his troopers [Waxer](/wiki/Waxer "Waxer") and [Boil](/wiki/Boil "Boil") to take out a bunker. After securing the wall perimeter Kenobi ordered Cody to send his best men to scout ahead, and the commander ultimately selected Waxer, Boil, and [Wooley](/wiki/Wooley "Wooley"). Scouting yielded useful intelligence, leading Cody to report to Kenobi and Windu the placements of the gun encampments as well as the Separatists' use of living Twi'lek shields. However, one of the tactical droid commander [TX-20](/wiki/TX-20 "TX-20")'s [probe droids](/wiki/Ringneck_recon_droid "Ringneck recon droid") recorded their strategy session and provided it to the leader. When Waxer and Boil failed to report in from scouting after meeting the Twi'lek child [Numa](/wiki/Numa "Numa"), Kenobi became concerned.[[93]](#cite_note-Innocents_of_Ryloth-93)

 [![Kenobi distracting gutkurrs](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d3/Obi-Wan_distracts_gutkurrs.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110921012102) [![Kenobi distracting gutkurrs](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d3/Obi-Wan_distracts_gutkurrs.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20110921012102)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d3/Obi-Wan_distracts_gutkurrs.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110921012102) 

Kenobi distracting gutkurrs

 

The general and his troops decided to move forward without the missing troopers, entering the village outskirts. They soon encountered starved native [gutkurrs](/wiki/Gutkurr "Gutkurr") that began to attack them. The Jedi lured the creatures into an alley using the Force so that the clones could trap them by collapsing a bridge between them. Shortly after, a pothole near them began to rattle, though Kenobi ordered his men to hold fire. When Waxer and Boil then emerged out of an underground tunnel with Numa, Kenobi talked to the girl in [Twi'leki](/wiki/Twi%27leki "Twi'leki") and learned that she could lead them to the prisoners. Tasking Cody with creating a diversion for the droids, Kenobi went with Waxer, Boil, and Numa to the underground passages and freed the Twi'lek hostages who fled into the tunnels.[[93]](#cite_note-Innocents_of_Ryloth-93)

 [![TX-20's tank targeted Kenobi and Numa.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/TX-20_targets_Obi-Wan_and_Numa.png/revision/latest?cb=20121005024846) [![TX-20's tank targeted Kenobi and Numa.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/TX-20_targets_Obi-Wan_and_Numa.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20121005024846)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/TX-20_targets_Obi-Wan_and_Numa.png/revision/latest?cb=20121005024846) 

TX-20's tank targeted Kenobi and Numa.

 

Then, the general proceeded to take control of a proton cannon and managed to take out their cannons with the help of Waxer and Boil loading fuel cartridges in. However, TX-20 blasted the three aside and threatened Kenobi, who was holding Numa in his arms. Before the droid could blast them, other Twi'leks rushed the droid and protected Kenobi, with the Jedi attempting to shield Numa's eyes from the violence. As Windu's transports from the *Acclamator*landed, Windu commended Kenobi on his victory and they continued with their next mission.[[93]](#cite_note-Innocents_of_Ryloth-93)

As the Republic's forces departed for the capital city [Lessu](/wiki/Lessu_City "Lessu City") Waxer and Boil inquired Kenobi about the meaning of "nerra," which the Jedi General translated as "brother."[[93]](#cite_note-Innocents_of_Ryloth-93) After Windu and and his forces reached Lessu, Kenobi led his contingent to capture the southern hemisphere of Ryloth and was able to successfully capture the [Jixuan desert](/wiki/Jixuan_desert "Jixuan desert"). With Windu taking Lessu and capturing Wat Tambor, the two Jedi Generals freed the planet from Separatist rule.[[95]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-95)

##### A stolen holocron

:   "*A holocron is no good without a Jedi to open it. What are they up to?*"  
    "*They must be trying to gain access to the communications center from the vault.*"  
    "*Let's get in there.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker pursuing Cad Bane[[96]](#cite_note-Holocron_Heist-96)

 [![Kenobi and Skywalker during the First Battle of Felucia](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/94/BattleOfFelucia-HH.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090926192328) [![Kenobi and Skywalker during the First Battle of Felucia](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/94/BattleOfFelucia-HH.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20090926192328)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/94/BattleOfFelucia-HH.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090926192328) 

Kenobi and Skywalker during the First Battle of Felucia

 

During the [First Battle of Felucia](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Felucia "First Battle of Felucia"), Kenobi was sent along with Skywalker and Tano to the Separatist-invaded planet [Felucia](/wiki/Felucia "Felucia"). While Kenobi stayed with the main body of troops to defend their clearing-based emplacement of AT-TE walkers, Tano led two AT-TE walkers and a [Juggernaut](/wiki/HAVw_A6_Juggernaut "HAVw A6 Juggernaut") tank on a patrol of the dense jungle. Kenobi realized that they were outnumbered, seeing that droids would soon outflank their position. He ordered an immediate retreat as soon as General Koon arrived to help them, prompting clones to prepare gunships for fleeing. The Jedi Master contacted Tano to do so as well, but the Padawan refused to retreat—claiming her foes were retreating. When Skywalker and Kenobi arrived to pick her up, she refused to pull back until Skywalker convinced her that the battle was lost. As their gunship flew away, Kenobi, Skywalker, and Tano observed the position she had been at erupt in flames.[[96]](#cite_note-Holocron_Heist-96)

 [![Kenobi and Skywalker tracked Bane as he stole a Jedi holocron.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/11/Stolen_holocron.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090904002734) [![Kenobi and Skywalker tracked Bane as he stole a Jedi holocron.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/11/Stolen_holocron.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20090904002734)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/11/Stolen_holocron.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090904002734) 

Kenobi and Skywalker tracked Bane as he stole a Jedi holocron.

 

Once back at the Jedi Temple, Kenobi reported to rest of the Jedi Council about Tano's reckless actions during the battle. As a result, she was assigned to guard duty in the Jedi Archives under the supervision of Jocasta Nu. Kenobi and Skywalker attended a strategy session after the meeting to discuss the effects of Felucia's loss. As they talked, Yoda felt a disturbance in the Force and warned the pair that there would be intruders in the Temple soon. Kenobi and Skywalker surmised that any intruders would likely be breaking in to steal Jedi transmitter codes and military information, and set out to protect the [communications center](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_communication_center "Jedi Temple communication center"). However by using the assistance of the helper droid [Todo 360](/wiki/Todo_360 "Todo 360"), the bounty hunter [Cad Bane](/wiki/Cad_Bane "Cad Bane") managed to [sneak](/wiki/Raid_on_the_Jedi_Temple "Raid on the Jedi Temple") into the Temple. The Jedi pair noticed their systems rebooting and acting strangely and located a disturbance in the Temple's ventilation shafts with advice from Yoda.[[96]](#cite_note-Holocron_Heist-96)

Kenobi and Skywalker discovered the vent Bane had entered, but were unable to locate the criminal despite their best efforts. Yoda informed them that their intruders were deep in the Temple and had likely received outside help. From the Archives, Tano captured Bane's [changeling](/wiki/Changeling "Changeling") associate [Cato Parasitti](/wiki/Cato_Parasitti "Cato Parasitti") and informed the pair of this. Kenobi and Skywalker assumed that Bane would try to access the communications tower from the [Holocron Vault](/wiki/Holocron_Vault "Holocron Vault") and headed to the tower. Bane took the opportunity to steal a Jedi holocron and sneak out of the building while Kenobi and Skywalker narrowly avoided a bomb set off by Todo 360 in the ventilation shafts. Parasitti revealed Bane's next target would be the Jedi [Bolla Ropal](/wiki/Bolla_Ropal "Bolla Ropal"), the keeper of a [kyber memory crystal](/wiki/Kyber_memory_crystal "Kyber memory crystal") that stored the names of every Force-sensitive child in the galaxy. Kenobi then proceeded to lead Parasitti away while Skywalker and Tano set out to warn Ropal.[[96]](#cite_note-Holocron_Heist-96)

##### Pursuit on Rodia

:   "*There are thousands of children on that list. Which will he go after first?*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi[[97]](#cite_note-Children_of_the_Force-97)

 [![Kenobi meeting Mahtee Dunn](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/MahteeDunnHoldup-CotF.png/revision/latest?cb=20120829224618) [![Kenobi meeting Mahtee Dunn](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/MahteeDunnHoldup-CotF.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120829224618)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/MahteeDunnHoldup-CotF.png/revision/latest?cb=20120829224618) 

Kenobi meeting Mahtee Dunn

 

Bane managed to capture and [torture](/wiki/Torture "Torture") Ropal, only stopping when Jedi arrived on his ship. Despite Skywalker and Tano's best efforts, the criminal escaped in his ship.[[98]](#cite_note-Cargo_of_Doom-98) Both reported back to Kenobi and Yoda afterward, who worried about the future harm done to the children on the list. Kenobi and other Jedi meditated to sense through the Force which children would be harmed first, coming up with a small list of locations for their efforts—including a child on[[97]](#cite_note-Children_of_the_Force-97) the planet[[4]](#cite_note-USW_NE-4) Rodia that he sensed. Kenobi then flew to the planet and met the [Rodian](/wiki/Rodian "Rodian") [Mahtee Dunn](/wiki/Mahtee_Dunn "Mahtee Dunn"), the child's mother, and informed her that her child [Wee Dunn](/wiki/Wee_Dunn "Wee Dunn") had been taken by a bounty hunter posing as a Jedi. He caught up to Bane shortly after while he was holding the child while using a Jedi cloak as a disguise.[[97]](#cite_note-Children_of_the_Force-97)

 [![Kenobi defending against Bane's automated laser defense system on Black Stall Station](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/KenobiBlackStallStation-CotF.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101111205624) [![Kenobi defending against Bane's automated laser defense system on Black Stall Station](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/KenobiBlackStallStation-CotF.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20101111205624)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/KenobiBlackStallStation-CotF.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101111205624) 

Kenobi defending against Bane's automated laser defense system on Black Stall Station

 

Using a [grappling hook](/wiki/Grappling_hook "Grappling hook"), Kenobi pursued Bane across several rooftops, but eventually watched the bounty hunter escape in a [*Rogue*-class Porax-38 starfighter](/wiki/Rogue-class_Porax-38_starfighter "Rogue-class Porax-38 starfighter") *[Xanadu Blood](/wiki/Xanadu_Blood "Xanadu Blood")*. Though the bounty hunter successfully delivered two children to the planet [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar"), he was caught on Naboo by Skywalker and Tano in his third kidnapping attempt. Kenobi interrogated Bane aboard a *Venator*-class Star Destroyer, and used a combined Force mind trick alongside Skywalker and Windu to compel him into agreeing to locate the holocron. Though Windu felt that this was an internal matter, Skywalker insisted on reporting to Palpatine of the discover, which the younger Jedi's former Master eventually agreed to.[[97]](#cite_note-Children_of_the_Force-97)

Kenobi and Windu then traveled with a restrained Bane to [Black Stall Station](/wiki/Black_Stall_Station "Black Stall Station") and retrieved the missing holocron, but were forced to let him escape through an escape pod after being caught in the station's traps. After Tano and Skywalker [retrieved](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar_(Skywalker_and_Tano) "Mission to Mustafar (Skywalker and Tano)") the pair of missing children, they reported to the full Jedi Council.[[97]](#cite_note-Children_of_the_Force-97) Kenobi's efforts to assist the stolen child were remembered by the Rodian [Chekkoo clan](/wiki/Chekkoo_clan "Chekkoo clan"). Stories of the event were circulated shortly after and he was regarded by many on the world as a hero.[[99]](#cite_note-HOTJ-99)

##### Felucia and bounty hunters

:   "*We can't just wander around aimlessly. We need a plan.*"  
    "*You always taught me to go on instinct, and my instincts tell me to go that way.*"  
    "*No that—that doesn't seem right. I think we should go this way.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker[[100]](#cite_note-Bounty_Hunters-100)

 [![Kenobi, Skywalker, and Tano made a crash landing on Felucia.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/Survival_capsules_open.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110923025948) [![Kenobi, Skywalker, and Tano made a crash landing on Felucia.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/Survival_capsules_open.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20110923025948)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/Survival_capsules_open.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110923025948) 

Kenobi, Skywalker, and Tano made a crash landing on Felucia.

 

The [disappearance](/wiki/Destruction_of_the_Felucia_medical_station "Destruction of the Felucia medical station") of a [medical station](/wiki/Felucia_Medical_Station_HCTFF2 "Felucia Medical Station HCTFF2") orbiting over Felucia prompted the Jedi Council to send Kenobi, Skywalker, and Tano to investigate the issue. Once in the system, their ship was shot down by Separatist [vulture droids](/wiki/Vulture-class_starfighter "Vulture-class starfighter") from an [automated vulture droid deployment station](/wiki/Automated_vulture_droid_deployment_station "Automated vulture droid deployment station"). Forced to make a crash landing, the trio ejected from the ship moments before it exploded. Kenobi and Skywalker proceeded to argue about which direction to go, but eventually followed Tano's lead after seeing smoke in the sky indicating civilization. They soon came across a [nysillin](/wiki/Nysillin "Nysillin") farm village, confounded by its apparent desertion.[[100]](#cite_note-Bounty_Hunters-100)

After discovering that the village had been undergoing pirate raids, the three Jedi met the four bounty hunters that the local [Felucian](/wiki/Felucian "Felucian") [farmers](/wiki/Farmer "Farmer") had hired to protect them—[Sugi](/wiki/Sugi_(bounty_hunter) "Sugi (bounty hunter)"), [Embo](/wiki/Embo "Embo"), [Rumi Paramita](/wiki/Rumi_Paramita "Rumi Paramita"), and [Seripas](/wiki/Seripas "Seripas"). The village elder [Casiss Midagatis](/wiki/Casiss_Midagatis "Casiss Midagatis") explained their current situation, pleading for the Jedi's help. However, Kenobi declined and insisted on reporting the missing medical station even though Tano disagreed. Ohnaka's pirates arrived at the village shortly after, and Kenobi conversed with their leader while the rest of the gang looked on as they reflected on[[100]](#cite_note-Bounty_Hunters-100) their past meeting on Florrum.[[89]](#cite_note-The_Gungan_General-89)

 [![Sugi, Kenobi, and others coming to the aid of Embo.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/88/Embo_hurt.png/revision/latest?cb=20120910211120) [![Sugi, Kenobi, and others coming to the aid of Embo.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/88/Embo_hurt.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120910211120)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/88/Embo_hurt.png/revision/latest?cb=20120910211120) 

Sugi, Kenobi, and others coming to the aid of Embo.

 

The Jedi Master proposed a deal to the pirates to trade a large sum of credits for a ride to the nearest Republic outpost. However, Ohnaka declined and left, insisting that he would stay for his share of nysillin. Though not willing to directly commit to fighting pirates, Kenobi and the other Jedi agreed to help train the Felucian farmers to fight for themselves. Kenobi expressed skepticism with Sugi's methods, but grudgingly resolved to hope she could do her job. Skywalker struggled to train the civilians with him as his former Master watched, but eventually helped the villagers learn some skills.[[100]](#cite_note-Bounty_Hunters-100)

After a [pirate scout](/wiki/Unidentified_pirate_scout "Unidentified pirate scout") was killed by Embo near the village when caught, Kenobi noted that when the spy failed to report it would be noticed by Ohnaka. A [skirmish](/wiki/Skirmish_on_Felucia "Skirmish on Felucia") ensued shortly after, ultimately ending in a win for the villagers, Jedi, and bounty hunters. Sugi then offered Kenobi, Skywalker, and Tano a ride back to the nearest Republic outpost, which they accepted.[[100]](#cite_note-Bounty_Hunters-100)

##### The Zillo Beast

:   "*Why would the Chancellor want to bring the beast here? He thinks that by studying it, the knowledge could prove beneficial, but from what you reported, it hardly seems worth the effort.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi[[101]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast_Strikes_Back-101)

 [![Kenobi worked with Republic forces to subdue the Zillo Beast.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/03/RexConfers-ZBSB.png/revision/latest?cb=20120912230505) [![Kenobi worked with Republic forces to subdue the Zillo Beast.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/03/RexConfers-ZBSB.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20120912230505)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/03/RexConfers-ZBSB.png/revision/latest?cb=20120912230505) 

Kenobi worked with Republic forces to subdue the Zillo Beast.

 

Following the discovery of the [Zillo Beast](/wiki/Zillo_Beast "Zillo Beast") during the [Battle of Malastare](/wiki/Battle_of_Malastare "Battle of Malastare")[[102]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast-102) and its transference to Coruscant, Windu shared his concerns with Kenobi while in the Temple. He agreed with the other Jedi Master, he suggested to let Skywalker convince Palpatine to send the beast back to its origins. Kenobi then approached Senator Amidala to help him—who in turn helped him convince Skywalker to reason with Palpatine. However, the Chancellor had already ordered [Doctor](/wiki/Doctor "Doctor") [Sionver Boll](/wiki/Sionver_Boll "Sionver Boll") to kill the beast to extract its scales by using poison. When the administration of it agitated the creature, it smashed its way out of the laboratory and started [rampaging](/wiki/Zillo_Beast_incident "Zillo Beast incident") across Coruscant to reach the [Senate](/wiki/Imperial_Senate_Building "Imperial Senate Building") building with Palpatine in it.[[101]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast_Strikes_Back-101)

Deployed to contain the beast, Kenobi and Windu managed to save the Chancellor using the Force and, later, commanded gunships to distract the beast together with Yoda and the Jedi [Aayla Secura](/wiki/Aayla_Secura "Aayla Secura") while the Chancellor escaped with Skywalker, Amidala, R2-D2, and C-3PO. Kenobi and Windu worked to use the Force to hold their escape ship from falling off the edge of a roof, saving Palpatine. As the gunships arrived and killed the creature by firing poison gas bombs into into its mouth, they and the others looked on in regret. When the Zillo Beast succumbed to the poison, it fell from the roof of the Senate to its death below.[[102]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast-102)

### The war drags on

#### Many meetings

Kenobi later participated in a meeting in which he and the council assigned Amidala to spy on [Rush Clovis](/wiki/Rush_Clovis "Rush Clovis"), whom they believed to be a Separatist spy.[[103]](#cite_note-Senate_Spy-103) He was also present alongside Master Yoda and Master Windu to assign Billaba and her [battalion](/wiki/Depa_Billaba%27s_battalion "Depa Billaba's battalion") to [engage](/wiki/Third_Battle_of_Mygeeto "Third Battle of Mygeeto") the enemy on [Mygeeto](/wiki/Mygeeto "Mygeeto").[[104]](#cite_note-Kanan_9-104)

#### Second Battle of Geonosis

:   "*I cannot believe we're back here again.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi[[55]](#cite_note-Landing_at_Point_Rain-55)

 [![Kenobi, other Jedi and the Chancellor plan their invasion of Geonosis.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/52/GeonosisPlanning.png/revision/latest?cb=20120831044545) [![Kenobi, other Jedi and the Chancellor plan their invasion of Geonosis.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/52/GeonosisPlanning.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20120831044545)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/52/GeonosisPlanning.png/revision/latest?cb=20120831044545) 

Kenobi, other Jedi and the Chancellor plan their invasion of Geonosis.

 

Assigned to capture Geonosis, alongside [Ki-Adi-Mundi](/wiki/Ki-Adi-Mundi "Ki-Adi-Mundi"), [Luminara Unduli](/wiki/Luminara_Unduli "Luminara Unduli"), Skywalker, and Tano, Kenobi participated in a conference to delineate the [invasion](/wiki/Second_Battle_of_Geonosis "Second Battle of Geonosis") plans to destroy [Poggle the Lesser](/wiki/Poggle_the_Lesser "Poggle the Lesser")'s primary droid factory, which was being protected by a massive ray shield. With their primary target being the shield generator at the Ray Shield Fortress the Jedi mounted a three-pronged attack on the Geonosian defenses. Kenobi and Cody commenced the central push while Mundi and Skywalker led the northern and southern assaults, respectively. Though Kenobi was able to reach the landing zone, which was known as [Point Rain](/wiki/Point_Rain "Point Rain"), the Jedi General was injured and forced to wait for Skywalker and Mundi's arrival who, despite their crashing, managed to fight their way up and join Kenobi. In a combined effort, they managed to destroy the shield generator, and Kenobi and Mundi returned to the fleet with the rest of the wounded for treatment.[[55]](#cite_note-Landing_at_Point_Rain-55)

Following the Republic's hard-won victory that was cemented after the factory's destruction by Skywalker, Tano, Unduli, and Unduli's Padawan [Barriss Offee](/wiki/Barriss_Offee "Barriss Offee")[[105]](#cite_note-Weapons_Factory-105) Kenobi returned to the planet and mounted an intense campaign to find Poggle, with Unduli spearheading the search only to follow Poggle to the [Progate Temple](/wiki/Progate_Temple "Progate Temple"), where she was captured by the Archduke and taken to the lair of Geonosian Queen [Karina the Great](/wiki/Karina_the_Great "Karina the Great") in the catacombs below. Tracking Unduli's last known location, Kenobi and Skywalker set out with a clone [platoon](/wiki/Platoon "Platoon") to rescue her, and entered the catacombs only to find themselves before the Queen and her "undead" servants. Soon enough, and thanks to Kenobi's plans, they freed Luminara, captured Poggle and escaped the temple, while destroying much of the Queen's lair during their escape, burying Karina the Great and her warriors beneath.[[106]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Terror-106) Kenobi, Mundi, Unduli, and Skywalker, then, took Poggle to Coruscant for interrogation, while Offee and Tano brought to supplies to Windu and [Kit Fisto](/wiki/Kit_Fisto "Kit Fisto") on [Dantooine](/wiki/Dantooine "Dantooine").[[107]](#cite_note-Brain_Invaders-107)

#### Saleucami

:   "*The story of Obi-Wan Kenobi ends here.*"
:   ―General Grievous, about to finish Kenobi[[59]](#cite_note-Grievous_Intrigue-59)

Soon after Jedi Master and Council member [Eeth Koth](/wiki/Eeth_Koth "Eeth Koth") was [captured](/wiki/Capture_of_Eeth_Koth "Capture of Eeth Koth") by Grievous, Kenobi, Skywalker, and [Adi Gallia](/wiki/Adi_Gallia "Adi Gallia") volunteered to [engage](/wiki/Battle_of_Saleucami "Battle of Saleucami") the Confederacy at Saleucami, rescue Koth, and capture General Grievous.[[59]](#cite_note-Grievous_Intrigue-59)

 [![Kenobi engages Grievous in the docking tube.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/Grievous_vs._Kenobi_Saleucami.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110918195404) [![Kenobi engages Grievous in the docking tube.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/Grievous_vs._Kenobi_Saleucami.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20110918195404)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/Grievous_vs._Kenobi_Saleucami.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110918195404) 

Kenobi engages Grievous in the docking tube.

 

General Kenobi was the first of the Jedi to arrive at Saleucami and engaged Grievous's forces with a fleet under the command of Admiral Yularen. Early in the battle, Kenobi's [light cruiser](/wiki/Arquitens-class_light_cruiser "Arquitens-class light cruiser"), the *[Surrogator](/wiki/Surrogator "Surrogator")*, was caught in a tractor beam from Grievous's [warship](/wiki/Grievous%27s_Recusant-class_light_destroyer "Grievous's Recusant-class light destroyer") and boarded by the cyborg himself. Once Skywalker and Gallia rescued Koth, Grievous dueled Kenobi until understanding that the Jedi Master had the upper hand. As the cyborg retreated to his destroyer, he ordered his ship to destroy Kenobi's—who managed to board Grievous' ship with Cody and two other clones before it was too late thanks to Gallia's help. Afterwards, they reunited with Skywalker on the hangar so that they could escape from Grievous' ship. Meanwhile, Grievous was forced to flee in an [escape pod](/wiki/Escape_pod "Escape pod") and landed on the planet.[[59]](#cite_note-Grievous_Intrigue-59)

While his fellow Jedi generals continued the battle in orbit, Kenobi led a force of clone troopers to the planet's surface to hunt down Grievous. The cyborg general evaded and fled from the Republic forces, hoping to reach an escape pod with a functioning transmitter in order to call for an evacuation transport. When Kenobi caught up with and engaged Grievous, the cyborg fled the battle once a shuttle arrived to ferry him away. Seeing as the mission had failed, Kenobi contacted Rex and told him to meet them to leave the planet.[[108]](#cite_note-TD-108)

#### Mandalore's Death Watch

:   "*We'll have to stand and fight. Or in your case, just stand.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi to Satine Kryze — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cc/StandAndFight-TMP.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250328200119)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:StandAndFight-TMP.flac "File:StandAndFight-TMP.flac"))[[32]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot-32)

 [![The memorial shrine being bombed as Kenobi and Duchess Satine Kryze looked on.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/Memorial_Shrine_bombing.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100130044121) [![The memorial shrine being bombed as Kenobi and Duchess Satine Kryze looked on.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/Memorial_Shrine_bombing.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20100130044121)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/Memorial_Shrine_bombing.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100130044121) 

The memorial shrine being bombed as Kenobi and Duchess Satine Kryze looked on.

 

When rumors spread that the new leader of the [Council of Neutral Systems](/wiki/Council_of_Neutral_Systems "Council of Neutral Systems"), Duchess Satine Kryze, was secretly building her own army to fight for the Separatist cause, Kenobi was [sent](/wiki/Mandalore_Defense_Resolution "Mandalore Defense Resolution") to [Sundari](/wiki/Sundari "Sundari") by the Jedi Council to investigate the matter. There, he met [Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister "Prime Minister") [Almec](/wiki/Almec "Almec") and re-encountered his old friend, Kryze, who assured him that she was not behind an [attack](/wiki/Attack_on_a_Republic_cruiser "Attack on a Republic cruiser") on a Republic cruiser. Angered at the accusations, she claimed the Senate was eager to intervene in the planet's affairs before being corrected by Kenobi, who claimed to be there on the Jedi Order's interest. Assuaged, the Duchess then took Kenobi for a walk on [Peace Park](/wiki/Peace_Park "Peace Park") and informed him of a renegade group of warriors known as [Death Watch](/wiki/Death_Watch "Death Watch") when a terrorist [blew up](/wiki/Attack_on_the_Memorial_Shrine "Attack on the Memorial Shrine") the [Memorial Shrine](/wiki/Memorial_Shrine "Memorial Shrine") where Kryze and Kenobi were walking. When Kenobi had the guards round up everyone at the scene, a [man](/wiki/Death_Watch_bomber "Death Watch bomber") fled with Kenobi after him and committed suicide instead of being captured. As the Duchess spoke to the dying man, she realized he came from [Concordia](/wiki/Concordia "Concordia") and helped Kenobi reach the moon, where the Jedi Master met its [Governor](/wiki/Governor "Governor"), [Pre Vizsla](/wiki/Pre_Vizsla "Pre Vizsla").[[32]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot-32)

 [![Kenobi engaging Pre Vizsla in a duel.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3c/Kenobi_vs_Vizsla.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100130031114) [![Kenobi engaging Pre Vizsla in a duel.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3c/Kenobi_vs_Vizsla.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20100130031114)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3c/Kenobi_vs_Vizsla.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100130031114) 

Kenobi engaging Pre Vizsla in a duel.

 

Kenobi went out to investigate the [mines](/wiki/Concordian_mines "Concordian mines") and discovered that the Death Watch was using one of the facilities as a base. Taken hostage by the Death Watch, he contacted Kryze, who freed him, and together, they tried to escape when they were attacked and the Commander of the Death Watch arrived. Revealing himself to be Vizsla, he returned Kenobi's lightsaber and dueled him with the [Darksaber](/wiki/Darksaber "Darksaber"), until he ordered his warrior to kill him with missiles. Kenobi and Kryze managed to escape, barely surviving, and returned to Mandalore. The next day, Kenobi told the Duchess that he believed the Separatists were involved, which only angered her; the Jedi Master, then, was joined by Skywalker so as to bodyguard her during her and other senators' trip to Coruscant onboard the *[Coronet](/wiki/Coronet "Coronet")*.[[32]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot-32)

On their way to the Republic's capital, Kenobi took part of a heated debate with the Duchess over what the best course of action was to deal with the conflict until they took a small break. Then, Skywalker asked him Kenobi of their past, which Kenobi explained he and his master, Jinn, had been protecting her during a year-long, dangerous mission during a civil war on Mandalore. It was then that [assassin droids](/wiki/Assassin_droid "Assassin droid") were activated, prompting Kenobi to defend Kryze. When the droids were stopped, Skywalker reported to Kenobi that one of the senators was a traitor, and Kenobi then devised a plan to uncover the traitor's identity by using the last active droid.[[34]](#cite_note-Voyage_of_Temptation-34)

 [![Kryze safely arriving on Coruscant thanks to Kenobi's help.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/63/Obi-Wan_Satine_VoT.png/revision/latest?cb=20120906224122) [![Kryze safely arriving on Coruscant thanks to Kenobi's help.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/63/Obi-Wan_Satine_VoT.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20120906224122)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/63/Obi-Wan_Satine_VoT.png/revision/latest?cb=20120906224122) 

Kryze safely arriving on Coruscant thanks to Kenobi's help.

 

It turned out to be [Tal Merrik](/wiki/Tal_Merrik "Tal Merrik"), who took Kryze as a hostage and made his way to the [cockpit](/wiki/Cockpit "Cockpit") to jump out of hyperspace, so that droid reinforcements could enter the ship. While Skywalker engaged the droids, Kenobi found and followed Merrik, who would blow up the ship, as he got near the escape pods, unable to make a move on the senator. Afraid she might not see Kenobi again, Kryze confessed her feelings for him, to which Kenobi replied he would have left the Order if she had told him earlier. Then, Kryze took the opportunity to escape a disgusted Merrik and take his blaster. However, neither Kenobi nor Kryze made a move to stop him, leaving Skywalker to sneak up from behind and stab him in the back, branding himself as a "cold-blooded killer." After arriving on Coruscant, Kenobi and Kryze reflected upon the situation, and the Duchess flirted with him, saying his beard hid too much of his "handsome face."[[34]](#cite_note-Voyage_of_Temptation-34)

When Kryze's pleas to the Senate to not interfere with Mandalore's internal affairs went unheard, Kenobi reunited with the Duchess, advising her not to be rash, angering her. Soon enough, she fell victim to another terrorist attack and barely survived, prompting the Senate to accelerate the vote—with the Republic deciding to occupy Mandalore. Despite Kenobi's plea to help her, Kryze took matters in her own hands, only to framed with murder by the Death Watch.[[109]](#cite_note-Duchess_of_Mandalore-109)

 [![Chancellor Palpatine apologizing to Duchess Satine Kryze.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/SKASOWKPAPMA-DoM.png/revision/latest?cb=20120907214500) [![Chancellor Palpatine apologizing to Duchess Satine Kryze.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/SKASOWKPAPMA-DoM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20120907214500)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/SKASOWKPAPMA-DoM.png/revision/latest?cb=20120907214500) 

Chancellor Palpatine apologizing to Duchess Satine Kryze.

 

Asking for his help, Kenobi met her and accepted to give Senator Amidala the disc she had obtained from his contact. Despite an attack by a Death Watch assassin and Kryze turning herself in, Kenobi got the disc through to Amidala, who then played the complete recording from Deputy Prime Minister [Jerec](/wiki/Jerec "Jerec") in front of the Senate—prompting the Senate to vote against Mandalore's occupation. When the Duchess received the apologies and thanks from the Chancellor and Mas Amedda, Kenobi received her thanks, though the two reflected about not knowing who tried to drag Mandalore into war and have the Duchess framed for murder.[[109]](#cite_note-Duchess_of_Mandalore-109)

#### Kamino under attack

:   "*All too easy.*"  
    "*Define 'easy,' General.*"
:   ―Grievous and Kenobi[[110]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-110)

 [![Kenobi leading clone troops in defense of Tipoca City](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b0/KnowledgeAndDefense-CWCS.png/revision/latest?cb=20190724045930) [![Kenobi leading clone troops in defense of Tipoca City](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b0/KnowledgeAndDefense-CWCS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190724045930)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b0/KnowledgeAndDefense-CWCS.png/revision/latest?cb=20190724045930) 

Kenobi leading clone troops in defense of Tipoca City

 

After the destruction of the Rishi Moon tracking station, Kenobi and Skywalker intercepted a coded message between Ventress and Grievous about an impending attack on the clone homeworld. Generals Kenobi and Skywalker, Commander Cody, Captain Rex, and troopers of the [501st Legion](/wiki/501st_Legion "501st Legion") subsequently rushed to Kamino to aid in its defense. As their ship docked and hundreds of clones exited, Kenobi and Skywalker met with Shaak Ti and [Lama Su](/wiki/Lama_Su "Lama Su") to warn them of the attack. When the [Battle of Kamino](/wiki/Battle_of_Kamino "Battle of Kamino") began, Kenobi and Cody joined Shaak Ti in the command center as Skywalker flew up with a squadron to participate in the space battle.[[110]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-110)

As the battle in the space above Kamino raged on, Kenobi noticed that something was amiss as the Separatist transports took heavy damage. As debris rained down into the seas on Kamino, Kenobi warned Skywalker not to attack, believing that not even Grievous would attack so recklessly and that the enemy was up to something. He took a submarine and discovered Ventress's forces readying their assault crafts under water. Several [AQ-series battle droids](/wiki/AQ-series_battle_droid "AQ-series battle droid") attacked his submarine, forcing him to eject, but he escaped thanks to a passing [aiwha](/wiki/Aiwha "Aiwha"). Rejoining the fight, which had now been taken to Tipoca City, Kenobi worked alongside Skywalker again and determined that the sparse Separatist forces must be a distraction and directed his former Padawan to go defend the [clone DNA room](/wiki/Clone_DNA_room "Clone DNA room") while he sought out Grievous. Inside the city, he found the cyborg general and engaged him in a duel.[[110]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-110)

Using the Force to his advantage, Kenobi chased Grievous outside, where he was surprise-attacked and knocked off of the platform by a [*Trident*-class assault ship](/wiki/Trident-class_assault_ship "Trident-class assault ship"). However, he was once again rescued by an aiwha. As the clone forces won the battle, Kenobi recovered and the Republic won the day. However, Grievous and Ventress were able to escape once again.[[110]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-110) At some stage of the war, Kenobi was involved in another incident on Kamino; amid a rainstorm, he wielded his lightsaber and deflected a blaster bolt as he led clones in battle.[[111]](#cite_note-Knowledge_and_Defense-111)

#### Ziro hunted

:   "*I never did enjoy hanging out with you.*"
:   ―Kenobi to Quinlan Vos, hanging off the side of a cliff[[112]](#cite_note-Hunt_for_Ziro-112)

 [![Kenobi dueling Bane on Teth.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/BaneKenobi-Showdown.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101111151446) [![Kenobi dueling Bane on Teth.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/BaneKenobi-Showdown.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20101111151446)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/BaneKenobi-Showdown.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101111151446) 

Kenobi dueling Bane on Teth.

 

Later during the war, after the [Senate hostage crisis](/wiki/Senate_hostage_crisis "Senate hostage crisis"), Kenobi was assigned to track down Ziro the Hutt and Cad Bane with his old friend, Jedi Master [Quinlan Vos](/wiki/Quinlan_Vos "Quinlan Vos"). The two of them headed to [Nal Hutta](/wiki/Nal_Hutta "Nal Hutta"), where they informed [Gardulla](/wiki/Gardulla_Besadii_the_Elder "Gardulla Besadii the Elder") the Hutt and the rest of the [Hutt council](/wiki/Grand_Hutt_Council "Grand Hutt Council") of Ziro's escape and of Bane's help in this act. Though the Hutt Council denied involvement in this, Vos was able to [psychometrically](/wiki/Psychometry "Psychometry") scan a cup, telling him and Kenobi that Ziro had been there. When they got to the [prison](/wiki/Prison "Prison") level, however, Ziro had already escaped due to help from his lover, [Sy Snootles](/wiki/Sy_Snootles "Sy Snootles"). Kenobi and Vos then tracked Ziro down in the [swamp](/wiki/Swamp "Swamp"), where they saw Bane following Ziro as well, and found [Ziro's mother](/wiki/Mama "Mama") who told them that his son had gone to Teth, where he would secretly recover the [Hutt Council records](/wiki/Hutt_Council_records "Hutt Council records").[[112]](#cite_note-Hunt_for_Ziro-112)

Kenobi and Vos then proceeded to Teth, where they found Ziro shot and dead at his [father's](/wiki/Papa "Papa") grave, and were then confronted by Bane. Though Bane tried to leave, Kenobi attempted to arrest Bane for taking the Senate hostage and engaged in a [duel](/wiki/Showdown_on_Teth "Showdown on Teth") with the bounty hunter. Despite the Jedi's best efforts, Bane used his flamethrowers to throw them off the cliff, leaving the two to hang on a cliff, and escaped.[[112]](#cite_note-Hunt_for_Ziro-112)

#### Dathomirian threat

:   "*Warrior-like men, witches—this place has all kinds of fun.*"
:   ―Anakin Skywalker to Kenobi, on Dathomir[[113]](#cite_note-Witches_of_the_Mist-113)

During the [Battle of Sullust](/wiki/Battle_of_Sullust "Battle of Sullust"), Kenobi was chased by Asajj Ventress in her [*Ginivex*-class fanblade starfighter](/wiki/Ginivex-class_fanblade_starfighter "Ginivex-class fanblade starfighter"). Skywalker managed to dispatch the [tri-fighter](/wiki/Droid_tri-fighter "Droid tri-fighter") that the assassin had sent for him and came to the aid of his former master. He then crippled Ventress's vessel, but not before she managed to shoot down the Jedi Master. The two opposing commanders crash-landed in the hangar of the Separatist [command ship](/wiki/Unidentified_Providence-class_carrier/destroyer_(Battle_of_Sullust) "Unidentified Providence-class carrier/destroyer (Battle of Sullust)"), Kenobi and Skywalker quickly engaged Ventress in lightsaber combat. Count Dooku, upon orders from his own master, interrupted the duel by ordering the destruction of the Separatist command ship to ensure Ventress's death. The two Jedi fled in their interceptors, presuming Ventress to be doomed, but she escaped and Dooku ordered the remaining Separatist forces to retreat, thinking she was dead.[[114]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-114)

 [![Kenobi facing Savage Opress on Toydaria](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/ShowdownOnToydaria-WOTM.png/revision/latest?cb=20130524040641) [![Kenobi facing Savage Opress on Toydaria](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/ShowdownOnToydaria-WOTM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130524040641)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/ShowdownOnToydaria-WOTM.png/revision/latest?cb=20130524040641) 

Kenobi facing Savage Opress on Toydaria

 

After the [massacre](/wiki/Devaron_massacre "Devaron massacre") on [Devaron](/wiki/Devaron "Devaron"),[[115]](#cite_note-Monster-115) Kenobi and Skywalker were sent to [Dathomir](/wiki/Dathomir "Dathomir"), as footage had shown the Council of a [Dathomirian's](/wiki/Savage_Opress "Savage Opress") role during the attack on Devaron. Once on Dathomir, they made their way to a [village](/wiki/Nightbrother_village "Nightbrother village"), where they were ambushed by the [Nightbrothers](/wiki/Nightbrothers "Nightbrothers") until Skywalker took [their leader](/wiki/Viscus "Viscus") hostage; the Zabrak then told the Jedi that a [Nightsister](/wiki/Nightsisters "Nightsisters") had taken one of their [fortress](/wiki/Nightsister_lair "Nightsister lair"), prompting the Jedi to go there. Kenobi and Skywalker questioned [Mother](/wiki/Mother_(title) "Mother (title)") [Talzin](/wiki/Talzin "Talzin") who told them his name—Savage Opress—and whereabouts. The two Jedi then headed to Toydaria where they confronted Opress, but failed to stop him from killing Katuunko. Using the king's ship as their was destroyed, Kenobi and Skywalker caught up with their target on Dooku's Separatist flagship; however, Opress managed to overpower them, forcing the two to retreat and leave the ship.[[113]](#cite_note-Witches_of_the_Mist-113)

#### Horain

 [![Obi-Wan Kenobi fights alongside Captain Rex during the Battle of Horain.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/96/Rex-Obi-Wan-team-up.png/revision/latest?cb=20231120023245) [![Obi-Wan Kenobi fights alongside Captain Rex during the Battle of Horain.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/96/Rex-Obi-Wan-team-up.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20231120023245)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/96/Rex-Obi-Wan-team-up.png/revision/latest?cb=20231120023245) 

Obi-Wan Kenobi fights alongside Captain Rex during the Battle of Horain.

 

At some point, Kenobi and Rex [participated](/wiki/Battle_of_Horain "Battle of Horain") in a battle on the world [Horain](/wiki/Horain "Horain"). During the conflict, the battle droid [B1-0516](/wiki/B1-0516 "B1-0516") was hit, gaining a conscience as a result, and began fighting on the side of the Republic. Kenobi and his partner were confused, using the opportunity caused in the chaos to escape the situation. They later rescued the droid, which had been slated for reprogramming due to the malfunction. The trio managed to fight off several waves of droids and make it to a Republic checkpoint, where Kenobi introduced the droid, now nicknamed "Bats," to Skywalker.[[116]](#cite_note-IDW_RogerRoger-116)

#### Mortis

:   "*Obi-Wan, have you done as I asked? Have you trained the boy?*"
:   ―Qui-Gon Jinn to Obi-Wan Kenobi[[117]](#cite_note-Overlords-117)

 [![Kenobi converses with the Force ghost of his master, Jinn.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9b/ObiWanQuiGon-Overlords.png/revision/latest?cb=20130524215723) [![Kenobi converses with the Force ghost of his master, Jinn.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9b/ObiWanQuiGon-Overlords.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20130524215723)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9b/ObiWanQuiGon-Overlords.png/revision/latest?cb=20130524215723) 

Kenobi converses with the Force ghost of his master, Jinn.

 

When the Jedi Council received a 2,000 year old Jedi distress code, Kenobi along with Skywalker and Tano were [sent](/wiki/Mission_to_Mortis "Mission to Mortis") to the [Chrelythiumn system](/wiki/Chrelythiumn_system "Chrelythiumn system"), where they were supposed to meet up with Captain Rex and an armed cruiser. Though they both made to the rendezvous point, neither Rex nor the Jedi's ship could see each other. In fact, the Jedi's ship was guided to a [mysterious planet](/wiki/Mortis "Mortis"), where they were met by a [mysterious figure](/wiki/Force_wielder "Force wielder") called the [Daughter](/wiki/Daughter "Daughter") who wanted to lead them to [The Father](/wiki/Father_(Mortis) "Father (Mortis)"). Shortly after, Skywalker and the Daughter were separated from Kenobi and Tano.[[117]](#cite_note-Overlords-117)

Trying to return to the [ship](/wiki/Jedi_shuttle_634 "Jedi shuttle 634"), Kenobi and Tano met the [Son](/wiki/Son "Son"), who suggested them to take shelter from the oncoming storm. In a cave, when Tano was asleep, his late master, Qui-Gon Jinn, [appeared](/wiki/Force_spirit "Force spirit") before him, explaining the purpose of the planet they were on and that the three figures they encountered, like Jinn, believed Skywalker was the Chosen One. As Jinn disappeared, Kenobi woke Tano up and they resolved to find Skywalker together, only for the Daughter and the Son to capture them for Skywalker's test. In danger of being killed by the Daughter, Kenobi was saved when Skywalker subdued their captors, proving himself to be the Chosen One, and the three Jedi tried to leave the planet.[[117]](#cite_note-Overlords-117)

 [![Kenobi trying to hand Skywalker the Dagger.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a1/KenobiMortisDagger-AOM.png/revision/latest?cb=20130525022122) [![Kenobi trying to hand Skywalker the Dagger.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a1/KenobiMortisDagger-AOM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20130525022122)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a1/KenobiMortisDagger-AOM.png/revision/latest?cb=20130525022122) 

Kenobi trying to hand Skywalker the Dagger.

 

However, Tano was abducted by the Son, which prompted Kenobi and Skywalker to go their separate ways. While Kenobi went to ask the Father—whom he thought would know what to do—for help, Skywalker went after the Son, fearing he would kill Tano. When he reached the [monastery](/wiki/Mortis_monastery "Mortis monastery"), he witnessed as the Son mortally wounded his Father, and asked the Daughter for help. She then showed him the [Altar](/wiki/Altar_of_Mortis "Altar of Mortis"), where he obtained a [dagger](/wiki/Dagger_of_Mortis "Dagger of Mortis") that would allow them to kill the Son, and together they faced the Son on his [cathedral](/wiki/Son%27s_cathedral "Son's cathedral"), only for the darksider to tell him of Skywalker and corrupted Tano's duel. Kenobi then helped Skywalker subdue Tano, until the Father's appearance interrupted them.[[118]](#cite_note-Altar_of_Mortis-118)

As the Son was about to kill the Father, Kenobi tried to hand Skywalker the dagger, but Tano grabbed it and gave it to the Son, who killed her as her usefulness came to an end. The darksider then killed his sister as she stepped in to save her Father. Then, Kenobi witnessed as the Daughter used Skywalker as a conduit to channel the last of her life force into Tano, resurrecting her. The Father then commanded Kenobi, Skywalker, and Tano to leave the planet before the Son used their ship to do so;[[118]](#cite_note-Altar_of_Mortis-118) however, their ship's repairs forced them to stay a bit longer, so Kenobi let Skywalker go to the Father for guidance.[[119]](#cite_note-Ghosts_of_Mortis-119)

 [![Kenobi trying to climb himself out of the Well of the Dark Side.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/29/ObiWanWell-GOM.png/revision/latest?cb=20130525234211) [![Kenobi trying to climb himself out of the Well of the Dark Side.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/29/ObiWanWell-GOM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20130525234211)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/29/ObiWanWell-GOM.png/revision/latest?cb=20130525234211) 

Kenobi trying to climb himself out of the Well of the Dark Side.

 

The Father then, appeared before Kenobi and told him Skywalker had gone to the [Well of the Dark Side](/wiki/Well_of_the_Dark_Side "Well of the Dark Side") to confront the Son, only to be shown his future and be corrupted by the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force"). Kenobi, who had gone to the well, was left stranded in there by Skywalker. Concerned, Kenobi contacted Tano and ordered her to disable the ship, fetch him on the well and meet with Skywalker—whose memories had been erased—and the Father on his Monastery. There, they confronted a newly arrived Son with the Dagger, but only the Father's sacrifice could stop the Son, with Skywalker finally killing the now-vulnerable darksider. As Mortis' conflict came to an end, Kenobi, Tano and Skywalker woke up in the ship, as if nothing had happened, and reunited with Captain Rex at the rendezvous point.[[119]](#cite_note-Ghosts_of_Mortis-119)

#### The Citadel

:   "*Obi-Wan, what took you guys so long?*"
:   ―Even Piell, on his rescue[[120]](#cite_note-The_Citadel-120)

Following the [capture](/wiki/Capture_of_Even_Piell "Capture of Even Piell") of Jedi Master [Even Piell](/wiki/Even_Piell "Even Piell") and his imprisonment in the [Citadel](/wiki/Citadel "Citadel")[[120]](#cite_note-The_Citadel-120) one year and nine months into the Clone Wars,[[121]](#cite_note-Citadel_Date-121) Kenobi, Skywalker, Commander Cody, Captain Rex, and other troopers were sent to rescue the imprisoned Jedi. Joined by a rebellious Tano, who joined the mission despite Skywalker's orders, Kenobi and the rest [froze](/wiki/Carbon-freezing "Carbon-freezing") themselves in [carbonite](/wiki/Carbonite "Carbonite") to prevent the prison's [life scanners](/wiki/Life-form_scanner "Life-form scanner") from detecting them and infiltrated the prison. During their free climbing to the entry point, surrounded by [electromines](/wiki/Electro-mine "Electro-mine"), Tano snuck through a ventilation duct to disable their entrance's [ray shield](/wiki/Ray_shield "Ray shield"). However one trooper fell, alerting the prison of their presence. Despite this, the team made its way to Piell and freed him.[[120]](#cite_note-The_Citadel-120)

 [![Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker after freeing Master Piell.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/PiellRescued-TC.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111016004057) [![Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker after freeing Master Piell.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/PiellRescued-TC.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111016004057)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/PiellRescued-TC.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111016004057) 

Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker after freeing Master Piell.

 

Piell then revealed that when the ship crashed, he and [Captain Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin") each memorized one half of the intel on the [Nexus Route](/wiki/Nexus_Route "Nexus Route") so that if one of them broke, the information would still be useless without the other half. Changing plans, the team managed to rescue the other officers, and were introduced to Tarkin by Piell. Kenobi then suggested for them to split up — Tarkin accompanying Skywalker and Tano, while Kenobi and Piell would create a diversion to allow R2-D2 and his droids to take them off planet.[[120]](#cite_note-The_Citadel-120) However, Kenobi and his team were captured before making it to the rendezvous point and encountered the prison's commander, [Osi Sobeck](/wiki/Osi_Sobeck "Osi Sobeck"). R2-D2 and his squad freed them and met with Skywalker's team back at the shuttle, which was then destroyed during the [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Lola_Sayu "Battle of Lola Sayu") that ensued, seemingly taking Echo's life with it. Forced to escape, Kenobi and Skywalker contacted the Jedi Council to send a [rescue force](/wiki/Lola_Sayu_task_force "Lola Sayu task force") to extract them, and continued their escape through the tunnels surrounding the tower.[[122]](#cite_note-Counter_Attack-122)

Piell contacted the Council to inform them of their extraction point, and Sobeck sent [anoobas](/wiki/Anooba "Anooba") to track down the Jedi's team. Kenobi, Skywalker and R2-D2 posed as bait so that the rest of the team could ambush them. Despite being successful, Piell died during the confrontation after telling Tano the intel. She then reunited with the rest of the team, taking a moment to honor his death as Kenobi and Skywalker lowered his body into a river of lava using the Force. Nevertheless, they managed to get to the extraction point on time despite Sobeck's intervention, and fleed on [Plo Koon](/wiki/Plo_Koon "Plo Koon")'s rescue shuttle, with [Saesee Tiin](/wiki/Saesee_Tiin "Saesee Tiin") providing cover fire to aid their escape to Coruscant.[[123]](#cite_note-Citadel_Rescue-123)

#### Mon Cala and Umbara

:   "*Congratulations on your capture of the Umbaran airbase, general.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to Pong Krell[[124]](#cite_note-The_General-124)

When the Jedi Council were looking for a underwater race that close enough to reinforce the Republic's forces [fighting](/wiki/Battle_of_Mon_Cala "Battle of Mon Cala") on the planet of [Mon Cala](/wiki/Mon_Cala "Mon Cala"), Kenobi was the one who suggested that Naboo may be close enough to help.[[125]](#cite_note-Gungan_Attack-125)

 [![Kenobi during the briefing prior to the invasion of Umbara](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/41/CloneBriefing-Umbara.png/revision/latest?cb=20121126025904) [![Kenobi during the briefing prior to the invasion of Umbara](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/41/CloneBriefing-Umbara.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121126025904)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/41/CloneBriefing-Umbara.png/revision/latest?cb=20121126025904) 

Kenobi during the briefing prior to the invasion of Umbara

 

Kenobi, along with fellow Jedi Tiin, Skywalker, Skywalker's Padawan Ahsoka Tano, Padawan Barriss Offee, and [Pong Krell](/wiki/Pong_Krell "Pong Krell"), was deployed to [retake](/wiki/Battle_of_Umbara "Battle of Umbara") the planet of [Umbara](/wiki/Umbara "Umbara"). Kenobi's battalion's mission was to take the [capital](/wiki/Umbaran_capital_city "Umbaran capital city") and met fierce resistance from the [Umbaran](/wiki/Umbaran "Umbaran") [militia](/wiki/Umbaran_militia "Umbaran militia").[[126]](#cite_note-Darkness_on_Umbara-126) Kenobi then contacted Krell and the 501st, to order them to secure a [Umbaran airbase](/wiki/Umbaran_airbase "Umbaran airbase") that was resupplying the capital.[[124]](#cite_note-The_General-124)

After his battalion had been pushed away from the capital due to the Umbaran's long-rage missiles, Kenobi congratulated on his success on taking the airbase and informed him that the capital still receiving supplies, this time from a [Separatist supply ship](/wiki/Unidentified_Separatist_supply_ship "Unidentified Separatist supply ship") in the atmosphere. He also informed Krell of oncoming, but delayed reinforcements, only for the [Besalisk](/wiki/Besalisk "Besalisk") to tell him he would take his battalion to the city regardless of the capital's defenses. Kenobi's transmission was then jammed by the Umbarans.[[127]](#cite_note-Plan_of_Dissent-127) Despite Krell's efforts to sabotage the Republic effort by tricking the 501st and the 212th battalions into attacking each other, Kenobi was successful in taking the capital and routing the remaining Umbaran forces, securing all sectors of the planet for the Republic.[[128]](#cite_note-Carnage_of_Krell-128)

#### Zygerrian slave crisis

:   "*If such Jedi as Skywalker and Kenobi can fall, how many other will follow? Imagine an army of Jedi in your service.*"
:   ―Miraj Scintel, to Count Dooku[[129]](#cite_note-Escape_from_Kadavo-129)

 [![Kenobi willingly getting pummeled by Zygerrian commander Darts D'Nar](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a8/DNarPummelsKenobi-Kidnapped.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111126180936) [![Kenobi willingly getting pummeled by Zygerrian commander Darts D'Nar](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a8/DNarPummelsKenobi-Kidnapped.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111126180936)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a8/DNarPummelsKenobi-Kidnapped.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111126180936) 

Kenobi willingly getting pummeled by Zygerrian commander Darts D'Nar
