Ten rotations after Master Yoda's last contact with the [Togruta](/wiki/Togruta "Togruta") colony of [Kiros](/wiki/Kiros "Kiros"), Kenobi, Skywalker, Tano, Captain Rex, and Commander Cody landed on the colony, where they found no inhabitants and [fought](/wiki/Battle_on_Kiros "Battle on Kiros") their way through droid contingents on BARC speeders to the [governor's tower](/wiki/Governor%27s_tower "Governor's tower"). Once they had the Separatist headquarters surrounded inside the governor's tower, Cody showed Kenobi a message from the Separatist commander, [Darts D'Nar](/wiki/Darts_D%27Nar "Darts D'Nar"), asking him to come to the tower to negotiate terms of "surrender." When Skywalker became angry at recognizing D'Nar as a [Zygerrian](/wiki/Zygerrian "Zygerrian") [slaver](/wiki/Slavery "Slavery"), Kenobi told his old apprentice to look for the colonists while he negotiated with D'Nar and explained Skywalker's history with slavery to Tano, who assured Kenobi she would keep an eye on him.[[130]](#cite_note-Kidnapped-130)

Kenobi then went into the tower and interrupted D'Nar's meeting with Dooku and Zygerrian Prime Minister [Atai Molec](/wiki/Atai_Molec "Atai Molec") to negotiate terms of surrender—the Republic's surrender. Kenobi then turned his [comlink](/wiki/Comlink "Comlink") on so that Skywalker and Ahsoka could hear the fact that the Zygerrian had several [bombs](/wiki/Thermal_annihilator_bomb "Thermal annihilator bomb") planted throughout the city. Kenobi then surrendered, but challenged D'Nar to a duel in the Zygerrian way (with no weapons) to distract him while Skywalker and Tano disarmed the bombs. Though he received a good beating from D'Nar, Kenobi successfully beguiled the Zygerrian, who set off his last bomb located on his tactical droid and escaped from the Jedi Master. Unable to pursue him, he told Skywalker and Tano of his departure. After Skywalker captured D'Nar and his ship, Kenobi, Skywalker, and Tano then contacted the Jedi Council, informing them of the Zygerrians' abduction of the colonists.[[130]](#cite_note-Kidnapped-130)

 [![Kenobi, Rex, and Governor Roshti trying to escape.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/BrezakEscape-SOTR.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111225014545) [![Kenobi, Rex, and Governor Roshti trying to escape.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/BrezakEscape-SOTR.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20111225014545)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/BrezakEscape-SOTR.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111225014545) 

Kenobi, Rex, and Governor Roshti trying to escape.

 

Using D'Nar's ship, Kenobi, along with Skywalker, Tano, Captain Rex, and R2-D2, [traveled](/wiki/Mission_to_Zygerria "Mission to Zygerria") to Zygerria. Upon arrival they formed two teams; Skywalker and Tano went to talk to [Queen](/wiki/Queen "Queen") [Miraj Scintel](/wiki/Miraj_Scintel "Miraj Scintel") disguised as master and slave, respectively, while Kenobi and Rex, disguised as Zygerrian traders, tried to locate the kidnapped colonists from Kiros. The two proceeded to the [Royal palace's](/wiki/Royal_Palace_of_Zygerria "Royal Palace of Zygerria") slave pits where they found the Togrutan Governor of Kiros, [Gupat Roshti](/wiki/Gupat_Roshti "Gupat Roshti"), weak and broken from his ordeal. With Rex, Kenobi decided to take him to safety on a [brezak](/wiki/Brezak "Brezak"), only for Kenobi to be shot in the shoulder and captured along with Roshti, with Rex safely escaping. Chained to a wall and tortured for information, Kenobi was recognized as a Jedi by Prime Minister Atai Molec, and prepared to sell him at that night's auction block.[[131]](#cite_note-Slaves_of_the_Republic-131)

At the auction, Roshti and Kenobi were the first slaves to be put on offer, and Queen Scintel ordered Skywalker to torture Kenobi with a shock whip before the eyes of the assembled bidders. Once Skywalker entered the arena however, he signaled to R2-D2, who launched Kenobi's, Skywalker's, and Tano's lightsabers to their owners, while Rex aided them with a blaster. Despite their efforts, however, the whole team was soon captured and separated. While Skywalker and Tano were kept in Zygerria, Kenobi, Rex and Roshti were taken to [Kadavo](/wiki/Kadavo "Kadavo"), where the rest of the Kiros colonist were kept. There, the Jedi General was forced into submission by the center's warden, [Agruss](/wiki/Agruss "Agruss"), who emphasized his point by dropping several Togrutan prisoners to their deaths and threatening to do worse to the others, should Kenobi ever think of rebellion.[[131]](#cite_note-Slaves_of_the_Republic-131)

 [![Kenobi and Rex during their enslavement on Kadavo.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fb/RexTogrutasKadavo.png/revision/latest?cb=20121204060749) [![Kenobi and Rex during their enslavement on Kadavo.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fb/RexTogrutasKadavo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20121204060749)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fb/RexTogrutasKadavo.png/revision/latest?cb=20121204060749) 

Kenobi and Rex during their enslavement on Kadavo.

 

On Kadavo, Kenobi and Rex were soon forced into working in the mines, where he had a hard time scrounging up any spark of hope for himself or the unfortunate prisoners, since every time he did so, one of the Togrutans was punished in his place in order to heighten his despair. Following the Queen's death at the hands of Dooku and her last words telling Skywalker where Kenobi was, Kenobi was part of a conference with Count Dooku in the facility control room. Despite Dooku's wish to execute Kenobi, Skywalker arrived to Kadavo with Jedi reinforcements. During the [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Kadavo "Battle of Kadavo") that ensued, Kenobi and Rex fought in the room, killed Agruss and escaped the facility, while Tano and troopers rescued the Togruta prisoners before the Republic forces destroyed the labor facility.[[129]](#cite_note-Escape_from_Kadavo-129)

#### Plot to kidnap the Chancellor

:   "*How do I look?*"  
    "*Like a criminal. Should buy you all the credibility you need in prison.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Mace Windu[[132]](#cite_note-Deception-132)

 [![Kenobi, disguised as Rako Hardeen](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e5/RakoHardeen-BHUSC.png/revision/latest?cb=20221123062449) [![Kenobi, disguised as Rako Hardeen](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e5/RakoHardeen-BHUSC.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20221123062449)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e5/RakoHardeen-BHUSC.png/revision/latest?cb=20221123062449) 

Kenobi, disguised as Rako Hardeen

 

Following [Moralo Eval](/wiki/Moralo_Eval "Moralo Eval")'s capture by the Republic and his imprisonment in the [Republic Judiciary Central Detention Center](/wiki/Republic_Judiciary_Central_Detention_Center "Republic Judiciary Central Detention Center"), Kenobi became part of a plot with Yoda and Mace Windu to stop Eval's machinations to kidnap Chancellor Palpatine. To do so, he allowed himself to be shot by a [sniper](/wiki/Sniper "Sniper"), [Rako Hardeen](/wiki/Rako_Hardeen "Rako Hardeen"), in front of Skywalker and Tano, who then believed him to be dead.[[132]](#cite_note-Deception-132)

Following his [funeral](/wiki/Funeral_of_Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Funeral of Obi-Wan Kenobi"), Kenobi assumed the identity of his apparent killer and had his physical appearance [altered](/wiki/Facial_transformation_program "Facial transformation program"). In addition, once Kenobi and Windu recorded a sample of Hardeen's voice in [Trueping's](/wiki/Trueping%27s "Trueping's"), Kenobi swallowed a [vocal emulator](/wiki/Vocal_emulator "Vocal emulator") to perfectly disguise his voice as Hardeen's. Kenobi would operate under the alias "Ben,"[[132]](#cite_note-Deception-132) the same name Kryze had referred to him with years prior,[[30]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-30) for the duration of the mission. Kenobi was then sent to the detention center, where he formed a partnership with Eval, who trusted Kenobi and thought he could be useful, and Cad Bane, who did not. When a [prison riot](/wiki/Riot_at_the_Republic_Judiciary_Central_Detention_Center "Riot at the Republic Judiciary Central Detention Center") broke out, courtesy of Boba Fett and [Bossk](/wiki/Bossk%27wassak%27Cradossk "Bossk'wassak'Cradossk"), Kenobi worked to escape with Bane and Eval. Kenobi discreetly used the Force to aid in their escape, opening a lock after Bane failed to bypass it. Bane was suspicious of Kenobi due to his unwillingness to kill the prison staff, but despite this, they left Coruscant for Nal Hutta.[[132]](#cite_note-Deception-132)

When they arrived at Nal Hutta, Kenobi crashed their ship in order to cover their trail. The trio then proceeded to try to find supplies and a new ship in the town of [Bilbousa](/wiki/Bilbousa "Bilbousa"). Bane grew even more distrustful of Kenobi after Kenobi's kind treatment of [Pablo](/wiki/Pablo "Pablo"), the owner of the [pawnshop](/wiki/Pablo%27s_pawnshop "Pablo's pawnshop") that the trio went to. Kenobi, suspecting betrayal, planted a tracking device on the new ship he bought, so that when Bane left Kenobi to be arrested by the local authorities, the Jedi turned the frequency of the tracking device over to his captors, who shot Bane and Eval's ship down. Kenobi, meanwhile, escaped from captivity and purchased another ship, and when Bane and Eval found him smugly waiting for them, they agreed to make him a partner in their scheme. When the trio reached [Orondia](/wiki/Orondia "Orondia"), Skywalker and Tano caught up with them. During a small [confrontation](/wiki/Showdown_on_Orondia "Showdown on Orondia"), Kenobi wrestled with Skywalker, whispering "Anakin, don't follow me," just before knocking him unconscious and escaping with Bane and Eval.[[133]](#cite_note-Friends_and_Enemies-133)

 [![Kenobi demonstrates his shooting skills in the fourth task.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/Task4Sharpshooting-TB.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120205070934) [![Kenobi demonstrates his shooting skills in the fourth task.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/Task4Sharpshooting-TB.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20120205070934)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/Task4Sharpshooting-TB.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120205070934) 

Kenobi demonstrates his shooting skills in the fourth task.

 

Eval, Bane, and Kenobi then traveled to the planet [Serenno](/wiki/Serenno "Serenno") to meet with Count Dooku, and Bane and Kenobi accepted an invitation to participate along with eleven other notorious bounty hunters in a [test of skill](/wiki/Tournament_on_Serenno "Tournament on Serenno") designed by Eval called the [Box](/wiki/Box "Box"). "Hardeen" surpassed Eval's tests, the [Phindian](/wiki/Phindian "Phindian") grew angrier with him after every test. In the fourth and final test, their shooting skills would be tested, with the bounty hunter's target being a moving spot on the wall. If they missed, they would fall into a floor of flame emitters. After [Sixtat](/wiki/Sixtat "Sixtat") failed, Kenobi stepped in to shoot the target. However, Eval had laid a trap for Kenobi, as his rifle ran out of shots before he could hit the last moving spot. Eval then removed the platforms in order to kill him, but Bane, now having respect for Kenobi and disgusted by Eval's actions, saved him. Dooku decided that Eval should not be exempted from the contest and dropped him to the now extinguished floor to fight with Kenobi. Though the Count wanted him to kill Eval, Kenobi refrained, disappointing the Sith Lord, who then chose to put Bane in charge of the operation to kidnap the Chancellor.[[134]](#cite_note-The_Box-134) Within a few hours, the team departed the planet for Naboo.[[135]](#cite_note-BaneStory-135)

Planning to abduct Palpatine during Naboo's [Festival of Light](/wiki/Festival_of_Light "Festival of Light"), the team commandeered a warehouse in Theed and each member of the team was assigned a role, with Kenobi being given the job of the sniper who would fire [stun](/wiki/Stun "Stun") blasts at the Chancellor. When he was in position, Kenobi contacted Windu to tell him what he knew of the plan. Later that night, despite Skywalker and Windu's efforts during the [skirmish](/wiki/Plan_to_kidnap_Chancellor_Palpatine "Plan to kidnap Chancellor Palpatine"), the Chancellor was kidnapped by Bane and Eval. Kenobi followed them with Windu and Skywalker close behind, and the criminal pair was arrested and the Chancellor recovered when they stopped at the rendezvous point.[[136]](#cite_note-Crisis_on_Naboo-136)

However, he agreed on Skywalker's doubts about knowing the full truth, and returned to the apartment where he had had his position as a sniper, and discovered an activated comlink in his rifle case. Realizing Dooku's hand in it, Kenobi rushed back to the Royal Palace, where he discovered Skywalker dueling with Dooku, while Palpatine was held by a [MagnaGuard](/wiki/IG-100_MagnaGuard "IG-100 MagnaGuard"). After Kenobi rescued the Chancellor and Dooku fled, Palpatine thanked the Jedi for their bravery.[[136]](#cite_note-Crisis_on_Naboo-136)

#### Maul's return

:   "*You know, when I cut you in half, I should have aimed for your neck instead.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to Maul[[137]](#cite_note-Revenge-137)

Like Master Yoda and Skywalker, Kenobi sensed a [disturbance in the Force](/wiki/Disturbance_in_the_Force "Disturbance in the Force"),[[138]](#cite_note-Brothers-138) one that signaled the return of his old enemy, former Sith Lord Maul, whom he believed to have killed on Naboo, only to have survived and make his way to a dump in [Lotho Minor](/wiki/Lotho_Minor "Lotho Minor"). Rescued by Savage Opress and his sanity restored by Mother Talzin, Maul sent a message to the Jedi Council, threatening to [execute](/wiki/Massacre_on_Raydonia "Massacre on Raydonia") innocent people on [Raydonia](/wiki/Raydonia "Raydonia") if Kenobi did not come to face him.[[137]](#cite_note-Revenge-137)

 [![Kenobi facing a vengeful Maul.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8f/MaulVsKenobi-Revenge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120317061819) [![Kenobi facing a vengeful Maul.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8f/MaulVsKenobi-Revenge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20120317061819)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8f/MaulVsKenobi-Revenge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120317061819) 

Kenobi facing a vengeful Maul.

 

Kenobi arrived in a burning village with Maul awaiting him. Though the Jedi Master was unsure if Maul was who he claimed to be, the Dathomirian proved it by telling him about their shared experience at the Battle of Naboo. The two engaged in a [fight](/wiki/Skirmish_above_Raydonia "Skirmish above Raydonia") and Kenobi was overpowered at the hands of his old enemy, who had the help of Opress. Kenobi was then brought aboard the [brothers' ship](/wiki/TR-RL3_Terrapin-class_bulk_tanker "TR-RL3 Terrapin-class bulk tanker"), who intended to have the Jedi awake so that his death would be as painful as the last ten years of his life had been. However, Kenobi was rescued by Asajj Ventress, who was trying to collect the bounty on Opress' head. After being freed, Kenobi used one of her lightsabers to duel Maul in the cargo area of their ship. Though he almost gave in to rage, Kenobi gained the upper hand with the help of Ventress and together, they managed to trap Maul and Opress in the back of the ship, leaving the brothers stranded, but alive, in space.[[137]](#cite_note-Revenge-137)

#### Aiding the Onderon rebels

:   "*Now, to be clear, we are not here to fight your war; rather, to show you how to conduct it in the most efficient and successful way possible.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi[[139]](#cite_note-A_War_on_Two_Fronts-139)

Kenobi attended a session of the Jedi Council when [rebels](/wiki/Onderon_rebels "Onderon rebels") [Saw Gerrera](/wiki/Saw_Gerrera "Saw Gerrera") and [Lux Bonteri](/wiki/Lux_Bonteri "Lux Bonteri") contacted them with a request for assistance in their [struggle](/wiki/Onderonian_Civil_War "Onderonian Civil War") against the Separatist forces on [Onderon](/wiki/Onderon "Onderon"), led by King [Sanjay Rash](/wiki/Sanjay_Rash "Sanjay Rash"). Kenobi pointed out that at the beginning of the war, Onderon made their intentions to join the Separatists, but Gerrera said that their [true king](/wiki/Ramsis_Dendup "Ramsis Dendup") was silenced by the fake. The Council refused to help, but did consent to send advisers to train and advise them. Kenobi went there with Skywalker, Tano, and Rex.[[139]](#cite_note-A_War_on_Two_Fronts-139)

On Onderon, Kenobi met the rebels and their charismatic leader [Steela Gerrera](/wiki/Steela_Gerrera "Steela Gerrera") – alongside his friends and together, they began to train the rebels in combat. When the Separatists discovered their outpost and attacked, Kenobi and his fellow Jedi assisted in battle, though cautious not to be in the thick of the battle. When the skirmish concluded, a strategy was devised to get into the capital city of [Iziz](/wiki/Iziz "Iziz").[[139]](#cite_note-A_War_on_Two_Fronts-139) Once in there, Kenobi, Skywalker and Rex decided to leave for Coruscant to report to the Council, leaving Tano as a liaison to the rebels. However, they decided to ensure that Tano did not reveal her Jedi identity, though allowing her to accompany the rebels on strike.[[140]](#cite_note-Front_Runners-140) After that, they kept in frequent communication with her.[[140]](#cite_note-Front_Runners-140)[[141]](#cite_note-The_Soft_War-141)[[142]](#cite_note-Tipping_Points-142) Kenobi attended the [funeral](/wiki/Funeral_of_Steela_Gerrera "Funeral of Steela Gerrera") service for Steela after the final battle after she had perished.[[142]](#cite_note-Tipping_Points-142)

#### Younglings in peril

:   "*For now, be proud. You have survived an ordeal few your age could. Welcome home, young Jedi.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi[[143]](#cite_note-A_Necessary_Bond-143)

While Kenobi was stationed aboard his flagship, the Star Destroyer *Negotiator*, he was contacted by Jedi initiates aboard the [transport](/wiki/Transport "Transport") *[Crucible](/wiki/Crucible "Crucible")*, who informed him that their guardian, Ahsoka Tano, had been kidnapped by Hondo Ohnaka's pirates. The younglings said they wanted to rescue Tano from the pirates, but Kenobi told them to stay on the *Crucible* for their safety.[[144]](#cite_note-Bound_for_Rescue-144)

 [![Kenobi faces off with Grievous in the Negotiator hangar.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/YoullRegretThat-BFR.png/revision/latest?cb=20131020050713) [![Kenobi faces off with Grievous in the Negotiator hangar.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/YoullRegretThat-BFR.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20131020050713)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/YoullRegretThat-BFR.png/revision/latest?cb=20131020050713) 

Kenobi faces off with Grievous in the *Negotiator* hangar.

 

Kenobi was intending to send Commander Cody to rescue the stranded Jedi, but his plans were interrupted by an unforeseen [attack](/wiki/Attack_on_Obi-Wan_Kenobi%27s_fleet "Attack on Obi-Wan Kenobi's fleet") by General Grievous on his fleet. Grievous's ships quickly gained the upper hand on Kenobi's, destroying several of his vessels. Upon learning that Grievous had sent a boarding party to board his ship, Kenobi and the clone forces on the ship stationed themselves in the hangar in order to repel it. Grievous himself accompanied the boarding party, and Kenobi began dueling with him as the clone troopers and battle droids engaged each other. Soon, however, Kenobi realized that this was a battle that he could not win, and as he retreated through the passageways of the Star Destroyer he ordered the crew to abandon ship and initiated the ship's [self-destruct sequence](/wiki/Self-destruct_mechanism "Self-destruct mechanism"). When Grievous arrived on the bridge, he found a hologram recording of Kenobi. Through it, Kenobi conceded the victory to Grievous, but informed him that the ship was about to explode. Kenobi escaped the destruction on an escape pod, as did Grievous, who evacuated Kenobi's ship on a shuttle just before it exploded.[[144]](#cite_note-Bound_for_Rescue-144)

Soon after, Kenobi joined Tano, the younglings, who had gone to [rescue](/wiki/Rescue_on_Florrum "Rescue on Florrum") Tano despite Kenobi's orders,[[144]](#cite_note-Bound_for_Rescue-144) and members of the pirate gang, including Ohnaka himself. After Grievous's defeat of Kenobi, he had [attacked](/wiki/Invasion_of_Florrum "Invasion of Florrum") the pirates' stronghold, and the Jedi and pirates had joined forces against Grievous and barely escaped with their lives.[[143]](#cite_note-A_Necessary_Bond-143)

#### D-Squad's mission

Kenobi was present when the Jedi Council sent Colonel [Meebur Gascon](/wiki/Meebur_Gascon "Meebur Gascon") and a [team](/wiki/D-Squad "D-Squad") of droids to [infiltrate](/wiki/Mission_to_steal_a_Separatist_encryption_module "Mission to steal a Separatist encryption module") a Separatist [dreadnought](/wiki/Aut-O%27s_flagship "Aut-O's flagship") located deep within Separatist-controlled space, and recover an [encryption module](/wiki/Encryption_module "Encryption module"), which had been scrambling Separatist communications within the region.[[145]](#cite_note-Secret_Weapons-145)

#### Mission to Bray

:   "*Life on Bray has always been hard, but since the arrival of the dark lord, it has been a living nightmare.*"
:   ―A Brayan to Obi-Wan Kenobi[[146]](#cite_note-Count_Dooku:_Prince_of_Darkness!-146)

 [![Dooku introduces the Jedi to Ravna](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b8/RavnaLordOfDarkness-TalesFromVadersCastle2.png/revision/latest?cb=20190724051714) [![Dooku introduces the Jedi to Ravna](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b8/RavnaLordOfDarkness-TalesFromVadersCastle2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20190724051714)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b8/RavnaLordOfDarkness-TalesFromVadersCastle2.png/revision/latest?cb=20190724051714) 

Dooku introduces the Jedi to Ravna

 

Kenobi, along with Gallia, Cody, and several troops [went](/wiki/Mission_to_Bray "Mission to Bray") to [Bray](/wiki/Bray "Bray") in response to a cry for help. Upon their arrival, the inhabitants told Kenobi about a Dark Lord that was plaguing their village was desecrating the [Citadel of Light](/wiki/Citadel_of_Light "Citadel of Light"). Kenobi was skeptical of the natives' claims until the power went out and came under attack by several [mynocks](/wiki/Mynock "Mynock"). Kenobi and Gallia decided to investigate the Citadel. They then discovered that the mynock had affected trooper [Peel](/wiki/Peel "Peel") and transformed into a [creature](/wiki/Ravna%27s_species "Ravna's species"). Kenobi came under attack by Peel until Cody stunned him and locked him away.[[146]](#cite_note-Count_Dooku:_Prince_of_Darkness!-146)

Kenobi, along with Gallia, entered the Citadel to find a cure. Inside, they found Dooku and the Dark Lord [Ravna](/wiki/Ravna "Ravna"). Kenobi attempted to use his lightsaber on Ravna to no avail. Ravna was able to subdue Kenobi, while Dooku used his lightning to subdue Gallia. Kenobi tried to convince Dooku not to use Ravna's powers. However, Ravna betrayed and affected Dooku. Kenobi was able to break through to Dooku by making him give in to his anger and make him attack Ravna. As Dooku used his lightning on Ravna, Kenobi and Gallia were able to use the Force to collapse the Citadel and entomb Ravna.[[146]](#cite_note-Count_Dooku:_Prince_of_Darkness!-146)

### Nearing the end of the war

#### Fighting Oppress and Maul

:   "*I lost someone important to me. And I understand anger in a way I never have.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi speaks to Anakin Skywalker after Satine Kryze's death[[35]](#cite_note-KenobiShadow-35)

When the two brothers [attacked](/wiki/Raid_on_the_Cybloc_Transfer_Station "Raid on the Cybloc Transfer Station") [Cybloc Transfer Station](/wiki/Cybloc_Transfer_Station "Cybloc Transfer Station") in the [Meridian sector](/wiki/Meridian_sector "Meridian sector"), the [space station](/wiki/Space_station "Space station") sent out a [distress signal](/wiki/Distress_signal "Distress signal"), leading Kenobi and Gallia there to investigate about the two brothers, who were now operating under [Maul's singular vision](/wiki/Rule_of_Two "Rule of Two"). The Jedi learned they were headed to Florrum. There, Kenobi contacted Hondo Ohnaka to inquire about the situation, who said that "two horned men" had appeared and threatened to attack his stronghold with pirates who had betrayed him. Kenobi told him he was unable to help him with his men, but that he could help stop the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith").[[147]](#cite_note-Revival-147)

 [![Obi-Wan Kenobi fights Maul and Savage Opress](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d0/TwoOnWan-Revival.png/revision/latest?cb=20131016204825) [![Obi-Wan Kenobi fights Maul and Savage Opress](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d0/TwoOnWan-Revival.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20131016204825)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d0/TwoOnWan-Revival.png/revision/latest?cb=20131016204825) 

Obi-Wan Kenobi fights Maul and Savage Opress

 

Kenobi and Gallia managed to engage Maul and Opress just as they began their [attack](/wiki/Skirmish_on_Florrum "Skirmish on Florrum") on Florrum. As the fight progressed, Gallia was slain by Opress and, after taking up his fallen comrade's lightsaber to help defend himself, Kenobi was forced to retreat and reunite with Ohnaka. Inside a cave, Ohnaka decided to ambush the men while Kenobi decided to confront Maul and Opress. With great skill and Gallia's lightsaber, Kenobi violently fought the pair, changing to Ataru and demonstrating mastery of his former fighting style. Eventually, he injures Opress' knee and cuts his left arm off. However, before Kenobi could continue the fight, Maul Force-pushed him into another part of the cave, bringing the fight to an end. Realizing their plan had failed, the Dathomirians left and headed off-planet to try again another time. Their ship, however, was shot down and the two were forced to head for an escape pod. As the ship fell, Kenobi went with Hondo to see "what riches [had] fallen from the sky," but there were no signs of Maul nor Opress, leaving Kenobi to doubt their demise.[[147]](#cite_note-Revival-147)

Following the confrontation, Kenobi returned to Coruscant where he explained to Chancellor Palpatine about the situation regarding Maul, but Palpatine dismissed the Maul's threat, saying that the Jedi needed to focus on the Separatist threat, despite Kenobi's fears of the criminal underworld being a place where Maul could flourish.[[147]](#cite_note-Revival-147)

#### Mandalore's fall and losing Satine Kryze

:   "*I know where you're from. I've been to your village. I know the decision to join the dark side wasn't yours. The Nightsisters made it for you.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi[[16]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-16)

Following Maul's [takeover](/wiki/Takeover_of_Mandalore "Takeover of Mandalore") of Mandalore, Kenobi was summoned to meet with Yoda and Ki-Adi-Mundi in the communications room. The two showed him a transmission that had been sent by Satine Kryze from Mandalore. In the message, she stated that her government had been overthrown by [rogue criminals](/wiki/Shadow_Collective "Shadow Collective"), only for the transmission to be abruptly cut.[[16]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-16) Kenobi noticed the super commandos surrounding his friend, wanting to go to Mandalore to help her. However, he simply chose to tell the Masters that the Death Watch was most likely responsible for any hostile takeover that took place.[[35]](#cite_note-KenobiShadow-35)

Yoda and Mundi expressed reluctance to take part in the internal affairs of Mandalore without Senate approval, despite Kenobi's protests.[[35]](#cite_note-KenobiShadow-35) Kenobi chose to go to Mandalore anyways, borrowing the *[Twilight](/wiki/Twilight "Twilight")* vessel[[16]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-16) with Skywalker's blessing and heading to Sundari. Though Skywalker wished to come as well, Kenobi insisted that one Jedi would be easier to hide than two. Kenobi brought the [armor](/wiki/Armor "Armor") of Rako Hardeen, which he had saved from that previous mission, to use in the endeavor. The Master, who despised the way the *Twilight* flew, was happy to leave it behind once on the planet.[[35]](#cite_note-KenobiShadow-35)

 [![Satine Kryze dying in the arms of Kenobi.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9f/HoldMeObiWanKenobi-TL.png/revision/latest?cb=20131025194032) [![Satine Kryze dying in the arms of Kenobi.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9f/HoldMeObiWanKenobi-TL.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20131025194032)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9f/HoldMeObiWanKenobi-TL.png/revision/latest?cb=20131025194032) 

Satine Kryze dying in the arms of Kenobi.

 

Kenobi proceeded to trick a [guard](/wiki/Mandalorian_super_commando "Mandalorian super commando") and took his [armor](/wiki/Mandalorian_armor "Mandalorian armor").[[16]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-16) Disguised, he entered the prison complex using a stolen code cylinder, wandering through a maze of cells.[[35]](#cite_note-KenobiShadow-35) When he freed Kryze from her cell, she expressed her relief to see him, despite their grim circumstances.[[16]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-16) Kenobi admitted that the Senate nor the Council had approved their mission, which could prove to make their escape more difficult. The Jedi acted as if Satine was his prisoner, transferring her through a turbolift until being questioned about the prisoner transfer. Kenobi responded to the query by knocking the asking commando out, hurriedly ushering Satine onto a speeder to make their escape.[[35]](#cite_note-KenobiShadow-35)

However, the pair was chased, leading them to quip about their many memories together.[[35]](#cite_note-KenobiShadow-35) After rushing up the ramp of their ship,[[16]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-16) Kenobi realized that his borrowed ship could not withstand an attack, and agreed to contacting Satine's sister, Bo-Katan, for help. The ship quickly took damage from enemy fire, resulting in Kenobi and Satine being forced to leave it behind. The Jedi used the Force to break their falls, but then crashed to the platform when their ship came down on top of them.[[35]](#cite_note-KenobiShadow-35) Realizing who was on planet, Maul personally hunted down Kenobi and managed to ensure that the *Twilight* was shot down before it could leave. Maul captured the now-dizzy and injured Kenobi as Opress lifted an unconscious Kryze, and ordered them taken back to the [royal palace](/wiki/Sundari_Royal_Palace "Sundari Royal Palace").[[16]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-16)

In the palace, Maul, realizing Kenobi's feelings for Satine, decided to execute her with Kenobi watching, hoping that he would feel the same pain Maul did when he was forced to live in exile after being brutally injured by Kenobi on Naboo. Maul again attempted to sway Kenobi to the dark side, but the Jedi Master refused, saying those who oppose it were more powerful than those use the dark side could ever be.[[16]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-16) Kenobi instead talked about the Dathomirian's own past, recognising that Maul had his future stolen and was groomed to become the creature of anger and vengeance who stood before him. He hoped that by matching the Sith's fury with understanding and sympathy he could reach Maul and both save Satine's life and turn the Dathomirian away from the dark path he had been forced on. But Kenobi's fear for Satine's life and anger towards Maul made his words more venomous than the Jedi intended.[[35]](#cite_note-KenobiShadow-35)

Angered by Kenobi's statements, the commandos forced Kenobi to his knees. Maul let Satine go briefly, but stabbed her with the Darksaber. She ultimately died in Kenobi's arms saying with her last breath, that she always loved him and always would. Maul taunted Kenobi, but Kenobi replied that only the weak embraced the dark side. Maul, then, had his guards escort Kenobi to a cell where he could "drown in his misery" and "rot."[[16]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-16) Kenobi deeply grieved her death, feeling strong anger after it as he envisioned revenge. However, he decided not to act on his emotions and betray what he had worked to become as a Jedi, and Maul had him imprisoned again.[[35]](#cite_note-KenobiShadow-35)

 [![Kenobi freed by Bo-Katan.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/aa/BoKatanFreesKenobi-TL.png/revision/latest?cb=20131025160409) [![Kenobi freed by Bo-Katan.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/aa/BoKatanFreesKenobi-TL.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/261?cb=20131025160409)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/aa/BoKatanFreesKenobi-TL.png/revision/latest?cb=20131025160409) 

Kenobi freed by Bo-Katan.

 

Satine's sister [Bo-Katan](/wiki/Bo-Katan_Kryze "Bo-Katan Kryze") and her renegade [Nite Owls](/wiki/Nite_Owls "Nite Owls") team, however, intercepted Kenobi as he was being transferred to the prison area. Katan freed Kenobi and gave him his lightsaber back, informing the Master that she was there to rescue him. In return, she had him help her find Maul and kill him. Meanwhile, unbeknownst to them, Darth Sidious appeared and engaged Maul and Opress in a duel, defeating the former and killing the latter. As the [conflict](/wiki/Battle_of_Mandalore "Battle of Mandalore") escalated, Kenobi made his way to his ship and was told by Bo-Katan to warn the Republic of what had happened. Kenobi told her that it would lead to an invasion of Mandalore, but she said that Maul's death would be worth it, and that they would survive. Kenobi, before leaving, asked Bo-Katan if Satine was her sister, and apologized for her loss.[[16]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-16)

Returning to Coruscant, Kenobi reunited with Skywalker, who asked his former master what had happened. Though his words came as a struggle, Kenobi admitted he had lost "someone important" to him. He also revealed that he understood anger in a new way and that he now knew how difficult it was to not give into the emotion. Skywalker held Kenobi's gaze for sometime before the two left for the Jedi Council together, as Kenobi knew he had to report what had happened.[[35]](#cite_note-KenobiShadow-35)

#### Temple bombing crisis

:   "*Surely we cannot do what Tarkin suggests. We need to stand together with Ahsoka.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi[[148]](#cite_note-The_Wrong_Jedi-148)

Following the [bombing](/wiki/Bombing_of_the_Jedi_Temple_hangar "Bombing of the Jedi Temple hangar") at the Jedi Temple, Kenobi took part of the Jedi Council meeting in which Yoda and Windu requested that Skywalker and Tano investigate the incident and find the culprit, telling to suspect even their fellow Jedi. When Tano and Skywalker told the Council of their progress―following a clue that led them to [Jackar Bowmani](/wiki/Jackar_Bowmani "Jackar Bowmani"), Kenobi was present again as a hologram.[[149]](#cite_note-Sabotage-149) Kenobi also attended to the [funeral for the victims](/wiki/Funeral_of_the_Jedi_Temple_bombing_victims "Funeral of the Jedi Temple bombing victims") of the bombing.[[150]](#cite_note-TJWKTM-150)

 [![Kenobi as part of the Council of Judgement.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/81/ChamberOfJudgement-TWJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20131029024016) [![Kenobi as part of the Council of Judgement.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/81/ChamberOfJudgement-TWJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/310?cb=20131029024016)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/81/ChamberOfJudgement-TWJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20131029024016) 

Kenobi as part of the Council of Judgement.

 

Later on, Kenobi was made aware of a Separatist attack on Saleucami. To alert his fellow Jedi in the Jedi Temple's war room, and held a conference where he was suggested for their fleets to move to the [Anoat system](/wiki/Anoat_system "Anoat system") and move across to Saleucami, when he was interrupted by Admiral Tarkin, who told the Council that Tano was requested by [Letta Turmond](/wiki/Letta_Turmond "Letta Turmond").[[150]](#cite_note-TJWKTM-150)

Following Tano's [escape](/wiki/Escape_from_the_Republic_military_base "Escape from the Republic military base") from authorities to prove her innocence, Kenobi along with the rest of the Jedi High Council, and Skywalker held a emergency meeting with Tarkin declaring to them that Tano was now accused of [sedition](/wiki/Treason "Treason"). With Skywalker and Plo Koon doubtful of her guilt, Grand Master Yoda sent the two to find her, but Windu attempted to have Skywalker left out of the matter, believing having him involved would only making things worse due to his emotional bond with Tano. However, Kenobi convinced the Council otherwise, stating Skywalker knew Tano best and that it would be foolish to take him off the mission.[[151]](#cite_note-To_Catch_a_Jedi-151)

After her [capture](/wiki/Capture_of_Ahsoka_Tano "Capture of Ahsoka Tano"), Kenobi listened to Tarkin as he informed the Council that the Senate requested for Tano to be expelled from the Jedi Order and turned over to the Republic military so she could receive more "impartial" judgement. Kenobi tried to convince his fellow Council members that they should side with Tano, but they all refused to do so, as they feared that protecting Tano would damage their ties with the Senate. Despite his reluctance to hand Tano over to the Republic, Kenobi took part in Tano's trial in the [Chamber of Judgment](/wiki/Chamber_of_Judgment "Chamber of Judgment"), where the Council stripped the young Togruta of her rank and status as a Jedi.[[148]](#cite_note-The_Wrong_Jedi-148)

Like other members of the Council, Kenobi was present during Tano's military [trial](/wiki/Trial_of_Ahsoka_Tano "Trial of Ahsoka Tano") as presided over by Chancellor Palpatine and during Barriss Offee's confession, which confirmed Tano's innocence. Along with the Council, Kenobi agreed that Tano should rejoin the Order and was present when Windu and Yoda proclaimed her to be a true Jedi, worthy of becoming a Jedi Knight, only for her to refuse readmission. When Skywalker ran after Tano, Kenobi started to follow, but Plo Koon placed a hand on his shoulder, silently advising him not to. Despite Skywalker's attempts to convince her to reconsider, Tano parted with the Jedi.[[148]](#cite_note-The_Wrong_Jedi-148) Following the event, Skywalker's regret at her departure soured his mood, which he reflected on to Amidala. Hesitant to lose more people close to him, Skywalker was reluctant to leave on his next mission, but eventually went with Kenobi on an assignment that ended successfully.[[152]](#cite_note-Alliances-152)

#### Kaminoan conspiracy

:   "*The clone in question is now dead, and the Jedi still suspect nothing.*"
:   ―Count Dooku, to Darth Sidious[[153]](#cite_note-Orders-153)

After clone trooper [Tup](/wiki/Tup "Tup") murdered Jedi General [Tiplar](/wiki/Tiplar "Tiplar") during a [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Ringo_Vinda "Battle of Ringo Vinda") on [Ringo Vinda](/wiki/Ringo_Vinda "Ringo Vinda") and had been sent to Kamino for examination,[[154]](#cite_note-The_Unknown-154) Jedi Master [Shaak Ti](/wiki/Shaak_Ti "Shaak Ti") held a meeting with the Jedi Council, of which Kenobi took part of. Between her wanting an atomic brain scan on Tup and Nala Se wanting to terminate the clone and do an autopsy, Kenobi asked what the Kaminoan thought of her and advised that Tup be brought back to the Jedi Temple where he could be examined through the Force.[[155]](#cite_note-Conspiracy-155) However, the full extent of the Kaminoans' plot was only discovered by Fives, who died before he could warn the Jedi of [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66").[[156]](#cite_note-Fugitive-156)[[153]](#cite_note-Orders-153)

#### Clovis returns

:   "*Anakin, I understand to a degree what is going on. You've met Satine. You know I once harbored feelings for her. It's not that we're not allowed to have these feelings. It's natural.*"  
    "*Senator Amidala and I are simply friends.*"  
    "*And friends you must remain. As a Jedi, it is essential you make the right choice, Anakin, for the Order.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker[[157]](#cite_note-The_Rise_of_Clovis-157)

Following Senator Amidala's [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Scipio "Mission to Scipio") to [Scipio](/wiki/Scipio "Scipio") where she cooperated with Rush Clovis to expose the [InterGalactic Banking Clan](/wiki/InterGalactic_Banking_Clan "InterGalactic Banking Clan")[[158]](#cite_note-An_Old_Friend-158) and Skywalker's continuous demonstrations of animosity towards Clovis, Kenobi visited Skywalker in his quarters to discuss his and Yoda's concerns that his judgment regarding Clovis were "clouded" after the [event](/wiki/Mission_to_Cato_Neimoidia "Mission to Cato Neimoidia") on Cato Neimoidia. Kenobi told Skywalker that he could not let his feelings for Amidala get in the way of his judgement. He tried to resonate with his former padawan by mentioning how he had similar feelings for Satine as Anakin did for Padmé, but Anakin was not receptive and Obi-Wan left after reiterating that he could not let his feelings get in the way of his decisions.[[157]](#cite_note-The_Rise_of_Clovis-157) Nevertheless, Skywalker was right to distrust Clovis, as his actions not only endangered Senator Amidala's life once again, but also put the Banking Clan under the direct control of Chancellor Palpatine, thus giving Darth Sidious more power in his quest to form a [New Order](/wiki/New_Order "New Order").[[159]](#cite_note-Crisis_at_the_Heart-159)

#### Sifo-Dyas' secret

:   "*The creation of the clone army, kept secret from us Sifo-Dyas did. How this was done we know not, yet now a new piece of the puzzle we have. Perhaps clarity it will bring us, yes.*"
:   ―Yoda[[160]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-160)

After Jedi Master Plo Koon intercepted a distress call from a shuttle once thought to have been lost and discovered Sifo-Dyas's lightsaber, he took of the meeting in which Plo Koon informed the Jedi Council of his findings, and Kenobi reminded them that Sifo-Dyas had spearheaded the creation of the Clone Army. Relaunching the investigation of the Jedi Master's death, Kenobi and Skywalker were sent to Felucia to find out what happened to Sifo-Dyas, where they spoke to the tribal leaders. Kenobi was told that the Felucians had cremated his body and that another Jedi had been with him when he was killed, and reported their findings to Master Yoda.[[160]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-160)

 [![Kenobi and Skywalker's meeting with the leader of the Pyke Syndicate.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/31/EpGuide610.png/revision/latest?cb=20140702093829) [![Kenobi and Skywalker's meeting with the leader of the Pyke Syndicate.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/31/EpGuide610.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20140702093829)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/31/EpGuide610.png/revision/latest?cb=20140702093829) 

Kenobi and Skywalker's meeting with the leader of the Pyke Syndicate.

 

The two were then [sent](/wiki/Mission_to_Oba_Diah_(Clone_Wars) "Mission to Oba Diah (Clone Wars)") to [Oba Diah](/wiki/Oba_Diah "Oba Diah") when former Chancellor, Finis Valorum told Yoda that Sifo-Dyas had been [sent](/wiki/Mission_to_Oba_Diah_(Sifo-Dyas) "Mission to Oba Diah (Sifo-Dyas)") to negotiate with the [Pyke Syndicate](/wiki/Pyke_Syndicate "Pyke Syndicate") to stop an underground war. Valorum, however, said that there was no other Jedi sent alongside Syfo-Dyas, but rather his personal aide [Silman](/wiki/Silman "Silman"). On Oba Diah, Kenobi and Skywalker met [Lom Pyke](/wiki/Lom_Pyke "Lom Pyke"), who denied any involvement until Kenobi noticed that he was wearing the crest of Valorum and Skywalker grabbed the necklace and told the [Pyke](/wiki/Pyke "Pyke") to "stop playing games." Lom finally complied with the Jedi, and told them that they had been paid by a man called Tyranus to shoot Sifo-Dyas's shuttle down. However, as they feared that anyone who paid for the death of a Jedi was dangerous, they kept Silman locked away for ten years as insurance.[[160]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-160)

However, once they met Silman, they realized he had gone mad after being locked up for so long, and were unable to learn much from him as Dooku arrived to kill him before Kenobi and Skywalker's eyes. After engaging Dooku in combat, they learned that the man called Tyranus was, in fact, the Count. After he managed to escape, they informed the Council of their findings, only for them to question why Dooku had been behind the creation of the clone army, and what the game of the yet-unidentified [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith") was.[[160]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-160)

#### Yoda's journey

:   "*Yet, open to us, a path remains that unknown to the Sith is. Through this path, victory we may yet find. Not victory in the Clone Wars but victory for all time.*"
:   ―Yoda, to Mace Windu and Obi-Wan Kenobi[[161]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-161)

 [![Yoda conferring with the High Council, including Kenobi.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b8/EpGuide611.png/revision/latest?cb=20200224044854) [![Yoda conferring with the High Council, including Kenobi.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b8/EpGuide611.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20200224044854)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b8/EpGuide611.png/revision/latest?cb=20200224044854) 

Yoda conferring with the High Council, including Kenobi.

 

During a meeting with the High Council, Kenobi, like the rest of his peers, noticed Grand Master Yoda's absent-mindedness following his communion with Kenobi's late master, Qui-Gon Jinn. Later, Windu conferred in private with Kenobi that he was worried about Yoda's turmoil and asked him to keep an eye on the old Jedi Master. Soon, however, Yoda revealed to the Council in full that a voice spoke to him from beyond, prompting Kenobi and the entire Council to perform a joint meditation with him, but they heard nothing. Though Master Mundi surmised it could be a deception by the Sith, but Kenobi dismissed the idea, believing Yoda could not be susceptible to such manipulation, but Windu replied that, even as wise and old as he was, Yoda was not beyond the corruption of the dark side.[[162]](#cite_note-Voices-162)

Submitting himself for medical examination, Kenobi, Windu and Mundi were told by [Rig Nema](/wiki/Rig_Nema "Rig Nema") that Yoda was in perfect mental health, even if he approached nine hundredth year of life. Though Mundi suggested the Dark Lord of the Sith could be using Yoda's connection to Dooku, Kenobi vehemently rejected the idea, saying they all had been apprenticed to Yoda at one point or another. Before the discussion could go on, Nema then suggested a [deprivation ritual](/wiki/Deprivation_ritual "Deprivation ritual") for Yoda to reach Jinn's voice. During the procedure, Kenobi, Skywalker, Mundi and Plo Koon watched over the small Jedi, Yoda managed to hear Jinn's instruction to go to the [Dagobah system](/wiki/Dagobah_system "Dagobah system") before Kenobi noticed his vital signs were dropping too low and stopped the test. When asked about the procedure by Windu, Kenobi told him Yoda was sure he had contacted the dead and, like most, he was in disbelief about the whole ordeal, only for Windu to place guards to keep an eye on Yoda and the small Jedi Master to escape with Skywalker's help and R2-D2's company, willing to go on a journey that would take him to [Dagobah](/wiki/Dagobah "Dagobah"), a [mysterious planet](/wiki/Wellspring_of_Life "Wellspring of Life") and [Moraband](/wiki/Moraband "Moraband").[[162]](#cite_note-Voices-162)[[163]](#cite_note-Destiny-163)[[161]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-161)

On Yoda's return to Coruscant, Kenobi and Windu greeted him, and Windu asked him if he had gained some insight on how to win the war, but the old Jedi Master told them that he no longer believed that the Jedi could win the Clone Wars but that, through hope and perseverance, the Jedi would ultimately triumph over the Sith.[[161]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-161)

#### Crystal crisis on Utapau

:   "*How well would you sleep, knowing that I failed you?*"  
    "*Not very well, I imagine. Luckily, that isn't true, and never will be.*"
:   ―Anakin Skywalker and Obi-Wan Kenobi[[164]](#cite_note-In_Search_of_the_Crystal-164)

During the last months of the war, Kenobi and Skywalker were sent to [Utapau](/wiki/Utapau "Utapau") to [investigate](/wiki/Mission_to_Utapau "Mission to Utapau") the mysterious death of Jedi Master [Tu-Anh](/wiki/Tu-Anh "Tu-Anh"). Once they landed on [Pau City](/wiki/Pau_City "Pau City"), they met [Inspector](/wiki/Inspector "Inspector") [Jen June](/wiki/Jen_June "Jen June") who immediately led them to the [morgue](/wiki/Pau_City_Morgue "Pau City Morgue") where the Jedi's corpse was located. The two Jedi examined her body, and later went to the location where she had been found, only to determine she had been hit in the optic nerve with a [precision laser dart](/wiki/Vilmarh%27s_Revenge "Vilmarh's Revenge") by a sniper. As they found the sniper's position, they found slime on the floor and interrogated the building's owner, [Garri](/wiki/Garri "Garri"), from whom the two Jedi learned of the involvement of MagnaGuards. Later, they asked Inspector June to analyze the slimy substance, with her concluding it was the secretion of an [Amani](/wiki/Amani "Amani")'s skin and added that Governor [Torul Blom](/wiki/Torul_Blom "Torul Blom") wanted to see them.[[165]](#cite_note-A_Death_on_Utapau-165)

 [![Kenobi and Skywalker speaking to Inspector June.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/A_Death_on_Utapau_Ep.png/revision/latest?cb=20150510174900) [![Kenobi and Skywalker speaking to Inspector June.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/A_Death_on_Utapau_Ep.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20150510174900)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/A_Death_on_Utapau_Ep.png/revision/latest?cb=20150510174900) 

Kenobi and Skywalker speaking to Inspector June.

 

Though the Governor asked them to leave Utapau, Kenobi and Skywalker persevered and rented two [dactillions](/wiki/Dactillion "Dactillion") to go to the city's lower levels and talk to the leader of an Amani tribe there. Told that an Amani outcast had been seen entering a cave not far from there, Kenobi thanked him, and he and Skywalker went to the cave, where they found the MagnaGuards, leading them to suspect of a Separatist conspiracy. Despite some resistance, they managed to get information from the droids that showed them the involvement of the [Sugi](/wiki/Sugi "Sugi") and went to see Inspector June once again. After she identified the Amani as coming from the plain, Kenobi contacted the Council to inform them of their findings and later attended together with Skywalker, attended the [funeral of Tu-Anh](/wiki/Funeral_of_Tu-Anh "Funeral of Tu-Anh").[[165]](#cite_note-A_Death_on_Utapau-165)

Soon after, they reached the Amani settlement they had been looking for, only for their dactillions to be killed and for the Amani to scatter in every direction during the ensuing confrontation, leaving Skywalker and Kenobi to follow the tracks of one that appeared to be their leader. During the hunt, Skywalker mentioned Tano for the first time since her departure, and Kenobi asked if he wanted to talk about it, yet Skywalker refused. Kenobi then suggested for them to set up a camp and rest. However, he insisted on the subject, prompting Skywalker to tell Kenobi he missed Tano and to voice his anger at the High Council for turning its back on her. In response, Kenobi asserted that it had been Tano's decision to leave, and that she had allowed her emotions to cloud her judgement, something against the Jedi way. Then, Kenobi suggested him to rest, but Skywalker declined so that he could keep the first watch. Finally, he questioned Kenobi on what would happen if he had turned out to be a "major disappointment," but Kenobi wanted to believe it would never happen.[[164]](#cite_note-In_Search_of_the_Crystal-164)

 [![Kenobi and Skywalker defending a massive kyber crystal.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/37/Crystal_Crisis_Ep.png/revision/latest?cb=20150510175802) [![Kenobi and Skywalker defending a massive kyber crystal.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/37/Crystal_Crisis_Ep.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20150510175802)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/37/Crystal_Crisis_Ep.png/revision/latest?cb=20150510175802) 

Kenobi and Skywalker defending a massive kyber crystal.

 

However, they both fell asleep and were captured by a group of Sugis led by [Chong](/wiki/Chong "Chong"), who brought them before [Endente](/wiki/Endente "Endente") as Kenobi told Chong of their "intention" to buy weapons. However, they learned Endente was, in fact, selling a [kyber crystal](/wiki/Kyber_crystal "Kyber crystal") and Skywalker prompted him to show it before they made the deal. The two Jedi were then brought to the starship where the crystal was being kept and escaped from their captors. Once Skywalker took out all the Sugi and recovered their lightsabers from Chong, they were unable to capture Endente and discovered the massive kyber crystal inside the ship.[[164]](#cite_note-In_Search_of_the_Crystal-164) Despite being attacked, the two Jedi managed to transport the crystal through Utapau's plains until they reached Pau City, where Governor Blom showed them his true colors and had the two Jedi surrounded with his men and Grievous's droids. As the kyber crystal was loaded into a shuttle and sent to ship on orbit, Kenobi and Skywalker took June and Blom as hostages, so that their underlings stopped shooting at them, and stole a [freighter](/wiki/Unidentified_freighter_(Utapau) "Unidentified freighter (Utapau)") to recover the crystal.[[166]](#cite_note-Crystal_Crisis-166)

 [![Kenobi and Skywalker planning to escape.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/Big_Bang_Ep.png/revision/latest?cb=20150510175746) [![Kenobi and Skywalker planning to escape.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/Big_Bang_Ep.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20150510175746)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/Big_Bang_Ep.png/revision/latest?cb=20150510175746) 

Kenobi and Skywalker planning to escape.

 

During the persecution, Kenobi contacted the High Council to inform them of their current course of action, and Grievous soon damaged their ship, forcing them to, performing a [number five special](/wiki/Number_five_special "Number five special"), crash the ship to damage the hyperdrive and board the ship where the crystal was then held. However, they got separated, and Kenobi landed in a [hangar](/wiki/Hangar "Hangar") full of droids, where he was soon confronted and captured by Grievous. Following Dooku's orders to execute him, Kenobi was being escorted to the execution room until Skywalker rescued him. Together, their made their way to the kyber crystal at the vault, where they were temporarily trapped until a squad discovered them. Using the crystal and the Force to knock them out, he managed to get to a hangar where Skywalker got a shuttle for them to escape. Meanwhile, Kenobi set several [AATs](/wiki/Armored_Assault_Tank_Mk_I "Armored Assault Tank Mk I") to shoot and overload the crystal, destroying the crystal and the ship, and escaping from the explosion in the nick of time.[[44]](#cite_note-The_Big_Bang-44)

Back on Coruscant, Kenobi and Skywalker reported to the Council about the outcome of their mission, when Yoda told them of the use of kyber crystals on weapons of unimaginable power in ancient times.[[44]](#cite_note-The_Big_Bang-44)

#### The dark disciples

:   "*You were fighting her and chatting at the same time?*"  
    "*It's... Banter.*"  
    "*You* flirted *with her?*"  
    "*Come now, Vos, you can't tell me you managed to go undercover in all sorts of shady places without flirting yourself.*"
:   ―Quinlan Vos and Obi-Wan Kenobi[[8]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-8)

 [![Even though he disagreed with the mission, Obi-Wan Kenobi suggested Quinlan Vos be deployed to assassinate Count Dooku.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Vosteth.png/revision/latest?cb=20130517040525) [![Even though he disagreed with the mission, Obi-Wan Kenobi suggested Quinlan Vos be deployed to assassinate Count Dooku.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Vosteth.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130517040525)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Vosteth.png/revision/latest?cb=20130517040525) 

Even though he disagreed with the mission, Obi-Wan Kenobi suggested Quinlan Vos be deployed to assassinate Count Dooku.

 

Upon [Mahranee](/wiki/Mahranee "Mahranee")'s [fall](/wiki/Atrocity_on_Mahranee "Atrocity on Mahranee") and the destruction of General [Chubor](/wiki/Chubor "Chubor")'s [refugee](/wiki/Refugee "Refugee")-carrier [Republic frigate](/wiki/Chubor%27s_Republic_frigate "Chubor's Republic frigate") by Dooku's decision, Kenobi participated in council meeting along with Skywalker, where it was decided to bring about the Count's assassination, for they had reached the conclusion that all that had transpired in the war had been because of Dooku. Though Kenobi was against the idea, he nevertheless suggested Quinlan Vos to be deployed for the mission.[[8]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-8)

Once Vos returned to Coruscant from his covert mission in [Otor's Hub](/wiki/Otor%27s_Hub "Otor's Hub") after ending [Sheb Valaad](/wiki/Sheb_Valaad "Sheb Valaad")'s [black market](/wiki/Black_market "Black market") operation, Kenobi greeted him at the Jedi Temple and accompanied him to the [Jedi Council Chamber](/wiki/Jedi_Council_Chamber "Jedi Council Chamber"). There, Vos was informed of his mission, and Ventress's role in it; Vos accepted. At the end of the session, Kenobi went to Vos' encounter at the dining hall and gave him more details about Ventress's character. Afterwards, Kenobi and Vos would prearrange to meet at a bar in [Level 1313](/wiki/Level_1313 "Level 1313") so that Vos would keep him appraised of his progress at regular intervals. Vos' absence in their third and fourth would-be encounters forced Kenobi to report to the Council.[[8]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-8)

At one such meeting, Ventress was the one to appear at the bar, after her [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Serenno_(Krayt%27s_Claw) "Mission to Serenno (Krayt's Claw)") to rescue Vos from Serenno after he had been captured following their [failed attempt](/wiki/Mission_to_Raxus_Secundus "Mission to Raxus Secundus") to kill Dooku, she told Kenobi that they had lost Vos to Dooku and the dark side; the two sat there, together, for a long time. Kenobi would later make mention of their encounter to his fellow Jedi, among them [Akar-Deshu](/wiki/Akar-Deshu "Akar-Deshu").[[8]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-8)

#### On Maul's tail

:   "*I sense your turmoil, Obi-Wan.*"  
    "*My last encounter with Maul didn't go so well.*"  
    "*He murdered the Duchess Satine. Someone you cared for deeply.*"  
    "*My emotions are under control, Master Tiplee. I will not fail you* or *this mission.* "
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi[[167]](#cite_note-DM:SoD-167)

Following the [Battle of Ord Mantell](/wiki/Battle_on_Ord_Mantell "Battle on Ord Mantell"), Kenobi was sent to [Ord Mantell](/wiki/Ord_Mantell "Ord Mantell") to investigate who the Separatist forces had been fighting, alongside Jedi Masters [Tiplee](/wiki/Tiplee "Tiplee"), Mace Windu and Aayla Secura. Though the Shadow Collective had managed to collect most traces of their presence in the [city](/wiki/Ord_Mantell_City "Ord Mantell City"), [Wolffe](/wiki/Wolffe "Wolffe") and his men uncovered a Mandalorian helmet outside the town, which led the four Jedi on the trail of Maul.[[167]](#cite_note-DM:SoD-167)

 [![Kenobi during the assault on Maul's hideout](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9e/Obi-Wan_Kenobi_Son_of_Dathomir.png/revision/latest?cb=20140812061038) [![Kenobi during the assault on Maul's hideout](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9e/Obi-Wan_Kenobi_Son_of_Dathomir.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140812061038)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9e/Obi-Wan_Kenobi_Son_of_Dathomir.png/revision/latest?cb=20140812061038) 

Kenobi during the assault on Maul's hideout

 

Aware of the [Black Sun](/wiki/Black_Sun "Black Sun")'s presence on the system, and the location of [Vizsla Keep 09](/wiki/Vizsla_Keep_09 "Vizsla Keep 09"), a Mandalorian supply outpost suspected to be Maul's hideout, Kenobi and Tiplee led an [assault](/wiki/Assault_on_Vizsla_Keep_09 "Assault on Vizsla Keep 09") to lock the place down until reinforcements arrived. Tiplee expressed concern that Obi-Wan would allow his feelings for Satine to cloud his judgement when facing Maul, but he assured her that he would be under control and wouldn't fail the mission. As the two Jedi tried to reach the command center, Maul and Count Dooku appeared to duel them, with Windu and Secura joining them soon afterwards. Despite their advantage over the Sith, Tiplee was killed by Dooku, and a Mandalorian assisted Maul by setting off an explosion that injured Windu and Secura. The Sith, then, managed to escape as Maul told Kenobi not to worry, as they would be seeing each other again soon; his alliance with Dooku leaving the Jedi perplexed as to what had just happened.[[167]](#cite_note-DM:SoD-167)

#### Vos' rescue

:   "*Ventress is at fault, yes, and of course Dooku. But this, Masters...this one is* our *responsibility. We owe Vos the chance to choose again, and, with our help, wisely.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to the Council[[8]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-8)

Upon Akar-Deshu's meeting with Asajj Ventress, Kenobi and Skywalker met with them and Kenobi promised her that she would come to no harm within the Temple, and brought her to the Council chambers. Despite Windu's open disapproval, Yoda allowed Kenobi and Skywalker to go with Ventress to rescue Vos. Soon enough, Kenobi, Skywalker, and Ventress were on the cockpit of her ship, the [*Banshee*](/wiki/Banshee_(starship) "Banshee (starship)"), to [infiltrate](/wiki/Rescue_of_Quinlan_Vos "Rescue of Quinlan Vos") the Separatist dreadnought where Vos, or rather "Admiral Enigma," was issuing orders from.[[8]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-8)

Stealthily, the three made their way to the bridge where Skywalker dueled Dooku, while Kenobi and Ventress discovered Vos was still being held captive by the Count. However, Ventress saw through his ruse and tried to relieve Vos from an existence consumed by hatred, but Kenobi convinced her to escape before taking such an extreme action. Barely escaping on the *Banshee*, they made their way back to Coruscant, and Kenobi saw as the Council welcomed Vos and pardoned Ventress.[[8]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-8)

#### Redemption of the fallen

:   "*You misunderstand, Master Windu. All of you. She didn't just save his life. She saved* Quinlan*. And...I believe she may have saved us.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, on Asajj Ventress[[8]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-8)

A month later, Kenobi was sent alongside Skywalker, Vos, and Akar-Deshu in a [mission](/wiki/Destruction_of_the_Separatist_supply_storage_base "Destruction of the Separatist supply storage base") to take over a [Separatist supply storage base](/wiki/Separatist_supply_storage_base "Separatist supply storage base") and redistribute the supplies to worlds in need of them. However, their mission went awry when Vos, unbeknownst to them, arranged the base's destruction. Later on, Kenobi and Vos would be [deployed](/wiki/Destruction_of_the_Vanqor_listening_station "Destruction of the Vanqor listening station") to a [listening post](/wiki/Vanqor_listening_station "Vanqor listening station") on Vanqor, but their second fruitless campaign in a row made Kenobi suspicious of a leak. He confided his feelings to Yoda and Windu, leading them to suspect Vos was the leak. Kenobi would later be summoned by Yoda to tell him that he had sensed concealed darkness in Vos' soul, and the Council arranged an emergency session, in which they entertained the option of executing Vos. Kenobi, however, protested against the idea, and suggested sending Vos again to assassinate Dooku to test his allegiances.[[8]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-8)

 [![Traveling to Christophsis, Obi-Wan Kenobi bore witness to Quinlan Vos's actions.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/37/Insider204-Kenobi.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210724021606) [![Traveling to Christophsis, Obi-Wan Kenobi bore witness to Quinlan Vos's actions.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/37/Insider204-Kenobi.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210724021606)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/37/Insider204-Kenobi.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210724021606) 

Traveling to Christophsis, Obi-Wan Kenobi bore witness to Quinlan Vos's actions.

 

Afterwards, Vos had Ventress tell the Council of the Count and Grievous' [presence](/wiki/Second_battle_of_Christophsis "Second battle of Christophsis") on Christophsis, and the two set out on their mission aboard the *Banshee*. Kenobi and Skywalker followed suit and spied on Vos, who reunited with Dooku; they observed as the two dueled, when Vos gained the upper hand just as he let Dooku live as long as he told him about his Master's whereabouts. It was then that Kenobi and Skywalker intervened, taking the pair by surprised, and placed them under arrest. The two soon escaped from the [*Vigilance*](/wiki/Vigilance_(Venator-class) "Vigilance (Venator-class)"), causing the death of Akar-Deshu and the [Chagrian](/wiki/Chagrian "Chagrian") [Kav Bayons](/wiki/Kav_Bayons "Kav Bayons"), and boarded the *Banshee*, but Skywalker's quick thinking forced the renegades to crash land on the planet.[[8]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-8)

The two Jedi pursued the three injured renegades to a [Separatist tower](/wiki/Christophsis_Separatist_tower "Christophsis Separatist tower"), where they surrounded them. There, Kenobi and Skywalker witnessed[[8]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-8) what appeared to be[[168]](#cite_note-TBB_article-168) Ventress' last moments before finding Vos. They transported Vos back to Coruscant where the fallen Jedi confessed all his crimes and Kenobi defended Ventress. After being placed under Yoda's supervision for some time, Vos was released to Kenobi's care so he could take Ventress' body back to Dathomir, where she would be finally reunited with her sisters.[[8]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-8)

#### Attack on the Jedi temple

Kenobi was present when Jedi Master Depa Billaba came out of a coma, having been in the state for six months. Pleased to see her feeling better, he welcomed her back to her duties. Kenobi participated in the Initiate Trials at the Temple, as well as in an evaluation of Billaba's mental state, meant to clear her for service. Though she was unsure of her past failures, Kenobi assured her that success is has never been a prerequisite for service before offering her his council seat.[[169]](#cite_note-Kanan_7-169) Nevertheless, Kenobi remained a member of the Council[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) and worked alongside her.[[169]](#cite_note-Kanan_7-169)

Sometime after Billaba grew interested in making the youngling [Caleb Dume](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus "Kanan Jarrus") her apprentice, Kenobi gave a lecture in the [Jedi Temple central security station](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_central_security_station "Jedi Temple central security station") for younglings to learn about the Jedi recall signal, when Dume asked whether the same system could be used to warn Jedi away. Kenobi was intrigued by the possibility,[[170]](#cite_note-A_New_Dawn-170) and the idea would later prove essential.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) Kenobi was later present at the temple when it was [attacked](/wiki/Bombing_at_the_Jedi_Temple "Bombing at the Jedi Temple") by Separatist general [Rackham Sear](/wiki/Rackham_Sear "Rackham Sear"). However, the attack was foiled by Depa Billaba just as he and Windu arrived on the scene.[[171]](#cite_note-Kanan_8-171)

#### Struggle for Anaxes

:   "*I hope you at least told Padmé I said hello.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to Anakin Skywalker[[172]](#cite_note-A_Distant_Echo-172)

After an [assault on Cato Neimoidia](/wiki/Assault_on_Cato_Neimoidia "Assault on Cato Neimoidia"),[[173]](#cite_note-Grand_Army_Encyclopedia-173) Kenobi became involved in the [Battle of Anaxes](/wiki/Battle_of_Anaxes "Battle of Anaxes").[[172]](#cite_note-A_Distant_Echo-172) Following amounting losses on the Republic side in and Captain Rex's successful mission to a Separatist [Cyber Center](/wiki/Cyber_Center "Cyber Center") with the assistance of [Clone Force 99](/wiki/Clone_Force_99 "Clone Force 99") to discover if General Trench was in possession of [Rex's battle strategy algorithm](/wiki/Rex%27s_battle_strategy_algorithm "Rex's battle strategy algorithm"),[[174]](#cite_note-The_Bad_Batch-174) Skywalker and Rex were to go on a [mission to Skako Minor](/wiki/Mission_to_Skako_Minor_(Clone_Wars) "Mission to Skako Minor (Clone Wars)"). [Clone Sergeant](/wiki/Clone_Sergeant "Clone Sergeant") "[Hunter](/wiki/Hunter "Hunter")" stated that Clone Force 99 would be heading to the planet as well. Skywalker believed Kenobi would approve the mission.[[172]](#cite_note-A_Distant_Echo-172)

While Rex was eager to go, believing ARC trooper Echo was still alive, Skywalker reminded his Captain that they had a "thing" to do: Skywalker was to contact his secret wife, Senator Amidala. Skywalker spoke to her via hologram inside the barracks with Rex keeping watch outside, but Kenobi approached Rex to ask where Skywalker was. Rex attempted to cover for his friend, but Skywalker soon exited, and the two began to depart for the [*Marauder*](/wiki/Marauder_(Omicron-class) "Marauder (Omicron-class)"). However, Kenobi called after Skywalker and revealed he knew his former Padawan had been speaking with Amidala.[[172]](#cite_note-A_Distant_Echo-172)

 [![Kenobi and Windu on Anaxes](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/EpGuide704.png/revision/latest?cb=20200331003655) [![Kenobi and Windu on Anaxes](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/EpGuide704.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/258?cb=20200331003655)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/EpGuide704.png/revision/latest?cb=20200331003655) 

Kenobi and Windu on Anaxes

 

After their success, Kenobi took part on Windu's debriefing on the strategy to take the [Separatist assembly complex](/wiki/Anaxes_assembly_complex "Anaxes assembly complex") by air, when Echo posed his plan to be escorted by the Bad Batch into Trench's new comm vault on a [dreadnought](/wiki/Providence-class_Dreadnought "Providence-class Dreadnought") on the planet's orbit and plug himself to feed the Separatist's strategic movements. Kenobi took part on the assault and the combined efforts managed to take the complex under their control and, with all other fronts falling to the Republic, Trench initiated a countdown for an explosion that could destroy most of Anaxes. While Windu deactivated the bomb, Kenobi assisted in the evacuation efforts; with Trench's death at the hands of Skywalker and his fleet's destruction, the battle was won. Thanking Captain Rex, Corporal Echo, and the Bad Batch, Kenobi told the clones they would receive [medals](/wiki/Unidentified_medal_(Battle_of_Anaxes) "Unidentified medal (Battle of Anaxes)") for their actions, but the Bad Batch intended to leave before the ceremony. Additionally, Echo decided to leave with the batch.[[175]](#cite_note-Unfinished_Business-175)

#### Battle of Yerbana

:   "*Yes, Cody. You can join in on the fun as well.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to Commander Cody[[176]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-176)

 [![Kenobi leads his Battalion in Yerbana](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/KenobiOnYerbana.png/revision/latest?cb=20200419191924) [![Kenobi leads his Battalion in Yerbana](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/KenobiOnYerbana.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200419191924)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/KenobiOnYerbana.png/revision/latest?cb=20200419191924) 

Kenobi leads his Battalion in Yerbana

 

A short time after they undertook a mission to Cato Neimoidia,[[52]](#cite_note-Anakin_Encyclopedia-52) Kenobi and Skywalker were sent to [Yerbana](/wiki/Yerbana "Yerbana") to take down the Separatist forces that were oppressing the people in the planet. During the battle, Kenobi took his 212th Attack Battalion to fight in one front, while Skywalker led his 501st [Legion](/wiki/Legion "Legion") into another offensive. The battle proved to be more brutal and problematic than expected to Kenobi and his clone troopers, who were suffering heavily damages from the Droids attacks, and were unable to destroy the commander droid. After saving Cody from a missile, Kenobi ordered his troopers to take cover. Kenobi wondered where his Padawan was as he needed his assistance. Fortunately, Skywalker, who successfully defeated the Separatist army in his offensive, arrived and convinced Kenobi to let him act as he had planned. Knowing that Skywalker had already decided how to act and would not change his mind, Kenobi gave his Apprentice the leadership of the battle. Skywalker faked a surrender to draw out the droid commander. After using his Force abilities to destroy it, Skywalker ordered his 501st Legion led by Captain Rex to attack rest of the droid army.[[176]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-176)

Kenobi then gave permission to Cody to lead the 212th Attack Battalion in helping the 501st. Kenobi approached Skywalker complimenting him for his help, to which Skywalker thanked him for pretending to be defeated. Kenobi said he was always glad to help. Then, the two were contacted by Admiral Wullf Yularen who informed them of a transmission going under the code "Fulcrum." Skywalker guessed it might be Saw Gerrera, which worried Kenobi about the current state of the [siege at Onderon](/wiki/Siege_at_Onderon "Siege at Onderon"). Yularen denied it was Gerrera and requested the Generals to attend the call.[[176]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-176)

#### Locating Maul

:   "*I killed Maul once. Best to capture him. He doesn't seem to stay dead.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to Ahsoka Tano[[176]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-176)

At Yularen's ship, Kenobi and Skywalker entered the room only to witness Ahsoka Tano and Bo-Katan Kryze as the ones that had made the call. Kenobi asked Tano what was the information she had. Tano informed them that that Maul had been located on Mandalore and they had an opportunity to capture him.[[176]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-176)

While going to greet Tano and her allies, Skywalker, who was still emotionally shocked to see his former apprentice again, claimed that it all made sense, in an attempt to understand Tano's decision to leave the Jedi Order. Skywalker told Kenobi that if Tano had not left the Order, then Maul would have never been located. As always, Kenobi was more reserved about the situation and decided to wait and see how the events were to develop, remaining cautiously optimistic.[[176]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-176)

After a quick greeting, Tano, Kryze, and her Mandalorians were led by Kenobi to a private room to discuss Maul's whereabouts. However, Kenobi was not willing to help Tano and her allies unless the Jedi Council gave their permission, saying the Republic could not get involved with Mandalorian affairs. Kryze explained that there was not time to turn that into a bureaucratic decision, as Maul could escape before they made an offensive. Kryze reminded Kenobi that the former Sith Lord killed Satine and confronted Kenobi about how could he not want to capture Maul as Satine was supposedly important to him. Kenobi reassured Bo-Katan that he still cared deeply about Satine, but he could not allow his feelings to cloud his judgment. Kenobi proceeded to consult the Jedi Council.[[176]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-176)

#### Rescue of the Chancellor

:   "*So that's it? You're going to abandon Bo-Katan and her people?*"  
    "*Ahsoka, surely you understand this is pivotal moment in the Clone Wars? The heart of the Republic is under attack!*"  
    "*I understand that as usual you're playing politics. This is why the people have lost faith in the Jedi! I had too, until I was reminded of what the Order means to people who truly needed us.*"  
    "*Right now, people on Coruscant need us.*"  
    "*No. The Chancellor needs you.*"  
    "*That's not fair.*"  
    "*I'm not trying to be.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Ahsoka Tano's argument, prior to the Battle of Coruscant[[176]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-176)

When Kenobi contacted the Council, he was informed that General Grievous had attacked the capital of the Republic, and that they lost contact with Shaak Ti, Chancellor Palpatine's assigned protector.
