He immediately informed Tano and Skywalker of this, at the same time ordering their fleet to travel to Coruscant, reassuring Anakin who asked after Palpatine, that they could reach the planet within the hour. This angered Tano, who accused her former masters of choosing to abandon Mandalore. Somewhat shocked by the accusation, Kenobi urged Tano to understand that they were entering a pivotal moment in the Clone Wars, as the heart of the Republic was under attack. Tano countered that Kenobi was playing politics, stating that it was proof as to how the Jedi Order had lost their way by forgetting that their duty was to help people and not politicians.[[176]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-176)

Upon hearing Tano explain why so many had lost faith in the Jedi, Kenobi countered that the people of Coruscant needed them, but Tano believed that it was really about saving the Chancellor. Kenobi told Tano to be fair, but Tano retorted that she wasn't trying to play fair. Skywalker heard the argument and weighed in. So as to help Tano in the upcoming siege without compromising Mandalore's neutrality and the mission to rescue the Chancellor, Skywalker promoted Rex to Commander so he could lead the mission and had Tano assisting him as an advisor. When Kenobi agreed, Tano accepted the proposal. Instead of allowing his meeting with Tano to end on a sour note, Kenobi advised Tano to capture Maul, joking the former Sith did not seem to stay dead, before leaving the room to prepare the troops, leaving Skywalker and Tano behind.[[176]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-176)

 [![Kenobi and Skywalker inadvertently enter an elevator full of battle droids after boarding Invisible Hand.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/Drop_Em_AtG.png/revision/latest?cb=20190424233052) [![Kenobi and Skywalker inadvertently enter an elevator full of battle droids after boarding Invisible Hand.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/Drop_Em_AtG.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190424233052)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/Drop_Em_AtG.png/revision/latest?cb=20190424233052) 

Kenobi and Skywalker inadvertently enter an elevator full of battle droids after boarding *Invisible Hand*.

 

After Skywalker and Tano wished each other good luck on their respective missions,[[176]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-176) Kenobi and Skywalker traveled to Coruscant to rescue the Chancellor. The two Jedi fought their way through a Separatist blockade and managed to board the *[Invisible Hand](/wiki/Invisible_Hand "Invisible Hand")*, only to find the Chancellor being held prisoner at the top of the ship's observation spire. Not long after they arrived to the room, Count Dooku appeared before them and the two Jedi engaged him in a duel.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

Though Dooku managed to gain the upper hand and knocked Kenobi out cold, Skywalker was able to defeat the Sith Lord, and subsequently executed him at Palpatine's urging. He then rescued Kenobi, carrying him until he woke up when they were hanging in an elevator. As they got out of there and ran through hallway 328, Grievous had them trapped in a ray shield and brought to the *Invisible Hand*'s control room. The cyborg General personally taunted them, giving R2-D2 enough time to free them and for Kenobi and Skywalker to confront Grievous. The General, however, escaped in an escape pod and forced the two Jedi to pilot the ship and land on Coruscant as safely as they could. Following the ordeal, they escorted the Chancellor to the Senate building, where they separated, with Kenobi going back to Jedi Temple to report to the Council of Dooku's demise and what it meant to the Clone Wars.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

#### Dividing friendship

:   "*All of this is unusual, and it's making me feel uneasy.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, on Anakin's appointment with Palpatine[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

Later, Kenobi attended another meeting, concerning the reports on the Outer Rim Sieges, including Saleucami's fall and the move of Quinlan Vos' troops to [Boz Pity](/wiki/Boz_Pity "Boz Pity"). At the end of the session, he met with Skywalker and told him to be careful with Palpatine, and that Palpatine had requested his presence for unknown reasons. Soon enough, Kenobi and the Council were made aware that the Chancellor had Skywalker appointed as his Personal Representative on the Jedi Council; though the Council approved of the appointment, they denied Skywalker the rank of Jedi Master, a decision which greatly angered Skywalker, prompting him to question the Council's decision-making. Kenobi remained silent. After being admonished by Windu, Skywalker reluctantly accepted his position and took his seat on the Council. During the same meeting, Kenobi and Master Mundi discussed the importance of Kashyyyk, prompting Master Yoda to assist the [Wookiees](/wiki/Wookiee "Wookiee") himself.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

 [![Kenobi deliberating with the Council](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/Council_RotS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130726094932) [![Kenobi deliberating with the Council](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/Council_RotS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/306?cb=20130726094932)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/Council_RotS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130726094932) 

Kenobi deliberating with the Council

 

At the end of the meeting, Kenobi acknowledged to Skywalker that his appointment had been accepted so that, on behalf of the Council, Skywalker could spy on the Chancellor, an assignment that Anakin refused to partake in because he believed it to be an act of treason. He tried to convince Anakin that something out of place had to be happening for Palpatine to remain in office long after his two legitimate terms had expired and to have accumulated an unnatural amount of executive powers, but still, Anakin would have none of it. Later, before Yoda's departure to Kashyyyk, Kenobi conferred with Windu and Yoda of Skywalker's reluctant compliance on his task, when he heard of Windu's distrust of the Jedi Knight and Yoda's doubts about the prophecy of the "Chosen One."[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

Following the Chancellor's disclosure of General Grievous' location on Utapau to Skywalker, who then passed it onto the Council, Kenobi was sent to capture the fugitive General.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) Immediately prior to his voyage to Utapau, Kenobi contacted Tano and the Mandalorians on Mandalore via hologram. Kryze told him that the clones had been extremely effective against Maul's forces. While communing, Tano mentioned that Maul had said the name Darth Sidious while they confronted one another and Kryze asked who he was. Kenobi admitted that the Jedi did not know much about him, but told them that he orchestrated the Clone Wars and manipulated both sides of the conflict. He soon informed them about the death of Count Dooku during the Battle of Coruscant after Tano asked why they would no longer be able to get anymore information from him about Sidious. With this, he asked them once again to capture Maul so that they may finally be able to put an end to the mystery of Sidious. Tano asked for reinforcements, but Kenobi was forced to tell them that he was being sent to capture Grievous on Utapau and that he was unable to send support. Tano then asked if Skywalker could provide support to which Kenobi asked to speak to Tano in private.[[177]](#cite_note-Phantom_Apprentice2-177)

 [![Obi-Wan shares his knowledge of Sidious with Ahsoka, Bo-Katan, and Rex.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2f/KenobiConferenceCall-TPA.png/revision/latest?cb=20200430031700) [![Obi-Wan shares his knowledge of Sidious with Ahsoka, Bo-Katan, and Rex.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2f/KenobiConferenceCall-TPA.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/322?cb=20200430031700)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2f/KenobiConferenceCall-TPA.png/revision/latest?cb=20200430031700) 

Obi-Wan shares his knowledge of Sidious with Ahsoka, Bo-Katan, and Rex.

 

After Rex and Kryze left, he informed Tano of Skywalker's mission to spy on Supreme Chancellor Palpatine by the Jedi High Council. After Tano began to ask why they would give him such an assignment, Kenobi informed her that the Council wished to learn what Palpatine was truly plotting after remaining in the office of Supreme Chancellor long after his term's conclusion. Tano began to argue with Kenobi and said that she couldn't imagine Skywalker could be happy with the burden the Council had placed upon him. Kenobi knew this and informed Tano as much, asking her to speak with him after their meeting ended to help him with his burden. Tano began to grow increasingly agitated with the Council after Kenobi asked this, but Kenobi revealed that he knew the Council wasn't correct in every one of their decisions and that if Tano communicated with Skywalker, it could help them. Before Tano could respond, Rex rushed in and informed the two that there had been an attack and with that, Kenobi allowed her to leave. Before Tano left, she asked him to tell Skywalker something that she left unspoken. Kenobi assured her that he would and, with this, ended the transmission.[[177]](#cite_note-Phantom_Apprentice2-177)

With the destruction of R4-P17 and his Jedi interceptor during the Battle of Coruscant, Kenobi was assigned astromech droid [R4-G9](/wiki/R4-G9 "R4-G9"),[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) whom he had previously worked with during the [search for Asajj Ventress](/wiki/Search_for_Asajj_Ventress "Search for Asajj Ventress"),[[178]](#cite_note-Updated_Character_Encyclopedia-178) and a [blue Eta-2 *Actis*-class light interceptor](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi%27s_blue_Eta-2_Actis-class_interceptor "Obi-Wan Kenobi's blue Eta-2 Actis-class interceptor") before his search for Grievous. Before Kenobi's departure to engage Grievous, Skywalker apologized to Kenobi, who told him that he needed patience and that he would soon become a master. The two exchanged goodbyes in what would be their last meeting as friends and allies, a fact neither was aware of, before Kenobi departed for Utapau.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

#### Final clash with Grievous

:   "*Hello there!*"  
    "*General Kenobi! You are a bold one.* "
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and General Grievous[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

 [![Kenobi once again faces his longtime rival General Grievous on Utapau.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/Kenobi_faces_Grievous_ROTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130215052829) [![Kenobi once again faces his longtime rival General Grievous on Utapau.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/Kenobi_faces_Grievous_ROTS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/304?cb=20130215052829)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/Kenobi_faces_Grievous_ROTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130215052829) 

Kenobi once again faces his longtime rival General Grievous on Utapau.

 

Kenobi was accompanied to the planet by a fleet of Star Destroyers and battalions of clone troopers that were three times the size of what was normally required to take one minor star system.[[179]](#cite_note-The_End_of_the_Clone_Wars-179) Obi-Wan pushed the thoughts of his previous voyage aside as he traveled to the capital of Utapau, Pau City. On final approach, he noticed a significant difference: a Separatist core ship sphere that appeared to have blended with the sink hole's rock face.[[56]](#cite_note-HJJEncylopedia-56) Having arrived on Utapau, Kenobi discovered from Pau City [Port Administrator](/wiki/Port_Administrator "Port Administrator") [Tion Medon](/wiki/Tion_Medon "Tion Medon") that the inhabitants were secretly being held hostage by thousands of battle droids occupying the city's [tenth level](/wiki/Level_10 "Level 10"). Kenobi took this under advisement and hid out of sight after instructing R4-G9 to leave the [spaceport](/wiki/Spaceport "Spaceport") in his Jedi interceptor, tricking the spying droids into thinking that he had left.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) Allowing himself to be guided by the living Force,[[180]](#cite_note-Scarif_Encyclopedia-180) Obi-Wan visits the holding areas where Utapaun wranglers captured native winged and wingless lizards for transportation.[[181]](#cite_note-DB_Boga-181) He then addressed the Utai [varactyl](/wiki/Varactyl "Varactyl") tamers in search of a quick path there that wouldn't interfere with city life.[[180]](#cite_note-Scarif_Encyclopedia-180) Mounted on the varactyl [Boga](/wiki/Boga "Boga"), Kenobi made his way to the Separatist holdout and waited for the Separatist Council to depart. He then leaped down from the scaffolding where he had been hidden,[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) just as he had done years before on Geonosis[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39) and greeted General Grievous before being surrounded by various types of battle droids. Grievous ordered his MagnaGuards to dispatch Kenobi, who managed to crush them under a piece of the ceiling without engaging in combat.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

However, Grievous ordered them to back away as he decided to engaged Kenobi himself,[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) exactly as Obi-Wan predicted.[[179]](#cite_note-The_End_of_the_Clone_Wars-179) The cyborg was eager to be the one to directly kill Kenobi directly in retaliation for defeating him previously on Utapau, as well as vowed to prove Sidious' worth.[[182]](#cite_note-The_Dark_Side-182) Kenobi had fought Grievous many times before and was well prepared,[[183]](#cite_note-HC_24-183) and both were aware of the other's skill.[[179]](#cite_note-The_End_of_the_Clone_Wars-179) Each time proved inconclusive, but both realized that this could not always be the case;[[84]](#cite_note-The_Separatists-84) it would not be an easy fight,[[179]](#cite_note-The_End_of_the_Clone_Wars-179) but the Jedi was not willing to allow him to escape this time.[[184]](#cite_note-Cyborg_and_Jedi-184) Obi-Wan stood there watching Grievous shrug off his cloak, being told that he had been trained in the Jedi arts by Count Dooku himself. He extends his four menacing arms, ignites a lightsaber in each mechanical hand, laughs, and then the two engage in one final duel. Grievous has taken the lightsabers from his exploits against the Jedi,[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) [Shaak Ti's lightsaber](/wiki/Shaak_Ti%27s_lightsaber "Shaak Ti's lightsaber") being one of his four primary weapons.[[185]](#cite_note-Holocron_Lightsabers_of_the_Jedi-185) Kenobi would not allow him to do the same with his lightsaber; he learned patience, confidence in the Force, and lightsaber training from Grand Master Yoda and his late Master, Qui-Gon Jinn.[[186]](#cite_note-Duel_for_Peace-186) The two engaged on a walkway suspended above the hanger's lower levels. Grievous moved closer and closer, whirling two of his lightsabers above his head and the other two dragging along, burning the floor behind him, surprising Kenobi with his maneuver. Initially, Obi-Wan slowly retreated[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) and let go of his fear.[[187]](#cite_note-ROTS_Read-Along-187) Waiting for the right moment,[[184]](#cite_note-Cyborg_and_Jedi-184) he stab his lightsaber between Grievous' flashing blades. Grievous then straightened up and struck Obi-Wan with both lightsabers, but the Jedi parried. With the other two stabs narrowly missing Kenobi, he leapt over him and attacked him from the side.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) The Jedi take advantage of Grievous's surprise to slip through his defense,[[188]](#cite_note-ROTS_French_Novel-188) leaving him striking where he once stood.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) The cyborg continued to fight back, but Obi-Wan's lightsaber remained.[[186]](#cite_note-Duel_for_Peace-186)

 [![During their duel, Kenobi gained the upper hand and quickly severed Grievous' two hands.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/Obi-WanclasheswithGrievous.png/revision/latest?cb=20221227183751) [![During their duel, Kenobi gained the upper hand and quickly severed Grievous' two hands.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/Obi-WanclasheswithGrievous.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20221227183751)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/Obi-WanclasheswithGrievous.png/revision/latest?cb=20221227183751) 

During their duel, Kenobi gained the upper hand and quickly severed Grievous' two hands.

 

Obi-Wan was able to neutralize Grievous' customary more wide-ranging fighting technique by limiting his movement to the catwalk. Kenobi maintained the fight close to the cyborg, having grown accustomed to his maneuvers after so many encounters.[[179]](#cite_note-The_End_of_the_Clone_Wars-179) He kept his cool and aimed wisely for Grievous' vulnerable wrist[[189]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Use_the_Force-189) instead intercepting his blade, severing his hand. It didn't take long for a clawed mechanical hand clattered down onto the deck, along with the lightsaber he held.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) Grievous, furious, launched a wild attack, but he had lost focus.[[179]](#cite_note-The_End_of_the_Clone_Wars-179) A few seconds later, Kenobi took another hand and weapon away from him and hands and keep up a solid defense against his unrelenting attacks.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) The droids watched as their leader continued to lose ground, but before they could help Grievous fight back,[[184]](#cite_note-Cyborg_and_Jedi-184) a pause occurred. Not long into the duel, the 212th Attack Battalion arrived and [engaged](/wiki/Battle_of_Utapau "Battle of Utapau") Grievous's forces. As the battle intensified, Kenobi threw Grievous against a wall, knocking his remaining sabers out of his hands and forcing him to escape in his [wheelbike](/wiki/TSMEU-6_personal_wheel_bike "TSMEU-6 personal wheel bike"). Obi-Wan had just made the jump to the lower level when Grievous fired it up and tore back into the hanger in an attempt to crush him.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) All around them, laser blasts and explosions ring out, but Grievous rushes as if the road were clear, dodging collision after collision[[188]](#cite_note-ROTS_French_Novel-188) or unleashing devastation on any clone soldiers in his path[[179]](#cite_note-The_End_of_the_Clone_Wars-179) or crushing those unlucky enough to stand in his way.[[188]](#cite_note-ROTS_French_Novel-188) Kenobi chased after the fleeing [cyborg](/wiki/Cyborg "Cyborg") on Boga, though his lightsaber was knocked out of his hand and recovered by Commander Cody hundreds of [meters](/wiki/Meter "Meter") below.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) Obi-Wan would lose his chance to capture Grievous if he stopped to retrieve it, but the thought of going up against the cyborg without his lightsaber was frightening. Knowing he could trust the Force, the Jedi raced after him, leaving his lightsaber behind.[[186]](#cite_note-Duel_for_Peace-186)

Obi-Wan and Boga finally caught up with Grievous, he intended to reach his personal starfighter, the *Soulless One*, stationed at a landing platform distance from the main Separatist base he was aiming for[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) as a backup plan.[[179]](#cite_note-The_End_of_the_Clone_Wars-179) The tunnels become increasingly packed as they travel deeper into the city. Obi-Wan smiles as the General was forced to slow down to avoid a swarm of droids, his mount capable of achieving things that the General's speeder-wheel cannot. He directs it to the tunnel's ceiling, where he will no longer be disturbed by traffic congestion. The Jedi quickly gains ground on Grievous, while the tunnel in front of him leads to a small landing perform. He accelerates once more, catching up to the general.[[188]](#cite_note-ROTS_French_Novel-188) Obi-Wan had just pressed the general when the Separatist leader, able to control his bike and battle, used the [electrostaff](/wiki/Electrostaff "Electrostaff") that he stored on the wheelbike and began attacking him, eventually being pulled onto the vehicle itself along with him. They eventually arrived at a landing platform, Obi-Wan snatched the electrostaff and was clutching it as Grievous raised the [blaster](/wiki/DT-57_%22Annihilator%22_blaster "DT-57 \"Annihilator\" blaster"),[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) the [Grievance Striker](/wiki/Grievance_Striker "Grievance Striker").[[190]](#cite_note-Striker-190) He knocks the weapon out of Grievous's hand and lands a few solid blows on the General himself, his first to the chest, the second to the arm,[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) the metal bends, but does not break.[[188]](#cite_note-ROTS_French_Novel-188) Obi-Wan knocked Grievous to the ground and plunged the shaft into his abdomen, but the cyborg kicked him away[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) with such speed that the Jedi cannot.[[188]](#cite_note-ROTS_French_Novel-188)

 [![Obi-Wan ends Grievous with his own blaster.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/Obiwanshoots.png/revision/latest?cb=20130210053334) [![Obi-Wan ends Grievous with his own blaster.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/Obiwanshoots.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130210053334)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/Obiwanshoots.png/revision/latest?cb=20130210053334) 

Obi-Wan ends Grievous with his own blaster.

 

With no weapons, they engaged in a swift fight using hand-to-hand combat[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) that Grievous was coldly confident of winning.[[84]](#cite_note-The_Separatists-84) Grievous closed in on Kenobi, engaging him in a brawl, swinging his arm against him. Kenobi avoided his first swing but missed the second, backhanded across the platform, and bounce off the parked fighter,[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) putting him at a disadvantage.[[179]](#cite_note-The_End_of_the_Clone_Wars-179) The cyborg general's physical strength appeared to give him the advantage.[[191]](#cite_note-Ships_and_Vehicles_45-191) Continuing his assault,[[179]](#cite_note-The_End_of_the_Clone_Wars-179) Grievous lifted him and nearly punched his head out. Instead, he punched his own starfighter, leaving a huge dent in it. However, noticing that one of Grievous's plates was loose, Kenobi took advantage of his new action, grabbing the metal plates and pulling with all his might,[[188]](#cite_note-ROTS_French_Novel-188) managing to partially tear open Grievous's chest armor, exposing his gutsack. Alarmed, Grievous tossed Kenobi aside.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) Grievous laughed, he advanced on Obi-Wan, wounded but far from defeated.[[179]](#cite_note-The_End_of_the_Clone_Wars-179) Grievous attempted to crush Kenobi with his mechanical feet, but he avoided.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) With the Force,[[188]](#cite_note-ROTS_French_Novel-188) the Jedi attempted to knock down Grievous with a sweeping kick to the leg,[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) but Grievous, whose metal body was stronger than any droid's shell, hardly felt it[[188]](#cite_note-ROTS_French_Novel-188) and only feeling great pain in his own shin. Kenobi was eventually thrown to the edge of the platform, but was able to summon Grievous' blaster,[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) abandoned a few meters from him,[[188]](#cite_note-ROTS_French_Novel-188) forgotten by its owner,[[186]](#cite_note-Duel_for_Peace-186) and turned it against him[[27]](#cite_note-SW_Book-27) in defense of his own life,[[40]](#cite_note-Family_at_War-40) just before Grievous could finish him off, firing five shots into his gut sack, igniting it and burning Grievous from the inside-out.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) Screaming in pain,[[56]](#cite_note-HJJEncylopedia-56) letting out a sound that was halfway between a gasp of suffocation and a metal rustle. Then, a sequence of explosions ripped his body apart,[[188]](#cite_note-ROTS_French_Novel-188) bursting into flame and erupting from his helmet's eye slits.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) Grievous was already dead;[[179]](#cite_note-The_End_of_the_Clone_Wars-179) his charred metal body[[183]](#cite_note-HC_24-183) slumped lifelessly[[191]](#cite_note-Ships_and_Vehicles_45-191) and hit the ground over the hangar[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) with a clang.[[183]](#cite_note-HC_24-183) With his long-time rival and the Supreme Commander of the Droid Army slain, Kenobi headed off to rejoin his troops.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

Kenobi informed the clones that the general was dead but didn't have time to elaborate;[[188]](#cite_note-ROTS_French_Novel-188) victory looked inevitable.[[192]](#cite_note-HC_25-192) The battle of Utapau was one of the Clone Wars' last battles,[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) and with Grievous' death, the conflict that had claimed countless lives seemed to be coming to a conclusion, but the Jedi did not suspect it was also the beginning of the end.[[192]](#cite_note-HC_25-192)

#### Order 66

:   "*My clone troops turned on me. I need help.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi to Bail Organa[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

Following Windu's and other Council member's [duel](/wiki/Duel_in_Palpatine%27s_office "Duel in Palpatine's office") against Chancellor Palpatine, revealed to be Darth Sidious, and the issue of Order 66, Kenobi met up with Commander Cody and ordered him to contact the troops to move to the higher levels of the city. The clone then returned him his lightsaber, and Kenobi proceeded to climb with Boga, just as Cody received a direct message from Sidious, ordering him to execute the order. Before Kenobi went too far, Cody ordered his men to shoot at the Jedi Master, bringing his fall to the water below.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) Obi-Wan had no time or inclination to comprehend why his own men had turned against him. Hearing Boga's heartfelt tears, he felt a moment of sadness that he couldn't help her. Commander Cody, who was torn, saw Obi-Wan Kenobi as a threat to his operation. He knew from previous experience not to presume a Jedi was dead until he saw the body. Time and again, Obi-Wan, Anakin, and Ahsoka, not to mention the other Jedi he'd seen in action, had beaten seemingly impossible odds to come through.[[179]](#cite_note-The_End_of_the_Clone_Wars-179) However, unlike many others, he survived and swam towards a cave, fumbling his breather into place, then surfacing, stowing the breather, and managing to climb on his own while evading troops, only to discover the attack had been intentional.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) He knew his best chance of escaping lay with the ship Grievous had escaped from so many times.[[179]](#cite_note-The_End_of_the_Clone_Wars-179)

Fortunately, the clones were unaware of Grievous' escape ship's existence. Even if the cruisers orbiting the planet see him, they will believe he is a Separatist trying to escape from the fight. Of course, he still has to make his way past tens of thousands of clones to reach the ship's platform, but at least his enemies won't be waiting for him there.[[188]](#cite_note-ROTS_French_Novel-188) Kenobi took to the darkness of the caves, using his lightsaber as a torch, knowing he was still being pursued. At one point, he noticed approaching searchlights at one point. Before the Prowlers discovered him, they woken a nos monster, a gigantic predatory reptile that was protecting its nest. As the creature dealt with the droids, Obi-Wan slipped through.[[179]](#cite_note-The_End_of_the_Clone_Wars-179) Sneaking through Utapau's tunnels was difficult; not only did he have to avoid being discovered by the clones, but he also had to avoid the wild monsters that swarmed there.[[188]](#cite_note-ROTS_French_Novel-188) Kenobi avoided the clone troopers, battle droids, and even the Utapau locals by using all of his abilities.[[179]](#cite_note-The_End_of_the_Clone_Wars-179) Arriving at the main staging area, he witnessed with horror his former troops rounding up Pau'ans and Utai and overheard Cody asking if his search teams had discovered the fleeing Jedi. His worst fears confirmed, Obi-Wan headed for his escape route. Carefully, the Jedi made his way back and arrived at the site of his final battle with General Grievous,[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) he was relieved to find the small, flat-landing form deserted.[[188]](#cite_note-ROTS_French_Novel-188) Grievous' starfighter, the *Soulless One*, sat waiting near his former foe's smoking remains.[[192]](#cite_note-HC_25-192) He rushes into the fighter, running past the remains of his cyborg rival one final time[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) without even sparing a passing glance at Grievous's body,[[179]](#cite_note-The_End_of_the_Clone_Wars-179) and fires up the engines and takes off[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) as quickly as possible, relying on the element of surprise to fly past his old flagship and away.[[192]](#cite_note-HC_25-192)

 [![Kenobi and Bail Organa discussing with Yoda.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/70/Obi-Wan_Kenobi_and_Bail_Organa_Discuss_The_Situation.png/revision/latest?cb=20150108081639) [![Kenobi and Bail Organa discussing with Yoda.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/70/Obi-Wan_Kenobi_and_Bail_Organa_Discuss_The_Situation.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20150108081639)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/70/Obi-Wan_Kenobi_and_Bail_Organa_Discuss_The_Situation.png/revision/latest?cb=20150108081639) 

Kenobi and Bail Organa discussing with Yoda.

 

Taking Grievous' starfighter, he left Utapau and made contact with Senator Bail Organa, who had seen the [siege of the Jedi Temple](/wiki/Operation:_Knightfall "Operation: Knightfall") firsthand and was trying to locate other surviving Jedi. Reuniting on the *[Tantive III](/wiki/Tantive_III "Tantive III")*, Kenobi met with the Senator and Master Yoda, who told him of the retreat message telling all Jedi to return to the Temple, saying that the war was over. Kenobi then suggested to dismantle the signal, so that others wouldn't fall into the trap, and Yoda agreed.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

On their way to Coruscant, Organa was contacted by Vice Chancellor Amedda, who told him of an emergency session to be held by the Senate. Kenobi and Yoda entered the Jedi Temple and witnessed with their own eyes the massacre that just taken place. During that, Chancellor Palpatine told the Senate of the Jedi's "sedition" against the Republic and [declared](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") the birth of the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire").[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) Amidala's former handmaiden Sabé believed Kenobi died with the rest of the Jedi during the rise of the Empire.[[193]](#cite_note-Queen's_Shadow-193)

### Age of the Empire

:   "*This is Master Obi-Wan Kenobi. I regret to report that both our Jedi Order and the Republic have fallen, with the dark shadow of the Empire rising to take their place. This message is a warning and a reminder for any surviving Jedi: trust in the Force. Do* not *return to the Temple. That time has passed, and our future is uncertain.* Avoid Coruscant*. Avoid detection. Be* secret*... but be* strong*. We will each be challenged: our trust, our faith, our friendships. But we must persevere and, in time, I believe* a new hope *will emerge. May the Force be with you always.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi's warning in the recall signal[[194]](#cite_note-Kanan_2-194)

#### The fallen apprentice

:   "*It can't be. It can't be.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi learns that Anakin Skywalker has turned to the Dark Side[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

Intending to [infiltrate](/wiki/Infiltration_of_the_Jedi_Temple "Infiltration of the Jedi Temple") the building to shut off the Jedi recall beacon, Kenobi and Yoda made their way to the still-smoking Jedi Temple,[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) where they found clones were wearing Jedi robes in an attempt to trick Jedi survivors into a false sense of secruity.[[188]](#cite_note-ROTS_French_Novel-188) Both Jedi fought the 501st patrols outside and entered, finding the aftermath of a slaughter[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) that distressed Kenobi even more than the smoke and robe-wearing clones.[[188]](#cite_note-ROTS_French_Novel-188) When he made it to the central security station of the Jedi Temple,[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) Kenobi remembered Caleb Dume's suggestion that the signal could warn Jedi away;[[170]](#cite_note-A_New_Dawn-170) instead of disabling the Jedi recall signal,[[194]](#cite_note-Kanan_2-194) he changed it into a heartfelt holographic message of himself, warning any of the surviving Jedi to stay away from the Temple and the planet, to persevere for the future, and to trust in the Force.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)[[170]](#cite_note-A_New_Dawn-170) Copies of the message would persist and be seen by Jedi in hiding in the following years.[[195]](#cite_note-Spark_of_Rebellion-195)

 [![Kenobi watches a hologram of his one-time apprentice with Darth Sidious](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/Shock.png/revision/latest?cb=20130215045533) [![Kenobi watches a hologram of his one-time apprentice with Darth Sidious](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/Shock.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20130215045533)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/Shock.png/revision/latest?cb=20130215045533) 

Kenobi watches a hologram of his one-time apprentice with Darth Sidious

 

Desperate for answers and despite Yoda's warning that he would only find pain, Kenobi checked the security recordings to find that Skywalker had led his battalion of clones to attack the Temple, where he fought the Jedi & their Younglings and knelt to the newly-proclaimed [Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor"), who was proud of his [apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice"), now going by a new name—"Vader." Though Kenobi was horrified, Yoda determined that they had to destroy the Sith; Kenobi, however, refused to fight Vader and requested that he be sent to kill the Emperor instead, but Yoda vetoed the idea, claiming that Kenobi wasn't strong enough to go head-to-head with Sidious on his own. Kenobi expressed that Skywalker was like a brother to him and that he did not have the heart to kill him, but Yoda explained that the boy he had trained no longer existed and that he needed to be put out of his misery, and told Kenobi to use his instincts to find Vader.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

After that, he visited Senator Amidala, thinking she might know of Vader's location. He revealed what he'd discovered about Skywalker's betrayal of the Jedi and how the Clone Wars had been a lie orchestrated by Palpatine. Amidala harshly denounced Kenobi's accusations, believing that Obi-Wan intended to kill Anakin if she revealed where he'd gone. Correctly deducing that Anakin was the father of Amidala's child, knowing that the two had been together all that time, he apologized for everything wish he'd been supportive to them both and what he has no choice what he must do, as he left her apartment.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

#### Duel on Mustafar

:   "*You were the Chosen One! It was said that you would* destroy *the Sith, not* join *them! Bring balance to the Force, not leave it in darkness!*"  
    "*I HATE YOU!*"  
    "*You were my brother, Anakin. I* loved *you.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to the fallen Anakin Skywalker following their duel[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

Unbeknownst to Amidala, Kenobi stowed away in her star skiff, just as she and C-3PO departed for the [Mustafar system](/wiki/Mustafar_system "Mustafar system") to meet with Vader, who had already [killed](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar "Mission to Mustafar") the Separatist leaders taking refuge there. Hiding in one of the compartments, Kenobi emerged from the ship, only for Vader to think she had betrayed him and brought Kenobi to kill him, [choking](/wiki/Force_choke "Force choke") her in a paranoid rage. As Kenobi checked her vital signs, Vader accused him of turning her against him, but the Jedi Master stated Anakin betrayed her for himself and that his anger & lust for power had already done that, and that he had allowed Sidious to twist his mind becoming a Sith.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

 [![Kenobi battled his former apprentice in an intense and emotional duel](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/Kenobi_Vader_Mustafar.png/revision/latest?cb=20140322225501) [![Kenobi battled his former apprentice in an intense and emotional duel](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/Kenobi_Vader_Mustafar.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140322225501)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/Kenobi_Vader_Mustafar.png/revision/latest?cb=20140322225501) 

Kenobi battled his former apprentice in an intense and emotional duel

 

Unaffected by the Jedi's "lies" and unafraid of the dark side, Vader claimed that he'd brought peace, freedom, justice, and security to "[his] new Empire," and told Kenobi, who declared his allegiance was to the Republic and the democracy it represented, that if he was not on his side, then, he was his enemy. Realizing that his former apprentice was already too far gone to be reasoned with, Kenobi vowed to stop him at all costs, prompting the two to engage in a ferocious [duel](/wiki/Duel_on_Mustafar "Duel on Mustafar") that caused substantial damage to the facility, just as Yoda and Sidious [dueled](/wiki/Duel_in_the_Galactic_Senate "Duel in the Galactic Senate") in the Senate. Ultimately, Kenobi and Vader were hovering over the lava sea, when the Jedi Master reflected on his failure while Vader stated that he should have known about the Jedi's lust for power and domination. Kenobi tried again in vain to convince Vader to return to the light again and that Sidious was, in fact, an evil mastermind, but Vader continued to denounced the Jedi as the true evil.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

 [![Obi-Wan claimed the high ground in a pivotal move in his duel against Vader](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/ObiWanHighGround-RotS.png/revision/latest?cb=20231221231645) [![Obi-Wan claimed the high ground in a pivotal move in his duel against Vader](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/ObiWanHighGround-RotS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/276?cb=20231221231645)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/ObiWanHighGround-RotS.png/revision/latest?cb=20231221231645) 

Obi-Wan claimed the high ground in a pivotal move in his duel against Vader

 

Eventually, Kenobi jumped to high ground on the embankment of the lava river, gaining advantage over Vader. Despite Kenobi's warning not to try the jump, the Sith apprentice ignored him and did so anyway, allowing Kenobi to sever his remaining natural arm and both legs in one strike. Heartbroken over his former pupil's fall to the dark side, Kenobi retrieved Vader's lightsaber and tearfully expressed his disgust and sadness over Vader's betrayal of the Jedi Order, shouting that his destiny was to restore balance to the Force and defeat the Sith, not join them and leave the Force in darkness. Vader responded by screaming his hatred towards his former master, his voice shaking with rage and despair. This statement only further crushed Kenobi, who responded that he had loved him like a brother.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

Vader's garments then burst into flames from the lava, along with his sliced flesh, severely burning him. Unwilling to help his former friend or murder him in cold blood, Kenobi left him to his apparent fate and returned to Amidala's ship, where C-3PO had already brought her back on board. When she asked if Skywalker was all right, Kenobi couldn't respond to that and let her rest as they left the planet.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) Kenobi was left with the belief that his former apprentice had died, while thinking of how he's partly to blame for Anakin and Padme's relationship ending,[[196]](#cite_note-Kenobi_2-196) unaware of how the Emperor had arrived and saved his life by giving the new Sith Lord a [suit of life-support armor](/wiki/Darth_Vader%27s_armor "Darth Vader's armor").[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

#### Birth of the Skywalker twins

:   **GH-7**: "*Medically, she is completely healthy. For reasons we can't explain, we are losing her.*"
:   **Kenobi**: "*She's dying?*"
:   **GH-7**: "*We don't know why. She has lost the will to live. We need to operate quickly if we are to save the babies.*"
:   **Organa**: "*Babies?*"
:   **GH-7**: "*She's carrying twins.*"
:   ―GH-7 medical droid, Obi-Wan Kenobi and Bail Organa[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

 [![Kenobi during Amidala's final moments and the birth of the twins.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/Midwife_droid_1.png/revision/latest?cb=20130215034827) [![Kenobi during Amidala's final moments and the birth of the twins.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/Midwife_droid_1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20130215034827)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/Midwife_droid_1.png/revision/latest?cb=20130215034827) 

Kenobi during Amidala's final moments and the birth of the twins.

 

Just as the Emperor rescued Vader from the lava beach and gave him prosthetic limbs and the life-support suit, Kenobi, C-3PO, and R2-D2 took Amidala to [Polis Massa](/wiki/Polis_Massa "Polis Massa"). There, he, along with Bail Organa and Yoda, were informed that the dying Amidala was carrying twins. Kenobi was in the birthing room with Amidala as she gave birth to her two children, [Luke](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker") and [Leia](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo"). As she took her final breath, Amidala told Kenobi she knew there was still good in Skywalker.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

After arriving on Naboo so that [Amidala's funeral arrangements](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala%27s_funeral "Padmé Amidala's funeral") could be made, Yoda suggested that the children should be kept hidden and separated until the time was right: Organa would adopt Leia and take her to Alderaan as he and his wife, [Queen](/wiki/Alderaanian_monarchy "Alderaanian monarchy") [Breha](/wiki/Breha_Organa "Breha Organa"), had always talked about adopting a baby girl and promised that Leia would be loved. Kenobi volunteered to take Luke to Tatooine where the boy would live with Skywalker's step family, [Owen](/wiki/Owen_Lars "Owen Lars") and [Beru Lars](/wiki/Beru_Whitesun_Lars "Beru Whitesun Lars"). Kenobi also pledged that he would watch over him. As the trio prepared to go their separate ways, Yoda asked Kenobi to remain for a brief moment, revealing that he had training for him during his solitude on Tatooine and that Qui-Gon Jinn had reached the path to [immortality](/wiki/Immortality "Immortality"), having returned from the [Netherworld of the Force](/wiki/Netherworld_of_the_Force "Netherworld of the Force"). Yoda told Kenobi he would teach him on how to communicate with Jinn.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

#### Hiding on Tatooine

##### The beginning

:   "*And what of the boy?*"  
    "*To Tatooine. To his family, send him.*"  
    "*I will take the child and watch over him.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Yoda discuss the future of Luke Skywalker[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

 [![Kenobi giving Luke to Beru Lars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b1/DeliveringLuke-ROTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130207010946) [![Kenobi giving Luke to Beru Lars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b1/DeliveringLuke-ROTS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20130207010946)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b1/DeliveringLuke-ROTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130207010946) 

Kenobi giving Luke to Beru Lars.

 

Upon arriving on Tatooine, Kenobi purchased an [eopie](/wiki/Eopie "Eopie") he named [Akkani](/wiki/Akkani "Akkani"). While the twin suns set, Kenobi arrived at the [Lars moisture farm](/wiki/Lars_homestead "Lars homestead") to leave Luke with his uncle, Owen, and aunt, Beru.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) When he delivered Luke to them, Kenobi stood at the door, explaining what had happened and asking for their help.[[197]](#cite_note-Time_of_Death-197) Like Kenobi,[[196]](#cite_note-Kenobi_2-196) Owen believed his stepbrother had been killed and blamed the Jedi Master for his fate.[[198]](#cite_note-SW15-198) Owen agreed to the task of raising Luke, though he told Kenobi to play no role in his upbringing.[[197]](#cite_note-Time_of_Death-197) Fearing the boy would end up following his father's footsteps, Owen did not want the Jedi Master to see or train Luke,[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) so he told Kenobi to stay away and not speak to him, hoping that Luke would learn nothing of his father.[[197]](#cite_note-Time_of_Death-197)

After leaving them with Luke, Kenobi left on an Akkani, heading to his exile.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) He found a [home](/wiki/Ben_Kenobi%27s_home "Ben Kenobi's home") surrounded by [Western Dune Sea](/wiki/Western_Dune_Sea "Western Dune Sea").[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)[[4]](#cite_note-USW_NE-4) Kenobi had known immediately after finding this building, which was actually a long since abandoned prospector's hut, that it would serve him well.[[197]](#cite_note-Time_of_Death-197) Nonetheless, he instead set up living quarters in a [cave](/wiki/Ben_Kenobi%27s_cave "Ben Kenobi's cave"),[[199]](#cite_note-Kenobi_1-199) where he had little outside of a few necessities and keepsakes.[[6]](#cite_note-DoR:TVG-6) To conceal his identity, he would once again use the alias of "Ben Kenobi,"[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) as he had done with Satine Kryze[[30]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-30) and during the Clone Wars.[[132]](#cite_note-Deception-132) He also forfeited the use of his lightsaber for years.[[26]](#cite_note-SW7-26) He spent little time in the cities and kept to himself, spending most of his time watching over the young Skywalker, who he hoped to eventually train. However, to avoid becoming too recognizable, Kenobi worked temporary jobs, including that of a farmhand, a barback, a custodian, a [mechanic](/wiki/Technician "Technician"), and a laborer.[[6]](#cite_note-DoR:TVG-6)

Despite having taken the [Barash Vow](/wiki/Barash_Vow "Barash Vow"),[[40]](#cite_note-Family_at_War-40) he struggled to repress his sense of duty as a Jedi and spent years battling monotony and inactivity.[[26]](#cite_note-SW7-26) He was haunted by the horrific events of the Clone Wars, with no amount of soothing able to stop his recurring nightmares.[[6]](#cite_note-DoR:TVG-6) Over the course of his exile, he learned much about the noises and sights of Tatooine's wilds, including how to mimic the call of a [krayt dragon](/wiki/Krayt_dragon "Krayt dragon").[[200]](#cite_note-216_Nature-200) While Kenobi stayed on Tatooine to watch over Luke, the adopted parents of his twin, Leia, told her numerous stories of the Jedi Master during her youth. Over time, Leia came to cherish the memories of Bail Organa's Clone Wars adventures with Kenobi, regarding them as exciting and heroic,[[201]](#cite_note-LPOA-201) but she would not learn his name until she was ten.[[196]](#cite_note-Kenobi_2-196) Desperate to remain hidden, Kenobi buried his lightsaber, alongside Anakin's blade, in a box in the desert.[[199]](#cite_note-Kenobi_1-199) He also had [Qui-Gon Jinn's lightsaber](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn%27s_lightsaber "Qui-Gon Jinn's lightsaber") on-world.[[202]](#cite_note-Jedi_in_Hiding-202)

##### Sins of Skywalker

:   "*Don't destroy yourself to punish the Order for our failures! You're worth so much more than this!*"
:   ―What Obi-Wan Kenobi wished he had told Anakin Skywalker[[203]](#cite_note-POV_Story-203)

Within the first year of the [Age of the Empire](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era"), Kenobi visited the grave of [Shmi Skywalker Lars](/wiki/Shmi_Skywalker_Lars "Shmi Skywalker Lars"), mother of Anakin and spoke of how he was sad for what had happened to her once innocent and promising young son. During the early years of his exile, Kenobi began to meditate deeply on the force. On one of these occasions he began to experience visions of the past causing the Force spirit of Qui-Gon Jinn to counsel him to let go of his attachments.[[204]](#cite_note-Ahsoka-204) Kenobi came to wonder many times what would have happened if he had directly begged Anakin not to destroy himself for the Order's failings, yelling to his apprentice he was worth so much more.[[203]](#cite_note-POV_Story-203)

Unknown to Kenobi, who still believed his former Padawan to be dead,[[196]](#cite_note-Kenobi_2-196) Anakin carried on his path as the Sith Lord Darth Vader. During his attempt to [bleed](/wiki/Bleeding "Bleeding") the kyber crystal from [Kirak Infil'a's lightsaber](/wiki/Kirak_Infil%27a%27s_lightsaber "Kirak Infil'a's lightsaber"), the kyber crystal gave Vader a vision where Vader renounced the dark side, killed Darth Sidious, and then tracked down Kenobi to an unknown world, where he pleaded for forgiveness. However, Vader rejected the vision and remained on the path of the dark side,[[205]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_5-205) becoming obsessed with finding his former master and inflicting the pain he had received onto Kenobi.[[10]](#cite_note-Kenobi_3-10)

##### Protecting Luke Skywalker

:   "*We don't need your protection. We don't need you at all. I could have handled this alone.*"
:   ―Owen Lars, to Obi-Wan Kenobi[[197]](#cite_note-Time_of_Death-197)

 [![Obi-Wan Kenobi tried to hide his Jedi past as he worked to protect Luke Skywalker.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ce/ObiWanKenobi-NewsSlider.png/revision/latest?cb=20220210003048) [![Obi-Wan Kenobi tried to hide his Jedi past as he worked to protect Luke Skywalker.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ce/ObiWanKenobi-NewsSlider.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220210003048)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ce/ObiWanKenobi-NewsSlider.png/revision/latest?cb=20220210003048) 

Obi-Wan Kenobi tried to hide his Jedi past as he worked to protect Luke Skywalker.

 

On one particular morning, Kenobi was awoken by sensing a young 3-year-old Luke Skywalker and his family in danger. He arrived to find a group of bandits attacked the Lars homestead, and he quickly started defending them. After successfully defeating the last of the bandits, he was punched to the ground by Owen for his interference and his influence on Luke getting involved. Out of fear that the boy could become like his father, Owen shouted for Kenobi to never come back.[[197]](#cite_note-Time_of_Death-197)

Kenobi came to consider that morning the moment he had failed the young Skywalker. Both he and Owen had seen the defiance and bravery in the boy's eyes, yet Kenobi listened to Owen, staying away instead of training Luke.[[197]](#cite_note-Time_of_Death-197)

#### Hunted by the Inquisitorius

##### A simple life

:   "*What about the people that need us? What about the fight?*"  
    "*The fight is done. We lost.*"
:   ―Nari and Kenobi[[199]](#cite_note-Kenobi_1-199)

In [9 BBY](/wiki/9_BBY "9 BBY"),[[206]](#cite_note-KenobiDate-206) the Inquisitorius—including [the Grand Inquisitor](/wiki/The_Grand_Inquisitor "The Grand Inquisitor"), the [Fifth Brother](/wiki/Fifth_Brother "Fifth Brother"), and the [Third Sister](/wiki/Reva_Sevander "Reva Sevander")—arrived in Tatooine's Mos Eisley in search of a fugitive Jedi rumored to be hiding on the planet. By that same year, Kenobi had come to reside in a [cave](/wiki/Ben_Kenobi%27s_cave "Ben Kenobi's cave") in the Dune Sea desert. Working at[[199]](#cite_note-Kenobi_1-199) [Tibidon Station](/wiki/Tibidon_Station "Tibidon Station"),[[207]](#cite_note-Hasbro-207) a [sand whaling](/wiki/Tibidon_sand_whale "Tibidon sand whale") station, he rode a hovertrain into Anchorhead with his co-workers, continuing on his eopie[[199]](#cite_note-Kenobi_1-199) Akkani[[208]](#cite_note-Part_1_Guide-208) to his cave. One day, Kenobi was visited by the Jawa [Teeka](/wiki/Teeka "Teeka"), who presented the Jedi with several spare parts for a [toy T-16 skyhopper](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker%27s_T-16_skyhopper_model "Luke Skywalker's T-16 skyhopper model"). Teeka also offered to sell spare parts to Kenobi's malfunctioning moisture vaporator, but the Jedi realized that the Jawa had been stealing his parts and chastised Teeka. Before departing, the Jawa showed spare parts from an alleged Jedi starship that had crashed in the Dune Sea to Kenobi, who remarked that the Jedi were believed to be extinct.[[199]](#cite_note-Kenobi_1-199)

 [![Kenobi observes Luke at the Lars homestead.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/ISeeYouLuke-KenobiPartI.png/revision/latest?cb=20220703211518) [![Kenobi observes Luke at the Lars homestead.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/ISeeYouLuke-KenobiPartI.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220703211518)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/ISeeYouLuke-KenobiPartI.png/revision/latest?cb=20220703211518) 

Kenobi observes Luke at the Lars homestead.

 

That night, Kenobi was haunted in his [dreams](/wiki/Dream "Dream") by memories of Anakin Skywalker, Padmé Amidala, Qui-Gon Jinn, and Yoda. The following day, Kenobi rode his eopie to the Lars homestead, where he observed with macrobinoculars the young Luke Skywalker and Owen Lars from a distance. While riding his eopie through the desert the following night, Kenobi was confronted by the fugitive Jedi, a human male named [Nari](/wiki/Nari "Nari"), who had managed to escape the Inquisitors earlier and pleaded for the Jedi Master's help. However, Kenobi urged the Jedi to bury his [lightsaber](/wiki/Nari%27s_lightsaber "Nari's lightsaber") and flee, much to the disappointment of Nari, who still believed in the fight—which Kenobi believed to be over and lost.[[199]](#cite_note-Kenobi_1-199)

In Anchorhead, Kenobi met with Lars to hand over the toy parts he had acquired from Teeka earlier, but the farmer refused to accept the presents and asked Kenobi to stay away from his family. After arguing with Lars about the future of Skywalker, Kenobi hid nearby as the Fifth Brother and the Third Sister arrived to address the inhabitants regarding the fugitive Jedi they were looking for. The Third Sister took a particular liking to Lars and threatened to kill his family unless information about the fugitive was brought forward, but the farmer stayed quiet until the Fifth Brother intervened. Afterward, Kenobi thanked Lars for not revealing anything about him or his whereabouts.[[199]](#cite_note-Kenobi_1-199)

 [![Bail Organa's plea to rescue Leia prompted Kenobi to take up his lightsaber once again.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3b/ObiWanKenobi9BBY-CGSWG.png/revision/latest?cb=20250501235341) [![Bail Organa's plea to rescue Leia prompted Kenobi to take up his lightsaber once again.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3b/ObiWanKenobi9BBY-CGSWG.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20250501235341)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3b/ObiWanKenobi9BBY-CGSWG.png/revision/latest?cb=20250501235341) 

Bail Organa's plea to rescue Leia prompted Kenobi to take up his lightsaber once again.

 

Obsessed with finding Kenobi, the Third Sister plotted to lure out the fugitive Jedi Master and arranged for the [kidnapping of Leia Organa](/wiki/Ambush_on_Alderaan "Ambush on Alderaan") on Alderaan. As she suspected, Kenobi received a distress call from Bail and Breha Organa, who pleaded with the Jedi to help retrieve their daughter. However, Kenobi—intent on protecting Luke and believing himself to have been out of the game for too long—declined the request. Later, after witnessing the dead body of Nari in Anchorhead, Kenobi was visited in person by Bail Organa, who again pleaded with the Jedi to help him. After relenting, Kenobi retrieved his lightsaber from the desert and headed for a spaceport, where be boarded a freighter to depart Tatooine in a [commercial transport](/wiki/Unidentified_two-engined_passenger_transport "Unidentified two-engined passenger transport").[[199]](#cite_note-Kenobi_1-199)

##### Rescuing Leia Organa

:   "*You have no idea what I'm risking being here, Your Highness*"
:   ―Kenobi, to Leia Organa[[196]](#cite_note-Kenobi_2-196)

Arriving on [Daiyu](/wiki/Daiyu "Daiyu"),[[196]](#cite_note-Kenobi_2-196) the planet to where Bail had tracked the mercenaries who had kidnapped Leia,[[199]](#cite_note-Kenobi_1-199) Kenobi first encountered a [homeless veteran clone trooper](/wiki/Nax "Nax") and gave him some change, and then a female [spice dealer](/wiki/Spice_dealer "Spice dealer") named [Tetha Grig](/wiki/Tetha_Grig "Tetha Grig"). Eventually, [Jayco](/wiki/Jayco "Jayco"), a young boy, encouraged Kenobi to seek out [Haja Estree](/wiki/Haja_Estree "Haja Estree"), supposedly a Jedi who helped people, and took him to his lair, where Kenobi overheard Estree helping a mother and her Force-sensitive son, [Corran](/wiki/Corran "Corran"), by mind tricking a spaceport worker to let the two leave the planet. However, Kenobi correctly suspected that Estree was nothing more than a con artist and confronted him at gunpoint. Pressuring Estree into locating Leia, Kenobi was advised by the con artist to look in the Spice Den.[[196]](#cite_note-Kenobi_2-196)

 [![Kenobi sneaks around in the spice laboratory.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/KenobiOutplayed-KenobiPartII.png/revision/latest?cb=20220529162132) [![Kenobi sneaks around in the spice laboratory.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/KenobiOutplayed-KenobiPartII.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220529162132)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/KenobiOutplayed-KenobiPartII.png/revision/latest?cb=20220529162132) 

Kenobi sneaks around in the spice laboratory.

 

Infiltrating the [Spice](/wiki/Spice "Spice") Den in a stolen [cape](/wiki/Cape "Cape") and mask, Kenobi used the chaos brought on by the explosion of a small vat to steal a [keycard](/wiki/Keycard "Keycard") from an employee and access a closed-off area of the laboratory complex. Confronted by two employees, a Zabrak and a human, he managed to overpower both, before finding a room with a small human-like figure with a cloak. As Kenobi entered the room, [Vect Nokru](/wiki/Vect_Nokru "Vect Nokru")—who had kidnapped Leia from Alderaan—and two companions ambushed the Jedi, but he was able to defeat the trio with the help of a vial of red spice. Checking another room, Kenobi found Leia and told her he was sent by her father, Bail, to rescue her.[[196]](#cite_note-Kenobi_2-196)

As the two changed clothes to avoid detection and started making their way to a port on the other side of the city, the Third Sister arranged for Kenobi to be hunted by bounty hunters and criminals throughout the planet. However, Leia eventually became suspicious of Kenobi and his intentions, not believing him to be a real Jedi. After Kenobi knocked down a bounty hunter in pursuit, the two saw a hologram of the Jedi Master, leading Leia to believe that Kenobi lied to her and correctly deducing that the kidnappers used her as bait. As Leia tried to flee through the streets and to a rooftop, Kenobi attempted to catch her, only for the two to be ambushed by bounty hunters looking for the Jedi. As Kenobi returned fire, Leia attempted to make the jump to another building, but fell short; as the Jedi used his Force powers to stop her from falling to her death, Leia finally believed he was a real Jedi.[[196]](#cite_note-Kenobi_2-196)

 [![Kenobi prepares to confront the Third Sister.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/OlReliable-KenobiPartII.png/revision/latest?cb=20220529162718) [![Kenobi prepares to confront the Third Sister.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/OlReliable-KenobiPartII.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220529162718)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/OlReliable-KenobiPartII.png/revision/latest?cb=20220529162718) 

Kenobi prepares to confront the Third Sister.

 

Realizing the spaceport of Daiyu was closed for travel, Kenobi and Leia made their way to a cargo port on the recommendation of Estree, who confronted the two in an alleyway after having a change of heart. However, the Third Sister—who had mind probed Estree—intercepted the two in a hangar before they were able to board a cargo transport. Telling Leia to go for the transport, Kenobi prepared to confront the Third Sister, who informed him that he was to be taken to Lord Vader, only to realize that Kenobi was not aware of the fact that Vader survived their duel on Mustafar. Kenobi was horrified when she revealed Vader was indeed alive and has been hunting for him ever since. Before a confrontation could occur, however, The Grand Inquisitor arrived in the hangar and ordered the Third Sister to stand down; unwilling to let her superior take the credit for catching Kenobi, the Third Sister stabbed him while Kenobi used the ordeal to make his way to the cargo transport where Leia was waiting. As the transport departed, Kenobi was shaken by the revelation of Vader's survival.[[196]](#cite_note-Kenobi_2-196)

##### Arriving on Mapuzo

:   "*How does it work? The Force. What does it feel like?*"  
    "*Have you ever been afraid of the dark? How does it feel when you turn on the light?*"  
    "*I feel safe.*"  
    "*Yes, it feels like that.*"
:   ―Kenobi explains the nature of the Force to Leia[[10]](#cite_note-Kenobi_3-10)

 [![Kenobi and Leia make their way across Mapuzo.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ea/KenobiOrganaMapuzo-KenobiPartIII.png/revision/latest?cb=20220611234617) [![Kenobi and Leia make their way across Mapuzo.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ea/KenobiOrganaMapuzo-KenobiPartIII.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220611234617)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ea/KenobiOrganaMapuzo-KenobiPartIII.png/revision/latest?cb=20220611234617) 

Kenobi and Leia make their way across Mapuzo.

 

While cargo shuttle transported Kenobi and Organa to the planet [Mapuzo](/wiki/Mapuzo "Mapuzo"), the Jedi reflected on the news of his former apprentice's survival. As he repaired the princess' smashed [toy droid](/wiki/Toy_droid "Toy droid"), [Lola](/wiki/L0-LA59 "L0-LA59"), the two conversed about the nature of the Force, with Kenobi comparing it to the feeling of safety lights were turned on in a darkroom. After the shuttle landed on Mapuzo, Kenobi and Organa began traveling to a rendezvous point to meet a contact of Haja Estree. Walking across the barren desert planet, Kenobi told the princess of Mapuzo's past as a lush planet filled with life, before the age of the Empire. As the two continued toward the rendezvous point, Kenobi spotted a hooded figure on the horizon—a vision of Anakin Skywalker. To avoid attracting any unwanted attention, he fabricated a cover-up story, where the Jedi was a traveling farmer and the princess was his daughter.[[10]](#cite_note-Kenobi_3-10)

The two eventually reached the rendezvous point, but the contact was nowhere to be found. As they noticed a [vehicle](/wiki/FMR-385_cargo_speeder "FMR-385 cargo speeder") on the horizon, Organa waved it down despite Kenobi's protests. When the driver, [Freck](/wiki/Freck "Freck"), offered the two a ride to the nearest spaceport, Kenobi reluctantly followed Organa on the back of the vehicle. During the ride, Freck made conversation, revealing that he was a staunch supporter of the Empire; noticing a squad of stormtroopers, he pulled over and offered them a ride. The Imperial soldiers disclosed that they were searching for a nearby Jedi, and as they questioned Kenobi and Organa over their presence on Mapuzo, the Jedi accidentally used Organa's real name, instead of the fabricated name. However, Kenobi was able to cover up the mistake by claiming that his daughter reminded him of his late wife; satisfied with the explanation, the stormtroopers got off Freck's vehicle.[[10]](#cite_note-Kenobi_3-10)

 [![Kenobi shoots a stormtrooper attempting to use Organa as a human shield.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5e/MapuzoCheckpointShowdown-KenobiPartIII.png/revision/latest?cb=20220712044312) [![Kenobi shoots a stormtrooper attempting to use Organa as a human shield.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5e/MapuzoCheckpointShowdown-KenobiPartIII.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20220712044312)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5e/MapuzoCheckpointShowdown-KenobiPartIII.png/revision/latest?cb=20220712044312) 

Kenobi shoots a stormtrooper attempting to use Organa as a human shield.

 

After the close call, Kenobi was asked by the princess if he knew her actual mother or if he was her real father, with the Jedi denying both claims and telling Organa that he could barely remember his own family before his indoctrination into the Jedi Order. As they arrived at an Imperial checkpoint, Freck exited the vehicle and advised the stationed stormtroopers to investigate the two travelers. Asking Kenobi and Organa to step outside the vehicle, the stormtroopers called in a probe droid to perform a facial scan. Just as the probe droid identified Kenobi's face, he pulled out a blaster and quickly dispatched the droid and the stormtrooper squad before knocking Freck unconscious. Disabling the checkpoint barrier, a squad of stormtroopers led by [Imperial officer](/wiki/Imperial_officer "Imperial officer") [Tala Durith](/wiki/Tala_Durith "Tala Durith") intercepted the two—however, Durith killed the troopers, revealing herself to be Estree's contact.[[10]](#cite_note-Kenobi_3-10)

##### Rematch with Darth Vader

:   "*What have you become?*"  
    "*I am what you made me.*"
:   ―Kenobi and Darth Vader[[10]](#cite_note-Kenobi_3-10)

Durith brought Kenobi and Organa to a nearby [settlement](/wiki/Mapuzo_mining_village "Mapuzo mining village") and explained that they would have to wait several hours before one of her pilots could take them off-world. The trio sought shelter in Durith's workshop, where she revealed that she was working to help surviving Jedi and other Force-sensitives to escape the Empire as part of an underground organization called the [Hidden Path](/wiki/Hidden_Path "Hidden Path"). Kenobi was delighted to find that Quinlan Vos had passed through Durith's hideout at some point in the past. Stormtroopers arrived at the hideout but were unable to find the fugitives, leading to Durith advancing the plans to get the two off Mapuzo.[[10]](#cite_note-Kenobi_3-10)

 [![Darth Vader and Obi-Wan Kenobi duel again after ten years.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/81/ObiWanKenobi3-textless-cover.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250822073349) [![Darth Vader and Obi-Wan Kenobi duel again after ten years.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/81/ObiWanKenobi3-textless-cover.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20250822073349)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/81/ObiWanKenobi3-textless-cover.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250822073349) 

Darth Vader and Obi-Wan Kenobi duel again after ten years.

 

As they were about to leave for the spaceport, Kenobi felt a sudden disturbance in the Force: Darth Vader, accompanied by a contingent of Inquisitors and stormtroopers had arrived in the settlement after being alerted by the probe droid Kenobi had destroyed earlier. Hoping to draw out Kenobi, Vader walked through the town, terrorizing and killing civilians at random. Intending to distract Vader, Kenobi urged Durith to get Leia off-world and back to Alderaan. Fleeing into a nearby quarry, Kenobi wandered aimlessly until he was confronted by Vader, who ignited his lightsaber. The Jedi, however, ran deeper into the quarry without igniting his lightsaber, but he was again cut off by Vader.[[10]](#cite_note-Kenobi_3-10)

Fleeing once more, Kenobi was ambushed by the Sith Lord, and the Jedi engaged in a brief yet fierce duel with his old apprentice. Overpowered, Kenobi was forced back by Vader, who knocked over a container filled with flammable rocks. Thrown into the flames by Vader, Kenobi was dragged across the burning rocks before the Sith ordered a stormtrooper to seize the wounded Kenobi. However, before Kenobi was caught by the Empire, Durith, who was nearby watching the events unfold, shot the trooper and reignited the rocks. Blockaded by the sea of flames, Vader was unable to catch Kenobi, who managed to escape, albeit wounded, with Durith.[[10]](#cite_note-Kenobi_3-10)

##### Infiltrating the Fortress Inquisitorius

Following his rematch against his old apprentice, the barely-conscious Kenobi was taken by Durith to [Jabiim](/wiki/Jabiim "Jabiim"), one of the worlds where the Path helped move hunted Jedi to safety. He was submerged in a [bacta tank](/wiki/Bacta_tank "Bacta tank") tank to heal the burns on his upper body after Vader dragged him through the flames, but a mental link between he and Vader brought Kenobi back to consciousness. Durith took him to [Kawlan Roken](/wiki/Kawlan_Roken "Kawlan Roken"), one of the rebels helping Jedi and Force-sensitive individuals in the galaxy. Initially reluctant to help Kenobi [rescue the young Organa](/wiki/Rescue_of_Princess_Leia_(9_BBY) "Rescue of Princess Leia (9 BBY)"), Roken relented and assisted Kenobi in the operation. They used Durith's Imperial security clearance to fly to [Nur](/wiki/Nur "Nur"), a water moon in the Mustafar system, where the [Fortress Inquisitorius](/wiki/Fortress_Inquisitorius "Fortress Inquisitorius") was located. Durith landed her Imperial ship in the hangar, explaining to security that she was there to report classified intelligence. She then found a control room where she guided Kenobi in the stronghold via an underwater hatch.[[209]](#cite_note-Kenobi_4-209)

 [![Kenobi cuts down a stormtrooper during his mission to rescue Leia Organa.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/Kenobi-Skirmish_on_Nur.png/revision/latest?cb=20220714041141) [![Kenobi cuts down a stormtrooper during his mission to rescue Leia Organa.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/Kenobi-Skirmish_on_Nur.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20220714041141)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/Kenobi-Skirmish_on_Nur.png/revision/latest?cb=20220714041141) 

Kenobi cuts down a stormtrooper during his mission to rescue Leia Organa.

 

Once inside, Kenobi evaded [seeker droids](/wiki/Seeker_(droid) "Seeker (droid)") and stormtrooper patrols to eventually find Organa who was on the verge of torture at the hands of Third Sister. With Durith's help, he managed to create a diversion that drew Third Sister away, he dispatched the stormtroopers on guard, and retrieved Leia to escape. Rendezvousing with Durith, he donned a [gray](/wiki/Color "Color") Imperial [trench coat](/wiki/Jacket "Jacket") to blend in with the Imperial forces while they made their way back to the shuttle in the hangar. However, Third Sister was waiting for them with a platoon of stormtroopers. Vastly outmatched, the trio almost surrendered but [Sully](/wiki/Sully_Stark "Sully Stark") and [Wade](/wiki/Wade_Resselian "Wade Resselian") arrived in two [T-47 airspeeders](/wiki/T-47_airspeeder "T-47 airspeeder"), dispatching most of the Imperial ground forces in the hangar. Kenobi, Durith, and Organa boarded Sully's [airspeeder](/wiki/Airspeeder "Airspeeder"), though as they made their retreat Third Sister managed to destroy Wade's airspeeder, killing him. They arrived aboard Roken's ship and they departed Nur, mourning the death of Wade.[[209]](#cite_note-Kenobi_4-209)

After their departure, an infuriated Vader nearly killed Reva for disobeying his orders until she revealed that she planted a tracker that would lead them to Kenobi and the Path, revealing that she had modified Lola.[[209]](#cite_note-Kenobi_4-209)

##### The Siege of Jabiim

After arriving with Organa and Durith on Jabiim, Kenobi would reflect on a duel he had long ago with Skywalker when the latter was a padawan. Though Skywalker had been the stronger duelist and had skills to match his master's, Kenobi was still able to to defeat Skywalker because of his padawan's obsessive need to win. However, his thoughts on the matter were interrupted by an attack by Reva, now promoted to Grand Inquisitor, on the Path's base, locking their escape doors with Lola, which had been modified with a [restraining bolt](/wiki/Restraining_bolt "Restraining bolt") to make her obey the Inquisitor's commands. This began the [attack on Jabiim](/wiki/Attack_on_Jabiim "Attack on Jabiim"), as Reva and Vader's troops began bombarding the doors.[[51]](#cite_note-Kenobi_5-51)

To stall for time, Kenobi parlayed with Sevander, during which he was able to deduce her origin; she had been a padawan during the attack on the Jedi temple by Vader and the 501st, and had become an Inquisitor to hunt Vader down and kill him for his slaughter of her friends and fellow Jedi. She also revealed her hatred for Kenobi to be part of her quest for vengeance, as she believed he was to blame for Vader succumbing to the Dark side. As a result, she was distrustful of the Jedi Master as he was not at the Temple to help her and her "family" escape the massacre, and thus rejected his help, pointing out that the Dark Lord had been his own Padawan and asking why he did not stop him.[[51]](#cite_note-Kenobi_5-51)

After a brief but fierce exchange of fire between the Imperial troops and the members of the Path in which Kenobi fought beside the defenders, Kenobi was forced to watch as Durith sacrificed herself against the oncoming troops after explaining her reasons for turning against the Empire to help the Path after bering mortally wounded. Kenobi then decided to surrender with the intention of bringing Reva to Vader himself, asking her if she will let him slaughter more civilians, including children, and offered her the chance to stop him again. When asked if the Dark Lord would see it coming, the Jedi Master reassured her that he would be too fixated in settling the score with his former teacher to see her deception.[[51]](#cite_note-Kenobi_5-51)

Soon, Kenobi was able to escape with the Path and Organa, leaving Vader, who had just reached the fortress, behind, open to Sevander's attack. Playing upon Vader's desire to win the battle, he and the Path used an empty decoy ship to cover their escape. Vader predictably took the bait as Kenobi, Organa and the Path retreated into space. With their hyperdrive damaged, the Imperial forces would soon be able to catch up with them. Beyond this, Kenobi could sense something wrong, but was forced to put it aside for the time, unaware that Reva, after being defeated by Vader and mortally wounded, found his communicator with Bail Organa, and had learned of Luke's location on Tatooine.[[51]](#cite_note-Kenobi_5-51)

#### The Second Rematch

:   "*Anakin…*"  
    "*Anakin is gone. I am what remains.*"  
    "*I'm sorry. I'm sorry, Anakin. For all of it.*"  
    "*I am not your failure, Obi-Wan. You didn't kill Anakin Skywalker.* I *did. The same way, I will* destroy *you.*"  
    "*Then my friend is truly dead. Goodbye, Darth.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi says goodbye to Darth Vader[[210]](#cite_note-Kenobi_6-210)

 [![Darth Vader and Obi-Wan Kenobi dueled once more.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c1/DuelOnBarrenMoon-OWKpVI.png/revision/latest?cb=20220725003125) [![Darth Vader and Obi-Wan Kenobi dueled once more.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c1/DuelOnBarrenMoon-OWKpVI.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20220725003125)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c1/DuelOnBarrenMoon-OWKpVI.png/revision/latest?cb=20220725003125) 

Darth Vader and Obi-Wan Kenobi dueled once more.

 

With Vader aboard the *Devastator* as it pursued the Path's freighter, Kenobi knew that he would have to act in order to save the Path from the Sith lord's wrath. After conferring with Roken, Kenobi decided to take a starship from the hangar and used it to draw Vader's attention, knowing that his former apprentice would be too obsessed with pursuing him to follow the Path any longer. Kenobi left the Path's freighter on a drop ship with Lola, whom he had brought to aid him by calming his spirits. After landing in[[210]](#cite_note-Kenobi_6-210) the [dry lands](/wiki/Unidentified_barren_moon%27s_dry_lands "Unidentified barren moon's dry lands")[[211]](#cite_note-Iron_Vader_Sideshow-211) in an Imperial shuttle, Vader found Kenobi nearby and asked if he had come to destroy him. Kenobi replied that he will do as he must before igniting his lightsaber. Vader vowed that Kenobi would die and the two engaged in a lightsaber duel, with Vader utilizing a combination of one-handed and two-handed combat. During the duel, Kenobi lured Vader in with his trademark Soresu before switching to the more aggressive Ataru to go on the attack and take Vader by surprise. As the battle moved into the nearby[[210]](#cite_note-Kenobi_6-210) [labyrinth of rock pinnacles](/wiki/Labyrinth_of_rock_pinnacles "Labyrinth of rock pinnacles"),[[211]](#cite_note-Iron_Vader_Sideshow-211) Kenobi also attempted to collapse a pinnacle on Vader, who stopped it with the Force.
