Remarking that Kenobi's strength had returned since their last duel but that his weakness remained, Vader hurled the pinnacle at Kenobi before resuming their duel.[[210]](#cite_note-Kenobi_6-210)

Vader collapsed the ground beneath Kenobi and hurled rocks to keep him down there. Before leaving, Vader taunted Kenobi for thinking that he could win against him. However, Kenobi, drawing on his desire to protect Anakin's children, managed to break free and charged at Vader again. On the offensive, Kenobi used his superior use of Soresu and Ataru to overwhelm the Sith Lord before using the Force to hurl Vader against a rock. With Vader stunned, Kenobi then pummeled him with a maelstrom of stones, briefly overwhelming the Sith lord. Kenobi then resumed his lightsaber duel with Vader, critically damaging Vader's chest plate with multiple strikes from his lightsaber's pommel, pummeling him with a boulder, and slashing him across the back before pushing him back with the Force again, and then leaping at him, striking Vader's helmet with his lightsaber and revealing the scarred face of Anakin beneath. Horrified, Kenobi addressed him as Anakin Skywalker, prompting Vader to respond that Anakin was gone and that he was what that remained. Kenobi was visibly distraught and apologized to Anakin. Vader replied that he was not Kenobi's failure and that Kenobi did not kill Anakin: instead, Vader replied that he killed Anakin and vowed to destroy Kenobi as well.[[210]](#cite_note-Kenobi_6-210)

Kenobi responded that his friend was truly dead before bidding Vader, whom he simply called "Darth," farewell. As Kenobi left, Vader called out to him while trying to rise to his feet. As Kenobi fled off-world, he could sense Luke was in immediate danger and jumped into hyperspace towards Tatooine.[[210]](#cite_note-Kenobi_6-210)

#### Return to Tatooine

After arriving on Tatooine at the Lars homestead, Obi-Wan found Owen and Beru desperately searching for Luke, who had fled after Sevander, still badly wounded by her duel with Vader, had attacked the homestead, defeating both adults and chasing after Luke when he fled into the desert. Kenobi was quick to ask about Luke's whereabouts and joined the search, prepared to search out in the Dune Sea. Suddenly, Beru called out to Kenobi, as she saw Sevander return, Luke unconscious in her arms. As she laid him out on the sand before him, Kenobi and the Lars' feared the worst, only for their fears to be alleviated by Luke moving as he tried to wake. Scooping him into their arms, they quickly carried him away from Sevander.[[210]](#cite_note-Kenobi_6-210)

As Sevander broke down in tears, Kenobi approached, now assured she was no longer a threat. Stating that she tried to bring herself to kill the young Skywalker but could not, she broke down saying that she had failed all of her friends that Vader had murdered. Kenobi, kneeling beside her, told her she hadn't failed her fellow padawans, stating that through her mercy, she gave her deceased friends peace and honored them. When asked if she had become like Vader, Kenobi assured Sevander that through her refusal to commit any further to the dark side, she had redeemed herself and that who she decided to become was now her choice. Rising to her feet, Sevander abandoned her Inquisitor lightsaber, and was helped to stand by Kenobi, who stated they were both free from their grief before they parted ways. Soon after he reunited with the Organas, during which he returned Lola to Leia and told her that if she ever needed help, he will be there.[[210]](#cite_note-Kenobi_6-210)

After departing from his cave, Kenobi went to the Lars Homestead to speak with Owen. After being allowed to see the boy, Kenobi approached Luke with his customary greeting of "Hello there." Later, as Kenobi continued on through the Dune Sea, he finally saw the [Force Spirit](/wiki/Force_spirit "Force spirit") of his former master, Qui-Gon Jinn, appear to him. After Jinn revealed he had always been with his former Padawan, they ventured deeper into the Dune Sea together,[[210]](#cite_note-Kenobi_6-210) and Kenobi set up himself in the hut[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) he had found years prior.[[197]](#cite_note-Time_of_Death-197)

### Continued exile on Tatooine

#### The Journals of Ben Kenobi

 [![Kenobi saves a young Luke](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/65/BenKenobiSavesLuke-2015StarWars7.png/revision/latest?cb=20150729193801) [![Kenobi saves a young Luke](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/65/BenKenobiSavesLuke-2015StarWars7.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/208?cb=20150729193801)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/65/BenKenobiSavesLuke-2015StarWars7.png/revision/latest?cb=20150729193801) 

Kenobi saves a young Luke

 

In preparation for Luke's future training, Kenobi wrote a [set of journals](/wiki/The_Journals_of_Ben_Kenobi "The Journals of Ben Kenobi") and placed them in a box labeled "For Luke."[[212]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_6-212) In one of his journals, Kenobi wrote about how he stopped Jabba the Hutt's men from collecting their "[water tax](/wiki/Water_tax "Water tax")" on the local [farmers](/wiki/Moisture_farmer "Moisture farmer") during the [Great Drought](/wiki/Great_Drought "Great Drought"). He kept Jabba's thugs from extorting the Lars family into paying their water tax; following an action which involved subtle use of the Force to cause the thugs' firearms to misfire with the intention of preventing harm from coming to the townspeople, he decided not to go into town anymore.[[26]](#cite_note-SW7-26)

That same night, he sensed Skywalker to be in danger, for the boy had gone to take the water back from Jabba's men and give it back to the farmers. Kenobi went to the encounter, but blew their vehicle's lights with the Force to hide his identity and proceeded to disable all of Jabba's henchmen with the Force. One of them became startled and pushed Skywalker to the ground, causing him to hit his head and pass out. Once Kenobi handled all the thugs, he carried Skywalker to the Lars' homestead and left before he woke up. Luke's courage assured Kenobi that it wasn't the end of the Jedi and renewed his up-until-then waning hope.[[26]](#cite_note-SW7-26)

 [![Obi-Wan in exile](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/ForceCollection-Ben-Kenobi.png/revision/latest?cb=20230326153514) [![Obi-Wan in exile](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/ForceCollection-Ben-Kenobi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230326153514)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/ForceCollection-Ben-Kenobi.png/revision/latest?cb=20230326153514) 

Obi-Wan in exile

 

A year later the Great Drought had ended, and Kenobi found himself observing a young Luke piloting a [T-16 skyhopper](/wiki/T-16_skyhopper "T-16 skyhopper") through [Beggar's Canyon](/wiki/Beggar%27s_Canyon "Beggar's Canyon"). Kenobi noted how similar Luke was to his father Anakin, and expressed worry at the prospect. While attempting to impress his friends with an ostentatious maneuver through the canyon, Luke badly damaged the skyhopper and was subsequently grounded from flying by his uncle. Kenobi, feeling sympathy for the boy, took a job protecting a [Jawa](/wiki/Jawa "Jawa") [sandcrawler](/wiki/Sandcrawler "Sandcrawler") that had been experiencing troublesome raids by [Tusken Raiders](/wiki/Tusken_Raider "Tusken Raider"). That night, Kenobi meditated outside of the sandcrawler, communing with Qui-Gon and expressing his hope in Luke's abilities. Soon the Tusken Raiders arrived and Kenobi was able to easily dispatch the party with a disarmed raider's [Gaderffii stick](/wiki/Gaderffii_stick "Gaderffii stick"). He used whatever payment he earned from the job to hire the Jawas to deliver the necessary parts to fix the skyhopper. At a droid auction at an unidentified outpost, Luke received the the parts Kenobi had provided for him. Luke believed the parts had been a gift from his uncle and thanked Owen, as he eagerly rushed back home. Deriving pleasure from the boy's enthusiasm, Kenobi grinned fondly as he observed from behind a nearby tent.[[198]](#cite_note-SW15-198)

Later that day in his hut, Kenobi was cooking dinner when he was interrupted by a visit from Owen. Owen had put two and two together and sternly demanded that Kenobi have no part in his family's life. He had brought back the box of tools that he presumably confiscated from Luke, and dumped it on the floor of the hut. Kenobi responded back with several snarky replies before finally relenting and saying he that he only ever wanted to help. Owen continued to berate him, calling him dangerous and troublesome. As Owen departed, Kenobi regretfully admitted to himself that danger did in fact seem to follow him, remembering his confrontations with Count Dooku, General Grievous and Darth Maul. But he steeled his resolve and claimed that no danger would come to the young Skywalker boy as long as he lived. Coincidentally, Jabba the Hutt chose this time to send a Wookiee bounty hunter [Krrsantan](/wiki/Krrsantan "Krrsantan") after Owen, who he believed was responsible for roughing up his tax collectors during the Great Drought.[[198]](#cite_note-SW15-198)

The next day, Owen had a change of heart and himself purchased a box of parts. He searched through the Lars homestead looking for Luke, hoping to fix the skyhopper with the boy as a way to apologize for his coarse actions the previous day. However, he was ambushed by Black Krrsantan and kidnapped. Luke, in childish defiance, was running away from home. He made it a short distance out before sensing – likely through the Force – that something had gone awry at the homestead. Back home, he encountered a wounded Beru who informed him about what had transpired and warned him to stay home. She ran out of the house armed with a rifle, leaving Luke with the discarded pile of tools Owen had earlier dropped.[[213]](#cite_note-SW20-213)

 [![Black Krrsantan vs Obi-Wan Kenobi](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/Star_Wars_20_textless_cover.png/revision/latest?cb=20190118061401) [![Black Krrsantan vs Obi-Wan Kenobi](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/Star_Wars_20_textless_cover.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190118061401)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/Star_Wars_20_textless_cover.png/revision/latest?cb=20190118061401) 

Black Krrsantan vs Obi-Wan Kenobi

 

While meditating in the [Dune Sea](/wiki/Dune_Sea "Dune Sea") among a herd of [Banthas](/wiki/Bantha "Bantha"), Kenobi felt a disturbance in the Force. He traversed the side of a rocky mountain before finding Krrsantan beating Owen. In the ensuing conflict, Kenobi was trapped under a mesh of [stun net](/wiki/Stun_net "Stun net") that was dispatched by the Wookiee. Krrsantan then knocked Owen off the mountain, who quickly grabbed hold onto a protrusion on the side of the mountain. Kenobi escaped the net and stunned the Wookiee, sprinting over to Owen to grab him back up. However, Krrsantan intervened and threw an enormous boulder at Kenobi. Kenobi used his lightsaber to split the rock in two, also blinding Krrsantan in one eye during the process. The debris from the rock crashed into Owen's ledge and he nearly fell if not for Kenobi's use of the Force. Kenobi held Owen in place using the Force before losing focus as a result of Krrsantan's constant attacks. Owen fell, but was deftly saved by Luke, who used the repaired skyhopper's turret to break Owen's fall.[[213]](#cite_note-SW20-213)

Kenobi then used this opportunity to disarm the Wookiee, who plunged off the side of the mountain. He did not die, however, and proceeded off-world to escape Jabba's wrath. Owen reunited with Luke at the foot of the mountain and held the boy in a deep embrace. He cast a knowing glance up toward Kenobi who looked on in triumph. There were no words of thanks exchanged between Owen and Kenobi, but Kenobi was simply happy to see the family reunited. Kenobi then returned to his family, which was what he fondly called his herd of Banthas. Among them, he looked up into the sky to see Luke's skyhopper, soaring off into the sunset.[[213]](#cite_note-SW20-213)

Kenobi was later visiting [Mos Eisley](/wiki/Mos_Eisley "Mos Eisley") for supplies when he experienced a vision of a mysterious man. Kenobi recognized the man as [Garro](/wiki/Garro "Garro") from a tale Jedi Master Yoda had told him. He would go on to recount this in his journal.[[214]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_28-214)

#### Introducing himself once again

When Skywalker was twelve years old[[21]](#cite_note-Complete_Visual_New-21) in around [7 BBY](/wiki/7_BBY "7 BBY"),[[215]](#cite_note-WindyDate-215) he went on an adventure with his friend [Windy](/wiki/Windy "Windy"), riding a [dewback](/wiki/Dewback "Dewback"), but they soon encountered a [sandstorm](/wiki/Sandstorm "Sandstorm") and both lost consciousness. When Skywalker awoke, there was a krayt dragon nearby sneaking up on him. Just as the dragon attempted to attack, Kenobi, his hood over his face, appeared and beheaded the giant creature. When Skywalker asked who the hooded figure was, Kenobi answered that his name was "Ben Kenobi" and revealed that he was an old friend of Skywalker's father.[[216]](#cite_note-Line_Webtoon-216)

Kenobi took Skywalker and Windy back to their village, meeting with Skywalker's uncle, Owen Lars. Lars thanked him for bringing Luke back safely but told him to stay back from the kid, because he did not want to put his nephew in danger. In return, Kenobi said he was observing Skywalker and claimed that the Force was strong in him, telling Lars that he would leave the farm one day. Lars responded that the Jedi were done since the Republic had fallen, warning him once again to never visit their homestead again.[[216]](#cite_note-Line_Webtoon-216)

#### The knight and the dragon

:   "*Yet you have wronged the people of the town, for you have taken your pain and made it theirs. This too, shall cease, for if you ever raid the settlements of others, I shall learn of it, and I shall return with this dragon and your village shall be destroyed.*"
:   ―The knight to the Sand People[[217]](#cite_note-The_Knight_&_the_Dragon-217)

 [![The knight faces the dragon.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cf/The_Knight_and_the_Dragon_SWMaF.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200402010841) [![The knight faces the dragon.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cf/The_Knight_and_the_Dragon_SWMaF.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20200402010841)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cf/The_Knight_and_the_Dragon_SWMaF.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200402010841) 

The knight faces the dragon.

 

At some point in time, a story was spread on Tatooine of an altruistic knight, once a mighty warrior who had made the desert his home while guarding a treasure in solitude. The knight learned of the actions of a tribe of Sand People that had been raiding other settlements and capturing prisoners. Following one of these raiding parties back to their village, he learned that their actions were motivated by a desire for self-preservation due to the carnivorous demands of a dragon known as [Krayt](/wiki/Krayt "Krayt"). Upon being discovered, the knight was held in captivity with the others which gave him the opportunity to break out all of the other prisoners while he stayed behind. Angered by his actions, the nomadic tribe placed him in view of the dragon, offering him up in sacrifice. Slipping free of his bonds, the knight produced a glowing sword of light which he used to hold back the flying dragon for a time.[[217]](#cite_note-The_Knight_&_the_Dragon-217)

For more than an hour, he and the dragon engaged in a sort of dance, with neither one able to wound the other. Finally, the dragon sensed an opening when the knight seemed to tire. Just as the dragon was about to pounce, the knight held up his hand which seemed to put the dragon under a pacifying spell. Upon seeing the knight exercise control upon the creature, the nomads cheered. The knight, however, chastised them for their actions. He stated that while the dragon would no longer bother them, any whisper of wrongdoing from their end would lead to him and the dragon returning to punish them. The knight thus led the dragon away, never to be seen again. His actions eventually led to the nomadic tribe forever ceasing any attempts to raid or kidnap from other settlements, a trait which became unique to them.[[217]](#cite_note-The_Knight_&_the_Dragon-217)

#### The Oil-Bringer and aid to needy

At some point, Kenobi took actions to aid and repair the droids of Tatooine. His efforts resulted in his earning the moniker Oil-Bringer. Tales passed around said that his heroics took place on a single night once a year, and that he traversed the entire galaxy. Kenobi rescued one such droid, LA-R1, and its companions from the clutches of Jawas. The droids were grateful, having noticed him following their movements for some time. LA-R1, upon meeting Kenobi, felt that he matched the description of the Oil-Bringer legends.[[218]](#cite_note-LDT_AOH-218) At some point after, he escorted a lost Tusken home, out of compassion.[[219]](#cite_note-SandProvide-219)

On another occasion, Kenobi witnessed an individual being chased by a wild Massiff and used the force to calm it down. The individual would get extra supplies from [Bestine](/wiki/Bestine_(city) "Bestine (city)") for Kenobi who they referred to as an "Old Hermit". They later recounted the tale to a gambler in the [Bestine Cantina](/wiki/Bestine_Cantina "Bestine Cantina")[[220]](#cite_note-Outlaws-220) in [3 ABY](/wiki/3_ABY "3 ABY")[[221]](#cite_note-OutlawsDate-221). Also noting that they had not seen him in a couple of [cycles](/wiki/Cycle "Cycle") and hoping that he was alright.[[220]](#cite_note-Outlaws-220)

#### Encountering Maul

:   "*Look what has become of you. A rat in the desert.*"  
    "*Look what I've risen above.*"
:   ―Maul and Obi-Wan Kenobi[[222]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-222)

 [![Kenobi, before the arrival of his old enemy](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/84/Twin_Suns_thumb.png/revision/latest?cb=20170319040232) [![Kenobi, before the arrival of his old enemy](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/84/Twin_Suns_thumb.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20170319040232)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/84/Twin_Suns_thumb.png/revision/latest?cb=20170319040232) 

Kenobi, before the arrival of his old enemy

 

In [2 BBY](/wiki/2_BBY "2 BBY"),[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) Maul [arrived](/wiki/Mission_to_Tatooine_(Imperial_Era) "Mission to Tatooine (Imperial Era)") on Tatooine in search of Kenobi, following his vision of the twin suns. Kenobi managed to keep Maul from tracking him until Maul used a [Sith holocron](/wiki/Sith_holocron "Sith holocron") to lure [Rebel](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic") Padawan [Ezra Bridger](/wiki/Ezra_Bridger "Ezra Bridger") from his base on the planet [Atollon](/wiki/Atollon "Atollon") to Tatooine, hoping the young Jedi's pain would be enough to draw Kenobi out. Kenobi found Ezra unconscious in the Dune Sea and sheltered him from the storm. Ezra regained consciousness and, knowing of Maul's hatred towards Kenobi from his own encounters with the former Sith, tried to warn Obi-Wan of Maul's presence. Kenobi calmly replied that he knew of it already and that he hadn't gone into hiding unprepared. He told Ezra that it was Ezra's responsibility to help the Rebellion; not to handle Maul. That burden fell upon Kenobi himself.[[222]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-222)

 [![Kenobi duels his old foe Maul one last time](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bb/Bitter_Rivalry_AtG.png/revision/latest?cb=20181124201733) [![Kenobi duels his old foe Maul one last time](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bb/Bitter_Rivalry_AtG.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20181124201733)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bb/Bitter_Rivalry_AtG.png/revision/latest?cb=20181124201733) 

Kenobi duels his old foe Maul one last time

 

Soon thereafter Maul arrived, seething with rage upon seeing his old rival after so many years. Kenobi sent Bridger off on a dewback toward [Maul's ship](/wiki/Nightbrother_(Gauntlet_fighter) "Nightbrother (Gauntlet fighter)"), which Bridger would use to fly back to Atollon. Maul mocked Kenobi's lackluster living conditions, and wondered out loud whether it would be crueler to simply leave Kenobi to what Maul believed was a life of misery and squalor. But rather than responding with mockery in turn, as he might have in his younger years, Kenobi calmly and succinctly explained to Maul that because he defined himself by his empty desires to kill, possess, and dominate, the former Sith Lord had nothing at all.[[222]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-222)

This infuriated Maul, who ignited one of the blades of his saberstaff and struck the ground in front of Kenobi's small campfire, showering it with sand and putting it out. Maul questioned on his old nemesis's reasons for being on Tatooine, noting it wasn't simply to hide. He then began to speculate, quickly coming to the conclusion that Kenobi was there to protect someone. Stirred to action by the threat of Maul to Luke, Kenobi ignited his lightsaber and assumed his traditional Soresu ready stance. As Maul tightened his grip on his own saber and ignited his second blade, Kenobi shifted his stance to the one used by his old master Qui-Gon during the duel on Naboo in the [Theed power generator](/wiki/Theed_power_generator "Theed power generator").[[222]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-222)

 [![Maul dies in Kenobi's arms](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/Maul_dies_but_for_real_this_time.png/revision/latest?cb=20170319062616) [![Maul dies in Kenobi's arms](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/Maul_dies_but_for_real_this_time.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20170319062616)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/Maul_dies_but_for_real_this_time.png/revision/latest?cb=20170319062616) 

Maul dies in Kenobi's arms

 

Maul noted Kenobi's change in stance and after a few tense moments, attacked. He crossed blades with Kenobi twice before attempting to hit him with the same hilt-strike that had allowed him to kill Qui-Gon. However, Kenobi had evidently anticipated this, and he struck down at Maul's hilt as Maul struck upwards, bisecting Maul's lightsaber and carving a lethal laceration into the former Sith Lord's chest. Maul dropped his ruined weapon and collapsed to one knee, but Kenobi caught him before he could fall to the ground and held him. As Maul laid dying, he asked Kenobi whether the person whom he was protecting was the Chosen One; the one prophesied to destroy the Sith. Kenobi, who at that point believed that Vader would never turn from the dark side, replied that he was. Maul appeared to take some modicum of comfort from this knowledge, seemingly certain that he and Kenobi would ultimately be avenged.[[222]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-222)

Kenobi then traveled via dewback to the Lars' Homestead. Upon arriving there, he heard Beru Whitesun Lars calling to Luke and saw the teenager running back home against a binary sunset. Following the former Sith's death,[[222]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-222) Kenobi built a funeral pyre for Maul, honoring his old rival.[[197]](#cite_note-Time_of_Death-197)

#### Final days on Tatooine

:   "*I feel my time here may be drawing to an end. For these long and desolate years I have often felt alone. But truthfully… I never have been.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, in his journal[[223]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_5-223)

Shortly before the [Battle of Scarif](/wiki/Battle_of_Scarif "Battle of Scarif"), Kenobi wrote a set of journals, recounting his service to the Jedi Order as well as the Republic during the time of the Clone Wars and prior, in order to pass the time whilst a storm occoured on Tatooine. During his final days on the planet, Kenobi encountered and rescued an injured stormtrooper named [JM-909](/wiki/JM-909 "JM-909"), whom he nicknamed Jim, before bringing him to his hut. Jim eventually escaped, but remembered Kenobi's actions after being scolded by his superior officer upon returning to the Empire. Following this, Kenobi stated that he knew his time on the planet was coming to an end, and that despite having felt alone for so many years, he came to realise that he never had been.[[223]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_5-223)

### Galactic Civil War

#### Coming out of exile

:   "*We will need every advantage.*"  
    "*Your friend... the Jedi?*"  
    "*He served me well during the Clone Wars, but has lived in hiding since the Emperor's purge. Yes, I will send for him.*"
:   ―Bail Organa and Mon Mothma talk about the possibility of recruiting Kenobi to the Alliance[[224]](#cite_note-Rogue_One-224)

 [!["Ben" Kenobi during his last years in exile.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0b/Ben_Kenobi.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110307195133) [!["Ben" Kenobi during his last years in exile.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0b/Ben_Kenobi.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/154?cb=20110307195133)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0b/Ben_Kenobi.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110307195133) 

"Ben" Kenobi during his last years in exile.

 

As the Alliance to Restore the Republic foresaw [open war](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War") with the Empire becoming more of a possibility, they decided to take every advantage. Shortly before the [Battle of Scarif](/wiki/Battle_of_Scarif "Battle of Scarif"), in [1 BBY](/wiki/1_BBY "1 BBY"), Kenobi's old friend Bail Organa, who, by this point, was a high-ranking leader within the Alliance, decided to recruit the exiled Jedi Master to their cause at [Chancellor](/wiki/Chancellor_(Rebel_Alliance) "Chancellor (Rebel Alliance)") [Mon Mothma](/wiki/Mon_Mothma "Mon Mothma")'s urging.[[224]](#cite_note-Rogue_One-224) Unable to attend to it in person[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) because he had to travel to Alderaan to warn his people of the coming war,[[224]](#cite_note-Rogue_One-224) Organa sent his daughter Princess Leia Organa to request Kenobi's help.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) Barely escaping from the battle that had just taken place at [Scarif](/wiki/Scarif "Scarif") after having recovered the [schematics](/wiki/Death_Star_plans "Death Star plans") for the Empire's planet-destroying [Death Star](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station"),[[224]](#cite_note-Rogue_One-224) she was captured in a [battle](/wiki/Secret_mission_to_Tatooine "Secret mission to Tatooine") over Tatooine. Leia transferred the plans into R2-D2's memory systems and sent the droid off to find Kenobi, leading R2-D2 and C-3PO on a crusade that led them to be captured by a band of Jawas and being sold to Owen Lars and Luke Skywalker.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

However, R2-D2 ran off from the Lars homestead and off into the Jundland Wastes to try and find Kenobi. C-3PO, who was unaware of the mission given to R2-D2 by Princess Leia, encouraged Skywalker to go after the wayward astromech droid, but, before they could return to the homestead, they were attacked by a group of Tusken Raiders. It was at that moment when Kenobi showed up on the scene and scared the Tusken Raiders off[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) by imitating the cry of a krayt dragon.[[200]](#cite_note-216_Nature-200) Upon turning to see where the call had come from, the Tuskens saw Kenobi and remembered [Chieftain](/wiki/Chief "Chief") [A'Yark](/wiki/A%27Yark "A'Yark") had warned them of a mysterious "[shaman](/wiki/Shaman "Shaman")" who lived in the area. Remembering their chieftain's warnings, they quickly fled, although the young Tusken [A'Koba](/wiki/A%27Koba "A'Koba") intended to return in greater numbers to finally hunt down the hooded figure.[[225]](#cite_note-Rites-225) Indeed, Kenobi knew the Tuskens were likely to return in greater numbers if they stayed in the canyon for too long, meaning he had to awaken Skywalker but also lead him to safety.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

With the Tuskens gone, Kenobi approached the unconscious Skywalker and checked that he was still alive before greeting R2-D2.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) However, Kenobi acted as though he did not know the droid for Luke's benefit.[[226]](#cite_note-ANH:TP,tS,atFB-226) Restoring Skywalker to consciousness, the boy told him that R2-D2 was looking for someone named "Obi-Wan Kenobi," to which Kenobi replied that was, in fact, his real name. To avoid more Tusken Raider attacks, Kenobi brought the two droids and the farm boy to his home. There, Kenobi revealed that he had known Skywalker's father, and that he'd been a Jedi Knight during the Clone Wars, choosing to talk about him before his turn to the Dark Side.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

 [![Kenobi watches Leia's message.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e1/Leias_message.png/revision/latest?cb=20200915071603) [![Kenobi watches Leia's message.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e1/Leias_message.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/299?cb=20200915071603)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e1/Leias_message.png/revision/latest?cb=20200915071603) 

Kenobi watches Leia's message.

 

He then gave Skywalker his father's lightsaber, which he claimed that Anakin would have wanted Luke to have it. When Luke asked about how his father had died, Kenobi was careful not to tell him that Anakin Skywalker and Darth Vader were one and the same; instead he twisted the truth, claiming that Vader, his former apprentice, had fallen to the dark side of the Force and helped the Empire hunt down and kill the Jedi, including Anakin. Though he wasn't technically lying to Luke - the man who Anakin Skywalker had been had died when he became Darth Vader - he wasn't being directly truthful either, and Luke would not learn the whole truth for another several years. Afterward, Luke decided to show Kenobi the partial message from Leia Organa. The message finally played in its entirety, stating her father's request for him to aid the Alliance and that R2-D2 contained information vital to the survival of the Alliance. After the message concluded, Kenobi requested Skywalker's help to see the mission through and learn the ways of the Force, but Skywalker refused to get involved as he believed his duties at home were more important, but he offered to take Kenobi as far as [Anchorhead](/wiki/Anchorhead "Anchorhead").[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) At the age of 57, and after more than nineteen years of exile, Kenobi was done hiding and being cautious, regardless of Luke's answer he needed to leave Tatooine and confront the Empire by aiding the princess who had begged for his help.[[40]](#cite_note-Family_at_War-40)

On their way to the city, the two came across the skiff that had sold R2-D2 and C-3PO to Skywalker and his uncle; it had been destroyed and the Jawas had been killed. Initially believing it to be the casualty of another Tusken Raider attack, Kenobi correctly deduced that the attack was, in fact, the work of [stormtroopers](/wiki/Stormtrooper "Stormtrooper") who were searching for the droids. Worried that the stormtroopers may have gone after his aunt and uncle next, Skywalker headed back home despite Kenobi's claims that it was too dangerous. While Skywalker discovered that the Imperials had attacked the homestead and killed both Owen and Beru, Kenobi arranged a small funeral pyre for all the Jawas killed by the Empire's soldiers.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

At this time that, Kenobi was met by the Force Ghost of Jinn. Kenobi's old master helped ease his anxieties about Luke, specifically his fear that Luke would suffer a tragic fate such as Anakin's. Qui-Gon marveled at how Obi-Wan had remained so steadfast and resilient after suffering through years of war and losing everyone he ever truly loved to a terrible end: Anakin, Satine, Padmé, and Jinn himself. Qui-Gon reassured Kenobi that he was making the right decisions with Luke. Sensing that Luke was returning from the remains of the Lars homestead, Qui-Gon bade his former student farewell and told him that they would see each other again, though kept to himself that Obi-Wan only had a short time to live.[[22]](#cite_note-Master_and_Apprentice-22) When Skywalker returned, the young man agreed to go with him to Alderaan and be trained as a Jedi.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

#### Leaving Tatooine

:   "*If his ship is as fast as his boasting, we ought to do well.*"
:   ―Kenobi regarding Han Solo and the *Millennium Falcon*[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

The four ventured out to Mos Eisley and to pay a visit to [Chalmun's Spaceport Cantina](/wiki/Chalmun%27s_Spaceport_Cantina "Chalmun's Spaceport Cantina")[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)—a place Kenobi had made rare visits to throughout his exile[[227]](#cite_note-theirkind-227)—in hopes of recruiting a pilot that could take them to Alderaan. During their journey,[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) they were stopped by stormtrooper [Foot Patrol 7](/wiki/Foot_Patrol_7 "Foot Patrol 7"), as Commander [TD-110](/wiki/Wanten "Wanten") had spotted R2 and 3PO and thought they could be the droids they needed. One of his subordinates, trooper [TD-7556](/wiki/Sardis_Ramsin "Sardis Ramsin"), privately disagreed, thinking that the boy and whom he assumed to be his grandfather would never be chosen by the Rebel Alliance to protect their secrets.[[228]](#cite_note-Born_in_the_Storm-228) Claiming that he and Skywalker had owned the droids for several seasons, Kenobi used a mind trick to ensure the stormtroopers did not check for identification and to ensure they could move along.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) The trick worked, with it even making TD-7556 believe Kenobi had been an Imperial.[[228]](#cite_note-Born_in_the_Storm-228) TD-110, meanwhile, was eventually left with an awful headache from the trick.[[229]](#cite_note-Bump-229)

Explaining to Skywalker that he had used the Force to ensure they made it past Foot Patrol 7, the four made their way to the cantina. Skywalker was skeptical about the prospect of finding a pilot in the cantina, but Kenobi assured him that the best pilots could usually be found there, but warned him that the cantina could "be a little rough." They ran into a small bout of trouble when a pair of wanted criminals, [Cornelius Evazan](/wiki/Cornelius_Evazan "Cornelius Evazan") and [Ponda Baba](/wiki/Ponda_Baba "Ponda Baba"), began bullying Skywalker, but Kenobi was able to defuse the situation when he sliced off Baba's arm in defense of the young man.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) Although the patrons began to whisper of the lightsaber,[[228]](#cite_note-Born_in_the_Storm-228) Kenobi continued with his business of looking for transport.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

 [![Kenobi barters with Han Solo for passage off Tatooine.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bd/NoQuestionsAsked-AtG_Romana_Kendelic.png/revision/latest?cb=20200909234745) [![Kenobi barters with Han Solo for passage off Tatooine.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bd/NoQuestionsAsked-AtG_Romana_Kendelic.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200909234745)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bd/NoQuestionsAsked-AtG_Romana_Kendelic.png/revision/latest?cb=20200909234745) 

Kenobi barters with Han Solo for passage off Tatooine.

 

Kenobi soon met a Wookiee named [Chewbacca](/wiki/Chewbacca "Chewbacca"), who served as the first mate aboard a [freighter](/wiki/Freighter "Freighter") known as the *[Millennium Falcon](/wiki/Millennium_Falcon "Millennium Falcon")*, which was captained by a [Corellian](/wiki/Corellia "Corellia") [smuggler](/wiki/Smuggler "Smuggler") named [Han Solo](/wiki/Han_Solo "Han Solo"). Solo boasted about his ship's speed to entice Kenobi. Though Solo's initial rate was 10,000 [credits](/wiki/Galactic_Credit_Standard "Galactic Credit Standard") all paid in advance, Kenobi was able to compromise: offering to pay 2,000 credits upfront, with an additional 15,000 when they got to Alderaan, for a total of 17,000 credits. Solo was convinced and agreed to take them to Alderaan. Kenobi and Skywalker then exited the cantina when they saw stormtroopers,[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) actually the very same troops Kenobi had mind tricked,[[228]](#cite_note-Born_in_the_Storm-228) who had entered to investigate the earlier disturbance caused when Baba lost his arm. Having been saved by Jedi during the Clone Wars, [Wuher](/wiki/Wuher "Wuher")—the cantina bartender who had previously written Kenobi off as an old hermit—chose to lie to the soldiers, keeping the Jedi's presence a secret.[[227]](#cite_note-theirkind-227)

As they departed, the two were confronted by another [stormtrooper](/wiki/Unidentified_stormtrooper_(Mos_Eisley) "Unidentified stormtrooper (Mos Eisley)"), who demanded to see their identification. In response, Kenobi cut the trooper's blaster and killed the soldier by throwing pieces of metal at them with the Force. Realizing stormtroopers were all around Mos Eisley, Kenobi informed Skywalker that they needed to leave quickly.[[216]](#cite_note-Line_Webtoon-216) However, they had been spotted by an Imperial [spy](/wiki/Spy "Spy") named [Garindan ezz Zavor](/wiki/Garindan_ezz_Zavor "Garindan ezz Zavor"), who had entered the cantina after hearing Baba and Kenobi's fight, enabling the [Kubaz](/wiki/Kubaz "Kubaz") spy to overhear Kenobi's discussion with Solo. Waiting until he could see Kenobi and Skywalker with the droids,[[230]](#cite_note-The_Secrets_of_Long_Snoot-230) Zavor notified Imperial stormtroopers of their location[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) at [Docking Bay 94](/wiki/Docking_Bay_94 "Docking Bay 94").[[230]](#cite_note-The_Secrets_of_Long_Snoot-230) Fortunately, the *Millennium Falcon* was able to escape Tatooine.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) As Solo checked his ship's controls, Kenobi assured R2-D2 that he still remembered him and commented that it was good to fly with him again.[[226]](#cite_note-ANH:TP,tS,atFB-226)

As they waited for the *Falcon* to arrive at Alderaan, Kenobi arranged an exercise for Skywalker so that he would learned how to sense through the Force and deflect blaster fire from a [training remote](/wiki/Marksman-H_training_remote "Marksman-H training remote"), when the Jedi Master sensed a [disturbance in the Force](/wiki/Disturbance_in_the_Force "Disturbance in the Force") caused by [the Disaster](/wiki/Destruction_of_Alderaan "Destruction of Alderaan"). Soon enough, the *Falcon* exited hyperspace, and they discovered that the planet had been destroyed and replaced by an [asteroid](/wiki/Asteroid "Asteroid") [field](/wiki/Asteroid_field "Asteroid field"). As a [TIE fighter](/wiki/TIE/ln_space_superiority_starfighter "TIE/ln space superiority starfighter") approached them, Solo decided to shoot the small ship, but Skywalker noticed that the ship was coming from what, at first, seemed like a small moon - the Death Star. As the space station's tractor beam pulled them in, Kenobi told Solo not to resist, saying there were alternatives to fighting.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

#### Duel on the Death Star and death

:   "*You can't win, Darth. If you strike me down, I shall become more powerful than you can possibly imagine.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi to Darth Vader — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4d/YouCantWinDarth-ANH.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250410001853)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:YouCantWinDarth-ANH.flac "File:YouCantWinDarth-ANH.flac"))[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

 [![Kenobi duels his former apprentice.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/66/Jotr-macewindu-2-40thvariant.png/revision/latest?cb=20190118021729) [![Kenobi duels his former apprentice.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/66/Jotr-macewindu-2-40thvariant.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190118021729)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/66/Jotr-macewindu-2-40thvariant.png/revision/latest?cb=20190118021729) 

Kenobi duels his former apprentice.

 

As the *Millennium Falcon* was forced to land on Bay 327, Solo prompted everyone to hide on the ship's sensor-proof smuggling compartments, with Kenobi hiding alongside the two droids, to trick the Imperials into thinking they had abandoned the ship. As the Imperial scouts got off the ship, Kenobi told Solo he would take care of the tractor beam, which prompted Solo to call him a "damn fool"; soon enough, with Skywalker and Solo disguised as stormtroopers, they took control of the hangar's control room, where Kenobi learned the location of a terminal that, should one cut its power, it would allow the ship to leave. He decided to go alone, despite Skywalker's protest, to whom he told that his destiny lay on a different path than his own, and reassured Skywalker that the Force would be with him always.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

As Skywalker, Solo and Chewbacca learned of Organa's presence on the station and set out to [rescue](/wiki/Rescue_of_Princess_Leia "Rescue of Princess Leia") her, Kenobi managed to disable the tractor beam; however, as he made his way to the *Falcon*, he encountered Vader and the two engaged in one final duel. Vader claimed to be the true master of the Force, but Kenobi,[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) refusing to use Anakin's name and instead simply calling Vader "[Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth"),"[[197]](#cite_note-Time_of_Death-197) instead claimed that he was only a "master of evil." During the duel, Vader noted that his age had made him weak, but Kenobi told his former apprentice that he wouldn't win because he would become more powerful than Vader could ever imagine, even if he managed to kill him.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

 [![Kenobi is struck down by Darth Vader.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/11/Vaderstrike.png/revision/latest?cb=20201008105354) [![Kenobi is struck down by Darth Vader.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/11/Vaderstrike.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/222?cb=20201008105354)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/11/Vaderstrike.png/revision/latest?cb=20201008105354) 

Kenobi is struck down by Darth Vader.

 

The two made their way to Bay 327 just as the team reunited to board the *Falcon*, only for Kenobi to see the young Skywalker and give Vader a mysteriously knowing smile. As he raised his blade in surrender and took a deep breath, Vader struck him down and his body disappeared, for he had become one with the Force,[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) with only his Jedi robes and lightsaber left behind on the Death Star.[[231]](#cite_note-Remnants_of_Kenobi-231) Unable to attend to the body of his master, Skywalker was forced to escape on the *Falcon* with everyone else. Vader, meanwhile, stomped upon his former mentor's cloak[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) and collected his lightsaber.[[231]](#cite_note-Remnants_of_Kenobi-231)

### Post-mortem

#### Communion with Luke Skywalker

##### Ensuring the future

:   "*Remember… The Force will be with you. Always.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to Luke Skywalker — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4f/TheForceWillBeWithYouAlways.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250410001839)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:TheForceWillBeWithYouAlways.flac "File:TheForceWillBeWithYouAlways.flac"))[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

Kenobi's communion with Qui-Gon was successful as Kenobi did not vanish completely but instead became a Force spirit. As he did, he felt past, present, future collide, seeing the eventual [death of Solo](/wiki/Battle_of_Starkiller_Base "Battle of Starkiller Base") on [Starkiller Base](/wiki/Starkiller_Base "Starkiller Base"), and his apprentice's self-imposed exile on [Ahch-To](/wiki/Ahch-To "Ahch-To").[[197]](#cite_note-Time_of_Death-197) Using his new-found abilities, he was able to guide Skywalker during the [Battle of Yavin](/wiki/Battle_of_Yavin "Battle of Yavin") so that he could successfully destroy the Death Star with [proton torpedoes](/wiki/Proton_torpedo "Proton torpedo").[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

About five days later, the spirit of Kenobi would go to Dagobah, where he would visit Yoda regarding Skywalker. Kenobi listened as Yoda explained that Leia was by far the best candidate to pick up the mantle of Jedi, as Luke was impetuous, headstrong, unruly, and inattentive like Anakin. Nevertheless, Kenobi remained steadfast in his resolve that Luke be trained and was successful in gaining Yoda's approval to bring the boy to him.[[232]](#cite_note-There_is_Another-232)

Meanwhile, in the aftermath of the Yavin battle, Luke deeply grieved the loss of his mentor, having thought they would train together longer. He began to question whether he had heard the Jedi's voice in the Battle of Yavin, wondering if it was his own imagination. When he was [sent](/wiki/Mission_to_Rodia "Mission to Rodia") to the planet Rodia on an Alliance mission, Luke often contemplated what Kenobi would think of his surroundings, and told the Rodian [Taneetch Soonta](/wiki/Taneetch_Soonta "Taneetch Soonta") that he considered the Jedi Master the personification of honor. While on Rodia, Luke did his best to learn more about the Jedi from Soonta, whose uncle was the Jedi [Huulik](/wiki/Huulik "Huulik"). With his extremely limited training, Luke struggled to move objects with the Force, and felt dismay when recalling how easily Kenobi had mind tricked individuals on Tatooine. By repeating the few lessons about the Force he had received from Kenobi, the Alliance pilot became more determined to retain and build his knowledge base. After acquiring [Huulik's lightsaber](/wiki/Huulik%27s_lightsaber "Huulik's lightsaber") from [his mausoleum](/wiki/Huulik%27s_mausoleum "Huulik's mausoleum") with Soonta's help, Luke documented its inner workings, hoping to build another that would honor the Jedi that came before him.[[99]](#cite_note-HOTJ-99)

##### Cymoon 1 and Nar Shaddaa

:   "*Luke…Luke…listen to me carefully…Run.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to Luke Skywalker[[233]](#cite_note-SW1-233)

When Skywalker was about to confront Darth Vader in the [Weapons Factory Alpha](/wiki/Weapons_Factory_Alpha "Weapons Factory Alpha") on the [assault](/wiki/Assault_on_Cymoon "Assault on Cymoon") of [Cymoon 1](/wiki/Cymoon_1 "Cymoon 1"), Kenobi reached out to Skywalker through the Force and told him to run.[[233]](#cite_note-SW1-233) After he [recovered](/wiki/Duel_in_Ben_Kenobi%27s_home "Duel in Ben Kenobi's home") Kenobi's journal, which the Jedi Master had left behind to help Skywalker,[[234]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_2015_6-234) Skywalker tried to gain passage to the Jedi Temple on Coruscant by going to the "Smuggler's Moon" of [Nar Shaddaa](/wiki/Nar_Shaddaa "Nar Shaddaa"),[[235]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_2015_8-235) only to be captured by [Grakkus the Hutt](/wiki/Grakkus_Jahibakti_Tingi "Grakkus Jahibakti Tingi"), who forced the young Jedi into an arena battle against the [roggwart](/wiki/Roggwart "Roggwart") [Kongo](/wiki/Kongo "Kongo"). Although he tried to call upon the lessons Kenobi had taught him,[[236]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_2015_11-236) Skywalker was outmatched, so he tried to call upon his mentor for help. Instead, his friends [arrived to rescue him](/wiki/Rescue_of_Luke_Skywalker "Rescue of Luke Skywalker"), while Grakku's [gamemaster](/wiki/Kreel "Kreel") fought the Hutt, having secretly been an Imperial spy.[[237]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_2015_12-237)

##### Vrogas Vas

Later, while Luke was stationed above [Vrogas Vas](/wiki/Vrogas_Vas "Vrogas Vas"), he was attacked by Vader and crash-landed near an abandoned Jedi Temple[[238]](#cite_note-VD1-238) he had read about in one of Kenobi's journals, however while searching for something to use in the temple, he was contacted by Kenobi's voice, which told him to abandon the place, as he did not believe Luke was ready. As Luke asked how he should get ready, he was attacked and captured by General [Karbin](/wiki/Karbin "Karbin")'s stormtroopers. When Vader entered the temple, Kenobi called out to him, stating that Luke was the Chosen One and once again expressed his regret for Vader's fall; Vader dismissed Kenobi's presence as a delusion.[[239]](#cite_note-SW14-239)

##### Hoth

:   "*You will go to the Dagobah system. There you will learn from Yoda, the Jedi Master who instructed me.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to Luke Skywalker[[17]](#cite_note-Episode_V-17)

 [![Kenobi appeared to Luke on Hoth directing him to train with Yoda.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e8/ForceVision-EaW.png/revision/latest?cb=20201201013311) [![Kenobi appeared to Luke on Hoth directing him to train with Yoda.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e8/ForceVision-EaW.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201201013311)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e8/ForceVision-EaW.png/revision/latest?cb=20201201013311) 

Kenobi appeared to Luke on Hoth directing him to train with Yoda.

 

Three years later, Kenobi would reappear to Luke on the ice planet of [Hoth](/wiki/Hoth "Hoth"), where he instructed Skywalker to go to the Dagobah system to seek out Kenobi's former master, Yoda, for further Jedi training. Yoda once again expressed doubts concerning Skywalker, still believing him to be too old, impatient and reckless, as much as he had anger in him like his father once had. However, Kenobi reminded Yoda that he had been once similar to Luke, back when Yoda taught him.[[17]](#cite_note-Episode_V-17)

##### Dagobah

:   "*Luke, you will find that many of the truths we cling to depend greatly on our own point of view.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to Luke Skywalker[[240]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-240)

Over the weeks of Skywalker's training on Dagobah, Kenobi had needed to appear in six of Yoda's dreams to again and again convince him to continue the training, telling the old master that training the young Skywalker would be different from how Anakin's path had gone. Additionally, he needed to appear on Dagobah several times to serve as a mediator between Yoda and Skywalker. Throughout Luke's training, Kenobi often found himself thinking of his experiences with Anakin.[[20]](#cite_note-There_is_Always_Another-20) Later, when Skywalker received a vision of his friends in trouble on the [Cloud City](/wiki/Cloud_City "Cloud City") of [Bespin](/wiki/Bespin "Bespin"), Skywalker rushed to aid them. Appearing as a ghost on Dagobah to try to dissuade him,[[17]](#cite_note-Episode_V-17) Kenobi, who thought to himself that Anakin would never have been able to stay on the swamp world as long as Luke had,[[20]](#cite_note-There_is_Always_Another-20) warned him that he was at a crossroads and that his abilities were what the Emperor wanted; Kenobi did not want to lose Skywalker to the Emperor the way he had lost Vader.[[17]](#cite_note-Episode_V-17)

He also told the Jedi apprentice that, if he was to face Darth Vader, he would do it alone as he could not interfere. Finally, Kenobi gave Skywalker some final advice that he should not give into his hate, for hate led to the dark side. As Skywalker departed from Dagobah, Kenobi was worried that the Jedi may have lost their last hope, only for Yoda to say there was another hope for the Jedi.[[17]](#cite_note-Episode_V-17) Though Yoda was speaking of Luke's sister, Leia Organa,[[240]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-240) a long but quiet moment passed between the two Jedi as Kenobi remembered the hope was not Anakin, with Kenobi still believing that his old friend was as dead as he was[[20]](#cite_note-There_is_Always_Another-20) and had been replaced by Vader.[[240]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-240)

Later, Luke created a projection of himself and communed with Yoda on Dagobah, believing the experience was a product of his imagination. After Luke disappeared, Yoda asked Kenobi his thoughts. Kenobi appeared, voicing a concern that despite all the boy had learned, he was "not ready." Yoda affirmed that the young Skywalker would be prepared when the time was right.[[241]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_35-241)

About a year after Skywalker's initial visit, Kenobi reappeared after the death of Yoda to explain why he did not tell Luke the truth about his father. Though Luke wanted to believe that there was still good in his father, echoing Padmé's belief from twenty-three years ago, Kenobi no longer held that belief. He told Luke that he must face his destiny by confronting Vader once again. When Luke asked the meaning of Yoda's final words, "there is another Skywalker," Kenobi confessed that Leia was Luke's sister, and that they had been hidden from each other to keep them both safe. He also warned Luke about the powers of the Emperor.[[240]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-240)

 [![Anakin, Yoda, and Kenobi as Force spirits on Endor.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/JediGhosts-ROTJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20201008104501) [![Anakin, Yoda, and Kenobi as Force spirits on Endor.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/JediGhosts-ROTJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201008104501)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/JediGhosts-ROTJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20201008104501) 

Anakin, Yoda, and Kenobi as Force spirits on Endor.

 

Amid the climactic [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor"), Anakin Skywalker, rejecting his life as Darth Vader and killing Palpatine to save his son, was redeemed back to the light by Luke.[[240]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-240) As Skywalker passed away, Kenobi and Yoda appeared to him, forgiving their old friend.[[216]](#cite_note-Line_Webtoon-216) Kenobi appeared standing next to the spirits of Anakin Skywalker and Yoda as they watched Luke and the other rebels celebrate their momentous victory, although Luke was the only one able to see them.[[240]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-240) Afterward, Skywalker asked Yoda and Kenobi if his son would end up okay; Kenobi responded that he had been thus far, so it was possible.[[216]](#cite_note-Line_Webtoon-216)

For the next years, Kenobi's spirit, alongside Anakin and Yoda, continued to guide Luke in his late life.[[242]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-242) While visiting the vergence on Gazian[[62]](#cite_note-StarWars20-62) in [3 ABY](/wiki/3_ABY "3 ABY"),[[243]](#cite_note-SW20Date-243) Luke saw Kenobi's imprint in the world's [Living Sea](/wiki/Living_Sea "Living Sea").[[62]](#cite_note-StarWars20-62) Kenobi was fondly remembered by Luke, and the memories of their limited training together were something he treasured. However, after Ben Solo's fall, he blamed Kenobi and Yoda for his lack of knowledge on how to permanently stamp out the dark, feeling that his err in teaching led to his student's demise as Kylo Ren.[[244]](#cite_note-TLJ_Junior-244)

Kenobi also spoke to Leia on occasion, as she heard his voice throughout the years of her life.[[245]](#cite_note-TROS_Expanded_Edition-245) While on Ahch-To, after Luke Skywalker reconnected to the Force, he felt Kenobi's spirit, along with Yoda, and his father Anakin with him again and felt comfort in that.[[242]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-242) Sometime after as Skywalker was dying, he thought he heard the familiar voice of Kenobi urging him to let go and he did, joining Kenobi, Yoda, and his father in the Force.[[246]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_The_Last_Jedi:_Expanded_Edition-246)

#### Communion with Rey

##### Takodana

:   "*You will be tempted. But you can learn. The Force will be with you…The dark side…The Jedi…You will do it alone…Rey…These are your…first…steps…*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to Rey[[247]](#cite_note-The_Force_Awakens_Adaptation_4-247)

[Thirty years later](/wiki/34_ABY "34 ABY"), Obi-Wan spoke to the Force-sensitive [scavenger](/wiki/Scavenger "Scavenger") [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker") in the voice of his younger self during a vision she received upon touching the lightsaber that previously belonged to Luke Skywalker, and Anakin before him. Obi-Wan called out to Rey, telling her that these were her first steps, and that the Force would be with her in her fight against the dark side.[[248]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-248)

##### Exegol

:   "*These are your final steps, Rey. Rise and take them.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to Rey[[249]](#cite_note-Episode_9-249)

One year later in [35 ABY](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY"),[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) during the [Battle of Exegol](/wiki/Battle_of_Exegol "Battle of Exegol"), Kenobi's voice was again heard by Rey among the voices of many Jedi of the past who aided her with destroying the resurrected Darth Sidious once and for all. The first to call out to her, he echoed his first message to Rey, telling her to rise and take her final steps to becoming a true Jedi.[[250]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-250)

### Legacy

:   "*You are named after legends.*"  
    "*That's exactly it, Snoke. Obi-Wan Kenobi… Big famous Jedi. Everyone thinks I'm supposed to* be *like him. I never even* met *him.*"
:   ―[Snoke](/wiki/Snoke "Snoke") and Ben Solo[[251]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_2-251)

 [![The son of Han Solo and Leia Organa, Ben Solo was named after the Jedi Master who trained his grandfather and uncle.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/SoloFamily-PoeDameronAnnual2.png/revision/latest?cb=20230718031959) [![The son of Han Solo and Leia Organa, Ben Solo was named after the Jedi Master who trained his grandfather and uncle.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/SoloFamily-PoeDameronAnnual2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230718031959)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/SoloFamily-PoeDameronAnnual2.png/revision/latest?cb=20230718031959) 

The son of Han Solo and Leia Organa, Ben Solo was named after the Jedi Master who trained his grandfather and uncle.

 

Obi-Wan Kenobi was considered a legend by the time of the [New Republic Era](/wiki/New_Republic_Era "New Republic Era").[[251]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_2-251) In the aftermath of the Galactic Civil War,[[252]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-252) Han Solo and Leia Organa named their only son, [Ben Solo](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo"), after the famous Jedi Master. However, the fame of Kenobi's name and his deeds as a Jedi weighed on the young Ben, who harbored feelings of insecurity due to the expectations that had been thrust on him because of his heritage.[[251]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_2-251)

Solo grew resentful toward the late Jedi, especially as he thought that everyone expected him to be like his namesake despite never knowing Kenobi. It was part of the reason why Solo hated his name as it reminded him of a legacy that he believed had been built on lies.[[251]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_2-251) Ultimately, he renounced his ties to the Jedi and adopted a new identity, that of Kylo Ren, following in the example of[[253]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-253) Kenobi's fallen apprentice[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)—Solo's grandfather, Darth Vader.[[253]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-253)

In time, however, Solo [returned](/wiki/Mission_to_Kef_Bir "Mission to Kef Bir") to the light, destroying the dark persona of Ren.[[250]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-250) Where once he recoiled at the sound of his birth name, he regretted ever renouncing it.[[254]](#cite_note-TROS_JN-254) His redemption came when he sacrificed his life to [save](/wiki/Force_healing "Force healing") Rey—a selfless act mirroring that of Anakin Skywalker.[[255]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_DB-255) Once revived, Rey looked at Solo and smiled, calling him by his name "Ben," who shortly afterwards became one with the Force.[[250]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-250)

Kenobi's contributions during the Clone Wars were remembered long after the war's end, with citizens of Pau City on Utapau being able to recall Kenobi's name many decades after the Battle of Utapau. When the Force-sensitive human [Karr Nuq Sin](/wiki/Karr_Nuq_Sin "Karr Nuq Sin") embarked on a journey across the galaxy to learn more about the Force and the Jedi, he used his powers of psychometry to experience visions of Kenobi visiting Pau City in search of General Grievous as well as moments of him and Luke Skywalker onboard the *Millennium Falcon*.[[256]](#cite_note-Force_Collector-256)

## Personality and traits

:   "*Who's the more foolish, the fool, or the fool who follows him?*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9a/WhosTheMoreFoolish-ANH.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250410001850)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:WhosTheMoreFoolish-ANH.flac "File:WhosTheMoreFoolish-ANH.flac"))[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

Kenobi was a [human](/wiki/Human "Human") male[[4]](#cite_note-USW_NE-4) who stood at 1.82 meters[[5]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_DB-5) and weighed 81 [kilograms](/wiki/Kilogram "Kilogram").[[7]](#cite_note-SWJB-7) He had [fair](/wiki/Color "Color") skin,[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) gray-blue eyes, and auburn [hair](/wiki/Hair "Hair")[[8]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-8) which had turned white in his later years.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

 [![Kenobi was a headstrong Padawan, yet also showed wisdom](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4b/ObiWanKenobi-ChromeGalaxy2022.png/revision/latest?cb=20251105144105) [![Kenobi was a headstrong Padawan, yet also showed wisdom](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4b/ObiWanKenobi-ChromeGalaxy2022.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20251105144105)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4b/ObiWanKenobi-ChromeGalaxy2022.png/revision/latest?cb=20251105144105) 

Kenobi was a headstrong Padawan, yet also showed wisdom

 

During much of his time as a youngling, Kenobi was known to be rebellious and willful, described as breaking the rules laid out by the Jedi left and right. However, throughout much of his early apprenticeship to Qui-Gon Jinn, Kenobi possessed strong fondness for rigid rules and a largely by-the-book attitude when it came to matters such as the Jedi Code. He felt as if he never truly understood his master and yet nevertheless wished to please him and earn his respect. He also had trouble understanding his master's hobbies and interests, such as study of arcane Jedi prophecies. At various points, he considered the fact that Jinn could be kicked out of the Order and wondered what would happen to him if such a case were to occur.[[20]](#cite_note-There_is_Always_Another-20) The two later came to realization that Yoda intentionally placed Kenobi with a maverick master in the hope that he would rebel in the only way possible: by attempting to become a model Jedi.[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18)

Over time, Kenobi would become loyal and dedicated to Jinn, possessing a dry sense of humor and sarcastic wit. Yoda said that he sensed Qui-Gon Jinn's defiance in him, and Jinn himself reflected upon Kenobi's considerable knowledge and potential; he also considered his Padawan a lot wiser than he, if somewhat headstrong.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_I-14) Leading up to his Jedi Trials, Kenobi was very nervous and lost sleep worrying about them. Although he could sometimes be impertinent,[[232]](#cite_note-There_is_Another-232) he was often seen as wise beyond his years, his humble and soft-spoken demeanor belied his warrior prowess. Despite his numerous complaints during flight,[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) and deeply shaken by an experience involving [auto-pursuit](/wiki/Autopursuit "Autopursuit") in his youth,[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18) he was also a skilled pilot. In many ways, he represented the strength of the old Jedi Order: steadfast, selfless, and modest.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) A tireless defender of the Republic's ideals of democracy and justice,[[257]](#cite_note-Galactic_Defense-257) his later skill at resolving disputes without battle would earn him the sobriquet "The Negotiator."[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

Over time, Kenobi lost some of his youthful audacity and assumed the role of a more cautious mentor to Anakin Skywalker, who was in many ways his opposite in personality.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_I-14) The two had a very strange dynamic early on, with Kenobi feeling protective and responsible for his young Padawan and Skywalker worrying about Kenobi's commitment to him, having been abandoned in his life previously. Kenobi knew of these feelings, evidenced by waking up to see Skywalker had moved to sleep on the floor next to his bed. Kenobi often worried he was not fit to teach Skywalker and sometimes would lie awake at night thinking of things to teach his apprentice. As their relationship deepened over time, the two found that they could easily get on each other's nerves, with Kenobi becoming particularly annoyed by his Padawan's habit of grinding his teeth in frustration.[[20]](#cite_note-There_is_Always_Another-20) For all their bickering, they cared deeply for each other.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

 [![Kenobi preferred negotiation before action, but was also an accomplished swordsman.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/RepublicJediArmor-Convergence.png/revision/latest?cb=20190425005649) [![Kenobi preferred negotiation before action, but was also an accomplished swordsman.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/RepublicJediArmor-Convergence.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190425005649)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/RepublicJediArmor-Convergence.png/revision/latest?cb=20190425005649) 

Kenobi preferred negotiation before action, but was also an accomplished swordsman.

 

Kenobi carefully measured his actions in any situation, garnering him the aforementioned nom de guerre. Kenobi was also known to be an accomplished storyteller. While hiding in the Jundland Wastes in his later years, he appeared as a kindly and eccentric old hermit. Owen Lars described him as "a crazy old man" to those not familiar with the ways of the Jedi. In his final days, Kenobi retained his traits of patience and foresight as well as gaining some of the boldness reminiscent of his youth.[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_I-14)

Kenobi often thought out plans and strategies rather than leaping into action. He would usually place his hand on his chin or stroke his beard as he thought. This was a common trait of the Jedi Master, one that his apprentice Anakin Skywalker did not practice very often.[[80]](#cite_note-Rookies-80) He sometimes mentally repeated the Jedi Code to calm himself.[[8]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-8) He had also served as a mentor to Skywalker's Padawan, Ahsoka Tano. Tano recognized that Kenobi had more patience than Skywalker, but she also fondly remembered how they would bicker. Tano believed Kenobi would have enjoyed the strategy game [crokin](/wiki/Crokin "Crokin").[[204]](#cite_note-Ahsoka-204)

Kenobi's respect for the lives of others led him to emerge from hiding to save Ezra Bridger and the [C1-series astromech droid](/wiki/C1-series_astromech_droid "C1-series astromech droid") [Chopper](/wiki/C1-10P "C1-10P") from succumbing to the deserts of Tatooine. Kenobi then reproved Ezra for succumbing to Maul's manipulation and counselled the young rebel to return to his place with the rebellion. When faced with the Sith who slew his master, Kenobi did not hate Maul and tried to talk him down, but when he made his violent intent clear and sensed Luke Skywalker, Kenobi was forced to fight and kill him in self defense. After mortally wounding Maul, Kenobi comforted the former Sith and assured him that he was watching over the "Chosen One," Luke Skywalker, though Luke was not the Chosen One by prophecy.[[222]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-222) When he confronted Vader on the Death Star, Kenobi found himself unable to believe his foe was once his friend, even being unable to call him by his name; he used the title "Darth" instead, while he also realized his own anger was rising as Vader spoke.[[197]](#cite_note-Time_of_Death-197)

 [![Kenobi in his trademark defensive position](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/40/Obiwan-Soresu.png/revision/latest?cb=20130212055217) [![Kenobi in his trademark defensive position](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/40/Obiwan-Soresu.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20130212055217)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/40/Obiwan-Soresu.png/revision/latest?cb=20130212055217) 

Kenobi in his trademark defensive position

 

During his exile on Tatooine, Kenobi was forced to engage in self-reflection that he described as agonizing. Over the years, he was forced to dismantle systemic rituals and ingrained doctrines he had experienced during his time with the Jedi.[[20]](#cite_note-There_is_Always_Another-20) He was left broken and unwilling to fight[[199]](#cite_note-Kenobi_1-199) until his rematches with Vader[[209]](#cite_note-Kenobi_4-209) ten years after Order 66,[[199]](#cite_note-Kenobi_1-199) which left him with the belief that his friend had been destroyed by Vader. While he once blamed himself for Skywalker's fall, Kenobi, after hearing Vader's proclamation,[[209]](#cite_note-Kenobi_4-209) had come to believe that, while he and Jinn did have some blame, Skywalker had made his own choices and thus was at fault for his own fate.[[22]](#cite_note-Master_and_Apprentice-22) As he noted to Reva Sevander, the adventure had freed both of them from the past.[[209]](#cite_note-Kenobi_4-209) As he learned to forgive himself for mistakes he made during the war, he also learned to forgive others.[[20]](#cite_note-There_is_Always_Another-20) Nevertheless, despite finding himself unable to call Vader by his old name during their final duel on the Death Star, he did ponder if Anakin Skywalker still remained within,[[197]](#cite_note-Time_of_Death-197) but he later claimed to Luke that Anakin was truly gone. Luke proved him wrong when he redeemed his father, enabling Kenobi and Skywalker to renew their friendship as Force spirits.[[240]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-240)

### Romantic relationships

#### Siri Tachi

A fellow Jedi, Siri Tachi trained at the Coruscant's [Temple](/wiki/Jedi_temple "Jedi temple") at the same time as Kenobi. Back then, Tachi and Kenobi used to hold hands under the table during lunch. Years later, Kenobi mused that although the Jedi may have been exterminated, their dedication to posturing theatrics lived on in Yoda and that he needed just look back at moments with Tachi to feel as though he had deserved a punishment from the Jedi Council.[[20]](#cite_note-There_is_Always_Another-20)

#### Satine Kryze

:   "*I've loved you from the moment you came to my aid all those years ago.*" [**…**]  
    "*Had you said the word, I would have left the Jedi Order.*"
:   ―Satine Kryze and Obi-Wan Kenobi — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b4/ObiWanInLove-VoT.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250328195712)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:ObiWanInLove-VoT.flac "File:ObiWanInLove-VoT.flac"))[[34]](#cite_note-Voyage_of_Temptation-34)

During Mandalore's Civil War and his apprenticeship under Qui-Gon Jinn, Kenobi fell in love with the young Duchess Satine Kryze. The two lived on the run for over a year. Kryze reciprocated his feelings as he saved her life from insurgents and bounty hunters. When Kenobi's mission ended, he chose to honor his obligations to the Jedi Order in accordance to the Jedi Code. However, he regretted leaving the Duchess alone to rebuild Mandalore.[[34]](#cite_note-Voyage_of_Temptation-34)

 [![Kenobi and Kryze's many hardships strengthened their bond.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/Memorial_Shrine_bombing.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100130044121) [![Kenobi and Kryze's many hardships strengthened their bond.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/Memorial_Shrine_bombing.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/279?cb=20100130044121)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/Memorial_Shrine_bombing.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100130044121) 

Kenobi and Kryze's many hardships strengthened their bond.

 

Years later during the Clone Wars,[[32]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot-32) Kenobi and Kryze still had feelings for each other, but found themselves on opposing sides. Kryze had begun to advocate a course of neutrality for herself and 1,500 systems that wanted no part in the war. Meanwhile, Kenobi defended the use of military action to end the conflict with the Separatists, including a military presence on Mandalore to protect it from the Death Watch. As such, their inability to express their feelings led them to bicker relentlessly about their conflicting philosophies. Only when forced into action did their camaraderie return. When Kryze was taken hostage by Senator Merrick, she confessed that she had always loved him. Kenobi, despite the situation, confessed that he too loved her and would have left the Jedi Order if she asked it of him. Despite their confessions, Kenobi and Kryze continued with their responsibilities as peacekeepers.[[34]](#cite_note-Voyage_of_Temptation-34)

When Maul resurfaced on Mandalore, Kenobi attempted to rescue her from him, but the pair were captured. Kenobi was forced to watch Maul choke Kryze and ultimately kill her with the Darksaber. Kenobi mourned her, but refused to give in to his anger and desire to avenge her,[[16]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-16) only doing so out of peace and justice nearly twenty years later.[[222]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-222)

## Powers and abilities

### Lightsaber abilities

:   "*This weapon is your life.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to Anakin Skywalker[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39)

 [![Obi-wan Kenobi was master of Form III, also called Soresu.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/LE_Obi-Wan_Kenobi_Commander_Expansion.png/revision/latest?cb=20190906023428) [![Obi-wan Kenobi was master of Form III, also called Soresu.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/LE_Obi-Wan_Kenobi_Commander_Expansion.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190906023428)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/LE_Obi-Wan_Kenobi_Commander_Expansion.png/revision/latest?cb=20190906023428) 

Obi-wan Kenobi was master of Form III, also called Soresu.

 

Kenobi was a very capable lightsaber duelist, one of the greatest swordsmen of his time. Throughout his training years, he had learnt several forms of lightsaber combat, especially [Form III](/wiki/Form_III "Form III").[[8]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-8)[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_I-14) In contrast to the aggressive dueling styles of his master, Qui-Gon Jinn, and his apprentice Anakin Skywalker, Kenobi's combat style was mainly defensive, though he would use aggressive attacks when pressed. He faced some of the most dangerous people in the galaxy, such as the deadly Sith Lord Darth Maul and infamous Jedi Hunter General Grievous, respectively, the latter of whom he fought on at least seven occasions. Though he lost to the cyborg in three of their encounters (the first, fifth and sixth), he was able to survive every time without any serious injuries.

Kenobi was able to duel Grievous to a draw in their third and fourth encounters, and was able to overpower him in their second duel and ultimately killed him in the final round, albeit with a blaster rather than his lightsaber. However, his final victory may have been helped by Grievous' fresh injuries, which would have hampered the cyborg's fighting abilities.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) Although Kenobi usually used only one lightsaber, he also seemed to have been well-versed in the art of [Jar'Kai](/wiki/Jar%27Kai "Jar'Kai"), which was perhaps most prominently displayed during his duel with Maul and Savage Opress, in which he wielded both his own lightsaber and the blade of the slain Adi Gallia. His mastery of dual-blade combat allowed him to hold his own against both the Sith brothers, and he even managed to break Opress's left knee and sever his left arm. The duel ultimately ended as a stalemate when an angered Maul used his Force powers to briefly incapacitate Kenobi, giving the brothers time to escape.[[147]](#cite_note-Revival-147)

 [![Kenobi and Ventress engage in lightsaber combat](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/KenobiVsVentress-TCWf.png/revision/latest?cb=20121012035540) [![Kenobi and Ventress engage in lightsaber combat](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/KenobiVsVentress-TCWf.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121012035540)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/KenobiVsVentress-TCWf.png/revision/latest?cb=20121012035540) 

Kenobi and Ventress engage in lightsaber combat

 

Kenobi also situationally, and somewhat less successfully, used Jar'Kai against General Grievous and Cad Bane respectively.[[112]](#cite_note-Hunt_for_Ziro-112) He was also capable of using his lightsaber to ground Force lightning, as he demonstrated against Dooku on Geonosis.
