Kenobi was also able to defeat his former apprentice Anakin Skywalker, then Darth Vader, in an epic duel on Mustafar. Making use of his staunch Form III defense throughout the fight, Kenobi was eventually able to exploit Vader's aggressive nature, and dismembered the hate-filled Sith Lord when he recklessly jumped towards him.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) While initially not as skilled due to having lost his connection with the Force,[[10]](#cite_note-Kenobi_3-10) Kenobi was able to get the edge once again over his former apprentice Darth Vader on another duel ten years later.[[210]](#cite_note-Kenobi_6-210)

Decades later, he defeated his old nemesis Maul within seconds despite the former Sith Lord having demonstrated the ability to hold an advantage against three Inquisitors simultaneously,[[222]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-222) and duel his former master Darth Sidious for a short time.[[16]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-16) A few years later, during his rematch with Vader on the first Death Star, Kenobi proved formidable enough to hold his own against the Sith Lord for a short time. However, Vader's cautious but relentless assault ultimately overwhelmed Kenobi's defenses, and he was forced to begin retreating. Ultimately, he chose to become one with the Force rather than continue the fight and in doing this, he taught both of his Skywalker students one final lesson.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

### Force powers

:   "*The Force is what gives a Jedi his power. It's an energy field created by all living things. It surrounds us and penetrates us. It binds the galaxy together.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, instructing Luke Skywalker — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/Theforce.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250410001837)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:Theforce.flac "File:Theforce.flac"))[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

 [![Obi-Wan Kenobi uses the Jedi mind trick on a pair of stormtroopers aboard the Death Star](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/Jedi_Mind_Trick_SWL.png/revision/latest?cb=20190331043526) [![Obi-Wan Kenobi uses the Jedi mind trick on a pair of stormtroopers aboard the Death Star](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/Jedi_Mind_Trick_SWL.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190331043526)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/Jedi_Mind_Trick_SWL.png/revision/latest?cb=20190331043526) 

Obi-Wan Kenobi uses the Jedi mind trick on a pair of stormtroopers aboard the Death Star

 

Though Kenobi focused largely on lightsaber combat, he was also very skilled and powerful in use of the Force. He was trained in the use of the [mind trick](/wiki/Mind_trick "Mind trick"), making use of it whenever he wanted to avoid physical confrontations.[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39)[[89]](#cite_note-The_Gungan_General-89)[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)[[26]](#cite_note-SW7-26) He was also able to use the Force to [tame, control, and lead](/wiki/Taming_beasts "Taming beasts") a group of angry gutkurrs on Ryloth.[[93]](#cite_note-Innocents_of_Ryloth-93) As befitted a Jedi, Kenobi was adept at concealing his feelings in the Force when he chose to.[[8]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-8) Kenobi was adept at [Force healing](/wiki/Force_healing "Force healing"), improving his physical capabilities, [leaping around with the Force](/wiki/Force_jump "Force jump"), [knowing the future](/wiki/Precognition "Precognition"), and could, with great effort, make himself and his use of the Force go unnoticed by all.[[258]](#cite_note-Allies_and_Adversaries-258) He also [felt](/wiki/Disturbance_in_the_Force "Disturbance in the Force") when Alderaan was [destroyed](/wiki/Destruction_of_Alderaan "Destruction of Alderaan") and so many died.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

He was also capable of using telekinesis to [push](/wiki/Force_push "Force push") or levitate objects,[[26]](#cite_note-SW7-26) or to crush them, as seen when he destroyed two commando droids to recover his lightsaber after a difficult hand-to-hand fight with Darts D'Nar.[[130]](#cite_note-Kidnapped-130) He would also use the Force to augment his natural leaping ability. His ability to use the Force push technique was exceptional, as he was able to use it to blast back General Grievous dozens of meters with a single push during their duel. A short time later, he was even able to hold off a Force push from Anakin Skywalker during their duel, though after a short time the resulting telekinetic struggle launched both of them across a room.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) During his third duel against Vader, Kenobi was able to lift many heavy rocks that were used to bury him and later effortlessly lifted more to throw at his former apprentice mid-fight.[[210]](#cite_note-Kenobi_6-210)

Prior to his exile on Tatooine, Yoda instructed him on how to communicate his late master, Qui-Gon Jinn, who was unable to visibly manifest as a spirit due to his incomplete training under the [Force Priestesses](/wiki/Force_Priestesses "Force Priestesses").[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) Through Jinn, Kenobi eventually learned the ability to manifest his consciousness after death, a skill he would later put to good use to guide and counsel his apprentice, Luke Skywalker, during the Galactic Civil War.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)[[233]](#cite_note-SW1-233)[[17]](#cite_note-Episode_V-17)[[240]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-240)[[20]](#cite_note-There_is_Always_Another-20)

### Other abilities

:   "*Obi-Wan is a great mentor; as wise as Master Yoda, and as powerful as Master Windu.*"
:   ―Anakin Skywalker[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39)

 [![General Kenobi destroying battle droids in his Jedi Commander Armor](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e0/General_Kenobi_CWCS.png/revision/latest?cb=20190403045721) [![General Kenobi destroying battle droids in his Jedi Commander Armor](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e0/General_Kenobi_CWCS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190403045721)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e0/General_Kenobi_CWCS.png/revision/latest?cb=20190403045721) 

General Kenobi destroying battle droids in his Jedi Commander Armor

 

Obi-Wan Kenobi proved himself to be a great military strategist and a highly studious man, demonstrating good knowledge on galactic history and conventions of war, like the [Yavin Code](/wiki/Yavin_Code "Yavin Code").[[44]](#cite_note-The_Big_Bang-44) General Kenobi personally led his troops to many famous victories during the Clone Wars, and his persuasive demeanor earned him the moniker of "the Negotiator."[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

Despite his dislike of flying, Kenobi was an excellent pilot. During the Clone Wars, he led many attacks from the cockpit of his Jedi starfighter or his [Jedi interceptor](/wiki/Eta-2_Actis-class_light_interceptor "Eta-2 Actis-class light interceptor"), proving to be an outstanding pilot when navigating through an asteroid field in pursuit of Jango Fett's ship and evading his seismic charges unscathed.[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39) In fact, Kenobi had once rather enjoyed flying, prior to an incident during and his Qui-Gon Jinn's [mission to Pijal](/wiki/Mission_to_Pijal "Mission to Pijal").[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18)

Kenobi was also a skilled hand-to-hand combatant, having developed enough level of skill in unarmed combat so as to compete with Pre Vizsla, leader of the Death Watch, in unarmed techniques, though he outclassed the Mandalorian in lightsaber technique.[[32]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot-32) During his duel with Jango Fett on Kamino, Kenobi was briefly deprived of his lightsaber, and fought the bounty hunter in unarmed combat.[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39) Furthermore, while he preferred lightsabers, Kenobi was an excellent marksman, as demonstrated during his time as "Rako Hardeen" in Moralo Eval's Box and by his defeat of Grievous with his own blaster.[[134]](#cite_note-The_Box-134) While hiding on Tatooine, he carried a [BR-14](/wiki/BR-14_blaster "BR-14 blaster") [blaster pistol](/wiki/Blaster_pistol "Blaster pistol").[[6]](#cite_note-DoR:TVG-6) He manage to use it while saving young Princess Leia who was held at blasterpoint.[[10]](#cite_note-Kenobi_3-10)

He understood many languages, including [Galactic Basic Standard](/wiki/Galactic_Basic_Standard "Galactic Basic Standard"), Twi'leki,[[93]](#cite_note-Innocents_of_Ryloth-93) the [Amani language](/wiki/Amani_(language) "Amani (language)"),[[165]](#cite_note-A_Death_on_Utapau-165) Felucia's tribal language,[[160]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-160) Old Alderaanian,[[18]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-18) and [Shyriiwook](/wiki/Shyriiwook "Shyriiwook").[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) Though he admitted his skills were "rusty," Kenobi could read hand signals accurately enough to understand Eeth Koth's message to his location at the [Saleucami system](/wiki/Saleucami_system "Saleucami system").[[59]](#cite_note-Grievous_Intrigue-59)

## Behind the scenes

### The Original trilogy

Obi-Wan Kenobi, originally introduced as "Ben" Kenobi, made his first appearance in [*Star Wars*: Episode IV *A New Hope*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope"), played by Sir [Alec Guinness](/wiki/Alec_Guinness "Alec Guinness"), who was nominated for an [Academy Award for Best Supporting Actor](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Supporting_Actor "wikipedia:Academy Award for Best Supporting Actor") (the only acting-related Academy Award nomination for any *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* film).[[259]](#cite_note-Oscars-259) During the casting process for the part of Kenobi for *A New Hope*, director [George Lucas](/wiki/George_Lucas "George Lucas") was looking for an actor who brought a certain authority to the role and could be powerful and gentle. Lucas found these qualities in Guinness,[[260]](#cite_note-Remembered-260) who joined the cast because of the film's sense of moral good and the studio's doubling of his initial salary offer.[[261]](#cite_note-Cancer_Today-261) Guinness said working on the film provided many challenges. Lucas suggested Guinness to act like a [samurai](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Samurai "wikipedia:Samurai") [warrior](/wiki/Warrior "Warrior") and a wise, [monk](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Monk "wikipedia:Monk")-like character.[[262]](#cite_note-Return-262) Guinness reprised the role as Kenobi's force ghost in [*The Empire Strikes Back*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_V_The_Empire_Strikes_Back "Star Wars: Episode V The Empire Strikes Back") and [*Return of the Jedi*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VI_Return_of_the_Jedi "Star Wars: Episode VI Return of the Jedi"). Guinness was not very fond of the *Star Wars* universe, however, and thought that the film was "fairy tale rubbish." He disliked very much to be associated with the role of Kenobi.[[261]](#cite_note-Cancer_Today-261)

*[The Making of Star Wars: The Definitive Story Behind the Original Film](/wiki/The_Making_of_Star_Wars:_The_Definitive_Story_Behind_the_Original_Film "The Making of Star Wars: The Definitive Story Behind the Original Film")* stated that Lucas originally came up with the idea of having Kenobi die, to which Guinness initially objected. By explaining that the character would have little to do in the story after the *Millennium Falcon* escaped the Death Star, Lucas convinced him to allow it. However, other sources indicate that the idea to kill off Kenobi came from [Marcia Lucas](/wiki/Marcia_Lucas "Marcia Lucas"), after her husband complained he was unable to find a way to generate tension in the story.[[263]](#cite_note-Secret_Weapon-263) In the draft script for what became [*Star Wars*: Episode VI *Return of the Jedi*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VI_Return_of_the_Jedi "Star Wars: Episode VI Return of the Jedi"), Kenobi, along with Yoda, would have appeared as a Force spirit during the battle between Luke Skywalker and the Emperor in defense of their pupil: both Jedi Masters would deflect the Sith Lord's Force lightning. Kenobi, Yoda, and Anakin Skywalker would have all returned to life as well.[[264]](#cite_note-Rewind_of_the_Jedi-264)

### The Prequel trilogy

 [![Early concept for young Obi-Wan Kenobi in The Phantom Menace](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/84/Obi-Wan_Kenobi_Episode_1_Concept_Art.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090612044612) [![Early concept for young Obi-Wan Kenobi in The Phantom Menace](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/84/Obi-Wan_Kenobi_Episode_1_Concept_Art.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20090612044612)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/84/Obi-Wan_Kenobi_Episode_1_Concept_Art.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090612044612) 

Early concept for young Obi-Wan Kenobi in *The Phantom Menace*

 

Obi-Wan Kenobi was played by [Ewan McGregor](/wiki/Ewan_McGregor "Ewan McGregor") in the [1999](/wiki/1999 "1999") film [*The Phantom Menace*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace "Star Wars: Episode I The Phantom Menace").[[14]](#cite_note-Episode_I-14) When he began the casting process, he thought that *Star Wars* didn't feel right to him. He was skeptical about playing Kenobi and thought "Well, I'm this independent, urban-y, grungy actor over here. I'm not this kind of guy." McGregor's anxiety eventually turned into excitement,[[265]](#cite_note-17_year-265) and he was excited to play a younger Alec Guinness.[[266]](#cite_note-Kenobi_preparation-266) In [December](/wiki/December "December"), [1996](/wiki/1996 "1996"), the actor did an audition interview in [London](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/London "wikipedia:London"). Shortly after that, McGregor was told that the role was offered to him. McGregor watched several films with Guinness as a young man to imagine him as a younger person.[[262]](#cite_note-Return-262) He also studied Guinness and watched the [original trilogy](/wiki/Original_trilogy "Original trilogy") as preparation, but he didn't really think about the genre.[[266]](#cite_note-Kenobi_preparation-266) After director George Lucas showed McGregor around the studio, they went to the props-making department, and the prop master showed him a chest of lightsaber props. McGregor then got to choose which lightsaber he would use in the film.[[262]](#cite_note-Return-262) The first lightsaber work he did was when he trained for the duel against Darth Maul.[[267]](#cite_note-Series_of_Firsts-267) McGregor had lightsaber training with stunt coordinator [Nick Gillard](/wiki/Nick_Gillard "Nick Gillard").[[265]](#cite_note-17_year-265)

McGregor said that the crew were looking for a military sense or something in the world of monks for Kenobi's hairstyle. He said the [padawan braid](/wiki/Padawan_braid "Padawan braid") hairstyle was similar to the hair of people who shave their head for [religious](/wiki/Religion "Religion") orders. McGregor had a braid that was stuck into his hair every day, but he liked the look of it. Six to eight [months](/wiki/Standard_month "Standard month") after principal photography of *The Phantom Menace*, McGregor and other actors returned for reshoots. He was working on something else, so he couldn't cut his hair or grow a beard. The crew made a short hair wig for McGregor, but he found it difficult to hide longer hair under a wig.[[268]](#cite_note-Hair_Breakdown-268)

McGregor reprised his role in [*Attack of the Clones*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_II_Attack_of_the_Clones "Star Wars: Episode II Attack of the Clones").[[39]](#cite_note-Episode_II-39) McGregor and [Hayden Christensen](/wiki/Hayden_Christensen "Hayden Christensen"), the actor who played Anakin Skywalker, practiced lightsaber rehearsals, which Christensen said was the most fun he had, and he described it as "playing with your friend every day."[[265]](#cite_note-17_year-265) Kenobi's hairstyle was inspired by the [Bee Gees](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bee_Gees "wikipedia:Bee Gees") and was called a "Jedi mullet." The new hairstyle was meant to show a warrior and also progression.[[268]](#cite_note-Hair_Breakdown-268) In a [deleted scene](/wiki/Content_cut_from_Star_Wars "Content cut from Star Wars"), Kenobi used a pair of macrobinoculars on Geonosis.[[269]](#cite_note-Elegant_weapon-269) McGregor later played Kenobi in [*Revenge of the Sith*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_III_Revenge_of_the_Sith "Star Wars: Episode III Revenge of the Sith").[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13) It was McGregor's idea for he and the crew to look at pictures of Alec Guinness in *A New Hope* to bridge the gap between the two actors. Also, his hair and beard were grayed a little bit to get closer to Guinness's portrayal. Kenobi's hair was supposed to show a bit more age and show a master or teacher.[[268]](#cite_note-Hair_Breakdown-268)

### *Star Wars: The Clone Wars* and *Star Wars Rebels*

[James Arnold Taylor](/wiki/James_Arnold_Taylor "James Arnold Taylor") voiced Kenobi in the [*The Clone Wars*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars_(film) "Star Wars: The Clone Wars (film)") film and [TV series](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars"), as well as *[Star Wars Rebels](/wiki/Star_Wars_Rebels "Star Wars Rebels")*. In the *Star Wars Rebels* [third season](/wiki/Star_Wars_Rebels_Season_Three "Star Wars Rebels Season Three") episode "[Twin Suns](/wiki/Twin_Suns_(episode) "Twin Suns (episode)")," Kenobi was voiced by [Stephen Stanton](/wiki/Stephen_Stanton "Stephen Stanton").[[222]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-222)

### The Sequel trilogy

In [*The Force Awakens*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VII_The_Force_Awakens "Star Wars: Episode VII The Force Awakens"), Taylor returned to voice Kenobi in a brief scene during Rey's Force vision, but the voiceover was later replaced instead with one from McGregor.[[270]](#cite_note-TweetVoiceEwan-270) Guinness's voice was also used, with his line "Rey" extracted from audio of him saying "afraid."[[271]](#cite_note-271) Both Guinness and McGregor were heard again in [*Star Wars*: Episode IX *The Rise of Skywalker*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IX_The_Rise_of_Skywalker "Star Wars: Episode IX The Rise of Skywalker").[[250]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-250)

Kenobi's Force spirit was originally present in the early drafts of the [2017](/wiki/2017 "2017") film [*Star Wars*: Episode VIII *The Last Jedi*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VIII_The_Last_Jedi "Star Wars: Episode VIII The Last Jedi"), but director [Rian Johnson](/wiki/Rian_Johnson "Rian Johnson") ultimately decided to use Yoda instead, adding that the only version of Kenobi who interacted with Skywalker was the one of late Alec Guinness, and having Luke interacting with Ewan McGregor's Obi-Wan would have felt too weird, as Luke never met Obi-Wan during his younger years.[[272]](#cite_note-Chose_Wrong-272)

### *Obi-Wan Kenobi* television series

:   "*It was nice to come back and to bridge that gap between me and Alec Guinness. I got as much, or more, out of playing him this time than I did in the first three movies put together. That's to do with the writing, and the people we were making the series with, and the technology, and how different everything is. If we were to get an opportunity to do it again, I'd be totally up for that.*"
:   ―Ewan McGregor[[273]](#cite_note-McGregor_got_more-273)

In [2016](/wiki/2016 "2016"), McGregor said that he didn't have a burning need to play Kenobi again and he said he didn't have any fascination for the *Star Wars* movies. He said it was possibly because he had already been in the movies and had "seen behind the curtain." He added that the movies didn't "have the same type of wonderment" to him. McGregor met many people who were kids when the prequels were released who expressed how important the films were to them. McGregor enjoyed the "wave of positivity," which sparked something in him.[[265]](#cite_note-17_year-265)

In interviews, McGregor stated that he was open to returning as Kenobi in *Star Wars*, but he worried he was too open. He told people he'd be happy to play Kenobi if Lucasfilm wanted, and people thought that he was "touting for work at [Disney's](/wiki/The_Walt_Disney_Company "The Walt Disney Company") door." It was publicly believed that McGregor was happy to play Kenobi again.[[265]](#cite_note-17_year-265) In [2018](/wiki/2018 "2018"),[[274]](#cite_note-Rebellion_televised-274) a meeting was held to see how serious the actor was to play Kenobi in an Obi-Wan Kenobi film as part of a [series](/wiki/Star_Wars_Anthology_Series "Star Wars Anthology Series") of stand-alone movies outside of the [Skywalker saga](/wiki/Star_Wars_saga "Star Wars saga"). [Lucasfilm](/wiki/Lucasfilm "Lucasfilm")'s then head of story [Kiri Hart](/wiki/Kiri_Hart "Kiri Hart") and the people at the meeting said they were aware that McGregor was happy to do it, and Hart asked if he meant it or was just being polite. They asked if McGregor was in or not and he said he was in. Lucasfilm then actively began development on an Obi-Wan Kenobi film that would be directed by [Stephen Daldry](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stephen_Daldry "wikipedia:Stephen Daldry").[[265]](#cite_note-17_year-265)[[274]](#cite_note-Rebellion_televised-274) McGregor would be the producer, giving him more say over the story. He wanted Kenobi to start as a broken, faithless man and the film would show what gets him back together again.[[274]](#cite_note-Rebellion_televised-274) At some point, McGregor did some testing for the film.[[275]](#cite_note-costume_test-275)

When [Stuart Beattie](/wiki/Stuart_Beattie "Stuart Beattie") pitched his three Obi-Wan Kenobi stories to Lucasfilm, he explained that there are three different evolutions for the character to make to go from Obi-Wan to Ben. The first story was about surrendering to the will of the force and the second story was about Kenobi coming to terms with his own mortality. Lucasfilm and McGregor were on board with the idea of a trilogy.[[276]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Trilogy-276) In another meeting, Beattie explained that his two core ideas for the project involved Kenobi leaving Tatooine and coming face-to-face with Darth Vader. He was told that neither of those could happen, so he cited *Return of the Jedi* when Vader told Luke Skywalker that Kenobi once believed there was still good in him. Beattie explained that this never happened in *Revenge of the Sith*, which convinced them that he had a point. He added that people would need to believe that Vader killed Anakin Skywalker. This convinced the team to hire Beattie to write the script for the first of three Kenobi feature films. One of his main purposes in writing the story was to show Kenobi going on a journey to accept the fact that Anakin Skywalker had been killed by Vader.[[277]](#cite_note-Vader_originally_won_battle-277)

 [![Concept art of Obi-Wan Kenobi riding Akkani by ](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b2/Obi-WanKenobiRidingEopieConceptArt.png/revision/latest?cb=20220828194626) [![Concept art of Obi-Wan Kenobi riding Akkani by ](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b2/Obi-WanKenobiRidingEopieConceptArt.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20220828194626)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b2/Obi-WanKenobiRidingEopieConceptArt.png/revision/latest?cb=20220828194626) 

Concept art of Obi-Wan Kenobi riding Akkani by [Anton Grandert](/wiki/Anton_Grandert "Anton Grandert")

 

Beattie wrote Vader as being obsessed with Kenobi and revenge. From the beginning of Beattie's story, Emperor Palpatine would tell Vader to forget Kenobi and focus on the present problems. In one scene Palpatine sent Vader to crush a rebel uprising and he was trying to forget Kenobi. Vader told Palpatine that Kenobi and Yoda were the two biggest threats, causing Palpatine to get angry and remind Vader of his place.[[277]](#cite_note-Vader_originally_won_battle-277) When Cody went into a town on Tatooine, he would take Kenobi into an alley and hold a knife to his throat. Eventually, it would be revealed that Cody had his [inhibitor chip](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip") removed, allowing him to refrain from hunting Kenobi. Cody then became Kenobi's "secret buddy" and they would both feel overwhelmed by guilt. Beattie's idea was that when Kenobi left Tatooine, he left Cody in charge of Luke Skywalker. Cody was planned as a way to show how disconnected Kenobi was from the Force due to forcing his will upon young Skywalker in a manner similar to when [Superman](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Superman "wikipedia:Superman") lost his powers in the [1980](/wiki/1980 "1980") film *[Superman II](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Superman_II "wikipedia:Superman II")*. Beattie wanted Kenobi to surrender to the will of the Force, allowing his powers to come back in a climactic moment similar to when Superman's powers returned in the film.[[278]](#cite_note-Cody_Scrapped_Role-278)

 [![Concept art of a duel between Obi-Wan Kenobi and Darth Vader](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f5/Obi-WanKenobiVsDarthVaderConceptArt.png/revision/latest?cb=20220828182913) [![Concept art of a duel between Obi-Wan Kenobi and Darth Vader](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f5/Obi-WanKenobiVsDarthVaderConceptArt.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20220828182913)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f5/Obi-WanKenobiVsDarthVaderConceptArt.png/revision/latest?cb=20220828182913) 

Concept art of a duel between Obi-Wan Kenobi and Darth Vader

 

Beattie created the Inquisitor Reva to give the Jedi someone to defeat or save because he'd be unable to save Vader. Kenobi told the Inquisitor Reva that Vader was Anakin Skywalker, allowing her to realize she had been wrong the whole time. Reva then told Vader that she killed Kenobi, prompting him to kill the Inquisitor. This action saved Kenobi and ended Vader's obsession with the Jedi.[[279]](#cite_note-Reva_killed_in_script-279) Vader and Kenobi would duel on a space station that was falling apart in the atmosphere of a large planet. The whole story would build up to Kenobi taking off or slashing Vader's helmet and giving him a scar. Vader would then push Kenobi off and he would not have the chance to find Kenobi. Seeing Skywalker's face convinced Kenobi that Vader killed Anakin Skywalker. Beattie found it important to separate the two during the duel because he believed Kenobi would kill Vader if he had the chance. At the end of the story, Vader would believe Kenobi was dead, which would explain why Vader stopped hunting Kenobi and justify why he was shocked to learn that his master was alive in *A New Hope*.[[277]](#cite_note-Vader_originally_won_battle-277) After the poor box office performance of *[Solo: A Star Wars Story](/wiki/Solo:_A_Star_Wars_Story "Solo: A Star Wars Story")*, it was decided that no more spin-off films would be made, and Beattie left the project.[[276]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Trilogy-276)

On [September 27](/wiki/September_27 "September 27"), 2019, [StarWars.com](/wiki/StarWars.com "StarWars.com") announced that [Deborah Chow](/wiki/Deborah_Chow "Deborah Chow") would direct the *[Star Wars: Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Star Wars: Obi-Wan Kenobi")* television series and it would be written by [Hossein Amini](/wiki/Hossein_Amini "Hossein Amini").[[280]](#cite_note-SW_Deborah-280) As the crew came together to work toward a summer, [2020](/wiki/2020 "2020") production start date, Lucasfilm president [Kathleen Kennedy](/wiki/Kathleen_Kennedy "Kathleen Kennedy") became concerned with the direction the scripts were heading in. The crew wanted to make a hopeful, uplifting story, but they found this to be difficult because of the bleak state that Kenobi was in after *Revenge of the Sith*. Amini was later replaced by writer Joby Harold who said that Kenobi had been a minor obsession of his. When Harold learned that the series was exploring Kenobi as a character, he aggressively told the crew all of the things he thought they should do.[[265]](#cite_note-17_year-265) Harold took Stuart Beattie's scripts and turned them into a six-hour series.[[276]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Trilogy-276) Harold and Chow crafted a new story that took place 10 years after *Revenge of the Sith*. Kenobi was meant to be a lost and broken man who felt responsible for what happened to Anakin Skywalker in *Revenge of the Sith*. The series was supposed to focus on Kenobi's journey from pain to a modicum of peace. Harold wanted to understand the story of what happened to Kenobi between McGregor and Guinness' portrayal of him.[[265]](#cite_note-17_year-265) Chow wanted the series to focus on who Ben Kenobi is instead of his Jedi identity.[[262]](#cite_note-Return-262) Chow said the crew inherited some of the original plot, but they made significant changes and added a few different elements.[[265]](#cite_note-17_year-265)

The main goal was to slow everything down so that the imagery can have as much weight as possible, especially when it was going to help articulate Kenobi's arc. Because of this, the [first episode's](/wiki/Part_I "Part I") closing image was Kenobi's lightsaber on his hip. This goal was also the reason the [second episode](/wiki/Part_II "Part II") ended with Kenobi holding his lightsaber and not using it, causing the use of the weapon to be meaningful.[[281]](#cite_note-Leia_Secret-281) Harold tried to think of something that would be seismic enough to make Kenobi leave Tatooine, which led to him writing young Leia Organa as a call to action for Kenobi.[[282]](#cite_note-Vader_terrifying-282) She was meant to bring out a maternal sense in Kenobi that told him life is not just about living by the book. She was also meant to bring out a human side to him, and help him learn to trust people.[[262]](#cite_note-Return-262) Per director [J.J. Abrams](/wiki/J.J._Abrams "J.J. Abrams")' advice, Harold decided that it should be a massive moment when Jedi use the Force and it must be earned, so Kenobi didn't use the Force until he saved Organa from a fall in the second episode. He looked at the films [*Paper Moon*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paper_Moon_(film) "wikipedia:Paper Moon (film)") and [*Midnight Run*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Midnight_Run "wikipedia:Midnight Run") for influence on Organa and Kenobi's relationship after the former's rescue on Daiyu. Harold wanted the series to begin with Order 66 to remind the audience of where Kenobi's journey began and to establish that the stakes are high for everyone.[[282]](#cite_note-Vader_terrifying-282) During the writing process, Harold thought of having Kenobi learn that Anakin Skywalker survived their duel on Mustafar to get the series to a place of intense drama for Kenobi. He first had to ask[[283]](#cite_note-Harold_justified-283) *Star Wars* lore advisor[[199]](#cite_note-Kenobi_1-199) [Pablo Hidalgo](/wiki/Pablo_Hidalgo "Pablo Hidalgo") how much Kenobi knows during the show's time period, and Harold was given permission to use the scene.[[283]](#cite_note-Harold_justified-283) Harold had Kenobi and Vader duel in the series because he found that there was no line in a *A New Hope* that said they couldn't. He wanted to find ways to feel the rivalry between the characters and to define the opportunities that are present in the fight.[[281]](#cite_note-Leia_Secret-281)

 [![Obi-Wan Kenobi's costume was designed by Suttirat Anne Larlarb](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/62/Obi-WanKenobiCostumeSDCC.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220828195402) [![Obi-Wan Kenobi's costume was designed by Suttirat Anne Larlarb](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/62/Obi-WanKenobiCostumeSDCC.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20220828195402)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/62/Obi-WanKenobiCostumeSDCC.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220828195402) 

Obi-Wan Kenobi's costume was designed by Suttirat Anne Larlarb

 

To prepare for portraying Kenobi again, McGregor watched all nine movies in the [Skywalker saga](/wiki/Star_Wars_saga "Star Wars saga") and he started reading [science fiction](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Science_fiction "wikipedia:Science fiction"), including books by [Iain M. Banks](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Iain_Banks "wikipedia:Iain Banks").[[266]](#cite_note-Kenobi_preparation-266) To relearn his Kenobi voice, McGregor listened to a sound file that has all of Alec Guinness' lines from *A New Hope*.[[284]](#cite_note-Rotten_Tomatoes_TV-284) McGregor wanted Kenobi to have an unkempt hairstyle and appearance to represent how Kenobi is faithless and somewhat given up.[[268]](#cite_note-Hair_Breakdown-268) When playing Kenobi, he made it seem like the character would grow up to be Alec Guinness by trying to sound and feel like Guinness, but he did not want to do an impersonation.[[284]](#cite_note-Rotten_Tomatoes_TV-284)

On the first day of production, McGregor starting filming his scenes in the Sandwhale Farm set.[[262]](#cite_note-Return-262) Kenobi's costume was designed by costume designer [Suttirat Anne Larlarb](/wiki/Suttirat_Anne_Larlarb "Suttirat Anne Larlarb"). She wanted to make Kenobi recognizable to fans, but his costume needed to show that he is a Jedi in hiding. For the story to make sense, Kenobi needed to match other residents of Tatooine by wearing clothes of simple construction and in readily available colors. A "woady" blue top was added to contrast with the shades of brown, beige, and cream associated with the Jedi.[[285]](#cite_note-Suttirat_interview-285) McGregor and Christensen trained with lightsabers for the flashback of Kenobi and Skywalker training[[262]](#cite_note-Return-262) in the [fifth episode](/wiki/Part_V "Part V").[[51]](#cite_note-Kenobi_5-51) They both had dots on their face for the de-aging technology.[[262]](#cite_note-Return-262)

### Influence in popular culture

#### Meme culture

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Hello there](/wiki/Hello_there "Hello there")

:   "*Hello there.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bd/HelloThere-RotS.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250403185053)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:HelloThere-RotS.flac "File:HelloThere-RotS.flac"))[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_III-13)

Amongst the *Star Wars* fandom, the line "[hello there](/wiki/Hello_there "Hello there")"—which Obi-Wan Kenobi says upon confronting General Grievous on Utapau in *Revenge of the Sith*—has become an [internet meme](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internet_meme "wikipedia:Internet meme").[[286]](#cite_note-Screen_Rant_article-286) The line was first uttered by Kenobi in *A New Hope*.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) The meme has even been referenced in official material, with Kenobi saying the line to raiders in [*Age of Republic - Obi-Wan Kenobi* 1](/wiki/Age_of_Republic_-_Obi-Wan_Kenobi_1 "Age of Republic - Obi-Wan Kenobi 1"),[[11]](#cite_note-Age_Kenobi-11) to Luke Skywalker in *Kenobi* [Part VI](/wiki/Part_VI "Part VI"),[[210]](#cite_note-Kenobi_6-210) and to stormtrooper [JM-909](/wiki/JM-909 "JM-909") in [*Obi-Wan* 5](/wiki/Obi-Wan_5 "Obi-Wan 5").[[223]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_5-223) The line was repeatedly featured in *[The LEGO Star Wars Holiday Special](/wiki/The_LEGO_Star_Wars_Holiday_Special "The LEGO Star Wars Holiday Special")*, a non-[canon](/wiki/Canon "Canon") [Disney+](/wiki/Disney%2B "Disney+") special in which Kenobi is voiced by Taylor.[[287]](#cite_note-Lego_Special-287)

#### Ulica Obi-Wana Kenobiego

 [![Ulica Obi-Wana Kenobiego](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Kenobi_Street.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20060506180412) [![Ulica Obi-Wana Kenobiego](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Kenobi_Street.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20060506180412)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Kenobi_Street.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20060506180412) 

Ulica Obi-Wana Kenobiego

 

Ulica Obi-Wana Kenobiego ("Obi-Wan Kenobi's Street") is a street in the town of [Grabowiec](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Grabowiec,_Toru%C5%84_County "wikipedia:Grabowiec, Toruń County"), [Poland](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Poland "wikipedia:Poland") that was named after Kenobi in [April](/wiki/April "April") [2005](/wiki/2005 "2005"). The initiator of naming the street was Leszek Budkiewicz, a *Star Wars* fan and a Community Council member. His motion was accepted by the Lubicz Community Council in resolution XXVIII/373/04 of [December 30](/wiki/December_30 "December 30"), [2004](/wiki/2004 "2004"), and came into force fourteen days later.[[288]](#cite_note-bip-288) Since then, the street has become a significant spot for fan activities, to the point of holding large fan conventions attended by fans from Europe.[[289]](#cite_note-StarForce-289)

In May [2008](/wiki/2008 "2008"), Polish fans received a letter from [Stephen J. Sansweet](/wiki/Stephen_J._Sansweet "Stephen J. Sansweet") and [Mary Franklin](/wiki/Mary_Franklin "Mary Franklin") on behalf of [Lucasfilm](/wiki/Lucasfilm "Lucasfilm"), containing a congratulatory note and an official recognition of the street.[[290]](#cite_note-YouTube-street-290) The street was visited by the *Star Wars* actors [Gerald Home](/wiki/Gerald_Home "Gerald Home") and [Paul Blake](/wiki/Paul_Blake "Paul Blake") in 2008.[[291]](#cite_note-Imperial_City-291)

### *LEGO Star Wars: The Freemaker Adventures*

In the non-canon series *[LEGO Star Wars: The Freemaker Adventures](/wiki/LEGO_Star_Wars:_The_Freemaker_Adventures "LEGO Star Wars: The Freemaker Adventures")* [Season One](/wiki/LEGO_Star_Wars:_The_Freemaker_Adventures_Season_One "LEGO Star Wars: The Freemaker Adventures Season One") episode, "[Crossing Paths](/wiki/Crossing_Paths "Crossing Paths")," Kenobi was voiced by [Michael Donovan](/wiki/Michael_Donovan "Michael Donovan").[[292]](#cite_note-CP-292) Kenobi would later make an appearance in a hologram in "[Duel of Destiny](/wiki/Duel_of_Destiny "Duel of Destiny")."[[293]](#cite_note-DOD-293)

[↑](#cite_ref-Mandalore_date_33-0) According to [*The Official Star Wars Fact File Part* 98](/wiki/The_Official_Star_Wars_Fact_File_Part_98 "The Official Star Wars Fact File Part 98") MAN 1-4: Mandalore, the [Mandalorian](/wiki/Mandalorian "Mandalorian") Civil War took place around 20 [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"). *[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas "Star Wars: Galactic Atlas")* establishes that the [Clone](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") Wars took place starting in [22 BBY](/wiki/22_BBY "22 BBY") through [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"). Therefore, the Mandalorian Civil War can be dated to around [42 BBY](/wiki/42_BBY "42 BBY") to [39 BBY](/wiki/39_BBY "39 BBY"). By the [time](/wiki/Time "Time") of [*Padawan*](/wiki/Padawan_(novel) "Padawan (novel)"),*[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates the events of to [41 BBY](/wiki/41_BBY "41 BBY"), author [Kiersten White](/wiki/Kiersten_White "Kiersten White") establishes that the novel's plot was [explicitly written](https://web.archive.org/web/20220226214721/https://dorksideoftheforce.com/2022/02/26/kiersten-white-talks-star-wars-padawan/) to convey that he had not met [Satine Kryze](/wiki/Satine_Kryze "Satine Kryze"). As Obi-Wan Kenobi is established to have met Kryze during the Mandalorian Civil War in [TCW mini logo](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars") *[Star Wars: The Clone Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars")* — "[Voyage of Temptation](/wiki/Voyage_of_Temptation "Voyage of Temptation")", the war must have taken place between around [41 BBY](/wiki/41_BBY "41 BBY") and [39 BBY](/wiki/39_BBY "39 BBY"). 34. ↑ [34.0](#cite_ref-Voyage_of_Temptation_34-0) [34.1](#cite_ref-Voyage_of_Temptation_34-1) [↑](#cite_ref-SW20Date_243-0) [*Star Wars* (2020) 20](/wiki/Star_Wars_(2020)_20 "Star Wars (2020) 20") takes place after the [Escape from Cloud City](/wiki/Escape_from_Cloud_City "Escape from Cloud City"), which is dated to [3 ABY](/wiki/3_ABY "3 ABY") by *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")*. Additionally, [Sliro Barsha](/wiki/Sliro_Barsha "Sliro Barsha") dies during the events of *[Star Wars Outlaws](/wiki/Star_Wars_Outlaws "Star Wars Outlaws")*, which [Premium-Era-real](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/Premium-Era-real.png/revision/latest?cb=20241019125517) [Visit a Galaxy Far, Far Away with our Star Wars liveblog direct from San Diego Comic-Con 2024!](https://www.thepopverse.com/live-star-wars-stories-from-galaxy-far-away-san-diego-comic-con-2024-high-republic) on [Popverse](https://www.thepopverse.com) ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20240805210120/https://www.thepopverse.com/live-star-wars-stories-from-galaxy-far-away-san-diego-comic-con-2024-high-republic) archived on [August 5](/wiki/August_5 "August 5"), [2024](/wiki/2024 "2024")) dates to 3 ABY. As he is alive during [*Crimson Reign* 5](/wiki/Crimson_Reign_5 "Crimson Reign 5"), and the events of *Star Wars* (2020) 20 precede the comic, it must also take place during that year. 244.
